# Question 151 — Crohn Disease with Perianal Fistula / 克罗恩病伴肛周瘘管

## Question Stem / 题干

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 100%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><p>A <strong>67-year-old woman</strong> comes to the physician because of a <strong>2-month history of perirectal pain</strong> that <strong>worsens with bowel movements</strong> and a <strong>thick, yellow rectal discharge</strong>. She has hypertension and <strong>psoriasis</strong>. Her medications are metoprolol and topical fluocinolone cream. There is no family history of serious illness. She does not smoke cigarettes, drink alcohol, or use illicit drugs. Her temperature is 37°C (98.6°F), pulse is 80/min, respirations are 14/min, and blood pressure is 136/70 mm Hg. The abdomen is soft, nontender, and nondistended. Rectal examination shows brown stool. <strong>The skin of the posterior perineal wall is erythematous with a draining sinus tract.</strong> Test of the stool for occult blood is <strong>positive</strong>.</p>
<p><strong>Q: Which of the following is the most likely diagnosis?</strong></p>
<p>A) Clostridium difficile colitis<br />
B) Colon cancer<br />
C) Crohn disease<br />
D) Diverticular abscess<br />
E) Ulcerative colitis</p>
<p><strong>Correct Answer: C</strong></p></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
</tbody>
</table>

## 1. Key Stem Clues / 题干关键词抓考点

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 50%" />
<col style="width: 50%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Key Stem Clue</strong><br />
<strong>关键词</strong></th>
<th><strong>Why It Matters</strong><br />
<strong>为什么重要</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>Perirectal pain worsening with bowel movements, 2-month course<br />
排便时加重的肛周疼痛，病程 2 个月</td>
<td>Chronic perianal symptoms favor IBD over acute infectious etiology; duration rules out simple abscess<br />
慢性肛周症状支持 IBD 而非急性感染；病程排除单纯脓肿</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Thick, yellow rectal discharge<br />
浓稠黄色直肠分泌物</td>
<td>Purulent drainage indicates fistula or sinus tract — hallmark of transmural inflammation<br />
脓性引流提示瘘管或窦道——透壁性炎症的标志性表现</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Draining sinus tract on posterior perineal wall<br />
后会阴壁引流窦道</td>
<td>Pathognomonic of fistula formation; only Crohn disease among options causes transmural inflammation enabling this complication<br />
瘘管形成的特征性表现；选项中只有克罗恩病可导致透壁性炎症形成此并发症</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Psoriasis<br />
银屑病</td>
<td>A recognized extraintestinal manifestation of IBD, particularly Crohn disease<br />
IBD（尤其是克罗恩病）公认的肠外表现</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Positive fecal occult blood<br />
大便隐血阳性</td>
<td>Indicates GI mucosal bleeding consistent with IBD-related ulceration<br />
提示胃肠道黏膜出血，与 IBD 相关溃疡一致</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>No fever, normal temperature, no leukocytosis mentioned<br />
无发热，体温正常，无白细胞增多</td>
<td>Argues against acute diverticular abscess (which typically presents with fever and leukocytosis)<br />
不支持急性憩室脓肿（通常伴发热和白细胞增多）</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

## 2. Mechanism / 机制理解

**Crohn disease** is characterized by **transmural (full-thickness) inflammation** of the GI tract, which uniquely enables the formation of **fistulas, sinus tracts, and abscesses** — complications absent in diseases limited to mucosal layers:

**克罗恩病**的特征是消化道**透壁（全层）炎症**，这一特性使其能够形成**瘘管、窦道和脓肿**——这些并发症在仅限于黏膜层的疾病中不会出现：

- Transmural inflammation penetrates through all layers of the bowel wall → tracking of infection along tissue planes → **sinus tract and fistula formation**\
  透壁炎症穿透肠壁全层 → 感染沿组织平面扩散 → 形成**窦道和瘘管**

- Chronic granulomatous inflammation triggers non-caseating granuloma formation — a histopathologic hallmark distinguishing Crohn from UC\
  慢性肉芽肿性炎症触发非干酪性肉芽肿形成——是区分克罗恩病与 UC 的组织病理学标志

- Disease can affect any GI segment from mouth to anus with **skip lesions** (discontinuous, patchy involvement)\
  疾病可累及从口腔到肛门任何消化道节段，呈**跳跃性病变**（不连续、斑片状受累）

- Terminal ileum predilection leads to malabsorption of vitamin B12 and bile salts with downstream nutritional consequences\
  末端回肠好发导致维生素 B12 和胆盐吸收障碍，引发一系列营养后果

**Anatomic rule of thumb:** Crohn = transmural = fistulas/abscesses/strictures; UC = mucosal/submucosal only = fistulas are rare.

**解剖小窍门:** 克罗恩病 = 透壁炎症 = 可出现瘘管/脓肿/狭窄；溃疡性结肠炎 = 仅黏膜/黏膜下层 = 罕见瘘管。

## 3. Correct Answer (C) — Crohn Disease with Perianal Fistula / 正确答案 (C) — 克罗恩病伴肛周瘘管

**Crohn disease** is a chronic, transmural inflammatory bowel disease that can affect any part of the GI tract and is uniquely associated with perianal complications occurring in up to 40% of patients:

**克罗恩病**是一种慢性、透壁性炎症性肠病，可累及消化道任何部位，与肛周并发症有独特相关性，发生率可达 40%：

- Perianal fistulas, sinus tracts, abscesses, and skin tags are classic perianal manifestations that no other option in this question can produce\
  肛周瘘管、窦道、脓肿和皮赘是经典的肛周表现，本题其他选项均无法产生

- Extraintestinal manifestations include skin (erythema nodosum, pyoderma gangrenosum, **psoriasis**), joints (arthritis), and eyes (uveitis, episcleritis)\
  肠外表现包括皮肤（结节性红斑、坏疽性脓皮病、**银屑病**）、关节（关节炎）和眼部（葡萄膜炎、巩膜外层炎）

- Endoscopy shows cobblestone mucosa, aphthous ulcers, skip lesions, and rectal sparing; biopsy reveals non-caseating granulomas\
  内镜下见鹅卵石样黏膜、口疮样溃疡、跳跃性病变和直肠豁免；活检示非干酪性肉芽肿

**Diagnosis:** Colonoscopy with biopsy showing transmural inflammation and non-caseating granulomas; elevated CRP/ESR; imaging (barium follow-through showing "string sign" at terminal ileum)

**诊断:** 结肠镜活检示透壁性炎症和非干酪性肉芽肿；CRP/ESR 升高；影像学（钡剂造影示末端回肠"线样征"）

**Treatment:** 5-ASA for mild disease; corticosteroids for acute flares; immunomodulators (azathioprine, 6-MP); anti-TNF biologics (infliximab, adalimumab) for fistulizing/refractory disease; surgery for abscesses/strictures

**治疗:** 轻度用 5-ASA；急性发作用糖皮质激素；免疫调节剂（硫唑嘌呤、6-MP）；瘘管/难治性病例用抗 TNF 生物制剂（英夫利昔、阿达木）；脓肿/狭窄需手术

## 4. Options Elimination / 错误选项排除逻辑

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 33%" />
<col style="width: 33%" />
<col style="width: 33%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Option</strong><br />
<strong>选项</strong></th>
<th><strong>Why Wrong</strong><br />
<strong>为什么错</strong></th>
<th><strong>Key Discriminator</strong><br />
<strong>鉴别要点</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>A — Clostridium difficile colitis<br />
A — 艰难梭菌结肠炎</td>
<td>Presents with watery or bloody diarrhea and pseudomembranes on colonoscopy; does NOT form fistulas or draining sinus tracts<br />
表现为水样或血性腹泻，结肠镜下见假膜；不形成瘘管或引流窦道</td>
<td>C. diff: acute onset, associated with antibiotic use, pseudomembranes; no perianal sinus tracts<br />
艰难梭菌：急性起病，与抗生素使用相关，见假膜；无肛周窦道</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>B — Colon cancer<br />
B — 结肠癌</td>
<td>May cause occult GI bleeding or altered bowel habits, but does NOT produce perianal fistulas or draining sinus tracts<br />
可引起隐性出血或排便习惯改变，但不产生肛周瘘管或引流窦道</td>
<td>Colon cancer: painless bleeding, mass lesion on imaging; perianal fistulas are not a feature<br />
结肠癌：无痛性出血，影像见肿块；肛周瘘管不是其特征</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>C — Crohn disease ✓<br />
C — 克罗恩病 ✓</td>
<td>CORRECT — Transmural inflammation creates the perianal sinus tract, purulent discharge, and fistula seen here; psoriasis confirms extraintestinal involvement<br />
正确——透壁性炎症形成本例的肛周窦道、脓性分泌物和瘘管；银屑病证实肠外受累</td>
<td>Transmural inflammation = fistula/abscess formation; perianal sinus tract is pathognomonic<br />
透壁性炎症 = 瘘管/脓肿形成；肛周窦道是特征性表现</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>D — Diverticular abscess<br />
D — 憩室脓肿</td>
<td>Presents with fever, left lower quadrant pain, leukocytosis, and localized tenderness; cutaneous draining tracts are uncommon sequelae<br />
表现为发热、左下腹疼痛、白细胞增多和局部压痛；皮肤引流窦道为罕见后遗症</td>
<td>Diverticular abscess: fever + LLQ pain + leukocytosis; this patient has none of these findings<br />
憩室脓肿：发热 + 左下腹疼痛 + 白细胞增多；本例均无这些表现</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>E — Ulcerative colitis<br />
E — 溃疡性结肠炎</td>
<td>Causes mucosal and submucosal inflammation only; transmural complications (fistulas, abscesses) are uncommon; always involves rectum continuously<br />
仅引起黏膜和黏膜下层炎症；透壁性并发症（瘘管、脓肿）少见；始终连续性累及直肠</td>
<td>UC: continuous disease from rectum, no skip lesions, no perianal fistulas; tenesmus is more prominent<br />
UC：从直肠连续受累，无跳跃性病变，无肛周瘘管；里急后重更突出</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

*The most tempting distractor is E (Ulcerative colitis) — both are IBD with rectal symptoms, but the draining sinus tract is the decisive discriminator: UC's inflammation is confined to mucosa/submucosa and cannot produce fistulas, whereas Crohn's transmural inflammation makes fistula formation a defining complication.*

最容易混淆的干扰项是 E（溃疡性结肠炎）——两者均为有直肠症状的 IBD，但引流窦道是决定性鉴别点：UC 炎症局限于黏膜/黏膜下层，无法产生瘘管，而克罗恩病的透壁性炎症使瘘管形成成为其定义性并发症。

## 5. High-Yield Summary Table — Crohn Disease vs. Ulcerative Colitis / 克罗恩病与溃疡性结肠炎对比

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 33%" />
<col style="width: 33%" />
<col style="width: 33%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Feature</strong><br />
<strong>特征</strong></th>
<th><strong>Crohn Disease</strong><br />
<strong>克罗恩病</strong></th>
<th><strong>Ulcerative Colitis</strong><br />
<strong>溃疡性结肠炎</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>GI location<br />
消化道部位</td>
<td>Any segment, mouth to anus<br />
任何节段，口腔至肛门</td>
<td>Colon only, always starts at rectum<br />
仅结肠，始终起于直肠</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Distribution<br />
分布模式</td>
<td>Skip lesions (discontinuous)<br />
跳跃性病变（不连续）</td>
<td>Continuous, retrograde from rectum<br />
连续性，从直肠向近端逆行</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Depth of inflammation<br />
炎症深度</td>
<td>Transmural (all layers)<br />
透壁（全层）</td>
<td>Mucosal + submucosal only<br />
仅黏膜 + 黏膜下层</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Fistulas / abscesses<br />
瘘管 / 脓肿</td>
<td>Common — defining complication<br />
常见——定义性并发症</td>
<td>Rare<br />
少见</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Rectal involvement<br />
直肠受累</td>
<td>Often spared (rectal sparing)<br />
常豁免（直肠豁免）</td>
<td>Always involved<br />
始终受累</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Biopsy hallmark<br />
活检标志</td>
<td>Non-caseating granulomas<br />
非干酪性肉芽肿</td>
<td>Crypt abscesses; no granulomas<br />
隐窝脓肿；无肉芽肿</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>PSC association<br />
原发性硬化性胆管炎</td>
<td>Less common<br />
较少见</td>
<td>Strongly associated<br />
显著相关</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

## 6. One-Sentence Summary & Memory Hook / 一句话总结 & 记忆钩

**In Crohn disease, transmural inflammation of any GI segment produces fistulas, sinus tracts, and skip lesions — a draining perianal sinus tract with purulent discharge is pathognomonic and decisively distinguishes Crohn from ulcerative colitis.**

**克罗恩病的消化道任意节段透壁性炎症可产生瘘管、窦道和跳跃性病变——伴脓性分泌物的引流性肛周窦道是其特征性表现，可决定性地将克罗恩病与溃疡性结肠炎区分开来。**

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 100%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><p><strong>Memory Hook — "SKIP" for Crohn Disease / 记忆钩 — "SKIP" 记克罗恩病四大特征:</strong></p>
<p>• <strong>S</strong>kip lesions — discontinuous, patchy bowel involvement / 跳跃性病变——不连续、斑片状肠道受累<br />
• <strong>K</strong>nife-cut ulcers → cobblestone mucosa, transmural depth / 刀切样溃疡 → 鹅卵石样黏膜，透壁深度<br />
• <strong>I</strong>leum (terminal) — most common site; B12 + bile salt malabsorption / 末端回肠——最常见受累部位；维生素 B12 + 胆盐吸收障碍<br />
• <strong>P</strong>erianal disease — fistulas, sinus tracts, abscesses in up to 40% / 肛周病变——瘘管、窦道、脓肿，发生率可达 40%</p></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
</tbody>
</table>

## 7. High-Yield Topic Knowledge — Crohn Disease Complications & Diagnosis / 高频知识表 — 克罗恩病并发症与诊断

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 50%" />
<col style="width: 50%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Topic</strong><br />
<strong>考点</strong></th>
<th><strong>Key Points</strong><br />
<strong>要点</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>Fistula types in Crohn<br />
克罗恩病瘘管类型</td>
<td>Enterocutaneous (bowel to skin), enterovesical (bowel to bladder → pneumaturia/fecaluria), rectovaginal, enteroenteric; perianal most common<br />
肠皮瘘（肠 → 皮肤），肠膀胱瘘（肠 → 膀胱 → 气尿/粪尿），直肠阴道瘘，肠肠瘘；肛周最常见</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Terminal ileum complications<br />
末端回肠并发症</td>
<td>B12 deficiency (megaloblastic anemia); bile salt malabsorption → fat-soluble vitamin deficiency (A, D, E, K) + gallstones; oxalate hyperabsorption → calcium oxalate kidney stones<br />
维生素 B12 缺乏（巨幼细胞性贫emia）；胆盐吸收障碍 → 脂溶性维生素缺乏（A、D、E、K）+ 胆石症；草酸过度吸收 → 草酸钙肾结石</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Extraintestinal manifestations<br />
肠外表现</td>
<td>Parallel IBD activity: peripheral arthritis, episcleritis, erythema nodosum; Independent of IBD: ankylosing spondylitis, uveitis, PSC (rare in Crohn)<br />
与 IBD 活动度平行：外周关节炎、巩膜外层炎、结节性红斑；独立于 IBD：强直性脊柱炎、葡萄膜炎、PSC（克罗恩少见）</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Imaging findings<br />
影像学表现</td>
<td>Barium follow-through: "string sign" (luminal narrowing at terminal ileum from stricture); CT/MRI: bowel wall thickening, creeping fat, mesenteric lymphadenopathy<br />
钡剂小肠造影："线样征"（狭窄导致末端回肠管腔变窄）；CT/MRI：肠壁增厚、爬行脂肪征、肠系膜淋巴结肿大</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Biologic therapy for fistulas<br />
瘘管的生物制剂治疗</td>
<td>Infliximab (anti-TNF-α) — ACCENT II trial demonstrated sustained fistula closure; combined with antibiotics (metronidazole, ciprofloxacin) for perianal Crohn<br />
英夫利昔单抗（抗 TNF-α）——ACCENT II 试验证实持续瘘管闭合；肛周克罗恩病联合抗生素（甲硝唑、环丙沙星）治疗</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Colorectal cancer surveillance<br />
结直肠癌监测</td>
<td>Risk increases after 8-10 years of disease; annual or biennial colonoscopy surveillance recommended in extensive colonic Crohn<br />
病程 8-10 年后风险增加；广泛结肠型克罗恩病建议每年或每两年结肠镜监测</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

## 8. Extensions / 延伸扩展

- **Perianal fistula imaging:** MRI pelvis is the gold standard for mapping fistula anatomy (relation to sphincters) before surgical intervention; Parks classification divides fistulas by relation to external sphincter\
  **肛周瘘管影像学:** 盆腔 MRI 是手术前定位瘘管解剖（与括约肌关系）的金标准；Parks 分类按与外括约肌的关系划分瘘管

- **Smoking paradox in IBD:** Smoking worsens Crohn disease (doubles relapse risk) but paradoxically protects against ulcerative colitis — a classic board distinction\
  **IBD 中的吸烟悖论:** 吸烟加重克罗恩病（复发风险翻倍），但对溃疡性结肠炎有矛盾性保护作用——经典考试鉴别点

- **Differential for perianal sinus tracts:** Crohn disease (most likely in young patients), hidradenitis suppurativa, actinomycosis, tuberculosis, and complex cryptoglandular fistula-in-ano\
  **肛周窦道的鉴别诊断:** 克罗恩病（年轻患者最常见），化脓性汗腺炎，放线菌病，结核病，复杂性肛隐窝腺源性肛瘘

- **Surgical indications in Crohn:** Bowel obstruction from stricture, intra-abdominal abscess (drainage + delayed resection), perforation, medically refractory disease, and fistulas unresponsive to biologics\
  **克罗恩病手术指征:** 狭窄导致肠梗阻，腹腔内脓肿（引流 + 延期切除），穿孔，药物难治性疾病，以及生物制剂无效的瘘管

# Question 152 — Thymic-Parathyroid Dysplasia (DiGeorge Syndrome) / 胸腺-甲状旁腺发育不良（DiGeorge 综合征）

## Question Stem / 题干

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 100%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><p>Twelve hours after discharge from the hospital, a <strong>2-day-old male newborn</strong> is brought to the emergency department after having a <strong>seizure</strong>. His parents report that he <strong>stiffened, and his eyes rolled back for 3 or 4 minutes</strong>; then he went limp. He was delivered vaginally at term to a 20-year-old woman, gravida 1, para 1, following an uncomplicated pregnancy; his weight on delivery was 3062 g (6 lb 12 oz). The patient's mother used to drink two glasses of wine each evening with dinner but stopped drinking alcohol when she learned she was pregnant at 4 weeks' gestation. She has never smoked cigarettes or used illicit drugs. On arrival, the infant is awake but <strong>sluggish</strong>. Examination shows <strong>hypertelorism</strong> and <strong>low-set ears</strong>. The lungs are clear to auscultation. There are no murmurs. A chest x-ray shows a <strong>narrow mediastinum</strong> and a <strong>right-sided aortic arch</strong>. Which of the following is the most likely diagnosis?</p>
<p><strong>Q: Most likely diagnosis?</strong></p>
<p>A) Down syndrome<br />
B) Severe combined immunodeficiency<br />
C) Thymic-parathyroid dysplasia<br />
D) Trisomy 13 syndrome<br />
E) Wiskott-Aldrich syndrome</p>
<p><strong>Correct Answer: C</strong></p></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
</tbody>
</table>

## 1. Key Stem Clues / 题干关键词抓考点

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 50%" />
<col style="width: 50%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Key Stem Clue</strong><br />
<strong>关键词</strong></th>
<th><strong>Why It Matters</strong><br />
<strong>为什么重要</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>2-day-old newborn with seizure, no murmur<br />
出生 2 天新生儿抽搐，无心杂音</td>
<td>Neonatal seizure without structural cardiac murmur → hypocalcemia from parathyroid failure is the top cause<br />
无心杂音的新生儿抽搐 → 甲状旁腺功能不全所致低钙血症是首要病因</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Hypertelorism and low-set ears<br />
眼距增宽，低位耳</td>
<td>Craniofacial dysmorphism from failed 3rd/4th pharyngeal pouch development (neural crest migration defect)<br />
第 3/4 咽囊发育失败所致颅面部畸形（神经嵴细胞迁移缺陷）</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Narrow mediastinum on chest x-ray<br />
胸片示纵隔狭窄</td>
<td>Absent or hypoplastic thymus leaves no thymic shadow → narrow superior mediastinum on CXR<br />
胸腺缺如或发育不全 → 无胸腺影 → 胸片上纵隔上部狭窄</td>

右位主动脉弓</td>
<td>Conotruncal cardiac anomaly — hallmark of 22q11.2 deletion affecting aortic arch derivatives<br />
圆锥干心脏异常——22q11.2 缺失影响主动脉弓衍生物的标志</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Awake but sluggish<br />
清醒但反应迟钝</td>
<td>Postictal state combined with ongoing neuromuscular irritability from hypocalcemia<br />
发作后状态叠加低钙血症持续的神经肌肉兴奋性改变</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Mother stopped alcohol at 4 weeks gestation<br />
母亲妊娠 4 周时停止饮酒</td>
<td>Deliberate red herring for fetal alcohol syndrome — exposure ceased before critical neural tube and cardiac development<br />
胎儿酒精综合征的刻意干扰项——暴露在神经管及心脏发育关键期之前已停止</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

## 2. Mechanism / 机制理解

The **22q11.2 microdeletion** disrupts neural crest cell migration, causing abnormal development of the **3rd and 4th pharyngeal pouches**, which give rise to the thymus, parathyroid glands, and conotruncal cardiac structures:

**22q11.2 微缺失**干扰了神经嵴细胞迁移，导致**第 3 和第 4 咽囊**发育异常，这两个咽囊正常情况下分化为胸腺、甲状旁腺及圆锥干心脏结构：

- Parathyroid hypoplasia → ↓PTH → hypocalcemia → neonatal tetany, seizures, laryngospasm\
  甲状旁腺发育不良 → PTH 减少 → 低钙血症 → 新生儿手足搐搦、抽搐、喉痉挛

- Thymic hypoplasia → depleted T-cell output → cellular and combined immunodeficiency\
  胸腺发育不良 → T 细胞输出减少 → 细胞免疫及联合免疫缺陷

- Conotruncal defects (truncus arteriosus, interrupted aortic arch, right-sided arch, tetralogy of Fallot) from failure of neural crest contribution to outflow tract septation\
  流出道间隔化的神经嵴贡献失败导致圆锥干缺损（永存动脉干、主动脉弓离断、右位主动脉弓、法洛四联症）

- Craniofacial dysmorphism: hypertelorism, low-set ears, micrognathia, cleft palate\
  颅面部畸形：眼距增宽、低位耳、小颌畸形、腭裂

**Anatomic rule of thumb:** The 3rd pharyngeal pouch → inferior parathyroids + thymus; the 4th → superior parathyroids. DiGeorge disrupts both, hence simultaneous hypocalcemia and immune deficiency.

**解剖小窍门:** 第 3 咽囊 → 下甲状旁腺 + 胸腺；第 4 咽囊 → 上甲状旁腺。DiGeorge 综合征使两者同时受累，因此低钙血症与免疫缺陷并存。

## 3. Correct Answer (C) — Thymic-Parathyroid Dysplasia (DiGeorge Syndrome) / 正确答案 (C) — 胸腺-甲状旁腺发育不良（DiGeorge 综合征）

**DiGeorge syndrome (22q11.2 deletion)** is the unifying diagnosis that simultaneously explains neonatal hypocalcemic seizures, conotruncal cardiac anomalies, absent thymic shadow, and craniofacial dysmorphism:

**DiGeorge 综合征（22q11.2 缺失）**是同时解释新生儿低钙性抽搐、圆锥干心脏异常、胸腺影消失和颅面部畸形的统一诊断：

- Parathyroid failure → ↓PTH → ↓Ca²⁺ → neonatal seizures within the first days of life (before any infections appear)\
  甲状旁腺衰竭 → PTH 降低 → 血钙降低 → 生后数日内即出现新生儿抽搐（早于任何感染表现）

- Thymic hypoplasia → T-cell lymphopenia → susceptibility to viral, fungal, and opportunistic pathogens; live vaccines contraindicated until T-cell function confirmed\
  胸腺发育不良 → T 细胞淋巴细胞减少 → 易感病毒、真菌及机会性病原体；T 细胞功能确认前禁用活疫苗

- Right-sided aortic arch + narrow mediastinum on CXR = nearly pathognomonic radiographic combination for 22q11.2 deletion\
  右位主动脉弓 + 胸片纵隔狭窄 = 22q11.2 缺失几乎特征性的影像学组合

**Diagnosis:** Confirm with FISH or chromosomal microarray for 22q11.2 deletion; workup includes serum Ca²⁺, PTH, CBC with differential; echocardiography and renal ultrasonography are standard

**诊断:** 通过 FISH 或染色体微阵列确认 22q11.2 缺失；检查包括血清钙、PTH、全血细胞计数及分类；超声心动图和肾脏超声是标准评估

**Treatment:** Acute IV calcium gluconate for seizures; long-term calcium + vitamin D supplementation; thymic transplant or HSCT for complete DiGeorge (absent T-cells); irradiated blood products to prevent transfusion-associated GVHD

**治疗:** 急性期静脉注射葡萄糖酸钙控制抽搐；长期口服钙剂 + 维生素 D；完全型 DiGeorge（T 细胞缺失）考虑胸腺移植或造血干细胞移植；使用辐照血制品预防输血相关移植物抗宿主病

## 4. Options Elimination / 错误选项排除逻辑

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 33%" />
<col style="width: 33%" />
<col style="width: 33%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Option</strong><br />
<strong>选项</strong></th>
<th><strong>Why Wrong</strong><br />
<strong>为什么错</strong></th>
<th><strong>Key Discriminator</strong><br />
<strong>鉴别要点</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>A — Down syndrome<br />
A — 唐氏综合征</td>
<td>Not characteristic — trisomy 21 causes upslanting palpebral fissures, single palmar crease, AV canal defects, and hypothyroidism; hypocalcemic seizures and absent thymus are not features<br />
不符合——21 三体引起上斜睑裂、通贯掌、房室管缺损和甲状腺功能减退；低钙性抽搐和胸腺缺如不是其表现</td>
<td>Down syndrome does not affect the 3rd/4th pharyngeal pouches and does not cause neonatal hypocalcemia<br />
唐氏综合征不影响第 3/4 咽囊，不引起新生儿低钙血症</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>B — Severe combined immunodeficiency<br />
B — 重症联合免疫缺陷</td>
<td>SCID presents with recurrent bacterial, viral, and fungal infections in early infancy — not neonatal seizures; no cardiac anomalies or craniofacial features<br />
SCID 表现为婴儿早期反复细菌、病毒和真菌感染——不是新生儿抽搐；无心脏异常或颅面部特征</td>
<td>SCID lacks parathyroid failure, conotruncal defects, and craniofacial dysmorphism<br />
SCID 无甲状旁腺衰竭、圆锥干缺损和颅面部畸形</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>C — Thymic-parathyroid dysplasia ✓<br />
C — 胸腺-甲状旁腺发育不良 ✓</td>
<td>CORRECT — 22q11.2 deletion accounts for all five clinical domains: neonatal seizures (hypocalcemia), narrow mediastinum (absent thymus), right-sided arch (conotruncal defect), hypertelorism and low-set ears (craniofacial)<br />
正确——22q11.2 缺失涵盖全部五个临床表现域：新生儿抽搐（低钙血症）、纵隔狭窄（胸腺缺如）、右位主动脉弓（圆锥干缺损）、眼距增宽和低位耳（颅面部畸形）</td>
<td>Only diagnosis that simultaneously explains cardiac, immune, metabolic, and craniofacial findings in a neonate<br />
唯一能同时解释新生儿心脏、免疫、代谢和颅面部表现的诊断</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>D — Trisomy 13 syndrome<br />
D — 13 三体综合征（Patau 综合征）</td>
<td>Trisomy 13 (Patau syndrome) presents with holoprosencephaly, midline cleft lip/palate, polydactyly, microphthalmia, and cutis aplasia; neonatal hypocalcemia and absent thymus are not dominant features<br />
13 三体（Patau 综合征）表现为前脑无裂畸形、中线唇腭裂、多指/趾、小眼畸形和皮肤发育不全；新生儿低钙血症和胸腺缺如不是主要特征</td>
<td>Trisomy 13 does not cause parathyroid or thymic hypoplasia; midline CNS defects distinguish it<br />
13 三体不引起甲状旁腺或胸腺发育不良；中线中枢神经系统缺陷是其鉴别点</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>E — Wiskott-Aldrich syndrome<br />
E — Wiskott-Aldrich 综合征</td>
<td>WAS gene mutation (X-linked) → classic triad of eczema, thrombocytopenia, and recurrent infections with encapsulated bacteria; no hypocalcemia, no cardiac defects, no craniofacial anomalies<br />
WAS 基因突变（X 连锁）→ 湿疹、血小板减少和荚膜菌反复感染的经典三联征；无低钙血症、心脏缺损和颅面部异常</td>
<td>Wiskott-Aldrich presents months after birth, not in the neonatal period with seizures<br />
Wiskott-Aldrich 在出生数月后才出现，不以新生儿期抽搐为首发</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

*The most seductive distractor is Choice A (Down syndrome) — both conditions involve congenital heart disease and dysmorphic features, but Down syndrome produces AV canal defects (not right-sided aortic arch), spares the thymus and parathyroids entirely, and does not cause neonatal hypocalcemic seizures.*

最易混淆的干扰项是 A 选项（唐氏综合征）——两者都有先天性心脏病和面部畸形，但唐氏综合征产生房室管缺损（非右位主动脉弓），完全不影响胸腺和甲状旁腺，也不引起新生儿低钙性抽搐。

## 6. One-Sentence Summary & Memory Hook / 一句话总结 & 记忆钩

**DiGeorge syndrome (22q11.2 deletion) classically presents in the neonate with hypocalcemic seizures, conotruncal cardiac defects (right-sided aortic arch, truncus arteriosus), absent thymic shadow on CXR, and craniofacial dysmorphism — all caused by failed 3rd and 4th pharyngeal pouch development.**

**DiGeorge 综合征（22q11.2 缺失）的经典表现是新生儿低钙性抽搐、圆锥干心脏缺陷（右位主动脉弓、永存动脉干）、胸片胸腺影消失和颅面部畸形——均由第 3 和第 4 咽囊发育失败所致。**

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 100%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><p><strong>Memory Hook — CATCH-22 for DiGeorge Syndrome / 记忆钩 — DiGeorge 综合征的 "CATCH-22":</strong></p>
<p>• <strong>C</strong>ardiac defects (conotruncal) — right aortic arch, truncus arteriosus, tetralogy of Fallot / 心脏缺陷（圆锥干型）——右位主动脉弓、永存动脉干、法洛四联症<br />
• <strong>A</strong>bnormal facies — hypertelorism, low-set ears, micrognathia, cleft palate / 面部异常——眼距增宽、低位耳、小颌畸形、腭裂<br />
• <strong>T</strong>hymic hypoplasia → ↓T-cells → viral/fungal infections, live vaccine contraindication / 胸腺发育不良 → T 细胞减少 → 病毒/真菌感染，活疫苗禁忌<br />
• <strong>C</strong>alcium low (parathyroid hypoplasia → ↓PTH → hypocalcemia → neonatal seizures) / 钙低（甲状旁腺发育不良 → PTH 降低 → 低钙血症 → 新生儿抽搐）<br />
• <strong>H</strong>ypoparathyroidism is the mechanism behind the seizure in this question / 甲状旁腺功能减退是本题抽搐的发生机制<br />
• <strong>22</strong>q11.2 microdeletion — the genetic basis, detectable by FISH or microarray / 22q11.2 微缺失——遗传基础，可通过 FISH 或微阵列检测</p></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
</tbody>
</table>

## 7. High-Yield Topic Knowledge — DiGeorge Syndrome (22q11.2 Deletion) / 高频知识表 — DiGeorge 综合征（22q11.2 缺失）

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 50%" />
<col style="width: 50%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Topic</strong><br />
<strong>考点</strong></th>
<th><strong>Key Points</strong><br />
<strong>要点</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>Genetics and inheritance<br />
遗传和遗传方式</td>
<td>Autosomal dominant; 90% are de novo mutations; 22q11.2 microdeletion confirmed by FISH or chromosomal microarray; also called velocardiofacial syndrome (VCFS) or Shprintzen syndrome<br />
常染色体显性遗传；90% 为新发突变；22q11.2 微缺失通过 FISH 或染色体微阵列确认；又称腭心面综合征（VCFS）或 Shprintzen 综合征</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Embryologic basis<br />
胚胎学基础</td>
<td>Defective neural crest cell migration → abnormal 3rd and 4th pharyngeal pouch derivatives: thymus (immune), inferior + superior parathyroids (calcium), and conotruncal cardiac structures (outflow tract)<br />
神经嵴细胞迁移缺陷 → 第 3/4 咽囊衍生物异常：胸腺（免疫）、上下甲状旁腺（钙调节）和圆锥干心脏结构（流出道）</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Cardiac anomalies spectrum<br />
心脏异常谱系</td>
<td>Interrupted aortic arch type B (most specific); truncus arteriosus; tetralogy of Fallot; right-sided aortic arch; VSD (most common overall); all involve outflow tract or arch development<br />
B 型主动脉弓离断（最具特异性）；永存动脉干；法洛四联症；右位主动脉弓；室间隔缺损（总体最常见）；均涉及流出道或弓发育</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Hypocalcemia workup and treatment<br />
低钙血症的检查和治疗</td>
<td>Labs: ↓Ca²⁺, ↓PTH, ↓phosphorus (acutely), ↑alkaline phosphatase; acute seizures: IV calcium gluconate; long-term: oral calcium + calcitriol (active vitamin D, bypasses parathyroid)<br />
化验：血钙低、PTH 低、磷低（急性期）、碱性磷酸酶升高；急性抽搐：静脉葡萄糖酸钙；长期：口服钙剂 + 骨化三醇（活性维生素 D，绕过甲状旁腺途径）</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Immune spectrum<br />
免疫谱系</td>
<td>Partial DiGeorge (most common): low but functional T-cells; complete DiGeorge (&lt;1% of cases): absent T-cells, SCID-like, requires thymic transplant or HSCT; irradiated blood products mandatory to prevent GVHD<br />
部分型 DiGeorge（最常见）：T 细胞减少但有功能；完全型 DiGeorge（&lt;1%）：T 细胞缺失，类 SCID，需胸腺移植或造血干细胞移植；必须使用辐照血制品以防移植物抗宿主病</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Adult psychiatric complication<br />
成人精神并发症</td>
<td>~30% of adults with 22q11.2 deletion develop schizophrenia-spectrum disorder; 22q11.2 deletion is the single largest genetic risk factor for schizophrenia, accounting for ~1–2% of all cases<br />
约 30% 的 22q11.2 缺失成人发展为精神分裂症谱系障碍；22q11.2 缺失是精神分裂症最大的单一遗传风险因素，占所有病例约 1–2%</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Live vaccine rule<br />
活疫苗规则</td>
<td>Contraindicated until T-cell function is confirmed; risk: disseminated disease from attenuated vaccine strains (e.g., BCG-osis, rotavirus viremia); applies to MMR, varicella, rotavirus, BCG<br />
在 T 细胞功能确认之前禁忌；风险：减毒疫苗株播散性感染（如 BCG 播散病、轮状病毒血症）；适用于 MMR、水痘、轮状病毒、BCG</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

## 8. Extensions / 延伸扩展

- **Differential of neonatal hypocalcemic seizures:** DiGeorge (↓PTH production), pseudohypoparathyroidism (PTH resistance, Gs-alpha mutation), maternal hyperparathyroidism (suppresses fetal parathyroids in utero), hypomagnesemia (blocks PTH secretion), late neonatal hypocalcemia (high-phosphate cow's milk formula at days 5–7)\
  **新生儿低钙性抽搐鉴别:** DiGeorge（PTH 生成减少）、假性甲状旁腺功能减退症（PTH 抵抗，Gsα 突变）、母亲甲状旁腺功能亢进（宫内抑制胎儿甲状旁腺）、低镁血症（阻断 PTH 分泌）、晚发新生儿低钙血症（生后 5–7 天高磷牛奶配方）

- **Key complication — transfusion GVHD:** Complete DiGeorge lacks mature T-cells to reject donor lymphocytes in blood products; even standard packed RBCs can cause fatal GVHD; always use irradiated, CMV-negative products\
  **关键并发症——输血相关 GVHD:** 完全型 DiGeorge 缺乏成熟 T 细胞来排斥血制品中的供体淋巴细胞；即使标准浓缩红细胞也可引起致死性 GVHD；务必使用辐照、CMV 阴性血制品

- **Variant — CHARGE syndrome:** Coloboma, Heart defect, Atresia choanae, Retarded growth, Genital abnormalities, Ear abnormalities; caused by CHD7 mutation; overlaps with DiGeorge in cardiac and ear findings but distinguished by choanal atresia and ocular coloboma rather than hypocalcemia\
  **题目变式——CHARGE 综合征:** 眼缺损、心脏缺陷、后鼻孔闭锁、生长迟缓、生殖器异常、耳异常；由 CHD7 基因突变引起；与 DiGeorge 在心脏和耳部表现上有重叠，但以后鼻孔闭锁和眼缺损为鉴别，而非低钙血症

- **Mnemonic extension — the psychiatric "P":** CATCH-22 + **P**sychiatric (schizophrenia) = the full adult sequela; boards frequently test that 22q11.2 deletion is a major schizophrenia risk gene — a high-yield extension from a pediatric question\
  **助记延伸——精神科的"P":** CATCH-22 + **精**神分裂症（Psychiatric）= 完整的成人后遗症；考试常考 22q11.2 缺失是精神分裂症的主要风险基因——一道儿科题的高频延伸考点

# Question 153 — Vesicoureteral Reflux Management / 膀胱输尿管返流处理

## Question Stem / 题干

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 100%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><p>A <strong>2-year-old girl</strong> is brought to the physician for a well-child examination. She has had <strong>two urinary tract infections since birth</strong>. She has not had pain with urination or urinary frequency or urgency. Examination shows <strong>no abnormalities</strong>. Renal ultrasonography shows <strong>no obstruction</strong>. Voiding cystourethrography shows <strong>grade II vesicoureteral reflux</strong>.</p>
<p><strong>Q: Which of the following is the most appropriate initial step to prevent future urinary tract infections in this patient?</strong></p>
<p>A) Monitor temperature curves daily<br />
B) Urine cultures weekly<br />
C) Oral antibiotic prophylaxis<br />
D) 2-Week course of intravenous antibiotic therapy<br />
E) Vesicoureteral reimplantation</p>
<p><strong>Correct Answer: C</strong></p></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
</tbody>
</table>

---

## 1. Key Stem Clues / 题干关键词抓考点

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 50%" />
<col style="width: 50%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Key Stem Clue</strong><br />
<strong>关键词</strong></th>
<th><strong>Why It Matters</strong><br />
<strong>为什么重要</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>2-year-old girl<br />
2岁女孩</td>
<td>Young children are at higher risk for renal scarring from recurrent UTIs; age guides management threshold<br />
幼儿因反复UTI引起肾瘢痕的风险更高；年龄决定处理门槛</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Two UTIs since birth<br />
自出生以来两次UTI</td>
<td>&gt;1 UTI in a child with VUR is the key indication for oral antibiotic prophylaxis<br />
VUR患儿UTI超过1次是口服抗生素预防的关键指征</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>No obstruction on renal ultrasound<br />
肾超声无梗阻</td>
<td>Rules out obstructive uropathy; isolated VUR is the working diagnosis<br />
排除梗阻性尿路病变；单纯VUR成为工作诊断</td>
</tr>
<tr>

<td>Grade I–III VUR is low-to-moderate severity; surgical correction is not yet indicated as first step<br />
I–III级VUR为轻中度；手术矫正尚不作为首选措施</td>
</tr>
<tr>

UTI间期无症状</td>
<td>Asymptomatic VUR is managed medically first; symptoms would not change the prophylaxis indication<br />
无症状VUR优先药物管理；症状的有无不改变预防指征</td>
</tr>
<tr>

儿童健康访视背景</td>
<td>This is preventive management, not acute treatment; the question asks for prophylaxis strategy<br />
这是预防性管理而非急性治疗；题目问的是预防策略</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

---

## 2. Mechanism / 机制理解

**Vesicoureteral reflux (VUR)** results from an incompetent **ureterovesical junction (UVJ)**: normally the intramural ureter runs obliquely through the bladder wall, creating a flap-valve mechanism that prevents retrograde urine flow during voiding. When this tunnel is too short or the angle is abnormal, voiding pressure drives urine retrograde into the ureters and renal pelvis:

**膀胱输尿管返流（VUR）**源于**输尿管膀胱连接部（UVJ）**功能不全：正常情况下壁内段输尿管斜行穿过膀胱壁，形成瓣膜机制，排尿时防止尿液逆流。当该隧道过短或角度异常时，排尿压力将尿液逆向驱入输尿管和肾盂：

- Retrograde urine flow carries bacteria from bladder → ureters → renal pelvis → pyelonephritis risk\
  逆流尿液将细菌从膀胱携带至输尿管→肾盂，增加肾盂肾炎风险

- Recurrent pyelonephritis → focal renal scarring → reflux nephropathy → hypertension and CKD\
  反复肾盂肾炎→局灶性肾瘢痕→返流性肾病→高血压和CKD

- Grade II: reflux reaches the renal pelvis without dilation — moderate anatomic defect, amenable to medical therapy\
  II级：返流达肾盂但无扩张——中度解剖缺损，适合药物治疗

- Low-dose continuous antibiotic prophylaxis suppresses bladder bacteriuria, preventing the upward seeding that causes pyelonephritis\
  低剂量持续抗生素预防抑制膀胱菌尿，阻止上行播种导致肾盂肾炎

**Anatomic rule of thumb:** The longer the intramural tunnel relative to ureter diameter, the more effective the flap valve — grade I–II often resolve spontaneously as the child grows and the tunnel lengthens.

**解剖小窍门:** 壁内段隧道相对输尿管直径越长，瓣膜机制越有效——I–II级VUR随患儿生长隧道延长常可自行消退。

---

## 3. Correct Answer (C) — Oral Antibiotic Prophylaxis / 正确答案 (C) — 口服抗生素预防

**Oral antibiotic prophylaxis** is the evidence-based first-line strategy for children with VUR who have experienced more than one UTI, protecting against pyelonephritis and renal scarring while awaiting spontaneous resolution or deciding on surgical repair:

**口服抗生素预防**是VUR患儿发生超过一次UTI后基于循证的一线策略，在等待自行消退或决定手术修复期间防止肾盂肾炎和肾瘢痕：

- Agents of choice: trimethoprim-sulfamethoxazole (TMP-SMX) or nitrofurantoin — both concentrate in urine at sub-inhibitory doses\
  首选药物：甲氧苄啶-磺胺甲噁唑（TMP-SMX）或呋喃妥因——两者均可在亚抑制剂量下在尿液中浓集

- Given once daily (typically at bedtime to maximize bladder contact time overnight)\
  每日一次给药（通常睡前服以最大化夜间膀胱接触时间）

- Duration: continued until VUR resolves spontaneously (common in grades I–III) or surgical correction is performed\
  疗程：持续至VUR自行消退（I–III级常见）或完成手术矫正

- Monitoring with periodic VCUG and urine cultures guides dose/duration decisions\
  定期VCUG和尿培养监测指导剂量/疗程决策

**Diagnosis:** Grade II VUR + \>1 UTI in a child → oral antibiotic prophylaxis is indicated before considering surgical reimplantation.

**诊断:** 儿童II级VUR + UTI超过1次→手术再植前应先行口服抗生素预防。

**Treatment:** Low-dose daily TMP-SMX or nitrofurantoin; escalate to ureteral reimplantation only if UTIs recur despite prophylaxis.

**治疗:** 低剂量每日TMP-SMX或呋喃妥因；仅在预防治疗下仍反复UTI时升级为输尿管再植手术。

---

## 4. Options Elimination / 错误选项排除逻辑

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 33%" />
<col style="width: 33%" />
<col style="width: 33%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Option</strong><br />
<strong>选项</strong></th>
<th><strong>Why Wrong</strong><br />
<strong>为什么错</strong></th>
<th><strong>Key Discriminator</strong><br />
<strong>鉴别要点</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>A — Monitor temperature curves daily<br />
A — 每日监测体温曲线</td>
<td>Detects febrile UTIs after they occur but does not prevent them — surveillance ≠ prophylaxis<br />
发热性UTI发生后才能检测，并不能预防——监测≠预防</td>
<td>Prevention is the goal; passive monitoring does nothing to reduce bacterial seeding<br />
目标是预防；被动监测无法减少细菌播种</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>B — Urine cultures weekly<br />
B — 每周尿培养</td>
<td>Similarly reactive, not preventive; also impractical and costly in an asymptomatic child<br />
同样是被动反应而非预防；在无症状患儿中也不切实际且代价高</td>
<td>Weekly cultures cannot prevent pyelonephritis, only detect it slightly earlier<br />
每周培养无法预防肾盂肾炎，仅能稍早发现</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>C — Oral antibiotic prophylaxis ✓<br />
C — 口服抗生素预防 ✓</td>
<td>CORRECT — First-line prevention for VUR children with &gt;1 UTI; suppresses bacteriuria and prevents upper-tract seeding<br />
正确——VUR患儿超过1次UTI的一线预防；抑制菌尿，防止上尿路播种</td>
<td>Directly addresses the pathophysiology by maintaining bladder sterility<br />
通过维持膀胱无菌直接针对病理生理机制</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>D — 2-Week course of IV antibiotic therapy<br />
D — 2周静脉抗生素疗程</td>
<td>Treats an acute infection but provides no ongoing prophylaxis; VUR persists after the course ends<br />
治疗急性感染但无持续预防效果；疗程结束后VUR仍存在</td>
<td>Short-course therapy cannot prevent future infections; long-term oral prophylaxis is required<br />
短疗程不能预防未来感染；需要长期口服预防</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>E — Vesicoureteral reimplantation<br />
E — 膀胱输尿管再植术</td>
<td>Surgical correction is reserved for failure of antibiotic prophylaxis or high-grade VUR; not the initial step<br />
手术矫正保留用于抗生素预防失败或高级别VUR；不是初始步骤</td>
<td>Medical management always precedes surgery in grade II VUR; "most appropriate initial step" directs away from surgery<br />
II级VUR始终先行药物治疗再考虑手术；"最合适的初始步骤"指向非手术方案</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

*The most tempting distractor is E (reimplantation) — many test-takers confuse "definitive fix" with "initial step"; the key is that grade II VUR is managed medically first, with surgery reserved for prophylaxis failure.*

手术再植（E）是最容易混淆的干扰项——许多考生将"根治"与"初始步骤"混淆；关键点是II级VUR首先药物管理，手术保留用于预防失败时。

---

## 5. High-Yield Summary Table — VUR Grading vs. Management Strategy / 膀胱输尿管返流分级与处理策略对比

IV–V级可能直接手术</td>

肾瘢痕风险</td>
<td>Low if treated promptly<br />
及时治疗则低</td>
<td>High; associated with reflux nephropathy<br />
高；与返流性肾病相关</td>

影像随访</td>
<td>Annual VCUG or DMSA scan<br />
年度VCUG或DMSA扫描</td>
<td>More frequent VCUG; nuclear cystogram to reduce radiation<br />
更频繁VCUG；核素膀胱造影以减少辐射</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

---

## 6. One-Sentence Summary & Memory Hook / 一句话总结 & 记忆钩

**In a child with grade II VUR and more than one UTI, oral antibiotic prophylaxis (TMP-SMX or nitrofurantoin) is the first-line prevention strategy, reserving surgical reimplantation for prophylaxis failure.**

**对于II级VUR且超过一次UTI的患儿，口服抗生素预防（TMP-SMX或呋喃妥因）是一线预防策略，手术再植保留用于预防失败时。**

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 100%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><p><strong>Memory Hook — "GRADE" for VUR Management / 记忆钩 — "GRADE" VUR处理口诀:</strong></p>
<p>• <strong>G</strong>rade I–II → <strong>G</strong>o medical first (antibiotics) / <strong>G</strong>rade I–II先走药物路线<br />
• <strong>R</strong>eflux nephropathy is the feared complication / <strong>R</strong>eflux肾病是最怕的并发症<br />
• <strong>A</strong>ntibiotics prophylaxis = TMP-SMX or nitrofurantoin daily / <strong>A</strong>ntibiotics预防=每日TMP-SMX或呋喃妥因<br />
• <strong>D</strong>o VCUG to grade it before deciding / <strong>D</strong>o VCUG先分级再决策<br />
• <strong>E</strong>scalate to surgery only on failure / <strong>E</strong>scalate失败才升级手术</p></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
</tbody>
</table>

## 7. High-Yield Topic Knowledge — Vesicoureteral Reflux in Pediatrics / 高频知识表 — 儿童膀胱输尿管返流

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 50%" />
<col style="width: 50%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Topic</strong><br />
<strong>考点</strong></th>
<th><strong>Key Points</strong><br />
<strong>要点</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>VUR grading system (International)<br />
VUR国际分级</td>
<td>Grade I: ureter only; II: ureter + pelvis, no dilation; III: mild dilation; IV: moderate dilation + blunting; V: severe dilation + ureteral tortuosity<br />
I级：仅输尿管；II级：输尿管+肾盂，无扩张；III级：轻度扩张；IV级：中度扩张+肾盏变钝；V级：严重扩张+输尿管迂曲</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Diagnostic gold standard<br />
诊断金标准</td>
<td>Voiding cystourethrography (VCUG): instill contrast via catheter, image during voiding; also detects posterior urethral valves in boys<br />
排尿性膀胱尿道造影（VCUG）：经导管注入造影剂，排尿时成像；也可检测男孩后尿道瓣膜</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Preferred prophylactic antibiotics<br />
首选预防抗生素</td>
<td>TMP-SMX (avoid in infants &lt;2 months) or nitrofurantoin (avoid in infants &lt;1 month and G6PD deficiency); amoxicillin for neonates<br />
TMP-SMX（&lt;2月龄避免）或呋喃妥因（&lt;1月龄及G6PD缺乏症避免）；新生儿用阿莫西林</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Spontaneous resolution<br />
自行消退</td>
<td>Grades I–III resolve spontaneously in most children by school age; grade IV partial resolution; grade V rarely resolves<br />
I–III级大多数患儿至学龄期自行消退；IV级部分消退；V级几乎不能自行消退</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Surgical options<br />
手术选项</td>
<td>Open ureteral reimplantation (Cohen or Politano-Leadbetter); endoscopic injection of bulking agent (STING/HIT procedure) — less invasive, lower success rate than open repair<br />
开放性输尿管再植（Cohen或Politano-Leadbetter法）；内镜注射填充剂（STING/HIT手术）——创伤小但成功率低于开放手术</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Long-term complication<br />
长期并发症</td>
<td>Reflux nephropathy: focal renal scarring → small kidney → hypertension + proteinuria + CKD; commonest cause of childhood CKD in some series<br />
返流性肾病：局灶性肾瘢痕→肾萎缩→高血压+蛋白尿+CKD；在某些系列中是儿童CKD最常见原因</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Epidemiology<br />
流行病学</td>
<td>Affects ~1% of children; found in ~30–40% of children investigated for first UTI; female predominance in symptomatic cases; familial (autosomal dominant pattern)<br />
影响约1%儿童；首次UTI检查中约30–40%发现VUR；症状病例女性多见；家族性（常染色体显性遗传模式）</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

---

## 8. Extensions / 延伸扩展

- **Posterior urethral valves (PUV):** The most important anatomic cause of VUR in males; always suspect in a boy with dilated upper tracts — VCUG will show the obstruction at the posterior urethra as well as secondary VUR\
  **后尿道瓣膜（PUV）:** 男性VUR最重要的解剖原因；男孩上尿路扩张时始终需考虑——VCUG将同时显示后尿道梗阻和继发性VUR

- **DMSA renal scan:** Used to detect renal cortical scarring (photopenic defects); performed after acute pyelonephritis has resolved; identifies children at highest risk for long-term renal damage\
  **DMSA肾扫描:** 用于检测肾皮质瘢痕（光子缺失区）；在急性肾盂肾炎消退后进行；识别长期肾损害风险最高的患儿

- **Breakthrough UTI on prophylaxis:** Indicates prophylaxis failure → indication to upgrade to surgical reimplantation; also reassess compliance with medication and urine culture susceptibility\
  **预防期间突破性UTI:** 提示预防失败→升级为手术再植的指征；同时重新评估用药依从性和尿培养药敏

- **Circumcision and VUR:** In male infants with VUR, circumcision reduces UTI risk by ~10-fold by eliminating periurethral bacterial colonization — may be offered as adjunct to antibiotic prophylaxis\
  **包皮环切与VUR:** 男婴VUR中，包皮环切通过消除尿道周围细菌定植将UTI风险降低约10倍——可作为抗生素预防的辅助措施

# Question 154 — Pervasive Developmental Disorder (Autism Spectrum Disorder) / 广泛性发育障碍（自闭症谱系障碍）

## Question Stem / 题干

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 100%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><p>A <strong>4-year-old boy</strong> is brought to the physician by his mother because she is concerned that he is <strong>having difficulty making friends</strong>. The mother reports that he attends preschool but <strong>does not socialize with the other children</strong> and spends most of the time playing by himself. At school, he is <strong>only interested in blocks</strong>, reports how tall he can build towers, and <strong>resists other activities</strong>. At home, he <strong>spends hours building towers out of blocks</strong> in his room and <strong>becomes very upset if he is interrupted</strong>. He does not talk about any of his classmates; when his mother invites another child to the house, he has <strong>little interest in socializing</strong>. His mother reports that he understands directions and communicates without difficulty but has <strong>never been very affectionate</strong>. He is generally well behaved but will have a <strong>temper tantrum if a daily routine is altered or if furniture is rearranged</strong>. Pregnancy, labor, and delivery were uncomplicated, and he has reached all appropriate motor milestones for his age. His mother does not recall if language emerged somewhat later in him than it did for her daughter but notes that he makes his needs and wants known without any problem. He is neatly dressed. Physical examination shows no abnormalities. On mental status examination, he <strong>makes no eye contact</strong> with the physician and <strong>perseverates about the towers</strong> that he built in the waiting room.</p>
<p><strong>Q: Which of the following is the most likely diagnosis?</strong></p>
<p>A) Attention-deficit/hyperactivity disorder<br />
B) Expressive language disorder<br />
C) Obsessive-compulsive disorder<br />
D) Pervasive developmental disorder<br />
E) Social anxiety disorder (social phobia)</p>
<p><strong>Correct Answer: D</strong></p></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
</tbody>
</table>

## 1. Key Stem Clues / 题干关键词抓考点

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 50%" />
<col style="width: 50%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Key Stem Clue</strong><br />
<strong>关键词</strong></th>
<th><strong>Why It Matters</strong><br />
<strong>为什么重要</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>Does not socialize; plays by himself<br />
不与人社交；独自玩耍</td>
<td>Core ASD domain: persistent deficits in social interaction across settings<br />
ASD核心领域：跨情境社交互动持续缺陷</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Only interested in blocks; resists other activities<br />
只对积木感兴趣；抵制其他活动</td>
<td>Restricted, fixated interest — DSM-5 ASD Criterion B3<br />
局限性、固着兴趣——DSM-5 ASD标准B3</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Becomes very upset if interrupted; temper tantrum if routine altered or furniture rearranged<br />
被打断时非常沮丧；例行程序改变或家具重新摆放时发脾气</td>
<td>Insistence on sameness / inflexible adherence to routine — hallmark of ASD<br />
坚持同一性/对例行程序的刻板坚持——ASD标志性特征</td>

<tr>

<td>Deficient nonverbal communication — key ASD finding on mental status exam<br />
非语言沟通缺陷——精神状态检查中的关键ASD发现</td>
</tr>
<tr>

反复谈论积木塔</td>
<td>Perseveration = repetitive, fixated ideation; supports restricted/repetitive behavior criterion<br />
持续言语=重复、固着思维；支持局限性/重复性行为标准</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Never been very affectionate<br />
从不亲密</td>
<td>Impaired social-emotional reciprocity — reduced affective sharing even with caregivers<br />
社交情感互动受损——即使与看护者的情感分享也减少</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Language and motor milestones within normal limits<br />
语言和运动里程碑在正常范围内</td>
<td>Distinguishes from intellectual disability; ASD can present with fully preserved language (formerly Asperger's)<br />
与智力残疾鉴别；ASD可表现为语言完全保留（以前称Asperger综合征）</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

## 2. Mechanism / 机制理解

**Autism spectrum disorder (ASD)** arises from atypical connectivity within **social brain networks** — including the amygdala, superior temporal sulcus, and prefrontal cortex — producing two core symptom domains that must both be present:

**自闭症谱系障碍（ASD）**源于**社交脑网络**（包括杏仁核、颞上沟和前额叶皮质）内的异常连接，产生两个必须同时存在的核心症状领域：

- **Social communication and interaction** deficits: impaired eye contact, facial expression, gesture, and social-emotional reciprocity\
  **社交沟通与互动**缺陷：眼神接触、面部表情、手势和社交情感互动受损

- **Restricted, repetitive behaviors (RRBs)**: stereotypies, insistence on sameness, fixated interests, sensory hyper/hyposensitivity\
  **局限性、重复性行为（RRBs）**：刻板行为、坚持同一性、固着兴趣、感觉过敏/低敏

- Unlike OCD compulsions, ASD RRBs are **ego-syntonic**: the child finds them pleasurable, not distressing\
  与OCD强迫行为不同，ASD重复行为是**自我协调的**：孩子认为它们令人愉悦，而非痛苦

- **Theory of Mind (ToM)** deficit: ASD patients cannot attribute mental states to others ("mind-blindness"), explaining both social indifference and the inability to engage in pretend play\
  **心理理论（ToM）**缺陷：ASD患者无法将心理状态归因于他人（"心盲"），解释了社交冷漠和无法进行假装游戏

**Anatomic rule of thumb:** Mirror neuron system dysfunction is proposed to underlie impaired imitation and ToM in ASD — the child cannot intuit what others think or feel.

**解剖小窍门:** 镜像神经元系统功能障碍被认为是ASD中模仿受损和ToM缺陷的基础——孩子无法直觉感知他人的想法或感受。

## 3. Correct Answer (D) — Pervasive Developmental Disorder / 正确答案 (D) — 广泛性发育障碍

**Pervasive developmental disorder (PDD)** is the DSM-IV umbrella term now unified under **autism spectrum disorder (ASD)** in DSM-5; both terms are accepted on USMLE:

**广泛性发育障碍（PDD）**是DSM-IV的总称，现在在DSM-5中统一归入**自闭症谱系障碍（ASD）**；两个术语在USMLE上均可接受：

- Social isolation: ignores peers, prefers solitary play, no eye contact with physician\
  社交孤立：忽视同伴，偏好独自玩耍，与医生无眼神接触

- Restricted, fixated interest: hours of block-building, speaks only of towers, resists other activities\
  局限性、固着兴趣：数小时搭积木，只谈论积木塔，抵制其他活动

- Insistence on sameness: meltdown when routine altered or furniture rearranged\
  坚持同一性：例行程序改变或家具重新摆放时崩溃

- Impaired social-emotional reciprocity: not affectionate, no interest in inviting or discussing peers\
  社交情感互动受损：不亲密，对邀请或讨论同伴毫无兴趣

- Preserved language and motor milestones (formerly consistent with Asperger's disorder under DSM-IV)\
  语言和运动里程碑保留（在DSM-IV下以前与Asperger障碍一致）

**Diagnosis:** DSM-5 requires persistent deficits across all three social communication/interaction criteria (Criterion A) plus ≥2 of 4 RRB patterns (Criterion B), with symptoms present from early developmental period causing functional impairment.

**诊断:** DSM-5要求所有三个社交沟通/互动标准持续缺陷（标准A）加上≥4种RRB模式中的2种（标准B），症状从早期发育阶段开始，导致功能损害。

**Treatment:** Applied Behavior Analysis (ABA) is gold-standard behavioral therapy; speech-language, occupational, and social skills therapy; early and intensive intervention significantly improves long-term outcomes.

**治疗:** 应用行为分析（ABA）是金标准行为治疗；言语-语言、职业和社交技能治疗；早期和强化干预显著改善长期预后。

## 4. Options Elimination / 错误选项排除逻辑

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 33%" />
<col style="width: 33%" />
<col style="width: 33%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Option</strong><br />
<strong>选项</strong></th>
<th><strong>Why Wrong</strong><br />
<strong>为什么错</strong></th>
<th><strong>Key Discriminator</strong><br />
<strong>鉴别要点</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>A — Attention-deficit/hyperactivity disorder<br />
A — 注意缺陷/多动障碍</td>
<td>No inattention, hyperactivity, or impulsivity described; social isolation and restricted fixated interests are not features of ADHD<br />
无注意力不集中、多动或冲动描述；社交孤立和局限性固着兴趣不是ADHD特征</td>
<td>ADHD children are disruptive in social settings due to impulsivity — they try to socialize but intrude; ASD children simply have no interest in peers<br />
ADHD儿童因冲动在社交场合具有破坏性——他们试图社交但会侵入；ASD儿童根本对同伴无兴趣</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>B — Expressive language disorder<br />
B — 表达性语言障碍</td>
<td>Child communicates his needs without difficulty; social withdrawal and restricted repetitive behaviors are absent in expressive language disorder<br />
孩子能无困难地表达需求；表达性语言障碍不存在社交退缩和局限性重复行为</td>
<td>Expressive language disorder: impaired language output with intact comprehension; NO social deficits or RRBs<br />
表达性语言障碍：语言输出受损，理解完整；无社交缺陷或重复行为</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>C — Obsessive-compulsive disorder<br />
C — 强迫症</td>
<td>OCD obsessions are ego-dystonic (experienced as intrusive and distressing); this child enjoys block-building and is not distressed by the activity itself<br />
OCD强迫思维是自我失调的（体验为侵入性和痛苦的）；该孩子享受搭积木，本身不感到痛苦</td>
<td>ASD RRBs: ego-syntonic and pleasurable; OCD compulsions: performed to relieve anxiety, not enjoyed<br />
ASD重复行为：自我协调且令人愉悦；OCD强迫行为：为缓解焦虑而执行，不令人愉悦</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>D — Pervasive developmental disorder ✓<br />
D — 广泛性发育障碍 ✓</td>
<td>CORRECT — All ASD domains are present: social deficits, restricted fixated interests, insistence on sameness, impaired nonverbal communication<br />
正确——所有ASD域均存在：社交缺陷、局限性固着兴趣、坚持同一性、非语言沟通受损</td>
<td>Classic ASD/PDD presentation with preserved motor and functional language milestones<br />
经典ASD/PDD表现，运动和功能性语言里程碑保留</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>E — Social anxiety disorder (social phobia)<br />
E — 社交焦虑障碍（社交恐惧症）</td>
<td>Social anxiety involves fear of negative evaluation and embarrassment; this child shows complete indifference to peers, not fear of them<br />
社交焦虑涉及对负面评价和尴尬的恐惧；该孩子表现出对同伴的完全冷漠，而非对他们的恐惧</td>
<td>Social anxiety: wants social connection but fears negative judgment; ASD: fundamentally lacks interest in social connection<br />
社交焦虑：想要社交联系但害怕负面评判；ASD：从根本上缺乏对社交联系的兴趣</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

*The trickiest distractor is C (OCD): obsessive block-building looks compulsive, but ASD stereotypies are ego-syntonic and pleasurable — the child is not trying to stop; OCD compulsions are ego-dystonic anxiety-driven rituals the patient wishes to eliminate.*

最容易混淆的干扰项是C（OCD）：强迫性搭积木看起来像强迫行为，但ASD刻板行为是自我协调且令人愉悦的——孩子并不试图停止；OCD强迫行为是自我失调的焦虑驱动仪式，患者希望消除它们。

## 6. One-Sentence Summary & Memory Hook / 一句话总结 & 记忆钩

**A child who shows no interest in peers, perseverates on a single restricted interest, insists on sameness to the point of meltdowns, and lacks eye contact and affective reciprocity has autism spectrum disorder (pervasive developmental disorder).**

**一个对同伴毫无兴趣、对单一局限性兴趣持续固着、坚持同一性到崩溃程度、缺乏眼神接触和情感互动的孩子患有自闭症谱系障碍（广泛性发育障碍）。**

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 100%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><p><strong>Memory Hook — ASD "SOCIAL" / 记忆钩 — ASD "SOCIAL" 六字口诀:</strong></p>
<p>• <strong>S</strong>ameness insisted upon — meltdown if routine or environment disrupted / <strong>坚</strong>持同一性——常规或环境被打乱时崩溃<br />
• <strong>O</strong>dd restricted interests — fixated on one thing (blocks, trains, numbers) / <strong>奇</strong>特局限性兴趣——固着于一件事（积木、火车、数字）<br />
• <strong>C</strong>ommunication deficit — impaired nonverbal (no eye contact, no gestures) / <strong>沟</strong>通缺陷——非语言受损（无眼神接触，无手势）<br />
• <strong>I</strong>ndifference to peers — not fear, not hostility, just zero interest / <strong>冷</strong>漠对待同伴——非恐惧，非敌意，只是毫无兴趣<br />
• <strong>A</strong>ffect not reciprocal — never affectionate, no social-emotional sharing / <strong>情</strong>感不互动——从不亲密，无社交情感分享<br />
• <strong>L</strong>anguage may be preserved — does NOT rule out ASD (key teaching point) / <strong>语</strong>言可能保留——不能排除ASD（关键教学点）</p></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
</tbody>
</table>

## 7. High-Yield Topic Knowledge — Autism Spectrum Disorder (ASD) / 高频知识表 — 自闭症谱系障碍（ASD）

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 50%" />
<col style="width: 50%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Topic</strong><br />
<strong>考点</strong></th>
<th><strong>Key Points</strong><br />
<strong>要点</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>DSM-5 Criterion A: Social communication deficits (all 3 required)<br />
DSM-5标准A：社交沟通缺陷（需满足全部3项）</td>
<td>(1) Impaired social-emotional reciprocity; (2) Impaired nonverbal communication (eye contact, gestures, facial expression); (3) Deficits in developing/maintaining relationships<br />
（1）社交情感互动受损；（2）非语言沟通受损（眼神、手势、面部表情）；（3）发展/维持关系缺陷</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>DSM-5 Criterion B: RRBs (≥2 of 4 required)<br />
DSM-5标准B：重复行为（需满足≥4项中的2项）</td>
<td>(1) Stereotyped/repetitive motor movements or speech; (2) Insistence on sameness; (3) Restricted/fixated interests; (4) Hyper- or hyposensitivity to sensory input<br />
（1）刻板/重复动作或言语；（2）坚持同一性；（3）局限/固着兴趣；（4）感觉输入过敏/低敏</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Epidemiology<br />
流行病学</td>
<td>Prevalence ~1 in 36 US children; male:female ≈ 4:1; heritability ~80%; NO causal link to MMR vaccine<br />
患病率约美国儿童1/36；男女比≈4:1；遗传率约80%；与MMR疫苗无因果关系</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>DSM-IV vs. DSM-5 nomenclature<br />
DSM-IV vs. DSM-5命名</td>
<td>DSM-IV subtypes (autistic disorder, Asperger's disorder, PDD-NOS) all collapsed into ASD in DSM-5; "PDD" remains a valid USMLE answer for this question<br />
DSM-IV亚型（自闭症障碍、Asperger障碍、非特指PDD）在DSM-5中全部归入ASD；"PDD"仍是本题的有效USMLE答案</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Gold-standard treatment<br />
金标准治疗</td>
<td>Applied Behavior Analysis (ABA) — structured, intensive behavioral therapy; early intervention (before age 5) produces best outcomes; no FDA-approved pharmacologic cure<br />
应用行为分析（ABA）——结构化、强化行为治疗；早期干预（5岁前）产生最佳结果；无FDA批准的药物治愈方法</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Comorbidities<br />
共病</td>
<td>Intellectual disability (~50%), epilepsy (20–30%), ADHD, anxiety disorders, GI dysmotility; preserved IQ does NOT exclude ASD<br />
智力残疾（约50%）、癫痫（20-30%）、ADHD、焦虑障碍、胃肠动力障碍；智商保留不排除ASD</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Screening tools<br />
筛查工具</td>
<td>M-CHAT-R at 18- and 24-month well-child visits; ADOS-2 and ADI-R are gold-standard diagnostic instruments used by specialists<br />
M-CHAT-R用于18和24个月儿保访视；ADOS-2和ADI-R是专科医生使用的金标准诊断工具</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

## 8. Extensions / 延伸扩展

- **Asperger's disorder vs. current ASD Level 1:** Under DSM-IV, Asperger's disorder described ASD with fully preserved language and average-to-above-average IQ; this boy (preserved language, high-functioning social/communication deficits) would have been labeled Asperger's under DSM-IV and now meets ASD Level 1 under DSM-5\
  **Asperger综合征vs.现在的ASD 1级:** 在DSM-IV下，Asperger综合征描述了语言完全保留、智商平均至高于平均的ASD；该男孩（语言保留、高功能社交/沟通缺陷）在DSM-IV下将被标记为Asperger，现在符合DSM-5的ASD 1级

- **Early red flags warranting immediate referral:** No babbling by 12 months, no single words by 16 months, no 2-word phrases by 24 months, or ANY regression of language or social skills at any age → immediate developmental evaluation regardless of other milestones\
  **需立即转诊的早期红旗:** 12个月无咿呀学语、16个月无单词、24个月无双词短语，或任何年龄的语言或社交技能退化→无论其他里程碑如何，立即进行发育评估

- **Theory of Mind deficit as unifying mechanism:** ASD patients fail the Sally-Anne false-belief task — they cannot attribute beliefs to others that differ from their own knowledge, explaining social obliviousness, difficulty with pretend play, and poor peer relationships\
  **心理理论缺陷作为统一机制:** ASD患者未通过Sally-Anne错误信念任务——他们无法将与自身知识不同的信念归因于他人，解释了社交无意识、假装游戏困难和同伴关系不佳

- **Vaccine safety (high-yield test fact):** The 1998 Lancet paper (Wakefield) claiming MMR causes autism was retracted due to data fraud; thimerosal was removed from childhood vaccines in 2001 but ASD rates continued to rise — vaccines do NOT cause ASD\
  **疫苗安全性（高频考试事实）:** 1998年《柳叶刀》论文（Wakefield）声称MMR导致自闭症因数据造假而被撤回；硫柳汞于2001年从儿童疫苗中去除，但ASD发病率继续上升——疫苗不会导致ASD

# Question 155 — Postpartum Blues / 产后忧郁

## Question Stem / 题干

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 100%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><p><strong>Two days</strong> after undergoing <strong>urgent cesarean delivery</strong> because of a <strong>nonreassuring fetal heart tracing</strong>, a <strong>37-year-old woman</strong>, gravida 1, para 1, has the onset of <strong>dysphoria, insomnia, and easy distractibility</strong>. Pregnancy was uncomplicated. She has no history of serious illness, and her only medication is a prenatal vitamin. Her paternal cousin had major depressive disorder, postpartum onset. The patient's vital signs are within normal limits. Pulse oximetry on room air shows an oxygen saturation of 97%. Physical examination shows no abnormalities. On mental status examination, she has an <strong>irritable mood</strong> and tired, concerned affect. Without treatment, which of the following is most likely to develop in this patient?</p>
<p><strong>Q: Without treatment, which of the following is most likely to develop in this patient?</strong></p>
<p>A) Alopecia<br />
B) Dissociative amnesia with dissociative fugue<br />
C) Loss of maternal bond with newborn<br />
D) Resolution of symptoms within 2 weeks<br />
E) Suicidality</p>
<p><strong>Correct Answer: D</strong></p></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
</tbody>
</table>

## 1. Key Stem Clues / 题干关键词抓考点

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 50%" />
<col style="width: 50%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Key Stem Clue</strong><br />
<strong>关键词</strong></th>
<th><strong>Why It Matters</strong><br />
<strong>为什么重要</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>Two days after cesarean delivery<br />
剖宫产后两天</td>
<td>Onset timing is hallmark of postpartum blues (days 2–5); distinguishes from MDD peripartum onset<br />
发病时间是产后忧郁的经典特征（第2–5天），有别于围产期重性抑郁</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Dysphoria, insomnia, easy distractibility<br />
情绪低落、失眠、注意力分散</td>
<td>Classic triad of postpartum blues; symptoms are mild and transient, not functionally impairing<br />
产后忧郁经典三联征；症状轻微且短暂，不影响日常功能</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Urgent cesarean delivery<br />
紧急剖宫产</td>
<td>Independent risk factor for postpartum blues via acute hormonal shift and psychological stress of unexpected delivery<br />
通过急性激素变化及意外分娩的心理应激，构成产后忧郁的独立危险因素</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Paternal cousin with MDD postpartum onset<br />
父系表亲有围产期重性抑郁史</td>
<td>Raises concern for familial risk, but this patient's mild, early-onset symptom profile still fits postpartum blues — monitor for escalation<br />
提示家族风险，但本患者症状轻微、发病早，仍符合产后忧郁——需监测是否加重</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Irritable mood, tired/concerned affect<br />
易激惹情绪、疲惫/忧虑的情感</td>
<td>Mild affective disturbance typical of postpartum blues; NOT the profound anhedonia or hopelessness of MDD<br />
产后忧郁典型的轻度情感障碍；不是重性抑郁的深度快感缺乏或绝望感</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>No history of serious illness<br />
无重大疾病史</td>
<td>Absence of prior psychiatric disorder supports postpartum blues over de novo MDD<br />
无精神科基础疾病史，支持产后忧郁而非初发重性抑郁的诊断</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

## 2. Mechanism / 机制理解

**Postpartum blues** arise from the **rapid hormonal withdrawal** following placental delivery, combined with sleep deprivation and psychosocial adjustment demands of new parenthood:

**产后忧郁**源于**胎盘娩出后激素的骤然撤退**，叠加睡眠剥夺和初为人母的心理社会适应压力：

- Estrogen and progesterone drop precipitously after delivery → transient monoaminergic dysregulation → mood lability\
  雌激素和孕激素在分娩后骤然下降 → 一过性单胺能系统失调 → 情绪波动

- HPA axis readjustment contributes to irritability, insomnia, and cognitive blunting\
  下丘脑-垂体-肾上腺轴的重新调定参与产生易激惹、失眠和认知迟钝

- Serotonergic and dopaminergic pathways stabilize as estrogen levels equilibrate — mechanism of spontaneous resolution\
  随雌激素水平重新平衡，血清素能和多巴胺能通路自行稳定——即自然缓解的机制

- No structural neuropsychiatric pathology; the syndrome is entirely hormonally driven and self-limited\
  无器质性神经精神病变；该综合征完全由激素驱动，属自限性

**Anatomic rule of thumb:** Postpartum blues = hormonal tide turning; postpartum psychosis = dopaminergic dysregulation on a structural (bipolar) substrate.

**解剖小窍门:** 产后忧郁 = 激素潮汐退去；产后精神病 = 多巴胺能失调叠加双相障碍的结构性易感基础。

## 3. Correct Answer (D) — Resolution of Symptoms Within 2 Weeks / 正确答案 (D) — 症状在两周内自行缓解

**Postpartum blues** is a self-limited syndrome in which mild affective symptoms resolve spontaneously within 2 weeks of delivery without any pharmacologic intervention:

**产后忧郁**是一种自限性综合征，轻度情感症状在产后两周内无需药物干预自行消退：

- Affects 50–80% of postpartum women; by far the most common postpartum mood disturbance\
  影响50–80%的产后女性，是目前最常见的产后情绪障碍

- Onset typically days 2–5 postpartum; peaks around day 4–5, then gradually remits\
  通常于产后第2–5天出现，第4–5天达高峰，随后逐渐缓解

- Key defining feature: symptoms do NOT impair maternal functioning or ability to bond with the newborn\
  核心定义特征：症状不影响母亲功能或与新生儿建立依恋关系的能力

- No pharmacologic treatment is warranted; supportive care (reassurance, rest, social support) is sufficient\
  无需药物治疗；支持性护理（安抚、休息、社会支持）即足够

**Diagnosis:** Postpartum blues is a clinical diagnosis — mild depressive symptoms appearing within days of delivery, lasting \< 2 weeks, without functional impairment, suicidality, or psychotic features.

**诊断:** 产后忧郁为临床诊断——分娩后数日内出现轻度抑郁症状，持续\<2周，无功能损害、自杀意念或精神病症状。

**Treatment:** Supportive only — reassurance, adequate sleep, social support network. If symptoms persist \> 2 weeks, intensify, or suicidal ideation emerges, reassess for MDD with peripartum onset.

**治疗:** 仅支持性治疗——安抚、充足睡眠、社会支持网络。若症状持续\>2周、加重或出现自杀意念，须重新评估是否为围产期重性抑郁障碍。

## 4. Options Elimination / 错误选项排除逻辑

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 33%" />
<col style="width: 33%" />
<col style="width: 33%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Option</strong><br />
<strong>选项</strong></th>
<th><strong>Why Wrong</strong><br />
<strong>为什么错</strong></th>
<th><strong>Key Discriminator</strong><br />
<strong>鉴别要点</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>A — Alopecia<br />
A — 脱发</td>
<td>Wrong — postpartum alopecia (telogen effluvium) occurs 2–4 months after delivery, not days; it is also unrelated to the current mood symptoms<br />
错误——产后脱发（休止期脱发）发生于产后2–4个月，非数天内；且与当前情绪症状无关联</td>
<td>Timing mismatch (months vs. days) and separate physiologic mechanism from postpartum blues<br />
时间不符（数月 vs. 数天），病理生理机制与产后忧郁完全不同</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>B — Dissociative amnesia with dissociative fugue<br />
B — 分离性遗忘伴分离性漫游</td>
<td>Wrong — postpartum blues does not produce dissociative symptoms; fugue states require severe trauma, dissociative identity disorder, or seizure disorder<br />
错误——产后忧郁不导致分离症状；漫游状态需要严重创伤、分离性身份障碍或癫痫发作等前提</td>
<td>Postpartum blues lacks the trauma or psychotic substrate required to generate dissociation<br />
产后忧郁不具备产生分离症状所需的创伤或精神病基础</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>C — Loss of maternal bond with newborn<br />
C — 母婴依恋丧失</td>
<td>Wrong — impaired bonding is a feature of MDD with peripartum onset, not postpartum blues; preserved maternal functioning is a defining criterion of postpartum blues<br />
错误——依恋受损是围产期重性抑郁的特征；母亲功能保留（含依恋）是产后忧郁的定义性标准</td>
<td>Preserved bonding = postpartum blues; impaired bonding = MDD peripartum onset<br />
依恋完好 = 产后忧郁；依恋受损 = 围产期重性抑郁</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>D — Resolution of symptoms within 2 weeks ✓<br />
D — 症状在两周内缓解 ✓</td>
<td>CORRECT — spontaneous resolution within 2 weeks is the defining natural history of postpartum blues; no treatment is required<br />
正确——两周内自发缓解是产后忧郁的经典自然病程；无需干预</td>
<td>Distinguishes from MDD peripartum onset, which persists &gt; 2 weeks and requires active treatment<br />
与围产期重性抑郁的核心区别：后者持续&gt;2周且需要积极治疗</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>E — Suicidality<br />
E — 自杀意念</td>
<td>Wrong — suicidality is absent in postpartum blues; its emergence is a red flag that mandates reclassification to MDD with peripartum onset or postpartum psychosis and emergent evaluation<br />
错误——产后忧郁无自杀意念；一旦出现即为红旗症状，须重新诊断为围产期重性抑郁或产后精神病并紧急评估</td>
<td>Any suicidality definitively rules out postpartum blues<br />
任何自杀意念均可排除产后忧郁诊断</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

*The most seductive distractor is (C) — loss of maternal bond — because it sounds like a natural postpartum complication, but the critical teaching point is that inability to bond defines MDD with peripartum onset, whereas postpartum blues, by definition, leaves maternal functioning fully intact.*

\(C\) 是最具迷惑性的干扰选项——"依恋丧失"听起来像产后并发症，但核心考点是：无法建立母婴依恋是围产期重性抑郁的标志，而产后忧郁的定义恰恰要求母亲功能（含依恋）完好保留。

## 5. High-Yield Summary Table — Postpartum Blues vs. MDD with Peripartum Onset vs. Postpartum Psychosis / 产后忧郁 vs. 围产期重性抑郁 vs. 产后精神病

自杀/伤婴风险</td>

仅支持性护理；自行缓解</td>
<td>SSRIs + psychotherapy (sertraline preferred if breastfeeding)<br />
SSRIs + 心理治疗（哺乳期首选舍曲林）</td>
<td>Hospitalization + antipsychotics ± mood stabilizers<br />
住院 + 抗精神病药 ± 情感稳定剂</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

## 6. One-Sentence Summary & Memory Hook / 一句话总结 & 记忆钩

**Postpartum blues is a self-limited, mild mood disturbance appearing days 2–5 after delivery that resolves spontaneously within 2 weeks, with maternal bonding and functioning fully preserved throughout.**

**产后忧郁是一种自限性轻度情绪障碍，于产后第2–5天出现，两周内自行缓解，整个过程中母婴依恋与母亲功能完好保留。**

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 100%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><p><strong>Memory Hook — MILD Blues / 记忆钩 — 产后忧郁"MILD"四要素:</strong></p>
<p>• <strong>M</strong>ood lability — irritability, dysphoria, tearfulness (not profound anhedonia) / 情绪波动——易激惹、情绪低落、哭泣（非深度快感缺乏）<br />
• <strong>I</strong>nsomnia + distractibility — mild cognitive/sleep symptoms only / 失眠 + 注意力分散——仅为轻度认知与睡眠症状<br />
• <strong>L</strong>asts &lt; 2 weeks then self-resolves — no pharmacotherapy needed / 持续&lt;2周后自行缓解——无需药物干预<br />
• <strong>D</strong>oesn't impair bonding or maternal function — key distinction from MDD peripartum onset / 不影响母婴依恋或母亲功能——与围产期重性抑郁的核心鉴别点</p></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
</tbody>
</table>

## 7. High-Yield Topic Knowledge — Postpartum Mood Disorders / 高频知识表 — 产后情绪障碍

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 50%" />
<col style="width: 50%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Topic</strong><br />
<strong>考点</strong></th>
<th><strong>Key Points</strong><br />
<strong>要点</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>Incidence of postpartum blues<br />
产后忧郁发生率</td>
<td>50–80% of postpartum women; most common postpartum mood disturbance — frequently underrecognized in clinical practice<br />
50–80%的产后女性受影响；是最常见的产后情绪障碍，临床中常被低估</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Hormonal mechanism<br />
激素机制</td>
<td>Rapid drop in estrogen and progesterone after placental delivery → transient serotonergic and dopaminergic dysregulation → self-corrects as levels restabilize<br />
胎盘娩出后雌激素和孕激素骤降 → 血清素能与多巴胺能系统一过性失调 → 随激素水平重新稳定后自行纠正</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Risk factors<br />
危险因素</td>
<td>Prior depression or anxiety, cesarean delivery (especially urgent), lack of breastfeeding, inadequate social support, primiparity, personal or family history of MDD<br />
既往抑郁或焦虑、剖宫产（尤其紧急）、未母乳喂养、社会支持不足、初产妇、本人或家族重性抑郁史</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Distinguishing MDD with peripartum onset<br />
与围产期重性抑郁鉴别</td>
<td>MDD: duration &gt; 2 weeks, functional impairment, suicidality, loss of maternal bonding; requires SSRIs + psychotherapy; sertraline preferred during breastfeeding<br />
围产期重性抑郁：持续&gt;2周、功能受损、自杀意念、母婴依恋丧失；需SSRIs+心理治疗；哺乳期首选舍曲林</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Postpartum psychosis<br />
产后精神病</td>
<td>Onset days 1–3; hallucinations, delusions, confusion; 50% have prior bipolar disorder; psychiatric emergency — admit and treat with antipsychotics ± mood stabilizers; infanticide risk requires safety assessment<br />
产后第1–3天发病；幻觉、妄想、意识混乱；50%有双相障碍史；精神科急症——收入院并给予抗精神病药±情感稳定剂；伤婴风险需评估安全性</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Edinburgh Postnatal Depression Scale (EPDS)<br />
爱丁堡产后抑郁量表（EPDS）</td>
<td>Validated screening tool for postpartum depression; score ≥ 10 warrants further clinical evaluation; score ≥ 13 suggests MDD; item 10 screens for suicidality<br />
产后抑郁筛查的验证工具；≥10分需进一步临床评估；≥13分提示重性抑郁；第10题专门筛查自杀意念</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>When to escalate from blues to MDD workup<br />
何时从产后忧郁升级为重性抑郁评估</td>
<td>Symptoms persist &gt; 2 weeks; suicidal ideation (any); inability to care for infant; psychotic features; significant functional impairment → urgent psychiatric referral<br />
症状持续&gt;2周；任何自杀意念；无法照料婴儿；精神病症状；显著功能损害 → 紧急精神科转诊</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

## 8. Extensions / 延伸扩展

- **Differential of postpartum mood changes:** Postpartum blues (\< 2 weeks, self-limited, no functional impairment) → MDD peripartum onset (\> 2 weeks, functionally impairing, suicidality) → Postpartum psychosis (days 1–3, psychiatric emergency, psychotic features, infanticide risk); always screen for prior bipolar disorder as postpartum psychosis risk increases dramatically in bipolar patients\
  **产后情绪变化的鉴别:** 产后忧郁（\<2周、自限性、功能不受损）→ 围产期重性抑郁（\>2周、功能受损、自杀意念）→ 产后精神病（第1–3天、精神科急症、精神病症状、伤婴风险）；需常规筛查既往双相障碍，双相患者产后精神病风险显著升高

- **Key complication to monitor:** If postpartum blues symptoms persist beyond 2 weeks or suicidal ideation appears, reclassify as MDD with peripartum onset and initiate SSRIs; sertraline is preferred in breastfeeding mothers due to minimal infant exposure via breast milk\
  **需监测的关键并发症:** 若产后忧郁症状超过2周或出现自杀意念，应重新诊断为围产期重性抑郁并启动SSRIs治疗；因母乳中婴儿暴露量极低，哺乳期首选舍曲林

- **Risk factor — cesarean delivery:** Urgent C-section is an independent risk factor for postpartum blues and MDD peripartum onset, via both the psychological distress of unexpected delivery experience and acute peripartum hormonal fluctuation; this case has two risk factors (C-section + family history)\
  **危险因素——剖宫产:** 紧急剖宫产通过意外分娩体验的心理创伤和围产期激素急剧波动，成为产后忧郁与围产期重性抑郁的独立危险因素；本例兼具两项危险因素（剖宫产+家族史）

- **Variant — somatic-predominant presentation:** Some patients present with fatigue and appetite changes rather than overt mood symptoms; these can mimic postpartum thyroiditis or iron-deficiency anemia — always rule out organic causes (TSH, CBC) before attributing symptoms to postpartum blues\
  **题目变式——以躯体症状为主:** 部分患者以疲劳和食欲改变为主诉而非明显情绪症状，易与产后甲状腺炎或缺铁性贫血混淆——归因于产后忧郁前须排除器质性病因（查TSH、全血细胞计数）

# Question 156 — Allergic Bronchopulmonary Aspergillosis / 变应性支气管肺曲霉菌病

## Question Stem / 题干

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 100%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><p>A <strong>32-year-old woman</strong> with <strong>asthma</strong> comes to the physician because of a <strong>3-month history of progressive wheezing</strong> and a <strong>cough occasionally productive of plugs of brownish sputum</strong>. She received the diagnosis of asthma 15 years ago. She has been taking an inhaled long-acting β-adrenergic agonist and inhaled glucocorticoid daily for 8 years and had good control of her symptoms until 3 months ago. She has no pets. She has no recent history of travel abroad or new occupational exposure. She appears well and is not in respiratory distress. Vital signs are within normal limits. Pulse oximetry on room air shows an oxygen saturation of 96%. Examination shows no cyanosis. <strong>Scattered inspiratory and expiratory wheezes</strong> are heard. There is no clubbing or peripheral edema. Her leukocyte count is <strong>20,000/mm³ (40% eosinophils)</strong>. Her <strong>serum IgE concentration is 2800 IU/mL</strong>. A chest x-ray shows <strong>alveolar infiltrates in the upper lungs bilaterally</strong>. Which of the following is the most likely diagnosis?</p>
<p><strong>Q: Which of the following is the most likely diagnosis?</strong></p>
<p>A) Allergic bronchopulmonary aspergillosis<br />
B) Eosinophilic leukemia<br />
C) Hypereosinophilic syndrome<br />
D) Polyarteritis nodosa<br />
E) Strongyloides stercoralis infection</p>
<p><strong>Correct Answer: A</strong></p></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
</tbody>
</table>

## 1. Key Stem Clues / 题干关键词抓考点

<td>Known asthma for 15 years<br />

</tr>

黏液嵌塞和中央性支气管扩张导致的反复或游走性上叶浸润是ABPA特征</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Symptoms worsened despite ICS + LABA for 3 months<br />
规律使用ICS+LABA仍进行性加重3个月</td>
<td>Treatment-refractory asthma should always trigger consideration of superimposed ABPA as a hypersensitivity process<br />
对哮喘治疗无效时，应始终考虑叠加的ABPA超敏反应</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>No travel, no occupational exposure, no pets<br />
无出行史、无职业暴露、无宠物接触</td>
<td>Eliminates parasitic infection (Strongyloides requires endemic exposure); ABPA occurs from ubiquitous environmental Aspergillus<br />
排除寄生虫感染（粪类圆线虫需流行区接触史）；ABPA源于环境中无处不在的曲霉菌</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

## 2. Mechanism / 机制理解

**Allergic bronchopulmonary aspergillosis (ABPA)** is a combined **Type I (IgE-mediated) and Type III (immune complex)** hypersensitivity reaction to **Aspergillus fumigatus** colonizing — not invading — the bronchial mucosa:

**变应性支气管肺曲霉菌病（ABPA）**是对定植——而非侵袭——支气管黏膜的**烟曲霉（Aspergillus fumigatus）**发生的**I型（IgE介导）和III型（免疫复合物）**混合超敏反应：

- Aspergillus spores inhaled → germinate in bronchi of susceptible hosts → release antigens → IgE-mediated sensitization\
  曲霉孢子吸入→在易感宿主支气管内萌发→释放抗原→IgE介导致敏

- Massive IgE production + Th2-driven eosinophil recruitment → airway inflammation → mucus hypersecretion → central bronchiectasis\
  大量IgE产生+Th2驱动嗜酸性粒细胞募集→气道炎症→黏液分泌亢进→中央性支气管扩张

- Immune complex deposition (Type III) → complement activation → neutrophil influx → additional airway wall destruction\
  免疫复合物沉积（III型）→补体激活→中性粒细胞浸润→气道壁进一步破坏

- Mucus plugs trap Aspergillus hyphae → appear brown/black → classic dark sputum plugs\
  黏液栓包裹曲霉菌丝→呈棕褐色/黑色→经典深色痰栓

- Repeated inflammatory cycles → permanent central bronchiectasis → eventual fibrosis if untreated\
  反复炎症发作→永久性中央性支气管扩张→若未治疗最终纤维化

**Anatomic rule of thumb:** ABPA causes central (proximal) bronchiectasis, unlike post-infectious bronchiectasis which is peripheral — CT chest shows pathognomonic "finger-in-glove" sign of mucoid impaction filling dilated central bronchi.

**解剖小窍门:** ABPA引起中央性（近端）支气管扩张，不同于感染后的周围性支气管扩张——胸部CT显示扩张的中央支气管内黏液嵌塞的特征性"手指状"（finger-in-glove）征。

## 3. Correct Answer (A) — Allergic Bronchopulmonary Aspergillosis / 正确答案 (A) — 变应性支气管肺曲霉菌病

**Allergic bronchopulmonary aspergillosis (ABPA)** is a hypersensitivity lung disease caused by immune sensitization to airway-colonizing Aspergillus fumigatus, exclusively in patients with pre-existing airway disease:

**变应性支气管肺曲霉菌病（ABPA）**是由对气道定植烟曲霉产生免疫致敏引起的超敏性肺病，仅发生于既往气道疾病患者：

- Classic diagnostic triad: peripheral eosinophilia + markedly elevated serum total IgE (\>1000 IU/mL) + pulmonary infiltrates (migratory, often upper lobe)\
  经典诊断三联征：外周血嗜酸性粒细胞增多+血清总IgE显著升高（\>1000 IU/mL）+肺部浸润影（游走性，常累及上叶）

- Predisposing conditions: asthma (~1–2%) and cystic fibrosis (~5–10%); never seen in otherwise healthy immunocompetent hosts (distinguishes from invasive aspergillosis)\
  易感疾病：哮喘（约1–2%）和囊性纤维化（约5–10%）；健康免疫正常宿主不患此病（区别于侵袭性曲霉菌病）

- Additional criteria (Rosenberg-Patterson): positive immediate Aspergillus skin test, Aspergillus-specific IgE and IgG precipitins, CT showing central bronchiectasis\
  附加诊断标准（Rosenberg-Patterson）：曲霉菌速发皮肤试验阳性、曲霉特异性IgE和IgG沉淀素、CT示中央性支气管扩张

**Diagnosis:** Clinical triad + serum total IgE \>1000 IU/mL + Aspergillus-specific IgE (positive skin prick test or serology) + CT chest showing central bronchiectasis and mucoid impaction

**诊断:** 临床三联征+总IgE\>1000 IU/mL+曲霉特异性IgE（皮肤点刺试验阳性或血清学阳性）+胸部CT示中央性支气管扩张和黏液嵌塞

**Treatment:** Oral corticosteroids first-line (prednisolone 0.5 mg/kg/day × 2 weeks then taper) to suppress hypersensitivity + antifungals (itraconazole or voriconazole) to reduce Aspergillus fungal burden + omalizumab (anti-IgE monoclonal antibody) for refractory/steroid-dependent cases

**治疗:** 口服糖皮质激素一线治疗（泼尼松龙0.5 mg/kg/天×2周后逐渐减量）以抑制超敏反应+抗真菌药（伊曲康唑或伏立康唑）以减少曲霉真菌负荷+奥马珠单抗（抗IgE单克隆抗体）用于难治性/激素依赖性病例

## 4. Options Elimination / 错误选项排除逻辑

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 33%" />
<col style="width: 33%" />
<col style="width: 33%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Option</strong><br />
<strong>选项</strong></th>
<th><strong>Why Wrong</strong><br />
<strong>为什么错</strong></th>
<th><strong>Key Discriminator</strong><br />
<strong>鉴别要点</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>A — Allergic bronchopulmonary aspergillosis ✓<br />
A — 变应性支气管肺曲霉菌病 ✓</td>
<td>CORRECT — asthma + brownish sputum plugs + eosinophilia 40% + IgE 2800 IU/mL + upper lobe infiltrates = classic ABPA pentad<br />
正确——哮喘+棕色痰栓+嗜酸性粒细胞占40%+IgE 2800 IU/mL+上叶浸润=经典ABPA五联征</td>
<td>Combination of underlying asthma + IgE &gt;1000 + eosinophilia + dark sputum plugs is diagnostic<br />
哮喘基础+IgE&gt;1000+嗜酸性粒细胞增多+深色痰栓组合具有诊断意义</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>B — Eosinophilic leukemia<br />
B — 嗜酸性粒细胞白血病</td>
<td>Neoplastic clonal eosinophil proliferation; would present with bone marrow involvement, hepatosplenomegaly, blast crisis; no link to asthma or brown sputum plugs<br />
肿瘤性克隆性嗜酸性粒细胞增殖；应有骨髓受累、肝脾肿大、急变危象；与哮喘或棕色痰栓无关</td>
<td>No malignant features; entire clinical picture is allergic/hypersensitivity, not neoplastic<br />
无恶性肿瘤特征；全部临床表现为过敏/超敏，非肿瘤性</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>C — Hypereosinophilic syndrome<br />
C — 高嗜酸性粒细胞综合征</td>
<td>HES requires eosinophil count &gt;1500/mm³ for &gt;6 months with end-organ damage AND exclusion of all secondary causes; ABPA is itself a common secondary cause of eosinophilia<br />
HES需嗜酸性粒细胞&gt;1500/mm³持续&gt;6个月伴终末器官损害，且须排除所有继发原因；ABPA本身就是嗜酸性粒细胞增多的常见继发原因</td>
<td>HES is a diagnosis of exclusion; this patient has an identified cause (ABPA)<br />
HES是排除性诊断；该患者已有明确病因（ABPA）</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>D — Polyarteritis nodosa<br />
D — 结节性多动脉炎</td>
<td>Medium-vessel necrotizing vasculitis targeting kidneys, mesenteric arteries, peripheral nerves; characteristically spares the lungs; presents with fever, weight loss, abdominal pain, renal failure, mononeuritis multiplex<br />
累及肾脏、肠系膜动脉、周围神经的中血管坏死性血管炎；特征性地不累及肺；表现为发热、体重减轻、腹痛、肾衰竭、多发性单神经炎</td>
<td>PAN spares the lungs — bilateral pulmonary infiltrates definitively exclude this diagnosis<br />
PAN不累及肺——双肺浸润影明确排除此诊断</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>E — Strongyloides stercoralis infection<br />
E — 粪类圆线虫感染</td>
<td>Causes peripheral eosinophilia + transient pulmonary infiltrates during larval pulmonary migration (Löffler syndrome); requires travel to or residence in endemic tropical/subtropical regions<br />
幼虫肺部移行期引起外周血嗜酸性粒细胞增多+一过性肺浸润（Löffler综合征）；需要前往或居住于流行性热带/亚热带地区</td>
<td>No travel history to endemic area; 15-year asthma history with IgE 2800 makes ABPA overwhelming favorite<br />
无流行区旅行史；15年哮喘史加IgE 2800使ABPA的可能性压倒性地高于此</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

*The most seductive distractor is Hypereosinophilic Syndrome (C) — the eosinophilia and pulmonary infiltrates fit superficially, but HES is a diagnosis of exclusion requiring ruling out all secondary causes; this patient's asthma + IgE 2800 + brownish sputum plugs constitutes a complete ABPA picture.*

最容易迷惑人的干扰项是高嗜酸性粒细胞综合征（C）——嗜酸性粒细胞增多和肺浸润表面看来符合，但HES是排除性诊断，需先排除所有继发原因；该患者的哮喘+IgE 2800+棕色痰栓已构成完整的ABPA诊断图像。

伏立康唑一线；两性霉素B</td>
