## 6. One-Sentence Summary & Memory Hook / 一句话总结 & 记忆钩

**In an asthmatic patient with treatment-refractory wheezing, brownish sputum plugs, markedly elevated IgE, and peripheral eosinophilia with upper-lobe infiltrates, the diagnosis is ABPA — a Type I + III hypersensitivity reaction to airway-colonizing Aspergillus fumigatus.**

**在哮喘患者中出现难治性喘鸣、棕色痰栓、IgE极度升高、外周血嗜酸性粒细胞增多伴上叶浸润影，诊断为ABPA——对气道定植烟曲霉的I型+III型超敏反应。**

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 100%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><p><strong>Memory Hook — ABPA "BITES" Mnemonic / 记忆钩 — ABPA "五咬" 记忆法:</strong></p>
<p>• <strong>B</strong>rown sputum plugs — dark hyphae-laden mucus plugs, pathognomonic / 棕色痰栓——含菌丝的深色黏液栓，具有诊断特异性<br />
• <strong>I</strong>gE markedly elevated (&gt;1000 IU/mL) — single most important lab finding / IgE显著升高（&gt;1000 IU/mL）——最重要的单项实验室检查<br />
• <strong>T</strong>reatment-refractory asthma — ABPA must be suspected whenever asthma fails to respond / 难治性哮喘——哮喘治疗无效时必须怀疑ABPA<br />
• <strong>E</strong>osinophilia — peripheral eosinophilia is a required diagnostic criterion / 嗜酸性粒细胞增多——外周血嗜酸性粒细胞增多是必需诊断标准<br />
• <strong>S</strong>ubsegmental central bronchiectasis — CT hallmark distinguishing ABPA from all others / 亚段中央性支气管扩张——CT标志性表现，与其他疾病相鉴别</p></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
</tbody>
</table>

## 7. High-Yield Topic Knowledge — Allergic Bronchopulmonary Aspergillosis (ABPA) / 高频知识表 — 变应性支气管肺曲霉菌病

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 50%" />
<col style="width: 50%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Topic</strong><br />
<strong>考点</strong></th>
<th><strong>Key Points</strong><br />
<strong>要点</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>Predisposing conditions<br />
易感疾病</td>
<td>Asthma (~1–2% of asthmatics) and cystic fibrosis (~5–10%); healthy immunocompetent hosts do not develop ABPA; Aspergillus colonizes (does not invade) damaged airways<br />
哮喘（约1–2%）和囊性纤维化（约5–10%）；健康免疫正常宿主不患ABPA；曲霉菌定植（不侵袭）受损气道</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Causative organism<br />
致病菌</td>
<td>Aspergillus fumigatus (responsible for &gt;95% of cases); ubiquitous environmental mold found in soil, compost, decaying vegetation; thermotolerant — survives at body temperature<br />
烟曲霉（占&gt;95%病例）；广泛存在于土壤、堆肥、腐烂植被中的环境霉菌；耐热——在体温下存活</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Diagnostic criteria<br />
诊断标准</td>
<td>Required: asthma or CF + immediate Aspergillus skin reactivity + total IgE &gt;1000 IU/mL + peripheral eosinophilia; Supportive: Aspergillus-specific IgG precipitins, pulmonary infiltrates, central bronchiectasis on CT<br />
必要条件：哮喘或CF+曲霉即刻皮肤反应+总IgE&gt;1000 IU/mL+外周血嗜酸性粒细胞增多；支持条件：曲霉特异性IgG沉淀素、肺浸润影、CT中央性支气管扩张</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Imaging findings<br />
影像学表现</td>
<td>CXR: migratory upper-lobe alveolar infiltrates (transient); CT chest (gold standard): central bronchiectasis + "finger-in-glove" mucoid impaction + high-attenuation mucus (HAM) on non-contrast CT<br />
胸片：游走性上叶肺泡浸润影（一过性）；胸部CT（金标准）：中央性支气管扩张+"手指套"黏液嵌塞+平扫CT高密度黏液（HAM）</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Disease stages (Rosenberg-Patterson)<br />
疾病分期（Rosenberg-Patterson）</td>
<td>Stage I (acute active); Stage II (remission, IgE falls); Stage III (exacerbation, IgE rises &gt;100% baseline); Stage IV (steroid-dependent chronic); Stage V (fibrotic end-stage, irreversible)<br />
I期（急性活动）；II期（缓解，IgE下降）；III期（加重，IgE较基线升高&gt;100%）；IV期（激素依赖慢性期）；V期（纤维化终末期，不可逆）</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Treatment<br />
治疗</td>
<td>Oral prednisolone (0.5 mg/kg/day × 2 weeks then taper over months) + itraconazole or voriconazole (antifungal to reduce Aspergillus burden, steroid-sparing) + omalizumab (anti-IgE, for refractory/steroid-dependent disease)<br />
口服泼尼松龙（0.5 mg/kg/天×2周后数月内逐渐减量）+伊曲康唑或伏立康唑（抗真菌减少曲霉负荷，节省激素）+奥马珠单抗（抗IgE，用于难治性/激素依赖性疾病）</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Monitoring disease activity<br />
疾病活动度监测</td>
<td>Serial serum total IgE is the primary monitoring tool; a rise &gt;100% above personal baseline signals exacerbation and warrants steroid dose increase; CT to assess bronchiectasis progression<br />
系列血清总IgE是主要监测指标；较个人基线升高&gt;100%提示加重，需增加激素剂量；CT评估支气管扩张进展</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>ABPA vs. invasive aspergillosis distinction<br />
ABPA与侵袭性曲霉菌病鉴别</td>
<td>ABPA: immunocompetent asthmatic, hypersensitivity mechanism, elevated IgE, eosinophilia, treatment = steroids + antifungals; Invasive: neutropenic/transplant patient, tissue invasion, normal IgE, no eosinophilia, treatment = high-dose voriconazole<br />
ABPA：免疫正常哮喘患者，超敏机制，IgE升高，嗜酸性粒细胞增多，治疗=激素+抗真菌；侵袭性：粒缺/移植患者，组织侵袭，IgE正常，无嗜酸性粒细胞增多，治疗=大剂量伏立康唑</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

## 8. Extensions / 延伸扩展

- **Differential of dark/brown sputum:** ABPA (hyphae-laden mucus plugs), old blood (hemoptysis with clotting), smoking (carbon-laden macrophages) — brownish plugs in an asthmatic are ABPA until proven otherwise\
  **深色/棕色痰鉴别:** ABPA（含菌丝黏液栓）、陈旧血液（咯血伴凝块）、吸烟（含碳巨噬细胞）——哮喘患者棕色痰栓排除前视为ABPA

- **Key complication:** Permanent central bronchiectasis and eventual pulmonary fibrosis (Stage V) if recurrently exacerbated; serial IgE monitoring and prompt steroid treatment prevent progression to irreversible lung destruction\
  **关键并发症:** 若反复加重可致永久性中央性支气管扩张和最终肺纤维化（V期）；系列IgE监测和及时激素治疗可防止进展为不可逆肺损伤

- **Variant — Aspergilloma (fungal ball):** Aspergillus colonizes a pre-existing lung cavity (old TB, sarcoidosis, bullae) forming a mycetoma; presents with hemoptysis (not wheezing or eosinophilia); IgG precipitins positive but IgE normal; treated with bronchial artery embolization or surgical resection\
  **题目变式——曲霉球（真菌球）:** 曲霉菌在既往肺空洞内（陈旧性TB、结节病、肺大疱）形成菌瘤；表现为咯血（非喘鸣或嗜酸性粒细胞增多）；IgG沉淀素阳性但IgE正常；支气管动脉栓塞或手术切除治疗

- **Mnemonic — asthma + CF as the two ABPA triggers:** Remember "A-CF" — Asthma and Cystic Fibrosis are the only two conditions that predispose to ABPA; all other immunocompromised states favor invasive aspergillosis instead\
  **记忆诀——哮喘+CF作为ABPA两大触发条件:** 记住"A-CF"——哮喘（Asthma）和囊性纤维化（Cystic Fibrosis）是仅有的两种易患ABPA的疾病；其他所有免疫受损状态更易患侵袭性曲霉菌病

# Question 157 — Physician-Patient Romantic Relationship Ethics / 医患恋爱关系伦理

## Question Stem / 题干

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 100%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><p>A <strong>24-year-old woman</strong> comes to the office for an <strong>annual employment physical examination</strong>. She feels well. Medical history is unremarkable and she takes no medications. Vital signs are within normal limits. Physical examination discloses no abnormalities. As the physician is preparing to leave the examination room the patient asks, <strong>"Do you think having a romantic relationship with my gynecologist is all right?"</strong></p>
<p><strong>Q: Which of the following is the most appropriate response?</strong></p>
<p>A) "I am under no obligation to report any romantic relationship to a disciplinary board."<br />
B) "If you switch gynecologists it would be acceptable for your former gynecologist to begin a romantic relationship with you immediately."<br />
C) "A mutually consensual romantic relationship between patient and physician can sometimes be justified."<br />
D) "A romantic relationship in this setting is always unethical."<br />
E) "Would you mind telling me who your gynecologist is?"</p>
<p><strong>Correct Answer: D</strong></p></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
</tbody>
</table>

---

## 1. Key Stem Clues / 题干关键词抓考点

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 50%" />
<col style="width: 50%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Key Stem Clue</strong><br />
<strong>关键词</strong></th>
<th><strong>Why It Matters</strong><br />
<strong>为什么重要</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>Annual employment physical — healthy patient<br />
年度体检——患者身体健康</td>
<td>Patient is not acutely ill or emotionally vulnerable, yet the physician-patient power asymmetry still fully applies regardless of visit type<br />
患者并非急性病或情绪脆弱状态，但无论就诊类型如何，医患权力不对等关系依然完全成立</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Romantic relationship with her gynecologist<br />
与妇科医生的恋爱关系</td>
<td>OB/GYN involves intimate physical examination, creating a heightened zone of vulnerability and trust — ACOG guidelines apply directly<br />
妇科涉及私密体格检查，构成高度脆弱性与信任区域——ACOG指南直接适用</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Patient asks "is it all right?"<br />
患者询问"这样可以吗？"</td>
<td>Patient is seeking physician's ethical guidance; the correct answer must unequivocally address the ethics, not deflect or partially approve<br />
患者正在寻求医生的伦理指导；正确回应必须明确表明立场，不能回避或部分认可</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Gynecologist specifically named<br />
明确指明是妇科医生</td>
<td>Specialties involving intimate examination (OB/GYN, psychiatry) are singled out by ACOG/AMA as areas of especially heightened ethical concern<br />
涉及私密检查的专科（妇产科、精神科）被ACOG/AMA专门列为伦理高度敏感领域</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Question asked as physician is leaving<br />
医生准备离开时才提问</td>
<td>Classic "doorknob question" — a sensitive disclosure made at the last moment; the physician must stop and address it fully rather than dismiss it<br />
经典"门把手问题"——患者在最后一刻才提出敏感事项；医生必须停下来充分处理，而非草草带过</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>No mention of consent or mutual interest<br />
未提及双方是否均有意愿</td>
<td>Even if fully consensual, the asymmetry of the physician-patient relationship precludes valid consent — "mutual" is irrelevant to the ethical prohibition<br />
即使双方均有意愿，医患关系的不对等性也使有效同意无法成立——"双方同意"与伦理禁止无关</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

---

## 2. Mechanism / 机制理解

The physician-patient relationship is **inherently asymmetrical**: the physician holds **authority, specialized knowledge, and intimate access** that the patient does not, making genuine autonomous consent to a romantic relationship structurally impossible within this context:

医患关系具有**内在的不对等性**：医生拥有患者所不具备的**权威、专业知识和私密接触权**，这使得在此背景下对恋爱关系的真正自主同意在结构上不可能实现：

- **Trust exploitation:** The patient's trust in a physician's judgment, placed out of medical necessity, cannot be repurposed for personal/romantic interests without corruption of that trust\
  **信任剥削：** 患者出于医疗需要而给予医生的信任，不能被转化为个人/恋爱目的而不损害该信任

- **Power differential:** Patients disclose vulnerabilities — physical, emotional, psychosocial — that create an inherently unequal power dynamic the physician must never exploit\
  **权力差异：** 患者披露身体、情感、心理社会方面的脆弱性，这构成医生绝不能利用的内在不平等权力动态

- **Consent invalidity:** Within the physician-patient relationship, a patient cannot provide meaningful informed consent to a romantic or sexual relationship regardless of apparent willingness\
  **同意无效：** 在医患关系框架内，无论表面上是否自愿，患者均无法对恋爱或性关系提供有意义的知情同意

- **Specialty amplification:** OB/GYN and psychiatry involve the most intimate forms of physical/psychological access, amplifying the potential for exploitation and the ethical prohibition\
  **专科放大效应：** 妇产科和精神科涉及最私密的身体/心理接触形式，放大了被利用的可能性和伦理禁止的力度

**ACOG / AMA rule of thumb:** Sexual or romantic relationships between a physician and a current patient are always unethical; even after relationship termination, subsequent romantic relationships may still be ethically problematic due to lingering influence of the prior relationship.

**ACOG/AMA核心原则：** 医生与现任患者之间的性或恋爱关系始终是不道德的；即使在终止医患关系之后，后续的恋爱关系也可能因前期关系的持续影响而存在伦理问题。

---

## 3. Correct Answer (D) — Physician-Patient Romantic Relationship Always Unethical / 正确答案 (D) — 医患恋爱关系始终不道德

**Absolute ethical prohibition** is the correct stance because ACOG guidelines leave no room for exceptions when a physician-patient relationship is ongoing:

**绝对伦理禁止** 是正确立场，因为在医患关系持续期间，ACOG指南不留任何例外空间：

- A romantic or sexual relationship between a gynecologist and a current patient is categorically unethical under ACOG guidelines regardless of mutual consent\
  根据ACOG指南，妇科医生与现任患者之间的恋爱或性关系无论是否双方同意，均属明确不道德行为

- The power imbalance inherent to the physician-patient relationship makes true autonomous consent impossible — "consensual" is not a valid defense\
  医患关系固有的权力不平衡使真正的自主同意不可能实现——"双方同意"不是有效辩护理由

- Such conduct may constitute sexual misconduct and is grounds for investigation by medical licensing boards and potential criminal prosecution\
  此类行为可能构成性行为不端，是医疗执照委员会调查的理由，并可能面临刑事起诉

- The physician's correct response is first to clearly state that the relationship is unethical, then compassionately explore what the patient has experienced with her gynecologist\
  医生的正确回应是首先明确声明该关系不道德，然后体贴地了解患者与其妇科医生之间发生了什么

**Diagnosis:** The patient's question raises concern for possible ongoing sexual misconduct by her gynecologist. The appropriate first step is to inform the patient the relationship is always unethical, then explore the circumstances before determining whether to report.

**诊断思路：** 患者的提问引发了对其妇科医生可能正在实施性行为不端的担忧。正确的第一步是告知患者此类关系始终不道德，然后了解具体情况，再决定是否上报。

**Treatment:** Clearly state the relationship is unethical → explore what has occurred → if sexual misconduct is suspected, report to medical licensing board, hospital disciplinary board, or other appropriate institutional authorities.

**处理方案：** 明确表示该关系不道德 → 了解已发生的情况 → 若怀疑存在性行为不端，向医疗执照委员会、医院纪律委员会或其他适当机构上报。

---

## 4. Options Elimination / 错误选项排除逻辑

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 33%" />
<col style="width: 33%" />
<col style="width: 33%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Option</strong><br />
<strong>选项</strong></th>
<th><strong>Why Wrong</strong><br />
<strong>为什么错</strong></th>
<th><strong>Key Discriminator</strong><br />
<strong>鉴别要点</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>A — "I am under no obligation to report any romantic relationship to a disciplinary board."<br />
A — "我没有义务向纪律委员会报告任何恋爱关系。"</td>
<td>WRONG — ACOG and AMA guidelines explicitly state that physicians ARE obligated to report suspected sexual misconduct to appropriate authorities including medical licensing boards and hospital disciplinary boards<br />
错误——ACOG和AMA指南明确规定，医生有义务向包括医疗执照委员会和医院纪律委员会在内的适当机构报告涉嫌性行为不端的情况</td>
<td>Reporting obligation is an affirmative professional duty, not optional<br />
报告义务是主动的职业责任，并非可选项</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>B — "If you switch gynecologists it would be acceptable for your former gynecologist to begin a romantic relationship with you immediately."<br />
B — "如果你换了妇科医生，你前任妇科医生立即与你开始恋爱关系是可以接受的。"</td>
<td>WRONG — Terminating the physician-patient relationship does not immediately resolve the ethical concerns; the prior relationship's power dynamics and influence persist and may create ongoing ethical dilemmas<br />
错误——终止医患关系并不能立即解决伦理顾虑；前期关系中的权力动态和影响持续存在，可能导致持续的伦理困境</td>
<td>"Immediate" is never acceptable; prior relationship creates lasting ethical complications<br />
"立即"从来都不可接受；前期关系产生持续的伦理复杂性</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>C — "A mutually consensual romantic relationship between patient and physician can sometimes be justified."<br />
C — "医患之间双方同意的恋爱关系有时可以被合理化。"</td>
<td>WRONG — The power asymmetry of the physician-patient relationship means patients cannot provide valid consent within this context; "mutually consensual" is a false premise and does not justify such relationships<br />
错误——医患关系的权力不对等意味着患者在此背景下无法提供有效同意；"双方同意"是错误前提，不能为此类关系提供合理依据</td>
<td>No circumstance justifies a romantic relationship with a current patient<br />
任何情况下与现任患者发展恋爱关系都不被允许</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>D — "A romantic relationship in this setting is always unethical." ✓<br />
D — "在这种情况下，恋爱关系始终是不道德的。" ✓</td>
<td>CORRECT — This directly reflects ACOG guidelines and correctly communicates to the patient that the relationship is categorically unethical, serving as the appropriate first step before further exploration<br />
正确——这直接反映了ACOG指南，正确地向患者传达了该关系属于明确不道德的信息，是进一步了解情况之前的恰当第一步</td>
<td>ACOG: current patient + romantic/sexual = always unethical, no exceptions<br />
ACOG：现任患者+恋爱/性关系=始终不道德，无例外</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>E — "Would you mind telling me who your gynecologist is?"<br />
E — "你介意告诉我你的妇科医生是谁吗？"</td>
<td>WRONG AS FIRST RESPONSE — While eventually appropriate, asking for the name before addressing the ethics of the situation may alarm the patient and shut down communication; the physician must first clearly state the relationship is unethical, then explore circumstances before seeking identifying information<br />
作为第一反应是错误的——虽然最终是合适的，但在阐明伦理问题之前就询问姓名可能会使患者感到警觉并中断沟通；医生必须首先明确声明该关系不道德，再了解情况，之后才寻求身份信息</td>
<td>Sequence matters: ethics statement → explore experience → then identify / gather info for reporting<br />
顺序至关重要：声明伦理立场 → 了解患者经历 → 然后获取信息以便上报</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

*Choice C is the strongest distractor — "mutual consent" sounds reasonable but fails because the power asymmetry of the physician-patient relationship structurally invalidates consent, a principle that overrides any appearance of voluntariness.*

选项C是最强的干扰项——"双方同意"听起来合理，但实际上无效，因为医患关系的权力不对等在结构上使同意失去效力，这一原则凌驾于任何表面上的自愿之上。

---

<td>Assuming termination of medical relationship immediately makes romance acceptable<br />
假设终止医疗关系后恋爱关系立即变得可接受</td>

<td>Specialties with heightened concern<br />
高度关注的专科</td>
<td>OB/GYN and psychiatry — involve the most intimate physical/psychological contact<br />
妇产科和精神科——涉及最私密的身体/心理接触</td>
<td>Applying stricter rules only to psychiatry and assuming OB/GYN is less restricted<br />
只对精神科适用更严格规则，认为妇产科限制较少</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

---

## 6. One-Sentence Summary & Memory Hook / 一句话总结 & 记忆钩

**Per ACOG guidelines, a romantic or sexual relationship between a physician and a current patient is always unethical — the correct first response is to state this clearly, then compassionately explore the patient's experience before reporting suspected misconduct.**

**根据ACOG指南，医生与现任患者之间的恋爱或性关系始终不道德——正确的第一步是明确声明这一点，然后体贴地了解患者的经历，再上报涉嫌的不端行为。**

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 100%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><p><strong>Memory Hook — ACOG "CLEAR" Protocol / 记忆钩 — ACOG "CLEAR" 处理规程:</strong></p>
<p>• <strong>C</strong>urrent patient = always unethical, no exceptions — any current physician-patient relationship forecloses romance / <strong>C</strong>urrent（现任患者）= 始终不道德，无例外——任何现存医患关系都排除恋爱可能<br />
• <strong>L</strong>abel it first — state the relationship is unethical before doing anything else / <strong>L</strong>abel（先定性）——在采取任何其他行动之前，先声明该关系不道德<br />
• <strong>E</strong>xplore the experience — ask what has happened between the patient and her gynecologist / <strong>E</strong>xplore（了解经历）——询问患者与其妇科医生之间发生了什么<br />
• <strong>A</strong>lways report suspected misconduct — to licensing board, hospital disciplinary board, or appropriate authorities / <strong>A</strong>lways report（必须上报）——向执照委员会、医院纪律委员会或适当机构上报涉嫌不端行为<br />
• <strong>R</strong>omantic aftermath is still complicated — even post-termination relationships carry ethical risk from prior power dynamics / <strong>R</strong>omantic aftermath（终止后的恋爱关系依然复杂）——即使终止医患关系后的恋爱关系，也因前期权力动态而存在伦理风险</p></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
</tbody>
</table>

---

## 7. High-Yield Topic Knowledge — Physician-Patient Relationship Ethics (ACOG/AMA Guidelines) / 高频知识表 — 医患关系伦理（ACOG/AMA指南）

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 50%" />
<col style="width: 50%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Topic</strong><br />
<strong>考点</strong></th>
<th><strong>Key Points</strong><br />
<strong>要点</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>ACOG stance on current patient relationships<br />
ACOG对现任患者关系的立场</td>
<td>Sexual or romantic relationships between a gynecologist and a current patient are ALWAYS unethical; may be grounds for investigation or criminal prosecution; no exceptions for mutual consent<br />
妇科医生与现任患者之间的性或恋爱关系始终不道德；可能构成调查或刑事起诉的理由；双方同意不构成例外</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>AMA stance on post-termination relationships<br />
AMA对终止关系后恋爱关系的立场</td>
<td>AMA Code of Ethics requires complete termination of physician-patient relationship before pursuing romance; even then, the prior relationship may exert influence creating ongoing ethical dilemmas<br />
AMA伦理守则要求在追求恋爱关系之前完全终止医患关系；即便如此，前期关系可能仍持续发挥影响，产生持续伦理困境</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Why consent is invalid within physician-patient context<br />
为何医患关系框架内同意无效</td>
<td>The power asymmetry — physician's authority, knowledge, intimate access — structurally prevents the patient from exercising true autonomous consent regardless of apparent willingness<br />
权力不对等——医生的权威、专业知识、私密接触权——在结构上阻止患者行使真正的自主同意，无论其表面意愿如何</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Specialties with heightened ethical scrutiny<br />
需要更高伦理关注的专科</td>
<td>OB/GYN and psychiatry are especially scrutinized because of the intimate nature of examination/therapy; the vulnerability of patients in these settings amplifies the prohibition<br />
妇产科和精神科因检查/治疗的私密性而受到特别审查；这些场景中患者的脆弱性放大了禁止行为的重要性</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Physician's reporting obligation<br />
医生的报告义务</td>
<td>When sexual misconduct is suspected, physicians are obligated — not optional — to report to medical licensing boards, hospital disciplinary boards, or other institutional authorities<br />
当怀疑存在性行为不端时，医生有义务（而非可选）向医疗执照委员会、医院纪律委员会或其他机构当局报告</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Correct sequence of response to patient disclosure<br />
对患者披露信息的正确应对顺序</td>
<td>(1) State relationship is always unethical; (2) Explore what the patient has experienced; (3) Identify the involved physician; (4) Report suspected misconduct to appropriate authorities<br />
（1）声明该关系始终不道德；（2）了解患者的经历；（3）确认相关医生身份；（4）向适当机构上报涉嫌不端行为</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>"Doorknob question" phenomenon<br />
"门把手问题"现象</td>
<td>Sensitive disclosures made as physician is leaving require the physician to stop, take the disclosure seriously, and address it fully rather than dismissing it as an afterthought<br />
在医生准备离开时才提出的敏感披露，要求医生停下来，认真对待该披露，充分处理，而非当作事后想法草草带过</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

---

## 8. Extensions / 延伸扩展

- **Differential of "always" vs. "sometimes" ethical prohibitions:** Physician-patient romance is one of the few absolute ("always") ethical prohibitions in USMLE ethics — contrast with most clinical ethics scenarios (truth-telling, end-of-life, resource allocation) that require contextual balancing\
  **"始终"与"有时"伦理禁止的区别：** 医患恋爱关系是USMLE伦理中少数绝对性（"始终"）禁止之一——对比大多数临床伦理场景（如告知真相、临终决策、资源分配），后者需要情境性权衡

- **Variant — psychiatry:** The prohibition is equally absolute in psychiatry due to transference dynamics; post-termination romantic relationships in psychiatry are also explicitly prohibited by the APA (unlike the AMA's more cautious but not absolute post-termination guidance)\
  **题目变式——精神科：** 由于移情动力学，精神科中的禁止同样是绝对的；精神科终止关系后的恋爱关系也被APA明确禁止（不同于AMA对终止关系后的更谨慎但非绝对的指导）

- **Key complication — "former patient" framing:** USMLE may phrase scenarios as "former patient" to test whether examinees know that prior relationships still carry ethical weight; the correct answer will still caution against such relationships rather than endorse them\
  **关键复杂情况——"前患者"表述：** USMLE可能将场景表述为"前患者"来测试考生是否知道前期关系仍具有伦理分量；正确答案仍应对此类关系发出警告，而非认可

- **Reporting scope — who receives the report:** Appropriate authorities include the state medical licensing board, hospital credentialing/disciplinary board, and where applicable law enforcement; the patient's confidentiality does not override the duty to report sexual misconduct\
  **上报范围——向谁上报：** 适当当局包括州医疗执照委员会、医院资质/纪律委员会，以及在适用情况下的执法机关；患者的保密权不能凌驾于报告性行为不端的义务之上

# Question 158 — Tubular Adenoma with Dysplasia: Post-Polypectomy Surveillance / 管状腺瘤伴不典型增生：息肉切除术后监测

## Question Stem / 题干

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 100%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><p>A <strong>healthy 52-year-old man</strong> comes to the physician for a <strong>routine total colonoscopy</strong>. He has <strong>no history of blood in his stool</strong> or rectal bleeding. There is no family history of colorectal polyps or cancer. He takes no medications and has never smoked cigarettes. Physical examination shows no abnormalities. Colonoscopy shows a <strong>3-mm pedunculated polyp in the cecum</strong>. No other abnormalities are noted. The polyp is <strong>completely excised</strong>. Histopathologic evaluation shows <strong>dysplastic-appearing columnar epithelial cells confined by the basement membrane</strong>, lining a <strong>fibrovascular stalk</strong>.</p>
<p><strong>Q: Which of the following is the most appropriate recommendation for future screening for colon cancer in this patient?</strong></p>
<p>A) Colonoscopy in 1 year<br />
B) Colonoscopy in 3 years<br />
C) Colonoscopy in 10 years<br />
D) Flexible sigmoidoscopy in 1 year<br />
E) No further screening is indicated unless annual test of the stool for occult blood is positive</p>
<p><strong>Correct Answer: B</strong></p></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
</tbody>
</table>

## 1. Key Stem Clues / 题干关键词抓考点

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 50%" />
<col style="width: 50%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Key Stem Clue</strong><br />
<strong>关键词</strong></th>
<th><strong>Why It Matters</strong><br />
<strong>为什么重要</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>52-year-old man, routine colonoscopy<br />
52岁男性，常规结肠镜</td>
<td>Age ≥45 triggers USPSTF colorectal cancer screening; this is a standard screening scenario<br />
年龄≥45岁符合USPSTF结直肠癌筛查指征；属于标准筛查场景</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>No symptoms, no rectal bleeding<br />
无症状、无直肠出血</td>
<td>Truly incidental finding — not symptom-driven; polyp found on routine exam<br />
真正偶然发现——非症状驱动；息肉于常规检查中发现</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>No family history of polyps or cancer<br />
无结直肠息肉或癌症家族史</td>
<td>Low hereditary baseline risk; surveillance interval is determined by histology, not family history<br />
遗传基线风险低；监测间隔由组织学决定，而非家族史</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>3-mm pedunculated polyp, single lesion<br />
3mm有蒂息肉，单发</td>
<td>Small (&lt;10 mm) and single — size and number alone would suggest low risk, but histology overrides<br />
小（&lt;10mm）且单发——仅凭大小和数量提示低危，但组织学结果凌驾其上</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Completely excised<br />
完全切除</td>
<td>Margin-clear resection is prerequisite for standard surveillance intervals (vs. piecemeal/incomplete removal)<br />
切缘阴性是标准监测间隔的前提（与分片/不完全切除相比）</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Dysplastic cells confined by basement membrane<br />
不典型增生细胞局限于基底膜内</td>
<td>Dysplasia without invasion = high-grade dysplasia within adenoma; presence of ANY dysplasia triggers 3-year follow-up<br />
有不典型增生但无浸润 = 腺瘤内高度不典型增生；任何不典型增生均触发3年随访间隔</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Fibrovascular stalk<br />
纤维血管茎</td>
<td>Pathologic hallmark of pedunculated (not sessile) adenoma; pedunculated morphology facilitates complete snare resection<br />
有蒂（非无蒂）腺瘤的病理标志；有蒂形态有利于圈套器完整切除</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

## 2. Mechanism / 机制理解

The **adenoma-carcinoma sequence** is the dominant pathway for colorectal cancer, driven by stepwise mutations (APC → KRAS → SMAD4 → TP53); **dysplasia** marks accelerated progression along this pathway:

**腺瘤-癌变序列**是结直肠癌的主要途径，由逐步累积的突变驱动（APC → KRAS → SMAD4 → TP53）；**不典型增生**标志着沿此途径的加速进展：

- Normal mucosa → **dysplastic adenoma** → **carcinoma in situ** (dysplastic cells above intact basement membrane) → **invasive carcinoma** (breach of basement membrane → lymphovascular access)\
  正常黏膜 → **不典型增生腺瘤** → **原位癌**（异型细胞位于完整基底膜上方） → **浸润性癌**（突破基底膜 → 获得淋巴血管通道）

- The **basement membrane** is the critical oncologic boundary: dysplasia above it carries no metastatic potential; invasion below it allows nodal and distant spread\
  **基底膜**是关键的肿瘤学界限：异型增生局限于其上方无转移潜能；突破其下方则具有淋巴结和远处转移能力

- Completely excised dysplastic adenoma = curative, but residual field risk elevates future cancer probability → mandates **shorter surveillance** than a normal colonoscopy\
  完全切除的不典型增生腺瘤=治愈性切除，但残余区域风险升高未来癌变概率 → 需要比正常结肠镜更短的监测间隔

**Anatomic rule of thumb:** A pedunculated polyp on a fibrovascular stalk is mechanically easier to snare en bloc than a flat sessile polyp; confirmed complete excision is what permits standard 3-year (not 3–6 month) surveillance.

**解剖小窍门:** 有纤维血管茎的有蒂息肉比扁平无蒂息肉更易整块圈套切除；确认完全切除才能采用标准3年（而非3-6个月）监测。

## 3. Correct Answer (B) — Colonoscopy in 3 Years / 正确答案 (B) — 3年后复查结肠镜

**Adenoma with dysplasia** is classified as a high-risk adenomatous polyp regardless of its small size (3 mm), triggering a 3-year surveillance colonoscopy after complete resection:

**伴不典型增生的腺瘤**无论大小（3mm）均归为高危腺瘤性息肉，完全切除后须安排3年监测结肠镜：

- The 3-year interval applies to: any adenoma with dysplasia (high- or low-grade), villous or tubulovillous histology, sessile polyps \<10 mm with dysplasia, 5–10 tubular adenomas, or one tubular adenoma ≥10 mm — all completely removed\
  3年间隔适用于：任何伴不典型增生（高度或低度）的腺瘤、绒毛状/管状绒毛状腺瘤、\<10mm伴不典型增生的无蒂息肉、5-10个管状腺瘤、或单个≥10mm管状腺瘤——均须完全切除

- This patient's polyp — though tiny (3 mm) and solitary — carries dysplasia; histology, not size or number alone, determines the surveillance category\
  本患者息肉虽然微小（3mm）且单发，但存在不典型增生；决定监测类别的是组织学，而非单纯大小或数量

- "Confined by the basement membrane" = no invasion → still an adenoma (not invasive carcinoma); complete excision is curative; no additional resection required\
  "局限于基底膜"=无浸润 → 仍为腺瘤（非浸润性癌）；完全切除即为治愈性；无需追加切除

**Diagnosis:** Pedunculated tubular adenoma with high-grade dysplasia (dysplastic columnar epithelium above intact basement membrane, fibrovascular stalk confirmed, completely excised).

**诊断:** 有蒂管状腺瘤伴高度不典型增生（基底膜完整上方异型柱状上皮，确认纤维血管茎，完全切除）。

**Treatment:** No additional resection needed; schedule repeat colonoscopy in 3 years per USPSTF/ACG post-polypectomy surveillance guidelines.

**治疗:** 无需追加切除；按USPSTF/ACG息肉切除术后监测指南安排3年后复查结肠镜。

## 4. Options Elimination / 错误选项排除逻辑

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 33%" />
<col style="width: 33%" />
<col style="width: 33%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Option</strong><br />
<strong>选项</strong></th>
<th><strong>Why Wrong</strong><br />
<strong>为什么错</strong></th>
<th><strong>Key Discriminator</strong><br />
<strong>鉴别要点</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>A — Colonoscopy in 1 year<br />
A — 1年后结肠镜</td>
<td>Too aggressive for a single dysplastic polyp; 1-year interval is reserved exclusively for &gt;10 adenomas found on a single exam<br />
对单个不典型增生息肉过于积极；1年间隔专门保留给单次检查发现&gt;10个腺瘤</td>
<td>Number threshold: &gt;10 adenomas → 1 year; this patient has only 1<br />
数量阈值：&gt;10个腺瘤→1年；本患者仅1个</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>B — Colonoscopy in 3 years ✓<br />
B — 3年后结肠镜 ✓</td>
<td>CORRECT — any dysplasia in a completely excised adenoma mandates 3-year surveillance per national guidelines<br />
正确——完全切除的腺瘤中存在任何不典型增生，依据国家指南须3年监测</td>
<td>Dysplasia present + completely excised → 3 years, regardless of size<br />
存在不典型增生+完全切除→3年，不论大小</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>C — Colonoscopy in 10 years<br />
C — 10年后结肠镜</td>
<td>Appropriate only for a normal colonoscopy (no adenomas); any adenoma with dysplasia cannot be deferred 10 years<br />
仅适用于正常结肠镜（无腺瘤）；任何伴不典型增生的腺瘤不可推迟10年</td>
<td>Abnormal histology = mandatory early follow-up; 10 years is for truly normal findings<br />
组织学异常=必须早期随访；10年仅适用于真正正常的结果</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>D — Flexible sigmoidoscopy in 1 year<br />
D — 1年后乙状结肠镜</td>
<td>Wrong modality after abnormal full colonoscopy; sigmoidoscopy visualizes only left colon and rectum, leaving the right colon (and cecum — the site of this polyp) unexamined<br />
异常全结肠镜后采用错误检查方式；乙状结肠镜仅观察左侧结肠和直肠，右侧结肠（及盲肠——本例息肉部位）无法评估</td>
<td>After abnormal colonoscopy → repeat full colonoscopy only; sigmoidoscopy is anatomically insufficient<br />
异常结肠镜后→仅重复全结肠镜；乙状结肠镜解剖覆盖不足</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>E — No further screening unless FOBT positive<br />
E — 除非FOBT阳性否则无需进一步筛查</td>
<td>Dangerously inadequate; FOBT is neither sensitive nor specific for adenomas or early cancer; active colonoscopic surveillance after dysplastic adenoma is mandatory<br />
危险地不充分；FOBT对腺瘤或早期癌既不敏感也不特异；不典型增生腺瘤后须主动结肠镜监测</td>
<td>FOBT detects bleeding, not adenomas; surveillance interval is dictated by histology, not FOBT result<br />
FOBT检测出血，非腺瘤；监测间隔由组织学决定，非FOBT结果</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

*The most dangerous distractor is Choice C (10 years) — the polyp is tiny and solitary, making "no worries" feel intuitive, but the presence of dysplasia is the single feature that overrides size and number.*

最危险的干扰项是C（10年）——息肉极小且单发，直觉上"无需担心"，但不典型增生的存在是凌驾于大小和数量之上的唯一关键特征。

## 6. One-Sentence Summary & Memory Hook / 一句话总结 & 记忆钩

**A completely excised adenoma with dysplasia — regardless of its small size or solitary nature — mandates follow-up colonoscopy in 3 years, because dysplasia is the single histologic feature that overrides size and number in risk stratification.**

**完全切除的伴不典型增生腺瘤——无论其大小或单发性——均需3年后复查结肠镜，因为不典型增生是风险分层中凌驾于大小和数量之上的唯一组织学特征。**

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 100%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><p><strong>Memory Hook — The N-D-M Surveillance Ladder / 记忆钩 — "NDM阶梯"监测间隔:</strong></p>
<p>• <strong>N</strong>ormal scope → 10 years (Nothing found, No worries, see you Next decade) / 正常结肠镜→10年（一切正常，10年后见）<br />
• <strong>D</strong>ysplasia / Villous / ≥3 adenomas → 3 years (Danger signs Demand closer follow-up) / 不典型增生/绒毛状/≥3个腺瘤→3年（危险信号需更密切随访）<br />
• <strong>M</strong>assive burden (&gt;10 adenomas) → 1 year (Maximum urgency, Must come back soon) / 大量腺瘤负荷（&gt;10个）→1年（最高紧迫性，必须尽快复查）</p></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
</tbody>
</table>

## 7. High-Yield Topic Knowledge — Colorectal Cancer Screening and Post-Polypectomy Surveillance / 高频知识表 — 结直肠癌筛查与息肉切除术后监测

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 50%" />
<col style="width: 50%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Topic</strong><br />
<strong>考点</strong></th>
<th><strong>Key Points</strong><br />
<strong>要点</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>USPSTF screening initiation age<br />
USPSTF筛查起始年龄</td>
<td>Average-risk adults: begin at age 45, continue until 75; ages 76–85 individualize; stop after 85<br />
普通风险成人：45岁开始，持续至75岁；76-85岁个体化；85岁后停止</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Normal colonoscopy interval<br />
正常结肠镜间隔</td>
<td>10 years if no polyps or only small (&lt;10 mm) hyperplastic polyps (non-adenomatous) found<br />
无息肉或仅发现小（&lt;10mm）增生性息肉（非腺瘤性），间隔10年</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>3-year rule: high-risk adenoma criteria<br />
3年规则：高危腺瘤标准</td>
<td>ANY of: ≥3 adenomas; adenoma ≥10 mm; villous or tubulovillous histology; any grade of dysplasia; completely removed — all trigger 3-year follow-up<br />
满足任一：≥3个腺瘤；腺瘤≥10mm；绒毛状或管状绒毛状组织学；任何程度不典型增生；完全切除——均触发3年随访</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>1-year rule: very high adenoma burden<br />
1年规则：腺瘤负荷极高</td>
<td>&gt;10 adenomas on a single colonoscopy → 1-year follow-up; also prompts consideration of FAP (APC mutation) or MUTYH-associated polyposis<br />
单次结肠镜&gt;10个腺瘤→1年随访；同时提示考虑FAP（APC突变）或MUTYH相关息肉病</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Incomplete excision exception<br />
不完全切除例外</td>
<td>Piecemeal or uncertain-margin polypectomy → repeat colonoscopy at 3–6 months (not 3 years) to confirm complete removal; confirmed complete excision is prerequisite for 3-year interval<br />
分片切除或切缘不确定→3-6个月内复查结肠镜以确认完全切除；确认完全切除是3年间隔的前提</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Why sigmoidoscopy is wrong here<br />
本题中乙状结肠镜为何错误</td>
<td>Flexible sigmoidoscopy only reaches the splenic flexure (~60 cm); the cecum is beyond its reach; after any abnormal full colonoscopy, only full colonoscopy is appropriate for surveillance<br />
乙状结肠镜仅达脾曲（约60cm）；盲肠超出其范围；任何异常全结肠镜后，仅全结肠镜适合监测</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>FOBT role after adenoma<br />
腺瘤后FOBT的作用</td>
<td>Fecal occult blood testing (FOBT/FIT) is a primary screening tool for average-risk patients, not a surveillance tool after known adenoma; negative FOBT does not reassure after dysplastic adenoma<br />
粪便隐血检测（FOBT/FIT）是普通风险患者的初级筛查工具，不是已知腺瘤后的监测工具；阴性FOBT不能在不典型增生腺瘤后提供保证</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>High-risk family history rules<br />
高危家族史规则</td>
<td>First-degree relative with CRC diagnosed &lt;60 → begin screening at age 40 or 10 years before relative's diagnosis age (whichever earlier); this patient has no family history so standard rules apply<br />
一级亲属&lt;60岁诊断CRC→40岁或亲属诊断年龄减10年时开始筛查（取较早者）；本患者无家族史故适用标准规则</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

## 8. Extensions / 延伸扩展

- **Adenoma-carcinoma sequence timeline:** Average progression from normal mucosa to invasive carcinoma takes 10–15 years; this long window is precisely why 10-year colonoscopy intervals are safe for normal findings — and why dysplasia (accelerated progression) warrants 3-year follow-up\
  **腺瘤-癌变序列时间轴:** 从正常黏膜到浸润性癌平均需10-15年；正是这一漫长窗口期使得正常结果可采用10年间隔——也因此不典型增生（加速进展）需要3年随访

- **Carcinoma in situ vs. T1 invasion — the basement membrane distinction:** "Dysplastic cells confined by the basement membrane" = Tis (in situ); if basement membrane is breached = pT1 invasive cancer, requiring consideration of surgical colectomy even if endoscopically removed\
  **原位癌与T1浸润的区别——基底膜的界定意义:** "异型增生细胞局限于基底膜"=Tis（原位）；若突破基底膜=pT1浸润性癌，即使内镜切除仍需考虑手术切除

- **Alternative screening modalities for average-risk patients:** Annual FIT; CT colonography every 5 years; stool DNA (Cologuard) every 1–3 years — all abnormal results require diagnostic colonoscopy; none replace surveillance colonoscopy after a known dysplastic adenoma\
  **普通风险患者的替代筛查方式:** 年度FIT；每5年CT结肠造影；每1-3年粪便DNA（Cologuard）——所有异常结果均需诊断性结肠镜；均不能替代已知不典型增生腺瘤后的监测结肠镜

- **Key distractor pattern on NBME — size illusion:** NBME frequently tests the principle that a tiny adenoma with dysplasia outranks a large adenoma without dysplasia in surveillance urgency; always read histology before assigning the surveillance interval\
  **NBME常见干扰模式——大小幻觉:** NBME频繁考查以下原则：伴不典型增生的微小腺瘤在监测紧迫性上优先于无不典型增生的大腺瘤；始终先阅读组织学结果再确定监测间隔

# Question 159 — Iron Deficiency Anemia from Cow's Milk / 牛奶喂养致缺铁性贫血

## Question Stem / 题干

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 100%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><p>A healthy <strong>18-month-old</strong> boy is brought for a well-child examination. He was born at <strong>37 weeks' gestation</strong>, needed no resuscitation, and had no neonatal problems. He was fed <strong>formula for the first 2 months</strong> of life, and then his mother <strong>substituted cow's milk</strong> because of the expense of the formula. He has received <strong>no supplements or medications</strong>. Examination shows <strong>no abnormalities</strong>.</p>
<p><strong>Q: This child is at greatest risk for which of the following?</strong></p>
<p>A) Iron deficiency anemia<br />
B) Pellagra<br />
C) Protein-calorie malnutrition<br />
D) Vitamin B12 (cobalamin) deficiency<br />
E) Vitamin D deficiency</p>
<p><strong>Correct Answer: A</strong></p></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
</tbody>
</table>

## 1. Key Stem Clues / 题干关键词抓考点

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 50%" />
<col style="width: 50%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Key Stem Clue</strong><br />
<strong>关键词</strong></th>
<th><strong>Why It Matters</strong><br />
<strong>为什么重要</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>18-month-old boy<br />
18个月男孩</td>
<td>Infants and toddlers are at peak risk for iron deficiency; rapid growth demands high iron intake<br />
婴幼儿是缺铁高峰风险期；快速生长需要大量铁摄入</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Formula for first 2 months only<br />
仅前2个月使用配方奶</td>
<td>Iron-fortified formula provides adequate iron; switching away removes this protection<br />
铁强化配方奶提供足够铁；切换后失去此保护</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Substituted cow's milk<br />
改用牛奶</td>
<td>Whole cow's milk: low iron bioavailability, impairs iron absorption, causes occult GI bleeding<br />
全脂牛奶：铁生物利用率低，抑制铁吸收，导致隐匿性消化道出血</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>No supplements or medications<br />
未服用任何补充剂</td>
<td>No exogenous iron source to compensate for cow's milk's inadequacy<br />
无外源性铁补充以弥补牛奶喂养的不足</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Examination shows no abnormalities<br />
体检无异常</td>
<td>Mild-to-moderate iron deficiency may be clinically silent; diagnosis requires labs<br />
轻中度缺铁可能临床无症状；需实验室检查诊断</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Born at 37 weeks (late preterm)<br />
37周出生（晚期早产）</td>
<td>Late preterm infants have lower iron stores than term infants, increasing baseline risk<br />
晚期早产儿铁储备低于足月儿，增加基础风险</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

## 2. Mechanism / 机制理解

**Iron deficiency anemia** in cow's milk-fed infants results from three converging mechanisms affecting **iron balance**:

**缺铁性贫血**在牛奶喂养婴儿中由三个共同影响**铁平衡**的机制所致：

- Cow's milk contains very low iron (~0.5 mg/L) with poor bioavailability (~10%) compared to breast milk (~50% bioavailability)\
  牛奶含铁量极低（约0.5 mg/L），生物利用率差（约10%），远低于母乳（约50%）

- Bovine milk proteins (casein) directly impair iron absorption in the infant gut by competing with iron uptake mechanisms\
  牛奶蛋白（酪蛋白）直接抑制婴儿肠道铁吸收，与铁摄取机制竞争

- Whole cow's milk causes occult intestinal microhemorrhage in infants under 12 months, leading to chronic iron loss that depletes stores over time\
  全脂牛奶在12个月以下婴儿中引起隐匿性肠道微出血，导致慢性铁丢失逐渐耗竭铁储备

**Developmental consequence:** Early iron deficiency causes irreversible impairment of myelination and neurotransmitter synthesis; neurocognitive and psychomotor deficits persist even after iron repletion.

**发育后果:** 早期缺铁导致髓鞘形成和神经递质合成不可逆损害；即使补铁后认知和精神运动缺陷仍可持续。

## 3. Correct Answer (A) — Iron Deficiency Anemia / 正确答案 (A) — 缺铁性贫血

**Iron Deficiency Anemia** is the most common nutritional deficiency in children worldwide, and whole cow's milk feeding is the prototypical cause in infancy:

**缺铁性贫血**是全球儿童最常见的营养缺乏症，牛奶喂养是婴儿期的典型病因：

- Whole cow's milk should NOT be introduced before 12 months; even after 12 months, intake should be limited to ≤24 oz/day to prevent milk from displacing iron-rich foods\
  全脂牛奶不应在12个月前引入；即使12个月后每日摄入也应限制在≤24盎司，防止牛奶取代富铁食物

- Iron-fortified formula or breast milk is the recommended feeding for the first year of life\
  建议婴儿出生后第一年使用铁强化配方奶或母乳

- Late preterm infants (34–37 weeks) have reduced iron stores compared to term infants, adding to this child's risk\
  晚期早产儿（34–37周）铁储备低于足月儿，进一步增加了该患儿的风险

**Diagnosis:** Microcytic hypochromic anemia; low serum ferritin (earliest marker), low serum iron, elevated TIBC, elevated RDW; peripheral smear shows microcytes and poikilocytes

**诊断:** 小细胞低色素性贫血；血清铁蛋白降低（最早标志），血清铁低，TIBC升高，RDW升高；外周血涂片见小红细胞和异形红细胞

**Treatment:** Oral elemental iron 3–6 mg/kg/day; dietary counseling to limit cow's milk and increase iron-rich foods; recheck CBC in 4 weeks to confirm reticulocyte response

**治疗:** 口服元素铁3–6 mg/kg/天；饮食咨询限制牛奶摄入并增加富铁食物；4周后复查血常规确认网织红细胞治疗反应

## 4. Options Elimination / 错误选项排除逻辑

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 33%" />
<col style="width: 33%" />
<col style="width: 33%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Option</strong><br />
<strong>选项</strong></th>
<th><strong>Why Wrong</strong><br />
<strong>为什么错</strong></th>
<th><strong>Key Discriminator</strong><br />
<strong>鉴别要点</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>A — Iron deficiency anemia ✓<br />
A — 缺铁性贫血 ✓</td>
<td>CORRECT — Whole cow's milk has poor iron bioavailability and causes occult GI bleeding, depleting iron stores<br />
正确——全脂牛奶铁生物利用率低且引起隐匿性消化道出血，耗竭铁储备</td>
<td>Classic high-yield association: cow's milk substitution in infancy → iron deficiency<br />
经典高频关联：婴儿期牛奶替代→缺铁</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>B — Pellagra<br />
B — 糙皮病</td>
<td>Pellagra = niacin deficiency; presents with diarrhea, dementia, dermatitis ("3 Ds"); not caused by cow's milk<br />
糙皮病=烟酸缺乏；表现为腹泻、痴呆、皮炎（"3D"）；非牛奶所致</td>
<td>No dietary history suggesting niacin deficiency; no 3 Ds on exam<br />
无烟酸缺乏饮食史；体检无3D表现</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>C — Protein-calorie malnutrition<br />
C — 蛋白质热量营养不良</td>
<td>Cow's milk provides adequate protein and calories; exam shows no abnormalities, ruling out failure to thrive or muscle wasting<br />
牛奶提供足够蛋白质和热量；体检无异常，排除生长迟滞或肌肉萎缩</td>
<td>Normal exam excludes malnutrition; PCM presents with stunted growth and muscle wasting<br />
体检正常排除营养不良；PCM表现为生长迟缓和肌肉萎缩</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>D — Vitamin B12 deficiency<br />
D — 维生素B12缺乏</td>
<td>Cow's milk contains adequate B12; infant B12 deficiency typically occurs in exclusively breastfed infants of vegan mothers<br />
牛奶含有足量B12；婴儿B12缺乏通常发生在素食母亲纯母乳喂养的婴儿中</td>
<td>Wrong dietary exposure; B12 deficiency → megaloblastic macrocytic anemia, not microcytic<br />
饮食暴露不符；B12缺乏→大细胞性贫血，非小细胞性</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>E — Vitamin D deficiency<br />
E — 维生素D缺乏</td>
<td>In the US, whole cow's milk is vitamin D-fortified; primary rickets risk is in breastfed infants without supplementation<br />
美国全脂牛奶已强化维生素D；佝偻病主要风险为未补充维生素D的母乳喂养婴儿</td>
<td>Cow's milk provides vitamin D; iron is the critical missing nutrient in this scenario<br />
牛奶提供维生素D；本题关键缺乏的是铁而非维生素D</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

*The most tempting distractor is (E) Vitamin D deficiency — many students associate cow's milk with inadequate vitamin D, forgetting that US cow's milk is fortified with vitamin D but critically lacks bioavailable iron.*

最容易误选的干扰项是维生素D缺乏（E）——许多学生将牛奶与维生素D不足联系起来，忽略了美国牛奶已强化维生素D，但关键缺乏的是生物可利用的铁。

## 6. One-Sentence Summary & Memory Hook / 一句话总结 & 记忆钩

**An 18-month-old exclusively on whole cow's milk without supplements is at greatest risk for iron deficiency anemia because cow's milk has poor iron bioavailability and causes occult intestinal bleeding, progressively depleting iron stores.**

**18个月大纯牛奶喂养（无补充剂）婴儿最易患缺铁性贫血，因为牛奶铁生物利用率低且引起隐匿性肠道出血，逐渐耗竭铁储备。**

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 100%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><p><strong>Memory Hook — COW's Milk Triple Iron Strike / 记忆钩 — 牛奶缺铁三重打击 "COW":</strong></p>
<p>• <strong>C</strong>ontent low — Iron concentration in cow's milk is very low (~0.5 mg/L) / 含量低——牛奶铁浓度极低（约0.5 mg/L）<br />
• <strong>O</strong>ccult bleeding — Cow's milk causes intestinal microhemorrhage in infants, adding chronic iron loss / 隐性出血——牛奶在婴儿中引起肠道微出血，造成慢性铁丢失<br />
• <strong>W</strong>eak absorption — Bovine casein blocks iron uptake; bioavailability only ~10% / 吸收弱——牛奶酪蛋白阻断铁摄取；生物利用率仅约10%</p></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
</tbody>
</table>

## 7. High-Yield Topic Knowledge — Iron Deficiency Anemia in Infancy / 高频知识表 — 婴儿期缺铁性贫血

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 50%" />
<col style="width: 50%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Topic</strong><br />
<strong>考点</strong></th>
<th><strong>Key Points</strong><br />
<strong>要点</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>Most common nutritional deficiency<br />
最常见营养缺乏</td>
<td>Iron deficiency is the #1 nutritional deficiency in children worldwide and the leading cause of anemia in the first 2 years of life<br />
缺铁是全球儿童第一大营养缺乏症，也是生后前2年贫血的主要原因</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Lab findings<br />
实验室检查</td>
<td>Microcytic (↓MCV) hypochromic anemia; ↓ferritin (first to fall), ↓serum iron, ↑TIBC, ↓transferrin saturation, ↑RDW (anisocytosis)<br />
小细胞（↓MCV）低色素性贫血；↓铁蛋白（最先下降），↓血清铁，↑TIBC，↓转铁蛋白饱和度，↑RDW（红细胞大小不等）</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Neurodevelopmental consequences<br />
神经发育后果</td>
<td>Iron is required for myelination and dopamine/serotonin synthesis; deficiency in infancy causes irreversible cognitive and psychomotor deficits that persist even after treatment<br />
铁是髓鞘形成和多巴胺/血清素合成所必需；婴儿期缺铁导致不可逆认知和精神运动缺陷，即使治疗后仍可持续</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Prevention guidelines<br />
预防指南</td>
<td>Breastfed infants: iron drops 1 mg/kg/day from 4 months; formula-fed: iron-fortified formula; do NOT introduce whole cow's milk before 12 months; limit cow's milk to ≤24 oz/day after 12 months<br />
母乳喂养：4个月起铁滴剂1 mg/kg/天；配方奶喂养：铁强化配方奶；12个月前不引入全脂牛奶；12个月后牛奶限制≤24盎司/天</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Treatment protocol<br />
治疗方案</td>
<td>Oral elemental iron 3–6 mg/kg/day between meals; reticulocytosis peaks at 7–10 days; Hgb normalizes in 4–8 weeks; continue iron 3 months after normalization to replenish stores<br />
口服元素铁3–6 mg/kg/天，两餐之间服用；7–10天网织红细胞达峰；4–8周Hgb恢复正常；Hgb正常后继续补铁3个月以补充铁储备</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>High-risk populations<br />
高危人群</td>
<td>Late preterm infants, exclusively breastfed infants after 4–6 months without iron supplementation, infants switched to whole cow's milk, toddlers with excessive milk intake<br />
晚期早产儿、4–6个月后未补铁的纯母乳喂养婴儿、换用全脂牛奶的婴儿、牛奶摄入过量的幼儿</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Screening<br />
筛查</td>
<td>AAP recommends universal hemoglobin screening at 12 months; risk-factor-based screening at 4, 15, 18, 24 months for high-risk groups (including cow's milk-fed infants)<br />
美国儿科学会建议12月龄普查血红蛋白；高危人群（包括牛奶喂养儿）在4、15、18、24月龄进行基于风险因素的筛查</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

## 8. Extensions / 延伸扩展

- **Differential of microcytic anemia:** Iron deficiency (↓ferritin, ↑TIBC), thalassemia (normal ferritin, normal/↑RBC count, target cells on smear), anemia of chronic disease (↓TIBC, normal/↑ferritin), lead poisoning (basophilic stippling)\
  **小细胞性贫血鉴别:** 缺铁性贫血（↓铁蛋白，↑TIBC），地中海贫血（铁蛋白正常，红细胞计数正常/升高，靶形红细胞），慢性病贫血（↓TIBC，铁蛋白正常/升高），铅中毒（嗜碱性点彩）

- **Variant — breastfed infant scenario:** Exclusively breastfed infants also need iron supplementation from 4 months; breast milk iron is highly bioavailable but total volume is insufficient to meet needs beyond 4–6 months\
  **题目变式——母乳喂养婴儿:** 纯母乳喂养婴儿同样需从4个月起补铁；母乳铁生物利用率高，但总量在4–6个月后不足以满足需求

- **Key manifestation — pica:** Craving and eating non-food items (dirt, ice, clay) is a classic behavioral sign of iron deficiency in toddlers; always screen for iron deficiency when pica is present\
  **关键表现——异食癖:** 渴望并食用非食物物质（泥土、冰、黏土）是幼儿缺铁的经典行为征象；出现异食癖时应常规筛查缺铁

- **Cause of late preterm risk:** Fetal iron accretion occurs predominantly in the third trimester (weeks 34–40); infants born at 37 weeks miss ~3 weeks of peak iron accretion, starting life with 10–15% lower iron stores\
  **晚期早产儿高危原因:** 胎儿铁储备主要在妊娠晚期（34–40周）积累；37周出生婴儿错过约3周铁储备高峰期，出生时铁储备低约10–15%

# Question 160 — Pediatric Renal Artery Stenosis / 儿童肾动脉狭窄

## Question Stem / 题干

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 100%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><p>A <strong>5-year-old girl</strong> is brought to the physician as a new patient for an examination prior to starting kindergarten. She was noted to have <strong>high blood pressure</strong> by a previous physician 3 years ago. Her blood pressure 2 years ago was within normal limits. She has not been seen by a physician since that time because her mother did not have adequate health insurance. The patient is at the 50th percentile for height and <strong>15th percentile for weight</strong>. Her temperature is 36.7°C (98°F), pulse is 80/min, respirations are 25/min, and <strong>blood pressure is 140/90 mm Hg</strong>. A <strong>bruit is heard over the right aspect of the midabdomen</strong>. No other abnormalities are noted. <strong>Renal arteriography shows stenosis of the right renal artery</strong>. Which of the following is the most appropriate next step in management?</p>
<p><strong>Q: Which of the following is the most appropriate next step in management?</strong></p>
<p>A) Weight loss program<br />
B) Warfarin therapy<br />
C) Angioplasty<br />
D) Renal transplant<br />
E) No treatment is indicated</p>
<p><strong>Correct Answer: C</strong></p></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
</tbody>
</table>

## 1. Key Stem Clues / 题干关键词抓考点

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 50%" />
<col style="width: 50%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Key Stem Clue</strong><br />
<strong>关键词</strong></th>
<th><strong>Why It Matters</strong><br />
<strong>为什么重要</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>5-year-old with hypertension<br />
5岁儿童伴高血压</td>
<td>Hypertension in young children is almost always secondary rather than primary/essential<br />
幼儿高血压几乎均为继发性，而非原发性</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>History of elevated BP 3 years ago<br />
3年前已有高血压记录</td>
<td>Persistent or recurrent hypertension over time suggests an underlying structural cause<br />
持续或反复高血压提示存在潜在结构性病因</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Blood pressure 140/90 mm Hg<br />
血压140/90 mm Hg</td>
<td>Significantly elevated for age; normal systolic for a 5-year-old is ~90–100 mm Hg<br />
该年龄显著偏高；5岁儿童正常收缩压约为90–100 mm Hg</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Bruit over right aspect of midabdomen<br />
右腹中部血管杂音</td>
<td>Turbulent flow through a stenotic renal artery produces an audible bruit; classic physical exam finding for RAS<br />
湍流通过狭窄肾动脉产生可闻杂音；肾动脉狭窄的经典体征</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>15th percentile for weight<br />
体重第15百分位</td>
<td>Relative failure to thrive may indicate chronic illness or end-organ hypoperfusion<br />
相对生长迟缓可能提示慢性疾病或终末器官灌注不足</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Renal arteriography: stenosis of right renal artery<br />
肾动脉造影：右肾动脉狭窄</td>
<td>Confirms renovascular hypertension; gold standard imaging for RAS<br />
确诊肾血管性高血压；肾动脉狭窄的金标准影像学检查</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

## 2. Mechanism / 机制理解

**Renal artery stenosis** reduces perfusion pressure to the affected kidney, triggering **activation of the renin-angiotensin-aldosterone system (RAAS)**:

**肾动脉狭窄**使患肾灌注压降低，触发**肾素-血管紧张素-醛固酮系统（RAAS）激活**：

- Reduced perfusion → juxtaglomerular cells release **renin** → cleaves angiotensinogen → **angiotensin I**\
  灌注减少 → 球旁细胞释放**肾素** → 裂解血管紧张素原 → **血管紧张素I**

- Angiotensin I → ACE converts to **angiotensin II** → potent vasoconstriction + stimulates aldosterone release\
  血管紧张素I → ACE转化为**血管紧张素II** → 强效血管收缩 + 刺激醛固酮释放

- Aldosterone → sodium and water retention → **increased blood volume** + elevated systemic vascular resistance → **sustained hypertension**\
  醛固酮 → 钠水潴留 → **血容量增加** + 体循环血管阻力升高 → **持续性高血压**

**Anatomic rule of thumb:** In children, renal artery stenosis is most often caused by fibromuscular dysplasia or neurofibromatosis type 1, not the atherosclerotic plaques seen in adults.

**解剖小窍门:** 儿童肾动脉狭窄最常见原因是纤维肌性发育不良或1型神经纤维瘤病，而非成人常见的动脉粥样硬化斑块。

## 3. Correct Answer (C) — Angioplasty / 正确答案 (C) — 经皮腔内肾动脉成形术

**Percutaneous transluminal renal angioplasty (PTRA)** is the preferred interventional treatment for renal artery stenosis in children, directly addressing the mechanical obstruction:

**经皮腔内肾动脉成形术（PTRA）**是儿童肾动脉狭窄的首选介入治疗，直接解除机械性梗阻：

- Balloon dilation of the stenotic segment restores normal renal perfusion pressure\
  球囊扩张狭窄段，恢复正常肾灌注压

- Restored perfusion suppresses pathological RAAS activation and normalizes blood pressure\
  改善肾灌注可抑制病理性RAAS激活，使血压恢复正常

- In children, angioplasty alone (without stenting) is often sufficient due to the elastic properties of pediatric vessels\
  儿童血管弹性好，通常单纯球囊扩张（无需支架）即可取得满意效果

**Diagnosis:** Renovascular hypertension secondary to right renal artery stenosis, confirmed by arteriography showing stenosis and supported clinically by an abdominal bruit and persistent severe hypertension in a young child.

**诊断:** 继发于右肾动脉狭窄的肾血管性高血压，经肾动脉造影证实，结合腹部血管杂音及幼儿持续严重高血压的临床表现。

**Treatment:** Angioplasty (PTRA) is the most appropriate next step given arteriography-confirmed stenosis. Calcium channel blockers (e.g., amlodipine) are an alternative medical option, but angioplasty provides definitive correction of the underlying structural lesion.

**治疗:** 动脉造影确认狭窄后，经皮血管成形术是最合适的下一步治疗。钙通道阻滞剂（如氨氯地平）为替代药物方案，但血管成形术可从根本上纠正潜在结构性病变。

## 4. Options Elimination / 错误选项排除逻辑

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 33%" />
<col style="width: 33%" />
<col style="width: 33%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Option</strong><br />
<strong>选项</strong></th>
<th><strong>Why Wrong</strong><br />
<strong>为什么错</strong></th>
<th><strong>Key Discriminator</strong><br />
<strong>鉴别要点</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>A — Weight loss program<br />
A — 减重计划</td>
<td>Useful for primary/essential hypertension where obesity drives BP elevation; this child's RAS is a structural lesion unaffected by weight loss<br />
适用于肥胖驱动的原发性高血压；该患儿肾动脉狭窄是结构性病变，减重无效</td>
<td>Weight loss targets metabolic syndrome; RAS requires mechanical or pharmacologic correction<br />
减重针对代谢综合征；肾动脉狭窄需机械性或药物纠正</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>B — Warfarin therapy<br />
B — 华法林治疗</td>
<td>Anticoagulation has no role in renal artery stenosis and increases bleeding risk without addressing the underlying obstruction<br />
抗凝治疗对肾动脉狭窄无效，且在不解决梗阻的情况下增加出血风险</td>
<td>Warfarin is used for thromboembolic disease, not renovascular stenosis<br />
华法林用于血栓栓塞性疾病，不用于肾血管性狭窄</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>C — Angioplasty ✓<br />
C — 血管成形术 ✓</td>
<td>CORRECT — Directly treats the confirmed stenotic lesion, restoring renal perfusion and eliminating RAAS-driven hypertension<br />
正确——直接治疗已确认的狭窄病变，恢复肾灌注并消除RAAS驱动的高血压</td>
<td>Arteriography-confirmed stenosis → proceed to interventional correction<br />
造影确认狭窄 → 进行介入治疗</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>D — Renal transplant<br />
D — 肾移植</td>
<td>Reserved for end-stage kidney disease (e.g., polycystic kidney disease, recurrent pyelonephritis); far too aggressive for a correctable vascular lesion<br />
适用于终末期肾病（如多囊肾、反复肾盂肾炎）；对可纠正的血管病变过于激进</td>
<td>Transplant indicated when renal parenchymal function is irreversibly lost, not for a vascular lesion<br />
移植适用于肾实质功能不可逆丧失，而非血管病变</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>E — No treatment is indicated<br />
E — 无需治疗</td>
<td>Untreated childhood hypertension leads to increased cardiovascular morbidity and mortality in adulthood; 140/90 at age 5 demands intervention<br />
未治疗的儿童高血压导致成年后心血管发病率和死亡率升高；5岁时血压140/90必须干预</td>
<td>Sustained 140/90 in a 5-year-old is never an observation-only scenario<br />
5岁儿童血压持续140/90绝非"仅观察"的情况</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

*The most tempting distractor is Choice A (weight loss), because weight management is a first-line intervention for hypertension in older children — but this approach applies only to primary/essential hypertension; the combination of abdominal bruit plus arteriographic stenosis unambiguously identifies a secondary structural cause.*

最诱人的干扰项是A（减重计划），因为体重管理是年长儿童高血压的一线干预措施——但此方法仅适用于原发性高血压；腹部杂音加上动脉造影狭窄明确指向继发性结构病因。

## 6. One-Sentence Summary & Memory Hook / 一句话总结 & 记忆钩

**In a young child with arteriography-confirmed renal artery stenosis driving secondary hypertension, angioplasty is the definitive intervention that directly corrects the mechanical obstruction and eliminates pathological RAAS activation.**

**在动脉造影确诊肾动脉狭窄导致继发性高血压的幼儿中，经皮血管成形术是直接纠正机械性梗阻、消除病理性RAAS激活的根治性干预措施。**

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 100%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><p><strong>Memory Hook — BRAS for Pediatric RAS / 记忆钩 — BRAS 助记儿童肾动脉狭窄:</strong></p>
<p>• <strong>B</strong>ruit (abdominal) — cardinal physical exam clue pointing to turbulent flow through stenosis / 腹部杂音——提示湍流流经狭窄处的关键体格检查线索<br />
• <strong>R</strong>enin-angiotensin activation — core pathophysiologic mechanism linking stenosis to hypertension / 肾素-血管紧张素激活——连接狭窄与高血压的核心病理生理机制<br />
• <strong>A</strong>ngioplasty — first-line interventional treatment once stenosis is confirmed on arteriography / 血管成形术——动脉造影确认狭窄后的一线介入治疗<br />
• <strong>S</strong>econdary HTN — always suspect structural cause when a child under 6 presents with significant hypertension / 继发性高血压——6岁以下儿童出现显著高血压时，始终警惕结构性病因</p></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
</tbody>
</table>

## 7. High-Yield Topic Knowledge — Renal Artery Stenosis and Secondary Hypertension in Children / 高频知识表 — 儿童肾动脉狭窄与继发性高血压

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 50%" />
<col style="width: 50%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Topic</strong><br />
<strong>考点</strong></th>
<th><strong>Key Points</strong><br />
<strong>要点</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>Causes of RAS in children<br />
儿童肾动脉狭窄病因</td>
<td>Fibromuscular dysplasia (most common), neurofibromatosis type 1, Takayasu arteritis; atherosclerosis is rare in this age group<br />
纤维肌性发育不良（最常见）、1型神经纤维瘤病、大动脉炎；动脉粥样硬化在该年龄段罕见</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Diagnosis of renovascular HTN<br />
肾血管性高血压的诊断</td>
<td>Renal arteriography is the gold standard; duplex ultrasound and CT/MR angiography are non-invasive screening options<br />
肾动脉造影为金标准；双功能超声及CT/MR血管造影是无创筛查手段</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Preferred medical therapy for pediatric RAS<br />
儿童肾动脉狭窄的首选药物治疗</td>
<td>Calcium channel blockers (amlodipine); avoid ACE inhibitors/ARBs, which reduce GFR and risk hyperkalemia<br />
钙通道阻滞剂（氨氯地平）；避免ACEI/ARB，可降低GFR并有高钾血症风险</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Why ACEI/ARBs are dangerous in RAS<br />
肾动脉狭窄中ACEI/ARB危险的原因</td>
<td>They dilate the efferent arteriole, dropping GFR in the already underperfused kidney below a critical threshold, worsening ischemia<br />
扩张出球小动脉使灌注不足肾脏的GFR降至临界值以下，加重缺血</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Secondary HTN causes in children<br />
儿童继发性高血压的病因</td>
<td>Renovascular (RAS most common), renal parenchymal disease, aortic coarctation, endocrine (pheochromocytoma, Cushing), neurofibromatosis<br />
肾血管性（肾动脉狭窄最常见）、肾实质疾病、主动脉缩窄、内分泌性（嗜铬细胞瘤、Cushing综合征）、神经纤维瘤病</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Consequences of untreated childhood HTN<br />
儿童高血压未治疗的后果</td>
<td>Left ventricular hypertrophy, early atherosclerosis, increased cardiovascular and cerebrovascular morbidity and mortality in adulthood<br />
左心室肥厚、早期动脉粥样硬化、成年后心血管及脑血管发病率和死亡率升高</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

## 8. Extensions / 延伸扩展

- **Fibromuscular dysplasia (FMD):** Most common non-atherosclerotic cause of RAS in children and young women; involves medial layer of the arterial wall; arteriography shows classic "string of beads" appearance\
  **纤维肌性发育不良（FMD）:** 儿童和年轻女性最常见的非动脉粥样硬化性肾动脉狭窄病因；累及动脉壁中层；动脉造影呈经典"串珠样"表现

- **NF1 association:** Neurofibromatosis type 1 can cause RAS through arterial dysplasia or neurofibroma compression; look for café-au-lait spots and axillary freckling as clinical clues\
  **NF1相关性:** 1型神经纤维瘤病可通过动脉发育异常或神经纤维瘤压迫导致肾动脉狭窄；注意咖啡牛奶斑和腋窝雀斑等临床线索

- **Aortic coarctation differential:** Another structural cause of secondary HTN in children; distinguished by upper extremity hypertension with diminished femoral pulses and rib notching on chest X-ray\
  **主动脉缩窄鉴别:** 儿童继发性高血压的另一结构性病因；以上肢高血压伴股动脉搏动减弱及胸片肋骨切迹为鉴别依据

- **Thiazide diuretics caution:** Avoid in RAS-associated HTN; by depleting intravascular volume they further stimulate RAAS, potentially worsening hypertension and reducing GFR\
  **噻嗪类利尿剂注意:** 避免用于肾动脉狭窄相关高血压；通过耗竭血管内容量进一步刺激RAAS，可能矛盾地加重高血压并降低GFR

# Question 161 — Hyperlipidemia with Low 10-Year ASCVD Risk: No Pharmacotherapy Indicated / 高脂血症合并低10年ASCVD风险：不适用药物治疗

## Question Stem / 题干

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 100%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><p>A <strong>42-year-old woman</strong>, gravida 1, para 1, comes to the office for a routine examination. She is concerned about her risk for coronary artery disease. She has irritable bowel syndrome and migraines. Medications are sumatriptan and ibuprofen as needed. Her <strong>father has hypertension and hyperlipidemia</strong>. Her <strong>paternal uncle was diagnosed with coronary artery disease at the age of 50 years</strong>. The patient <strong>smoked one pack of cigarettes daily for 10 years but quit 7 years ago</strong>. She drinks two glasses of wine weekly. She does not use illicit drugs. She runs 3 miles one to three times weekly. She is 168 cm (5 ft 6 in) tall and weighs 77 kg (170 lb); <strong>BMI is 27 kg/m²</strong>. Blood pressure is 118/70 mm Hg. Examination shows no other abnormalities. Results of fasting serum studies are shown: Glucose 82 mg/dL, <strong>Cholesterol total 255 mg/dL</strong>, <strong>HDL-cholesterol 85 mg/dL</strong>, <strong>LDL-cholesterol 155 mg/dL</strong>, Triglycerides 70 mg/dL. The <strong>risk assessment score for her 10-year probability of coronary artery disease is 0.4%</strong>. The patient is counseled about maintaining a diet low in saturated fat and continuing her exercise regimen. Which of the following is the most appropriate next step in management?</p>
<p><strong>Q: Most appropriate next step in management?</strong></p>
<p>A) Cardiac stress scintigraphy<br />
B) Daily aspirin therapy<br />
C) Echocardiography<br />
D) HMG-CoA reductase inhibitor therapy<br />
E) No intervention is indicated at this time</p>
<p><strong>Correct Answer: E</strong></p></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
</tbody>
</table>

## 1. Key Stem Clues / 题干关键词抓考点

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 50%" />
<col style="width: 50%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Key Stem Clue</strong><br />
<strong>关键词</strong></th>
<th><strong>Why It Matters</strong><br />
<strong>为什么重要</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>LDL-cholesterol 155 mg/dL<br />
低密度脂蛋白胆固醇 155 mg/dL</td>
<td>Below the automatic statin threshold of 190 mg/dL; below 190, the statin decision depends entirely on 10-year ASCVD risk<br />
低于自动启动他汀的190 mg/dL阈值；低于190时，他汀决策完全取决于10年ASCVD风险</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>HDL-cholesterol 85 mg/dL<br />
高密度脂蛋白胆固醇 85 mg/dL</td>
<td>High HDL is a "negative risk factor" — powerfully cardioprotective and lowers the calculated ASCVD score<br />
高HDL是"负性风险因素"——具有强大心脏保护作用，可降低ASCVD评分</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>10-year CAD risk score 0.4%<br />
10年冠心病风险评分 0.4%</td>
<td>Extremely low risk; when &lt;5%, statin and aspirin risks (bleeding, myopathy) consistently outweigh benefits<br />
风险极低；当&lt;5%时，他汀和阿司匹林的风险（出血、肌病）始终超过获益</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Paternal uncle with CAD at age 50<br />
父系舅父50岁时诊断冠心病</td>
<td>First-degree male relative with premature CAD (&lt;55 years) counts as a cardiovascular risk factor<br />
一级男性亲属早发冠心病（&lt;55岁）是心血管风险因素</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Ex-smoker, quit 7 years ago<br />
既往吸烟，已戒烟7年</td>
<td>Smoking cessation substantially reduces risk; a distant history contributes far less than active smoking to the current risk score<br />
戒烟可大幅降低风险；已戒烟7年的历史对当前风险评分的贡献远小于持续吸烟</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>BP 118/70, Glucose 82 mg/dL<br />
血压 118/70，血糖 82 mg/dL</td>
<td>No hypertension, no diabetes — two of the most heavily weighted modifiable ASCVD risk factors are absent<br />
无高血压、无糖尿病——两项权重最大的可干预ASCVD风险因素均不存在</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

## 2. Mechanism / 机制理解

The decision to initiate **statin therapy** for primary prevention of **atherosclerotic cardiovascular disease (ASCVD)** is governed by **10-year absolute risk**, not lipid values alone — a framework designed to ensure pharmacologic benefits outweigh harms:

在**动脉粥样硬化性心血管疾病（ASCVD）**一级预防中，是否启动**他汀治疗**取决于**10年绝对风险**，而非单纯血脂数值——这一框架旨在确保药物获益超过风险：

- LDL ≥ 190 mg/dL → statin indicated automatically regardless of calculated risk (suggests familial hypercholesterolemia)\
  LDL ≥ 190 mg/dL → 无论计算风险如何均自动启动他汀（提示家族性高胆固醇血症）

- 10-year ASCVD risk \< 5% → statin harms (myopathy, new-onset diabetes, cost) outweigh benefits; lifestyle counseling only\
  10年风险 \< 5% → 他汀危害（肌病、新发糖尿病、费用）超过获益；仅生活方式干预

- 10-year ASCVD risk 5–10% → borderline zone; shared decision-making incorporating risk-enhancing factors (hsCRP, ABI, coronary artery calcium)\
  10年风险 5–10% → 临界区；结合风险增强因素（hsCRP、踝肱指数、冠状动脉钙化积分）进行共同决策

- 10-year ASCVD risk \> 10% → moderate-intensity statin clearly indicated\
  10年风险 \> 10% → 明确适用中等强度他汀治疗

- 10-year ASCVD risk \> 20% → high-intensity statin; aspirin primary prevention also considered\
  10年风险 \> 20% → 高强度他汀；同时考虑阿司匹林一级预防

**Threshold rule of thumb:** Think "190 or 10%" — LDL ≥ 190 mg/dL is the automatic statin trigger; if LDL is below 190, you need a 10-year risk \> 10% to justify starting one.

**阈值小窍门:** 记住"190 或 10%"——LDL ≥ 190 mg/dL 是自动启动他汀的触发点；若LDL低于190，则需要10年风险 \> 10%才能证明启动他汀合理。

## 3. Correct Answer (E) — No Pharmacotherapy at Very Low 10-Year CVD Risk / 正确答案 (E) — 10年心血管风险极低时不启动药物治疗

**No intervention beyond lifestyle counseling** is the correct management when 10-year ASCVD risk is below 5% and LDL is below 190 mg/dL — the risk-benefit calculation does not favor any pharmacologic agent:

当10年ASCVD风险低于5%且LDL低于190 mg/dL时，**不进行超出生活方式咨询的干预**是正确处理——风险获益计算不支持任何药物治疗：

- 10-year risk of 0.4% is far below the 5% threshold where statin consideration begins\
  0.4%的10年风险远低于开始考虑他汀的5%阈值

- LDL of 155 mg/dL does not reach the 190 mg/dL automatic statin indication\
  LDL 155 mg/dL未达到190 mg/dL的自动他汀适应证

- High HDL (85 mg/dL) and normal BP and glucose are strongly protective, explaining the very low risk despite elevated total cholesterol\
  高HDL（85 mg/dL）及正常血压和血糖具有强保护作用，解释了尽管总胆固醇升高但整体风险极低的原因

- Lifestyle counseling (low saturated fat diet, continued exercise) has already been appropriately given and represents complete management at this risk level\
  生活方式咨询（低饱和脂肪饮食、继续锻炼）已适当给予，在此风险水平下代表完整的处理方案

**Diagnosis:** Hyperlipidemia (LDL 155, total cholesterol 255) with very low 10-year ASCVD risk (0.4%); no clinical indication for pharmacologic intervention currently.

**诊断:** 高脂血症（LDL 155，总胆固醇255）合并极低10年ASCVD风险（0.4%）；目前无药物干预的临床指征。

**Treatment:** Lifestyle modifications only — low saturated fat diet, regular aerobic exercise; repeat fasting lipid panel and risk reassessment in 4–6 years.

**治疗:** 仅生活方式干预——低饱和脂肪饮食、规律有氧运动；4-6年后复查空腹血脂并重新评估风险。

## 4. Options Elimination / 错误选项排除逻辑

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 33%" />
<col style="width: 33%" />
<col style="width: 33%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Option</strong><br />
<strong>选项</strong></th>
<th><strong>Why Wrong</strong><br />
<strong>为什么错</strong></th>
<th><strong>Key Discriminator</strong><br />
<strong>鉴别要点</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>A — Cardiac stress scintigraphy<br />
A — 心脏负荷核素显像</td>
<td>Wrong — patient is completely asymptomatic with no angina, no exertional chest pain, and a 0.4% pretest probability of obstructive CAD; stress imaging is not a screening tool<br />
错误——患者完全无症状，无心绞痛，无劳力性胸痛，梗阻性冠心病的验前概率为0.4%；负荷显像不是筛查工具</td>
<td>Stress nuclear imaging is indicated for symptomatic patients or those with intermediate-high pretest CAD probability — never for routine low-risk screening<br />
负荷核素显像适用于有症状患者或中-高验前概率患者——不用于低风险常规筛查</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>B — Daily aspirin therapy<br />
B — 每日阿司匹林疗法</td>
<td>Wrong — aspirin for primary prevention (USPSTF 2022) is not recommended for most adults; any benefit requires substantially higher CVD risk than 0.4%, and GI bleeding risk outweighs benefit<br />
错误——阿司匹林一级预防（USPSTF 2022）不推荐用于大多数成人；任何获益都需要远高于0.4%的心血管风险，且消化道出血风险超过获益</td>
<td>Aspirin primary prevention: only consider for ages 40–59 with ≥10% 10-year CVD risk after shared decision-making; never appropriate at &lt;5% risk<br />
阿司匹林一级预防：仅在40-59岁且10年风险≥10%时经共同决策后考虑；&lt;5%风险时绝不适用</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>C — Echocardiography<br />
C — 超声心动图</td>
<td>Wrong — echocardiography evaluates cardiac structure and function; this patient has a normal physical examination, no murmurs, no symptoms of heart failure, and no indication for structural evaluation<br />
错误——超声心动图评估心脏结构和功能；该患者查体正常，无杂音，无心力衰竭症状，无结构评估指征</td>
<td>Echocardiography indications: murmurs, suspected cardiomyopathy, heart failure symptoms, valvular disease — not cardiovascular risk stratification<br />
超声心动图适应证：杂音、疑似心肌病、心力衰竭症状、瓣膜病——不用于心血管风险分层</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>D — HMG-CoA reductase inhibitor therapy<br />
D — HMG-CoA还原酶抑制剂（他汀）治疗</td>
<td>Wrong — statin is indicated when LDL ≥ 190 mg/dL OR 10-year risk &gt; 10%; this patient has LDL 155 (below 190) and risk 0.4% (below 10%), meeting neither criterion<br />
错误——他汀适用于LDL ≥ 190 mg/dL或10年风险&gt;10%；该患者LDL 155（低于190）且风险0.4%（低于10%），两项均不符合</td>
<td>The appearance of an elevated total cholesterol (255) is misleading; high HDL (85) accounts for much of it; decisions require LDL-specific and risk-based reasoning<br />
总胆固醇升高（255）的表象具有误导性；高HDL（85）占了很大部分；决策需要基于LDL特异性和风险的推理</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>E — No intervention is indicated at this time ✓<br />
E — 目前无需干预 ✓</td>
<td>CORRECT — with 0.4% 10-year risk and LDL well below 190 mg/dL, the already-given lifestyle counseling constitutes complete and appropriate management<br />
正确——10年风险0.4%且LDL远低于190 mg/dL，已给予的生活方式咨询构成完整且适当的处理</td>
<td>"Treat the risk, not the number" — lipid values alone never drive the statin decision when LDL is below 190 mg/dL<br />
"按风险治疗，而非按数字治疗"——当LDL低于190 mg/dL时，单纯血脂数值不能驱动他汀决策</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

*The most dangerous distractor is D (statin): total cholesterol of 255 and LDL of 155 look alarming, but the high HDL of 85 substantially reduces risk, and the calculated 10-year score of 0.4% is the decisive number — far below any treatment threshold.*

D（他汀）是最危险的干扰项：总胆固醇255和LDL 155看似令人担忧，但高HDL 85大幅降低风险，而计算所得0.4%的10年评分才是决定性数字——远低于任何治疗阈值。
