## 6. One-Sentence Summary & Memory Hook / 一句话总结 & 记忆钩

**In primary CVD prevention, statin therapy requires either LDL ≥ 190 mg/dL or a 10-year ASCVD risk \> 10%; this patient's LDL of 155 and risk of 0.4% meet neither criterion, so no pharmacotherapy is warranted.**

**在心血管疾病一级预防中，启动他汀治疗需满足LDL ≥ 190 mg/dL 或10年ASCVD风险 \> 10%；该患者LDL 155且风险0.4%，两项均不符合，因此不需要任何药物治疗。**

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 100%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><p><strong>Memory Hook — The Statin START Thresholds / 记忆钩 — 他汀启动阈值 "START":</strong></p>
<p>• <strong>S</strong>ixty percent HDL rule: HDL &gt; 60 is a "negative risk factor" that lowers total ASCVD score / <strong>S</strong>ixty（60）：HDL &gt; 60 是"负性风险因素"，降低总ASCVD评分<br />
• <strong>T</strong>en percent: 10-year risk &gt; 10% → statin indicated; 5–10% → shared decision / <strong>T</strong>en（10%）：10年风险 &gt; 10% → 启动他汀；5-10% → 共同决策<br />
• <strong>A</strong>utomatic: LDL ≥ 190 mg/dL → statin regardless of calculated risk / <strong>A</strong>utomatic（自动）：LDL ≥ 190 mg/dL → 无论风险评分均启动他汀<br />
• <strong>R</strong>isk below 5% = lifestyle only; drug risks outweigh benefits / <strong>R</strong>isk below 5%（风险&lt;5%）：仅生活方式干预；药物风险超过获益<br />
• <strong>T</strong>reat the risk score, not the lipid number alone / <strong>T</strong>reat the risk（按风险治疗）：依据风险评分，而非单纯依据血脂数值</p></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
</tbody>
</table>

## 7. High-Yield Topic Knowledge — Primary Cardiovascular Prevention and Statin Decision Framework / 高频知识表 — 心血管初级预防与他汀决策框架

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 50%" />
<col style="width: 50%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Topic</strong><br />
<strong>考点</strong></th>
<th><strong>Key Points</strong><br />
<strong>要点</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>Automatic statin threshold: LDL ≥ 190<br />
自动启动他汀：LDL ≥ 190</td>
<td>Indicates probable familial hypercholesterolemia; statin started regardless of 10-year ASCVD risk score<br />
提示可能为家族性高胆固醇血症；无论10年ASCVD风险评分如何均启动他汀</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>ASCVD calculator inputs<br />
ASCVD计算器输入变量</td>
<td>Age, sex, race/ethnicity, total cholesterol, HDL, systolic BP, BP treatment, diabetes status, smoking status — all weighted<br />
年龄、性别、种族/民族、总胆固醇、HDL、收缩压、降压治疗状态、糖尿病、吸烟——均参与加权计算</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>HDL as a "negative risk factor"<br />
HDL作为"负性风险因素"</td>
<td>HDL &gt; 60 mg/dL subtracts from the ASCVD risk count; this patient's HDL of 85 is highly protective and largely explains her low risk despite elevated total cholesterol<br />
HDL &gt; 60 mg/dL 从ASCVD风险计数中扣除；该患者HDL 85具有高度保护作用，很大程度上解释了其尽管总胆固醇升高但风险仍低的原因</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Risk-enhancing factors for borderline patients<br />
临界患者的风险增强因素</td>
<td>LDL ≥ 160, hsCRP ≥ 2 mg/L, ABI &lt; 0.9, coronary artery calcium score &gt; 100, family history of premature ASCVD — can tip shared decision toward statin in 5–10% risk group<br />
LDL ≥ 160、hsCRP ≥ 2 mg/L、踝肱指数&lt;0.9、冠状动脉钙化积分&gt;100、早发ASCVD家族史——可在5-10%风险人群的共同决策中倾向启动他汀</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Aspirin primary prevention (USPSTF 2022)<br />
阿司匹林一级预防（USPSTF 2022）</td>
<td>Adults ≥ 60: recommend against initiating aspirin; ages 40–59 with ≥10% CVD risk: individualized decision; GI bleeding risk must always be weighed<br />
60岁及以上成人：建议不启动阿司匹林；40-59岁且CVD风险≥10%：个体化决策；始终需权衡消化道出血风险</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Statin adverse effects justifying risk-benefit analysis<br />
支持风险获益分析的他汀不良反应</td>
<td>Myalgia (most common, ~10%), rhabdomyolysis (rare), transaminase elevation (usually mild), new-onset diabetes (modest increase) — collectively justify withholding statin at low risk<br />
肌痛（最常见，约10%）、横纹肌溶解（罕见）、转氨酶升高（通常轻微）、新发糖尿病（小幅增加）——共同证明低风险时不启动他汀的合理性</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Premature family history definition<br />
早发家族史定义</td>
<td>First-degree male relative with MI or confirmed CAD &lt; 55 years; first-degree female relative &lt; 65 years — counts as one risk factor in ASCVD calculation<br />
一级男性亲属心肌梗死或确诊冠心病&lt;55岁；一级女性亲属&lt;65岁——在ASCVD计算中计为一项风险因素</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

## 8. Extensions / 延伸扩展

- **Risk-enhancing factors for future reassessment:** If this patient is re-evaluated in 4–6 years and falls into the 5–10% borderline zone, the clinician should then assess coronary artery calcium score, hsCRP, and ABI before deciding on statin initiation — these factors can resolve ambiguity in borderline cases\
  **未来重新评估时的风险增强因素:** 若该患者4-6年后重新评估时进入5-10%临界区，临床医生应在决定是否启动他汀前评估冠状动脉钙化积分、hsCRP和踝肱指数——这些因素可消除临界病例中的不确定性

- **Variant — if LDL were 195 mg/dL:** The identical clinical scenario with LDL of 195 mg/dL would require statin initiation automatically, regardless of a 0.4% calculated risk, because LDL ≥ 190 suggests familial hypercholesterolemia where the lifetime ASCVD risk is disproportionately high\
  **题目变式——若LDL为195 mg/dL:** 若同一临床场景LDL为195 mg/dL，则需自动启动他汀，无论计算风险为0.4%，因为LDL ≥ 190提示家族性高胆固醇血症，其终身ASCVD风险不成比例地高

- **Differential of elevated total cholesterol with low LDL risk:** Total cholesterol = LDL + HDL + (TG/5); a high total cholesterol driven by a high HDL (as here: 155 + 85 + 14 ≈ 254) is very different prognostically from one driven by high LDL — always decompose the lipid panel before drawing conclusions\
  **LDL风险低时总胆固醇升高的鉴别:** 总胆固醇 = LDL + HDL +（TG/5）；由高HDL驱动的总胆固醇升高（如本例：155 + 85 + 14 ≈ 254）与由高LDL驱动的预后截然不同——下结论前始终分解血脂全套

- **Key complication of deferring treatment at higher risk:** At risk levels above the treatment threshold, delaying statin initiation significantly increases the cumulative lifetime risk of myocardial infarction and ischemic stroke — but this concern does not apply to a patient at 0.4% risk where monitoring and lifestyle management are genuinely sufficient\
  **较高风险时推迟治疗的关键并发症:** 当风险水平超过治疗阈值时，推迟启动他汀会显著增加心肌梗死和缺血性卒中的累积终身风险——但这一顾虑不适用于0.4%风险的患者，对其而言监测和生活方式管理确实已足够

# Question 162 — Sampling Bias Limiting Study Generalizability / 抽样偏倚导致研究外部效度受限

## Question Stem / 题干

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 100%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><p>An investigator would like to determine if a new medication for <strong>chronic obstructive pulmonary disease (COPD)</strong> decreases <strong>hospitalization rates</strong> in adults who come to the <strong>emergency department (ED)</strong> because of an <strong>exacerbation</strong>. All patients with COPD who come to the ED because of an exacerbation will be invited to participate in the study. Patients will be <strong>randomly assigned</strong> to receive the new medication plus standard therapy or standard therapy alone during the hours that a study nurse is present (<strong>7 AM to 7 PM daily</strong>). <strong>Patients who come to the ED outside of these hours will not be enrolled in the study.</strong> Physicians treating the patients will be blinded to the group assignments. Outcomes will be assessed by a physician not involved in the care of the patients. Which of the following is the greatest limitation of this study design?</p>
<p><strong>Q: Which of the following is the greatest limitation of this study design?</strong></p>
<p>A) Generalizability<br />
B) Inadequate blinding of outcome assessors<br />
C) Lack of a placebo group<br />
D) Lead-time bias</p>
<p><strong>Correct Answer: A</strong></p></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
</tbody>
</table>

## 1. Key Stem Clues / 题干关键词抓考点

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 50%" />
<col style="width: 50%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Key Stem Clue</strong><br />
<strong>关键词</strong></th>
<th><strong>Why It Matters</strong><br />
<strong>为什么重要</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>Enrollment only 7 AM–7 PM<br />
仅在早7点至晚7点招募</td>
<td>Excludes nighttime ED presentations, creating a non-representative sample<br />
排除夜间急诊就诊者，导致样本缺乏代表性</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Patients outside these hours not enrolled<br />
非时段患者不纳入研究</td>
<td>Core source of sampling bias; ~50% of potential subjects systematically excluded<br />
抽样偏倚的核心来源；约50%的潜在研究对象被系统性排除</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Random assignment to groups<br />
随机分配至各组</td>
<td>Strengthens internal validity; reduces confounding within the enrolled sample<br />
增强内部效度；减少纳入样本内的混杂因素</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Physicians blinded to group assignment<br />
医生对分组设盲</td>
<td>Reduces performance bias; protects internal validity<br />
减少操作偏倚；保护内部效度</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Outcomes assessed by uninvolved physician<br />
由不参与诊疗的医生评估结局</td>
<td>Reduces detection bias; blinding of outcome assessment is adequate<br />
减少检测偏倚；结局评估的设盲充分</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>COPD exacerbation in ED setting<br />
COPD急性加重于急诊室就诊</td>
<td>Specific target population; generalization requires representative sampling across all presentation times<br />
特定目标人群；推广结论需要覆盖所有就诊时段的代表性抽样</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

## 2. Mechanism / 机制理解

**External validity** (generalizability) is the degree to which **study findings** can be applied to populations beyond the study sample. It is undermined when the **enrolled sample is systematically non-representative** of the broader target population:

**外部效度**（推广性）是研究结论能够应用于研究样本以外人群的程度。当**纳入样本系统性地无法代表更广泛的目标人群**时，外部效度受损：

- **Sampling bias** occurs when enrolled participants differ from the target population in a systematic, non-random way\
  **抽样偏倚**：当纳入的参与者与目标人群以系统性、非随机的方式存在差异时即发生

- Night-shift COPD exacerbations may differ in **disease severity, comorbidity burden, or socioeconomic profile** compared to daytime presentations\
  夜间COPD急性加重在**疾病严重程度、合并症负担或社会经济特征**方面可能与白天就诊者不同

- Restricting enrollment to 7 AM–7 PM introduces a **time-of-day selection bias** that limits who the results apply to\
  将招募限制在早7点至晚7点引入**时间选择偏倚**，限制了结果的适用范围

- **Internal validity** is well-preserved: randomization, blinding, and independent outcome assessment all reduce confounding and measurement error\
  **内部效度**保存完好：随机化、设盲和独立结局评估均能减少混杂和测量误差

**Anatomic rule of thumb:** Internal validity and external validity are independent — a highly controlled trial can have excellent internal validity yet poor generalizability if the sample is unrepresentative.

**设计小窍门:** 内部效度与外部效度相互独立——一项高度受控的试验可以有极佳的内部效度，但若样本缺乏代表性，推广性依然很差。

## 3. Correct Answer (A) — Generalizability / 正确答案 (A) — 推广性（外部效度）

**Generalizability** reflects the external validity of a study — whether its findings apply to the broader population from which the sample was drawn:

**推广性**反映研究的外部效度——研究结果是否适用于抽取样本的更广泛人群：

- By enrolling only patients presenting 7 AM–7 PM, the study excludes all nighttime COPD exacerbations\
  仅招募早7点至晚7点就诊的患者，研究排除了所有夜间COPD急性加重患者

- Nocturnal COPD exacerbations are associated with greater hypoxemia and may represent a more severely ill subgroup\
  夜间COPD急性加重与更严重的低氧血症相关，可能代表病情更重的亚组

- Even if the new medication works in the enrolled daytime cohort, the results cannot be confidently extrapolated to all adults with COPD exacerbations\
  即使新药在纳入的白天队列中有效，研究结果也无法可信地推广至所有COPD急性加重的成年患者

**Core concept:** Daytime-only enrollment → sampling bias → limits external validity (generalizability), even when internal validity is intact.

**核心概念:** 仅白天招募 → 抽样偏倚 → 限制外部效度（推广性），即便内部效度保持完整。

**Clinical implication:** When evaluating an RCT, always ask: Who was enrolled? Who was excluded? Does the sample reflect the patients I actually treat?

**临床意义:** 评估RCT时，始终追问：纳入了哪些人？排除了哪些人？样本是否反映了我实际诊疗的患者群体？

## 4. Options Elimination / 错误选项排除逻辑

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 33%" />
<col style="width: 33%" />
<col style="width: 33%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Option</strong><br />
<strong>选项</strong></th>
<th><strong>Why Wrong</strong><br />
<strong>为什么错</strong></th>
<th><strong>Key Discriminator</strong><br />
<strong>鉴别要点</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>A — Generalizability ✓<br />
A — 推广性 ✓</td>
<td>CORRECT — daytime-only enrollment creates sampling bias that prevents the findings from applying to all COPD exacerbation patients<br />
正确——仅白天招募造成抽样偏倚，使研究结果无法适用于所有COPD急性加重患者</td>
<td>Core issue is who is systematically excluded from enrollment<br />
核心问题是哪些人被系统性排除在外</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>B — Inadequate blinding of outcome assessors<br />
B — 结局评估者设盲不足</td>
<td>Outcome assessors ARE explicitly stated to be uninvolved in patient care; blinding of outcome assessment is adequate<br />
题目明确说明结局评估者不参与患者诊疗；结局评估的设盲是充分的</td>
<td>Study states outcomes assessed by a physician not involved in care<br />
题目明确说明结局由不参与诊疗的医生评估</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>C — Lack of a placebo group<br />
C — 缺乏安慰剂组</td>
<td>A placebo is ethically inappropriate when effective standard therapy exists; comparing new medication + standard therapy vs. standard therapy alone is the correct design<br />
在已有有效标准治疗时使用安慰剂在伦理上不适当；新药+标准治疗对比单独标准治疗是正确的设计</td>
<td>Active comparator vs. placebo — depends on whether standard of care exists<br />
主动对照 vs. 安慰剂——取决于是否存在标准治疗</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>D — Lead-time bias<br />
D — 超前时间偏倚</td>
<td>Lead-time bias applies to screening programs where earlier detection falsely appears to extend survival; this is a treatment trial, not a screening study<br />
超前时间偏倚适用于筛查项目，其中更早检测出疾病貌似延长生存期；本研究是治疗试验而非筛查研究</td>
<td>Lead-time bias requires a screening context; this is an RCT of a COPD treatment<br />
超前时间偏倚需要筛查背景；本研究是COPD治疗的RCT</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

*The most tempting distractor is Choice B — but outcome assessors in this study are explicitly independent and uninvolved in care, making blinding adequate. The real limitation is the daytime-only enrollment window creating sampling bias.*

最具迷惑性的干扰选项是B——但本研究的结局评估者明确独立且不参与诊疗，设盲充分。真正的局限性在于仅限白天时段的招募窗口造成了抽样偏倚。

## 5. High-Yield Summary Table — Internal Validity vs. External Validity in Clinical Trials / 临床试验中内部效度 vs. 外部效度

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 33%" />
<col style="width: 33%" />
<col style="width: 33%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Feature</strong><br />
<strong>特征</strong></th>
<th><strong>Internal Validity</strong><br />
<strong>内部效度</strong></th>
<th><strong>External Validity (Generalizability)</strong><br />
<strong>外部效度（推广性）</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>Core question<br />
核心问题</td>
<td>Did the intervention actually cause the observed outcome?<br />
干预措施是否确实导致了观察到的结局？</td>
<td>Can these findings be applied to the broader target population?<br />
这些结论能否应用于更广泛的目标人群？</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Primary threats<br />
主要威胁</td>
<td>Confounding, performance bias, detection bias, placebo effect<br />
混杂因素、操作偏倚、检测偏倚、安慰剂效应</td>
<td>Sampling bias, Hawthorne effect, volunteer bias, restrictive eligibility criteria<br />
抽样偏倚、霍桑效应、志愿者偏倚、过度限制性入组标准</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Protected by<br />
保护措施</td>
<td>Randomization, blinding, placebo controls, standardized protocols<br />
随机化、设盲、安慰剂对照、标准化操作流程</td>
<td>Representative sampling, broad inclusion criteria, pragmatic real-world settings<br />
代表性抽样、宽泛入组标准、真实世界临床环境</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Status in this study<br />
本题研究状态</td>
<td>Well-preserved — randomization + blinding + independent assessors all intact<br />
保存完好——随机化+设盲+独立评估者均完整</td>
<td>Compromised — daytime-only enrollment excludes ~50% of potential participants<br />
受损——仅白天招募排除约50%的潜在参与者</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Relevant study design<br />
相关研究设计</td>
<td>Tightly controlled RCTs, explanatory trials<br />
严格受控的RCT、解释性试验</td>
<td>Pragmatic trials, population-based cohort studies<br />
实用性试验、基于人群的队列研究</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

## 6. One-Sentence Summary & Memory Hook / 一句话总结 & 记忆钩

**Enrolling only daytime COPD exacerbation patients (7 AM–7 PM) creates sampling bias that limits the study's generalizability (external validity), despite strong internal validity through randomization, blinding, and independent outcome assessment.**

**仅纳入白天时段COPD急性加重患者（早7点至晚7点）造成抽样偏倚，限制了研究的推广性（外部效度），尽管随机化、设盲和独立结局评估确保了良好的内部效度。**

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 100%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><p><strong>Memory Hook — BIAS for External Validity Threats / 记忆钩 — "BIAS" 外部效度威胁口诀:</strong></p>
<p>• <strong>B</strong>road population — Is the sample representative of ALL patients, not just those enrolled during convenient hours? / <strong>B</strong>road population（广泛人群）——样本是否代表所有患者，而非仅在方便时段招募的患者？<br />
• <strong>I</strong>nclusion restriction — Enrollment limited to 7 AM–7 PM introduces systematic time-of-day selection / <strong>I</strong>nclusion restriction（纳入限制）——招募限制在早7点至晚7点引入系统性时间选择偏倚<br />
• <strong>A</strong>pplicability — Can results be applied beyond the study's restricted, non-representative sample? / <strong>A</strong>pplicability（适用性）——结果能否推广至研究受限的非代表性样本之外？<br />
• <strong>S</strong>ampling bias — The core mechanism undermining generalizability in this question / <strong>S</strong>ampling bias（抽样偏倚）——本题损害推广性的核心机制</p></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
</tbody>
</table>

## 7. High-Yield Topic Knowledge — Study Bias and Validity in Clinical Research / 高频知识表 — 临床研究中的偏倚与效度

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 50%" />
<col style="width: 50%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Topic</strong><br />
<strong>考点</strong></th>
<th><strong>Key Points</strong><br />
<strong>要点</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>Sampling bias<br />
抽样偏倚</td>
<td>Enrolled participants systematically differ from target population; threatens external validity; classic example: restricting enrollment to specific times, locations, or demographics<br />
纳入的参与者与目标人群系统性不同；威胁外部效度；经典示例：将招募限制在特定时间、地点或人口特征</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Hawthorne effect<br />
霍桑效应</td>
<td>Participants alter behavior simply because they know they are being observed; a form of external validity threat distinct from sampling bias<br />
参与者因知道自己被观察而改变行为；一种与抽样偏倚不同的外部效度威胁</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Lead-time bias<br />
超前时间偏倚</td>
<td>Screening detects disease earlier, making survival appear longer without true benefit; applies only to screening studies, not treatment RCTs<br />
筛查更早检测到疾病，使生存期看似延长但无真实获益；仅适用于筛查研究，不适用于治疗RCT</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Length bias<br />
病程长度偏倚</td>
<td>Screening preferentially detects slower-growing (less aggressive) disease; overestimates screening benefit; companion concept to lead-time bias<br />
筛查优先检测进展较慢（较不具侵袭性）的疾病；高估筛查获益；与超前时间偏倚的配套概念</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Performance bias<br />
操作偏倚</td>
<td>Differential care provided to intervention vs. control groups; reduced by blinding treating physicians<br />
干预组与对照组接受不同诊疗；通过对诊疗医生设盲来减少</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Detection (observer) bias<br />
检测（观察者）偏倚</td>
<td>Differential outcome assessment across groups; reduced by blinding outcome assessors, as done in this study<br />
不同组间结局评估不均衡；通过对结局评估者设盲来减少，本题研究已执行</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Volunteer (healthy user) bias<br />
志愿者（健康用户）偏倚</td>
<td>Study volunteers tend to be healthier and more adherent than non-volunteers; limits generalizability to less health-conscious populations<br />
研究志愿者往往比非志愿者更健康且依从性更高；限制了向健康意识较低人群的推广</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

## 8. Extensions / 延伸扩展

- **Fixing this study:** Extending enrollment to 24 hours by staffing study nurses across multiple shifts would restore representativeness and improve generalizability without sacrificing internal validity\
  **改进本研究:** 通过在多个班次配备研究护士将招募扩展至24小时，可在不牺牲内部效度的前提下恢复代表性并改善推广性

- **Pragmatic vs. explanatory trials:** Explanatory trials (like this one) optimize internal validity through strict controls; pragmatic trials prioritize external validity by enrolling diverse real-world patients with minimal exclusions\
  **实用性试验 vs. 解释性试验:** 解释性试验（如本题）通过严格控制优化内部效度；实用性试验通过纳入多样化的真实世界患者、最小化排除标准来优先考虑外部效度

- **Night vs. daytime COPD exacerbations:** Nocturnal exacerbations are linked to circadian changes in airway resistance and greater hypoxemia; systematically excluding these patients underrepresents more severe disease\
  **夜间 vs. 白天COPD急性加重:** 夜间急性加重与气道阻力的昼夜节律变化及更严重的低氧血症相关；系统性排除这些患者使更重症的疾病表现比例不足

- **Blinding nuance in this study:** Treating physicians are blinded but patients are not explicitly stated to be blinded — this is single-blind from the patient perspective, a minor limitation but far less impactful than the sampling restriction\
  **本研究的设盲细节:** 诊疗医生设盲，但未明确说明患者是否设盲——从患者角度这是单盲，是一个次要局限性，但其影响远小于招募时段限制

# Question 163 — Acute Respiratory Distress Syndrome (ARDS) / 急性呼吸窘迫综合征

## Question Stem / 题干

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 100%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><p>A <strong>57-year-old man</strong> is brought to the emergency department by his neighbors, who found him <strong>lying unconscious in a puddle of vomit</strong> in his apartment. He has a <strong>20-year history of alcohol use disorder</strong>. On arrival, he is <strong>lethargic</strong> and reports <strong>shortness of breath</strong>. He is unable to provide a medical history. His temperature is <strong>39°C (102.2°F)</strong>, pulse is 98/min, respirations are <strong>28/min</strong>, and blood pressure is 132/76 mm Hg. <strong>Diffuse crackles are heard bilaterally</strong>. Arterial blood gas analysis on room air shows: pH 7.44, PCO2 30 mm Hg, <strong>PO2 48 mm Hg</strong>. An x-ray of the chest shows <strong>pulmonary infiltrates bilaterally</strong>. Which of the following is the most appropriate next step in management?</p>
<p><strong>Q: Most appropriate next step in management?</strong></p>
<p>A) Hyperbaric oxygen therapy<br />
B) Intravenous administration of dobutamine<br />
C) Intravenous administration of methylprednisolone<br />
D) Bronchoscopy with lavage<br />
E) Intubation and mechanical ventilation</p>
<p><strong>Correct Answer: E</strong></p></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
</tbody>
</table>

---

## 1. Key Stem Clues / 题干关键词抓考点

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 50%" />
<col style="width: 50%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Key Stem Clue</strong><br />
<strong>关键词</strong></th>
<th><strong>Why It Matters</strong><br />
<strong>为什么重要</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>Found unconscious in puddle of vomit<br />
昏倒在呕吐物中</td>
<td>Classic aspiration event → chemical pneumonitis ± bacterial aspiration pneumonia → ARDS trigger<br />
经典误吸事件→化学性肺炎±细菌性吸入性肺炎→ARDS诱因</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>20-year alcohol use disorder<br />
20年酒精使用障碍</td>
<td>Impaired gag/cough reflex + immune suppression → increased aspiration risk and infection susceptibility<br />
咽反射/咳嗽反射减弱+免疫抑制→增加误吸及感染风险</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Lethargic, unable to provide history<br />
嗜睡，无法提供病史</td>
<td>Altered mental status = inability to protect airway → urgent intubation criterion<br />
意识改变=无法保护气道→紧急插管指征</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>PO2 48 mm Hg on room air<br />
吸室内空气时PO2仅48 mmHg</td>
<td>Severe hypoxemia; P/F ratio = 48/0.21 ≈ 229 → meets ARDS threshold (&lt; 300)<br />
严重低氧血症；P/F比值≈229→符合ARDS诊断阈值（&lt;300）</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>pH 7.44, PCO2 30 mm Hg<br />
pH 7.44，PCO2 30 mmHg</td>
<td>Respiratory alkalosis from tachypnea (RR 28) — compensatory response to hypoxemia, not yet hypercapnic<br />
呼吸急促（RR 28）引起呼吸性碱中毒——对低氧血症的代偿反应，尚未出现高碳酸血症</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Bilateral crackles + bilateral pulmonary infiltrates<br />
双侧湿啰音+双侧肺浸润影</td>
<td>Diffuse alveolar damage pattern — distinguishes ARDS from unilateral pneumonia or focal process<br />
弥漫性肺泡损伤表现——区别于单侧肺炎或局灶性病变</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Temperature 39°C, RR 28/min<br />
体温39°C，呼吸频率28次/分</td>
<td>SIRS criteria met → underlying sepsis/infection as concurrent ARDS trigger<br />
满足SIRS标准→脓毒症/感染作为ARDS的并发触发因素</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

---

## 2. Mechanism / 机制理解

**ARDS** results from a massive **inflammatory cascade** triggered by a direct (pulmonary) or indirect (extrapulmonary) insult, leading to disruption of the **alveolar-capillary membrane**:

**ARDS** 由直接（肺内）或间接（肺外）损伤触发的大规模**炎症级联反应**引起，导致**肺泡-毛细血管膜**完整性破坏：

- Aspiration of gastric contents activates **alveolar macrophages** → release of IL-1, IL-8, TNF-α\
  胃内容物误吸激活**肺泡巨噬细胞**→释放IL-1、IL-8、TNF-α

- Inflammatory mediators recruit **neutrophils** → oxidative burst damages type I and type II pneumocytes\
  炎症介质招募**中性粒细胞**→氧化爆发损伤Ⅰ型和Ⅱ型肺泡上皮细胞

- Loss of **surfactant** (type II pneumocyte injury) + increased alveolar permeability → protein-rich **non-cardiogenic pulmonary edema**\
  **表面活性物质**减少（Ⅱ型细胞受损）+肺泡通透性增高→富含蛋白的**非心源性肺水肿**

- Flooded alveoli become atelectatic → **intrapulmonary shunt** → refractory hypoxemia unresponsive to supplemental O2\
  肺泡被液体填充→肺不张→**肺内分流**→对补氧无反应的顽固性低氧血症

**Pathophysiologic rule of thumb:** In ARDS, hypoxemia is driven by shunt (V/Q = 0), which is why simple O2 supplementation fails and PEEP is required to recruite collapsed alveoli.

**病理生理小窍门:** ARDS低氧血症由分流（V/Q=0）驱动，这正是为何单纯补氧无效而需PEEP来复张塌陷肺泡。

---

## 3. Correct Answer (E) — Intubation and Mechanical Ventilation / 正确答案 (E) — 气管插管与机械通气

**Endotracheal intubation** is the definitive airway management for patients with acute hypoxic respiratory failure who cannot protect their airway:

**气管插管**是急性低氧性呼吸衰竭且无法保护气道患者的确定性气道管理措施：

- Indications met here: PO2 \< 60 on room air (PO2 48), RR 28, lethargy (airway protection failure)\
  本题满足插管指征：室内空气PO2\<60（PO2 48），RR 28，嗜睡（气道保护能力丧失）

- Lung-protective ventilation: tidal volume 6 mL/kg IBW + PEEP 5–8 cmH2O to reduce ventilator-induced lung injury (VILI)\
  肺保护性通气策略：潮气量6 mL/kg理想体重+PEEP 5–8 cmH2O，以减少呼吸机相关肺损伤（VILI）

- Goal: maintain PaO2 55–80 mmHg or SpO2 88–95% — avoid hyperoxia which worsens outcomes\
  目标：维持PaO2 55–80 mmHg或SpO2 88–95%——避免高氧血症（可加重预后）

**Diagnosis:** ARDS by Berlin criteria: acute onset (\< 7 days), bilateral opacities not explained by effusion/collapse, not fully explained by cardiac failure, PaO2/FiO2 \< 300 with PEEP ≥ 5 cmH2O

**诊断:** 依据柏林标准诊断ARDS：急性起病（\<7天），双侧浸润影（非渗出/肺不张所致），非心力衰竭完全解释，PaO2/FiO2\<300（PEEP≥5 cmH2O条件下）

**Treatment:** Intubation + lung-protective ventilation; treat underlying cause (aspiration pneumonia → antibiotics); prone positioning for severe ARDS (P/F \< 150); neuromuscular blockade if dyssynchrony

**治疗:** 插管+肺保护性通气；治疗基础病因（吸入性肺炎→抗生素）；重度ARDS（P/F\<150）行俯卧位通气；人机不同步时考虑神经肌肉阻滞

---

## 4. Options Elimination / 错误选项排除逻辑

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 33%" />
<col style="width: 33%" />
<col style="width: 33%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Option</strong><br />
<strong>选项</strong></th>
<th><strong>Why Wrong</strong><br />
<strong>为什么错</strong></th>
<th><strong>Key Discriminator</strong><br />
<strong>鉴别要点</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>A — Hyperbaric oxygen therapy<br />
A — 高压氧治疗</td>
<td>Wrong indication — hyperbaric O2 is for CO poisoning, not ARDS; no CO exposure history here<br />
适应证错误——高压氧用于一氧化碳中毒，非ARDS；本题无CO暴露史</td>
<td>CO poisoning: headache, nausea, cherry-red skin, COHb elevated — none present here<br />
CO中毒：头痛、恶心、皮肤樱桃红、COHb升高——本题均无</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>B — IV dobutamine<br />
B — 静脉多巴酚丁胺</td>
<td>Dobutamine is for cardiogenic shock (↓CO, ↑PCWP); BP is normal here and no cardiac history<br />
多巴酚丁胺用于心源性休克（↓CO，↑PCWP）；本题血压正常且无心脏病史</td>
<td>Cardiogenic shock: cool extremities, JVD, S3 gallop, low BP — not this presentation<br />
心源性休克：肢体湿冷、颈静脉怒张、S3奔马律、低血压——本题不符合</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>C — IV methylprednisolone<br />
C — 静脉甲泼尼龙</td>
<td>Steroids lack clear mortality benefit in early ARDS; not the immediate priority when airway is threatened<br />
激素在早期ARDS中缺乏明确死亡率获益；气道受威胁时激素非当务之急</td>
<td>Even if steroids help later in ARDS, securing the airway always takes precedence<br />
即使激素在ARDS后期有益，保护气道始终是首要任务</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>D — Bronchoscopy with lavage<br />
D — 支气管镜灌洗</td>
<td>BAL is diagnostic for PCP, TB, or atypical infections in immunocompromised hosts — not indicated here urgently<br />
支气管肺泡灌洗用于免疫缺陷患者的PCP/结核等诊断——本题无紧急指征</td>
<td>No known immunocompromise (HIV, transplant) to prompt PCP/TB workup as first step<br />
无已知免疫缺陷（HIV、移植）提示需首先排查PCP/结核</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>E — Intubation and mechanical ventilation ✓<br />
E — 气管插管与机械通气 ✓</td>
<td>CORRECT — severe hypoxemia (PO2 48), lethargy, RR 28, inability to protect airway all mandate emergent intubation<br />
正确——严重低氧血症（PO2 48）、嗜睡、RR 28、无法保护气道，均为紧急插管强制指征</td>
<td>When airway protection fails + refractory hypoxemia → intubate first, investigate later<br />
气道保护失败+顽固性低氧血症→先插管，再进一步检查</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

*The most tempting distractor is Choice C (steroids) — while steroids are sometimes used in late/fibro-proliferative ARDS, they are never the immediate first step and carry potential harm early in sepsis-triggered ARDS.*

激素（C选项）是最常见的干扰项——虽然激素偶用于ARDS晚期/纤维增殖期，但绝非急性期首要处理，且在脓毒症触发的ARDS早期可能有害。

---

## 5. High-Yield Summary Table — ARDS vs. Cardiogenic Pulmonary Edema / 急性呼吸窘迫综合征 vs. 心源性肺水肿

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 33%" />
<col style="width: 33%" />
<col style="width: 33%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Feature</strong><br />
<strong>特征</strong></th>
<th><strong>ARDS</strong><br />
<strong>急性呼吸窘迫综合征</strong></th>
<th><strong>Cardiogenic Pulmonary Edema</strong><br />
<strong>心源性肺水肿</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>Mechanism<br />
发病机制</td>
<td>Increased alveolar-capillary permeability (inflammatory)<br />
肺泡-毛细血管通透性增高（炎症性）</td>
<td>Elevated hydrostatic pressure (↑PCWP &gt; 18 mmHg)<br />
静水压升高（PCWP &gt; 18 mmHg）</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Edema fluid protein<br />
水肿液蛋白</td>
<td>Protein-rich (exudate)<br />
富含蛋白（渗出液）</td>
<td>Protein-poor (transudate)<br />
蛋白含量低（漏出液）</td>

肺毛细血管楔压</td>
<td>Normal (≤ 18 mmHg)<br />

<td>Elevated (&gt; 18 mmHg)<br />
升高（&gt;18 mmHg）</td>

<tr>
<td>CXR pattern<br />
胸片表现</td>
<td>Bilateral infiltrates, no cardiomegaly, no Kerley B lines<br />
双侧浸润影，无心脏扩大，无Kerley B线</td>
<td>Bilateral infiltrates + cardiomegaly + Kerley B lines + cephalization<br />
双侧浸润影+心脏扩大+Kerley B线+肺血重新分布</td>

<tr>
<td>Response to diuretics<br />
对利尿剂反应</td>
<td>Poor response<br />
反应差</td>
<td>Good response<br />
反应良好</td>

<tr>
<td>Precipitants<br />
诱因</td>
<td>Sepsis, aspiration, trauma, pancreatitis, pneumonia<br />
脓毒症、误吸、创伤、胰腺炎、肺炎</td>
<td>MI, CHF exacerbation, valvular disease, fluid overload<br />
心肌梗死、心衰加重、瓣膜病、液体超负荷</td>

<tr>
<td>Treatment<br />
治疗</td>
<td>Lung-protective ventilation, treat cause<br />
肺保护性通气，治疗基础病因</td>
<td>Diuretics, afterload reduction, treat underlying cardiac cause<br />
利尿剂、降低后负荷、治疗基础心脏病因</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

---

## 6. One-Sentence Summary & Memory Hook / 一句话总结 & 记忆钩

**In a lethargic patient with severe hypoxemia (PO2 \< 60), bilateral infiltrates, and inability to protect the airway, emergent intubation and lung-protective mechanical ventilation is the immediate life-saving intervention for ARDS.**

**对于嗜睡、严重低氧血症（PO2\<60）、双侧浸润影且无法保护气道的患者，紧急气管插管+肺保护性机械通气是ARDS即刻救命的干预措施。**

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 100%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><p><strong>Memory Hook — ARDS Berlin "3 Levels of Hypoxia" / 记忆钩 — ARDS柏林分级"三级低氧":</strong></p>
<p>• <strong>M</strong>ild ARDS — P/F 200–300, PEEP ≥ 5 / 轻度ARDS——P/F 200–300，PEEP≥5<br />
• <strong>M</strong>oderate ARDS — P/F 100–200, PEEP ≥ 5 / 中度ARDS——P/F 100–200，PEEP≥5<br />
• <strong>S</strong>evere ARDS — P/F &lt; 100, PEEP ≥ 5 → consider prone + NMBA / 重度ARDS——P/F&lt;100，PEEP≥5→考虑俯卧位+神经肌肉阻滞<br />
• <strong>T</strong>idalvolume 6 mL/kg IBW — lung-protective always / 潮气量6 mL/kg理想体重——始终肺保护<br />
• <strong>P</strong>EEP titrated to minimize FiO2 while avoiding overdistension / PEEP调节以最小化FiO2同时避免过度充气</p></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
</tbody>
</table>

## 7. High-Yield Topic Knowledge — ARDS: Diagnosis, Management & Complications / 高频知识表 — ARDS：诊断、管理与并发症

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 50%" />
<col style="width: 50%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Topic</strong><br />
<strong>考点</strong></th>
<th><strong>Key Points</strong><br />
<strong>要点</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>Berlin Definition criteria<br />
柏林定义标准</td>
<td>(1) Acute onset &lt; 7 days; (2) bilateral opacities on CXR/CT not explained by effusion, collapse, nodules; (3) not fully explained by cardiac failure/fluid overload; (4) PaO2/FiO2 &lt; 300 with PEEP ≥ 5 cmH2O<br />
（1）急性起病&lt;7天；（2）胸片/CT双侧浸润影（非渗出/不张/结节）；（3）不完全由心衰/液体超负荷解释；（4）PEEP≥5条件下P/F&lt;300</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Common precipitants<br />
常见诱因</td>
<td>Direct: aspiration, pneumonia, pulmonary contusion, near-drowning; Indirect: sepsis (most common), pancreatitis, massive transfusion, trauma<br />
直接：误吸、肺炎、肺挫伤、溺水；间接：脓毒症（最常见）、胰腺炎、大量输血、创伤</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Lung-protective ventilation (ARDSNet)<br />
肺保护性通气（ARDSNet策略）</td>
<td>TV 6 mL/kg IBW, plateau pressure &lt; 30 cmH2O, PEEP titration, permissive hypercapnia acceptable (pH &gt; 7.2)<br />
潮气量6 mL/kg理想体重，平台压&lt;30 cmH2O，PEEP滴定，允许性高碳酸血症（pH&gt;7.2可接受）</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Prone positioning<br />
俯卧位通气</td>
<td>Indicated for severe ARDS (P/F &lt; 150); improves V/Q matching by recruiting posterior atelectatic zones; ≥ 12 hours/day; reduces mortality (PROSEVA trial)<br />
适用于重度ARDS（P/F&lt;150）；通过复张背侧肺不张区改善V/Q匹配；每日≥12小时；降低死亡率（PROSEVA试验）</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Fluid management<br />
液体管理</td>
<td>Conservative fluid strategy (FACTT trial) reduces ventilator days; avoid aggressive fluid resuscitation once hemodynamically stable<br />
保守补液策略（FACTT试验）可减少机械通气天数；血流动力学稳定后避免积极补液</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Complications of mechanical ventilation<br />
机械通气并发症</td>
<td>Barotrauma (pneumothorax), VILI, VAP (ventilator-associated pneumonia), oxygen toxicity, ICU-acquired weakness<br />
气压伤（气胸）、呼吸机相关肺损伤、VAP（呼吸机相关肺炎）、氧毒性、ICU获得性肌无力</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Steroids in ARDS<br />
激素在ARDS中的应用</td>
<td>No proven mortality benefit in early ARDS; may be considered in late fibro-proliferative phase (&gt; 7–14 days) if no improvement; avoid early in sepsis<br />
早期ARDS中无明确死亡率获益；若无改善可考虑晚期纤维增殖阶段（&gt;7–14天）使用；脓毒症早期避免使用</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

---

## 8. Extensions / 延伸扩展

- **Aspiration pneumonitis vs. aspiration pneumonia:** Mendelson syndrome (chemical injury from acid) is sterile and often self-resolving; bacterial aspiration pneumonia requires antibiotics (cover anaerobes + gram-negatives)\
  **误吸性肺炎 vs. 吸入性肺炎:** Mendelson综合征（胃酸化学性损伤）为无菌性，常可自愈；细菌性吸入性肺炎需抗生素（覆盖厌氧菌+革兰阴性菌）

- **P/F ratio calculation:** Always divide PaO2 by FiO2 as a decimal (room air = 0.21); P/F \< 300 = ARDS, \< 200 = moderate, \< 100 = severe; this ratio is tested repeatedly on USMLE\
  **P/F比值计算:** 始终以小数形式除以FiO2（室内空气=0.21）；P/F\<300=ARDS，\<200=中度，\<100=重度；此比值在USMLE中反复考查

- **Indications for emergent intubation (mnemonic: HALO):** Hypoxia refractory to O2, Airway protection failure (lethargy/no gag), Labor of breathing exhaustion, Obstruction anticipated\
  **紧急插管指征（助记：HALO）:** 顽固性低氧血症、气道保护失败（嗜睡/咽反射消失）、呼吸功耗竭、预期气道梗阻

- **Why NOT hyperbaric O2 here:** HBO2 requires PaO2 elevation by dissolving O2 in plasma; it doesn't address diffusion barrier or shunt physiology of ARDS, and delays definitive airway management\
  **本题为何不选高压氧:** 高压氧依赖溶解于血浆的O2升高PaO2；它无法解决ARDS的弥散障碍或肺内分流，且会延误确定性气道管理

# Question 164 — Wrong-Site Surgery Prevention / 手术部位错误预防

## Question Stem / 题干

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 100%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><p>A <strong>37-year-old woman</strong> is scheduled for <strong>arthroscopic repair of a right medial meniscus tear</strong>. Her procedure is the surgeon's <strong>last scheduled operation of the day</strong>. <strong>All previous procedures this day involved the left knee</strong>. In the operating room, the <strong>resident prepares the left knee</strong> for the operation. The operation is discontinued after the surgeon discovers <strong>no meniscus tear</strong>, and the patient is informed about the error. Which of the following is the best approach to <strong>prevent future errors of this type</strong>?</p>
<p><strong>Q: Which of the following is the best approach to prevent future errors of this type?</strong></p>
<p>A) Asking the surgeon to resign from the medical staff<br />
B) Having the surgeon and resident present the case at the next morbidity and mortality conference<br />
C) Having the surgeon mark the surgical site with input from the patient prior to induction of anesthesia<br />
D) Having the surgeon review the chart just prior to the procedure<br />
E) Placing an incident report in the files of the resident and surgeon</p>
<p><strong>Correct Answer: C</strong></p></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
</tbody>
</table>

## 1. Key Stem Clues / 题干关键词抓考点

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 50%" />
<col style="width: 50%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Key Stem Clue</strong><br />
<strong>关键词</strong></th>
<th><strong>Why It Matters</strong><br />
<strong>为什么重要</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>Right medial meniscus tear (scheduled)<br />
右侧内侧半月板撕裂（计划手术）</td>
<td>Establishes the correct laterality; any deviation constitutes a wrong-site error<br />
确立了正确的手术侧别；任何偏差均构成手术部位错误</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Last scheduled operation of the day<br />
当天最后一台手术</td>
<td>End-of-day fatigue and cognitive depletion increase susceptibility to routine errors<br />
一天结束时的疲劳和认知耗竭增加了常规错误的风险</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>All previous procedures involved the left knee<br />
当天所有前序手术均涉及左膝</td>
<td>Repetition priming — team was cognitively primed to prepare the left side by default<br />
重复启动效应——团队在认知上被默认预设为准备左侧</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Resident prepares the left knee<br />
住院医师准备了左膝</td>
<td>Identifies the proximate cause: failure of preoperative surgical site verification<br />
识别近因：术前手术部位核验失败</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>No meniscus tear found<br />
未发现半月板撕裂</td>
<td>Confirms wrong-site surgery occurred; unnecessary procedure inflicted upon the patient<br />
确认发生了手术部位错误；对患者实施了不必要的手术</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Best approach to prevent future errors<br />
预防未来此类错误的最佳方法</td>
<td>Asks for a systemic, proactive prevention strategy — not retrospective punishment<br />
要求系统性、前瞻性的预防策略，而非事后惩罚</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

## 2. Mechanism / 机制理解

**Wrong-site surgery** is a sentinel event rooted in **system failure**, not merely individual negligence. The **Joint Commission Universal Protocol** was specifically designed to interrupt the chain of errors before they reach the patient:

**手术部位错误**是一种根源于**系统失误**（而非单纯个人疏忽）的哨兵事件。**The Joint Commission Universal Protocol** 专门用于在错误到达患者前切断错误链：

- **Preoperative verification** of patient identity, procedure, and site closes communication gaps between scheduling, chart, and team\
  **术前核验**患者身份、手术名称和部位，弥合预约、病历和团队之间的沟通盲区

- **Surgical site marking** by the operating surgeon makes the intended site unambiguous and visible even after draping\
  **由主刀医生标记手术部位**，使目标部位清晰明确，即便铺巾后仍可见

- **Patient participation** in verification leverages the patient as the final safety checkpoint before anesthesia renders them unable to respond\
  **患者参与**核验，将患者作为麻醉前最后一道安全关卡

- A pre-incision **"time out"** requires the entire surgical team to pause and verbally confirm site, procedure, and identity\
  切皮前**"暂停"确认**要求整个手术团队暂停并口头确认部位、手术和身份

**Anatomic rule of thumb:** Laterality errors (left vs. right) are the most common form of wrong-site surgery — bilateral structures such as knees, hips, and extremities carry the highest risk.

**解剖小窍门:** 左右侧错误是最常见的手术部位错误类型——膝关节、髋关节和四肢等双侧结构风险最高。

## 3. Correct Answer (C) — Universal Protocol Surgical Site Marking / 正确答案 (C) — 通用规程手术部位标记

**Surgical site marking with patient input** is the single most effective intervention mandated by The Joint Commission Universal Protocol for preventing wrong-site surgery:

**由患者参与的手术部位标记**是The Joint Commission Universal Protocol强制要求的、预防手术部位错误最有效的单一干预措施：

- The surgeon marks the site **before anesthesia induction**, while the patient is awake and can actively confirm the correct side\
  医生在**麻醉诱导前**标记部位，此时患者清醒并能主动确认正确侧别

- Patient participation directly catches discrepancies between the medical record and the patient's own understanding of the planned surgery\
  患者参与可直接发现病历记录与患者对手术计划理解之间的差异

- The mark must remain **visible after surgical draping** — positioned so the team can see it even when the operative field is covered\
  标记必须在**铺无菌巾后仍可见**——位置应确保覆盖术野后团队仍能看到

**Diagnosis:** The root cause here is the absence of a standardized site-marking protocol; had the right knee been marked before anesthesia, left-side preparation would have been immediately recognized as incorrect.

**诊断:** 根本原因是缺乏标准化的部位标记规程；若在麻醉前已标记右膝，准备左侧时将被立即识别为错误。

**Treatment:** Implement the three-step Joint Commission Universal Protocol: (1) preoperative verification checklist, (2) surgeon-performed site marking with patient input before anesthesia, (3) pre-incision "time out" with full team confirmation.

**治疗:** 实施三步骤The Joint Commission Universal Protocol：（1）术前核验清单，（2）主刀医生在患者参与下于麻醉前完成部位标记，（3）切皮前全团队"暂停"确认。

## 4. Options Elimination / 错误选项排除逻辑

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 33%" />
<col style="width: 33%" />
<col style="width: 33%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Option</strong><br />
<strong>选项</strong></th>
<th><strong>Why Wrong</strong><br />
<strong>为什么错</strong></th>
<th><strong>Key Discriminator</strong><br />
<strong>鉴别要点</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>A — Asking the surgeon to resign from the medical staff<br />
A — 要求外科医生辞职</td>
<td>Wrong — punitive individual action does not address the systemic root cause; a single error does not render a surgeon unfit to practice<br />
错误——惩罚性个体措施无法解决系统性根本原因；单次错误不代表外科医生不适合执业</td>
<td>Wrong-site errors are multifactorial and system-based; removing one person leaves the flawed process intact<br />
手术部位错误是多因素、系统性的；移除个人而保留缺陷流程毫无意义</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>B — Having the surgeon and resident present the case at M&amp;M conference<br />
B — 在死亡率与并发症讨论会上汇报案例</td>
<td>Insufficient alone — M&amp;M raises team awareness but does not constitute a proactive, standardized prevention protocol<br />
单独不足——M&amp;M提高团队意识但不构成主动、标准化的预防规程</td>
<td>Awareness is adjunctive; it does not replace the physical safeguard of surgeon-performed site marking with patient input<br />
意识提升是辅助手段；无法替代外科医生在患者参与下标记部位的物理保障</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>C — Having the surgeon mark the surgical site with input from the patient prior to induction ✓<br />
C — 在麻醉诱导前由医生在患者参与下标记手术部位 ✓</td>
<td>CORRECT — directly targets the mechanism of wrong-site surgery with the strongest evidence-based, protocol-mandated safeguard<br />
正确——以最强循证、规程要求的保障措施直接针对手术部位错误的发生机制</td>
<td>Joint Commission Universal Protocol mandates this exact step; patient input provides a critical independent verification<br />
联合委员会通用规程强制要求此确切步骤；患者参与提供了关键的独立核验</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>D — Having the surgeon review the chart just prior to the procedure<br />
D — 手术前由外科医生复查病历</td>
<td>Appropriate but insufficient — chart review does not prevent the error if the site is not physically marked before the patient is anesthetized<br />
适当但不充分——若患者麻醉前部位未被物理标记，仅查阅病历无法防止错误</td>
<td>Chart review is one component of verification but not a substitute for site marking; the chart was available here yet the error still occurred<br />
病历复查是核验的一个环节，但不能替代部位标记；此案例中病历存在但错误仍然发生</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>E — Placing an incident report in the files of the resident and surgeon<br />
E — 在住院医师和外科医生档案中放置事故报告</td>
<td>Wrong — documentation is administrative and retrospective, not preventive; does not reduce future error risk<br />
错误——记录是行政性、回顾性的，而非预防性的；无法降低未来错误风险</td>
<td>Incident reports support root cause analysis but do not themselves prevent recurrence; they are not a safety protocol<br />
事故报告支持根本原因分析，但其本身不能防止复发；它们不是安全规程</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

*The most tempting distractors are D (chart review, which is part of verification but not sufficient) and B (M&M conference, which is educational but not a proactive protocol) — neither replaces the physical act of marking the surgical site with the patient's direct participation.*

最具迷惑性的干扰项是D（病历复查，属于核验的一部分但不充分）和B（M&M讨论会，有教育价值但非主动规程）——两者均无法替代在患者直接参与下物理标记手术部位的行为。

## 6. One-Sentence Summary & Memory Hook / 一句话总结 & 记忆钩

**The most effective prevention for wrong-site surgery is pre-anesthesia surgical site marking by the operating surgeon with direct patient participation, as mandated by The Joint Commission Universal Protocol.**

**预防手术部位错误最有效的措施是：由主刀医生在麻醉前在患者直接参与下标记手术部位，这是The Joint Commission Universal Protocol的强制性要求。**

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 100%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><p><strong>Memory Hook — Universal Protocol "TIME OUT" / 记忆钩 — 通用规程"TIME OUT":</strong></p>
<p>• <strong>T</strong>ype of procedure — confirm the exact surgery before entering the OR / 确认手术类型——进入手术室前核实具体手术<br />
• <strong>I</strong>dentity of patient — verify with two identifiers / 确认患者身份——用两种方式核实<br />
• <strong>M</strong>ark the site — surgeon marks with patient input before anesthesia induction / 标记部位——主刀在麻醉诱导前在患者参与下标记<br />
• <strong>E</strong>veryone agrees — final team "time out" before the first incision / 全员确认——第一刀切皮前的最终团队"暂停"<br />
• <strong>O</strong>ut with discrepancies — any team member may halt if something is wrong / 发现差异立即叫停——任何团队成员发现问题均可暂停</p></th>
</tr>
</thead>

</tbody>
</table>

## 7. High-Yield Topic Knowledge — Wrong-Site Surgery & Joint Commission Universal Protocol / 高频知识表 — 手术部位错误与联合委员会通用规程

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 50%" />
<col style="width: 50%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Topic</strong><br />
<strong>考点</strong></th>
<th><strong>Key Points</strong><br />
<strong>要点</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>Definition of wrong-site surgery<br />
手术部位错误的定义</td>
<td>Surgery performed on the wrong body part, wrong side, wrong level, wrong patient, or wrong procedure; classified as a sentinel event by The Joint Commission<br />
在错误身体部位、错误侧别、错误节段、错误患者或进行错误手术；被The Joint Commission归类为哨兵事件</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Joint Commission Universal Protocol steps<br />
联合委员会通用规程步骤</td>
<td>Three required components: (1) preoperative verification process, (2) marking of the operative site, (3) pre-procedure "time out"; applies to all invasive procedures<br />
三个必要组成部分：（1）术前核验流程，（2）手术部位标记，（3）操作前"暂停"；适用于所有有创操作</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Who performs the site marking?<br />
谁执行部位标记？</td>
<td>The surgeon who will perform the procedure — not the resident, not the nurse, not a designee; the operating surgeon is responsible<br />
将要执行手术的外科医生——不是住院医师、不是护士、不是代理人；主刀医生负责</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Timing of site marking<br />
部位标记的时机</td>
<td>Before anesthesia induction, while the patient is awake and alert and can actively participate in confirming the correct site<br />
在麻醉诱导前，患者清醒且警觉、能够主动参与确认正确部位时</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Which procedures require marking?<br />
哪些手术需要标记？</td>
<td>Procedures involving laterality, multiple structures (fingers, toes, lesions), or multiple spinal levels; single midline organs (e.g., hysterectomy) typically do not require marking<br />
涉及侧别、多个结构（手指、脚趾、病变）或多个脊柱节段的操作；单一中线器官（如子宫切除术）通常不要求标记</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Root cause analysis after wrong-site surgery<br />
手术部位错误后的根本原因分析</td>
<td>A systematic RCA with hospital staff and risk management is required to identify system failures and implement corrective measures; blame alone is insufficient<br />
需与医院工作人员和风险管理部门进行系统性根本原因分析（RCA）以识别系统失误并实施纠正措施；单纯归责是不够的</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Malpractice and legal implications<br />
医疗事故与法律影响</td>
<td>Wrong-site surgery almost always constitutes negligence and is highly likely to result in malpractice litigation; designated a "never event" in many jurisdictions<br />
手术部位错误几乎总是构成过失，极有可能导致医疗事故诉讼；在许多司法管辖区被列为"永不应发生事件"</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

## 8. Extensions / 延伸扩展

- **Cognitive bias at play:** "Repetition priming" explains this case — after the same procedure on the same side all day, the team defaults to the familiar pattern without conscious re-verification; site marking physically breaks this cognitive autopilot\
  **认知偏见的作用:** "重复启动效应"解释了此案例——整天在同一侧进行相同手术后，团队无需有意识地重新核验便默认为熟悉的模式；部位标记在物理上打破了这种认知自动化

- **Swiss Cheese Model application:** Wrong-site errors exemplify Reason's Swiss Cheese Model — multiple safety layers (scheduling flag, preoperative briefing, team verbal check, chart review) all had holes that aligned simultaneously, allowing the error to reach the patient\
  **瑞士奶酪模型应用:** 手术部位错误是Reason瑞士奶酪模型的典型体现——多个安全层（预约标记、术前简报、团队口头核查、病历复查）同时出现漏洞并对齐，使错误得以到达患者

- **USMLE error prevention pattern:** On USMLE, when asked to "prevent future errors," always favor systemic/protocol-based answers (checklists, standardization, patient involvement) over individual blame answers (firing, mandatory reporting alone, punitive documentation)\
  **USMLE错误预防规律:** 在USMLE中，被问及"预防未来错误"时，始终优先选择系统性/基于规程的答案（核查清单、标准化、患者参与），而非个人归责答案（解雇、单纯强制报告、惩罚性记录）

- **Resident's role vs. attending's responsibility:** The resident made the proximate error, but the attending surgeon bears ultimate responsibility for site verification and marking; the Universal Protocol assigns site marking specifically to the operating surgeon, not trainees\
  **住院医师角色与主治医师责任:** 住院医师犯了近端错误，但主治外科医生对部位核验和标记承担最终责任；Universal Protocol明确将部位标记分配给主刀医生，而非受训者

# Question 165 — Gastric Cancer / 胃癌

## Question Stem / 题干

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 100%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><p>A <strong>52-year-old woman</strong> comes to the office because of a <strong>6-week history of moderate epigastric pain</strong> and an intermittent mild, midsternal burning sensation when she eats. She has had a <strong>4.5-kg (10-lb) weight loss during the past 6 months</strong> despite no change in appetite. During this time, she also occasionally has had <strong>dark stools</strong>. She has type 2 diabetes mellitus, hypertension, and osteoarthritis. Her medications are metformin, hydrochlorothiazide, and <strong>ibuprofen</strong>. She has <strong>smoked one pack of cigarettes daily for 36 years</strong>. She <strong>appears malnourished</strong>. She is 163 cm (5 ft 4 in) tall and weighs 54 kg (120 lb); BMI is 21 kg/m². Her pulse is 86/min, and blood pressure is 110/65 mm Hg. Examination shows mild epigastric tenderness. There is no hepatosplenomegaly. The remainder of the examination shows no abnormalities. Her <strong>hematocrit is 30%</strong>, leukocyte count is 6200/mm³, and <strong>platelet count is 530,000/mm³</strong>. Serum electrolyte concentrations are within the reference ranges. In addition to discontinuing ibuprofen therapy, which of the following is the most appropriate next step in management?</p>
<p><strong>Q: Most appropriate next step in management?</strong></p>
<p>A) Celecoxib therapy<br />
B) Esophagogastroduodenoscopy<br />
C) Follow-up examination in 6 weeks<br />
D) Pantoprazole therapy and follow-up examination in 6 weeks<br />
E) Serologic testing for Helicobacter pylori</p>
<p><strong>Correct Answer: B</strong></p></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
</tbody>
</table>

## 1. Key Stem Clues / 题干关键词抓考点

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 50%" />
<col style="width: 50%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Key Stem Clue</strong><br />
<strong>关键词</strong></th>
<th><strong>Why It Matters</strong><br />
<strong>为什么重要</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>Unintentional weight loss 4.5 kg over 6 months despite preserved appetite<br />
6个月内无意减重4.5公斤且食欲无变化</td>
<td>Classic alarm feature for malignancy; appetite-sparing weight loss distinguishes cancer cachexia from dietary causes<br />
恶性肿瘤经典报警症状；食欲正常却体重下降提示肿瘤恶病质而非饮食原因</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Dark stools (melena)<br />
黑便（柏油样便）</td>
<td>Indicates upper GI bleeding proximal to ligament of Treitz; blood digested during intestinal transit turns black<br />
提示Treitz韧带以上上消化道出血；血液在肠道转运过程中被消化变黑</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Malnourished appearance, BMI 21<br />
营养不良外观，BMI 21</td>
<td>Suggests a chronic, progressive wasting process beyond simple acid-peptic disease<br />
提示超出简单酸消化性疾病范畴的慢性进展性消耗性疾病</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>36 pack-year smoking history<br />
36包年吸烟史</td>
<td>Major independent risk factor for gastric adenocarcinoma<br />
胃腺癌的主要独立危险因素</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Hematocrit 30% (iron deficiency anemia)<br />
红细胞压积30%（缺铁性贫血）</td>
<td>Reflects chronic blood loss; alarm feature that mandates upper endoscopy rather than empirical therapy<br />
反映慢性失血；需行上消化道内镜而非经验性治疗的报警症状</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Platelet count 530,000/mm³ (thrombocytosis)<br />
血小板53万（血小板增多症）</td>
<td>Reactive thrombocytosis from chronic inflammation or occult malignancy; additional red flag not explained by NSAID use alone<br />
慢性炎症或隐匿性恶性肿瘤引起的反应性血小板增多；单纯NSAIDs使用无法解释的额外红旗信号</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Ibuprofen use<br />
服用布洛芬</td>
<td>NSAIDs cause gastric mucosal injury and may contribute to bleeding, but cannot explain weight loss, malnourishment, or thrombocytosis<br />
NSAIDs导致胃黏膜损伤并可能加重出血，但不能解释体重下降、营养不良或血小板增多</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

## 2. Mechanism / 机制理解

**Gastric cancer** arises through a stepwise progression of **chronic mucosal injury** → atrophic gastritis → intestinal metaplasia → dysplasia → adenocarcinoma, with **H. pylori** infection and smoking as the dominant drivers:

**胃癌**通过**慢性黏膜损伤**→萎缩性胃炎→肠化生→异型增生→腺癌的逐步进展发生，**幽门螺旋杆菌**感染和吸烟是主要驱动因素：

- Tumor surface erosion causes chronic capillary bleeding → iron deficiency anemia and melena\
  肿瘤表面侵蚀引起慢性毛细血管出血→缺铁性贫血和黑便

- Tumor-related **cachexia** and mechanical early satiety drive progressive weight loss independent of caloric intake\
  肿瘤相关**恶病质**和机械性早饱导致与热量摄入无关的进行性体重下降

- Chronic inflammation and malignancy trigger **reactive thrombocytosis** via IL-6–driven hepatic thrombopoietin release\
  慢性炎症和恶性肿瘤通过IL-6驱动的肝脏血小板生成素释放触发**反应性血小板增多**

- Alarm features mandate direct tissue diagnosis — PPI therapy may mask symptoms while the tumor progresses\
  报警症状要求直接组织学诊断——PPI治疗可能在肿瘤进展的同时掩盖症状

**Anatomic rule of thumb:** Gastric cancers arise most frequently at the antrum and lesser curvature; EGD uniquely allows direct visualization plus biopsy in one procedure.

**解剖小窍门:** 胃癌最常发生于胃窦和胃小弯；EGD是唯一能在同一操作中实现直接观察加活检的手段。

## 3. Correct Answer (B) — Esophagogastroduodenoscopy / 正确答案 (B) — 食管胃十二指肠镜检查

**Esophagogastroduodenoscopy (EGD)** is the gold standard for evaluating upper GI alarm features, providing direct mucosal visualization, targeted biopsy for histologic diagnosis, and hemostasis capability in a single procedure:

**食管胃十二指肠镜（EGD）** 是评估上消化道报警症状的金标准，在单次操作中实现黏膜直视、定向活检组织学诊断和止血三重功能：

- Alarm features that mandate EGD over empirical therapy: unintentional weight loss, melena/hematemesis, iron deficiency anemia, progressive dysphagia, persistent vomiting, palpable mass\
  要求以EGD代替经验性治疗的报警症状：无意体重下降、黑便/呕血、缺铁性贫血、进行性吞咽困难、持续呕吐、可触及包块

- This patient has three simultaneous alarm features plus smoking history and reactive thrombocytosis — empirical PPI or H. pylori serology cannot substitute for tissue diagnosis\
  该患者同时具备三项报警症状加吸烟史和反应性血小板增多——经验性PPI或H. pylori血清学检测不能替代组织学诊断

- All gastric ulcers found on EGD must be biopsied to exclude malignancy, even if they appear benign\
  EGD发现的所有胃溃疡均必须活检以排除恶性肿瘤，即使外观看似良性

**Diagnosis:** This clinical picture — 52-year-old smoker, three alarm features (weight loss, melena, anemia), malnourishment, and reactive thrombocytosis — constitutes a gastric malignancy until proven otherwise by EGD with biopsy.

**诊断:** 这一临床表现——52岁吸烟者，三项报警症状（体重下降、黑便、贫血），营养不良，反应性血小板增多——在EGD加活检证实之前，应被视为胃恶性肿瘤。

**Treatment:** If gastric cancer confirmed: staging CT + endoscopic ultrasound; resectable disease → subtotal/total gastrectomy ± perioperative FLOT chemotherapy; metastatic disease → palliative systemic chemotherapy ± HER2-targeted therapy (trastuzumab) if HER2-positive.

**治疗:** 若确诊胃癌：CT分期+超声内镜；可切除病变→胃次全/全切±围手术期FLOT化疗；转移性病变→姑息性系统化疗±HER2靶向治疗（曲妥珠单抗，如HER2阳性）。

<tr>

<strong>选项</strong></th>

<strong>为什么错</strong></th>

<tr>
<td>A — Celecoxib therapy<br />
A — 塞来昔布治疗</td>
<td>Still an NSAID — contraindicated with active upper GI bleeding; switching NSAIDs does not address the alarm features driving this presentation<br />
仍是NSAIDs——活动性上消化道出血时禁忌；换用NSAIDs无法解决导致此次就诊的报警症状</td>
<td>Celecoxib is COX-2 selective and has lower GI risk but remains contraindicated in active bleeding; no NSAID is safe here<br />
塞来昔布选择性抑制COX-2，GI风险较低，但活动性出血时仍属禁忌；此情况下任何NSAIDs均不安全</td>

只有EGD能同时提供观察、活检和止血功能</td>

危险的延误——消化道出血、体重下降和贫血需要立即检查；等待6周可能错过可切除阶段的恶性肿瘤</td>
<td>Even a single alarm feature warrants prompt evaluation; this patient has three<br />
即使单项报警症状也需及时评估；该患者有三项</td>

<tr>
<td>D — Pantoprazole therapy and follow-up in 6 weeks<br />
D — 泮托拉唑治疗并6周后随访</td>
<td>Appropriate for uncomplicated peptic ulcer disease without alarm features — empirical PPI here delays diagnosis and may symptomatically mask a growing cancer<br />
适用于无报警症状的非复杂性消化性溃疡——此处经验性PPI会延误诊断，并可能通过症状缓解掩盖进展中的癌症</td>
<td>PPI + follow-up is reasonable ONLY when alarm features are absent and patient age &lt;55<br />
只有在无报警症状且年龄&lt;55岁时，PPI+随访才合理</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>E — Serologic testing for H. pylori<br />
E — 幽门螺旋杆菌血清学检测</td>
<td>Appropriate for uncomplicated dyspepsia in younger patients without alarm features; H. pylori serology detects prior exposure (not active infection) and has limited specificity<br />
适用于无报警症状的年轻患者非复杂性消化不良；H. pylori血清学检测既往暴露（非活动性感染），特异性有限</td>
<td>Even if H. pylori positive, the presence of alarm features still mandates EGD before initiating eradication therapy<br />
即使H. pylori阳性，存在报警症状仍要求在启动根除治疗前先行EGD</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

*The most seductive distractor is D (Pantoprazole + follow-up): it plausibly addresses NSAID-induced injury and the burning sensation, but collapses on three simultaneous alarm features — weight loss, melena, and iron deficiency anemia — that cannot be managed empirically.*

最具迷惑性的干扰项是D（泮托拉唑+随访）：它似乎合理地处理了NSAIDs相关损伤和烧灼感，但在同时存在的三项报警症状（体重下降、黑便、缺铁性贫血）面前站不住脚——这些症状不能经验性处理。

## 6. One-Sentence Summary & Memory Hook / 一句话总结 & 记忆钩

**When upper GI symptoms are accompanied by alarm features — unintentional weight loss, melena, or iron deficiency anemia — EGD is mandatory and empirical therapy is never appropriate.**

**当上消化道症状伴随报警症状——无意体重下降、黑便或缺铁性贫血——EGD是必须的，经验性治疗永远不合适。**

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 100%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><p><strong>Memory Hook — ALARM for Upper GI Red Flags / 记忆钩 — 上消化道红旗症状 "ALARM":</strong></p>
<p>• <strong>A</strong>nemia (iron deficiency) — chronic blood loss from mucosal tumor erosion / 贫血（缺铁性）——肿瘤侵蚀黏膜引起慢性失血<br />
• <strong>L</strong>oss of weight (unintentional) — cancer cachexia despite preserved appetite / 体重减轻（无意识）——尽管食欲正常的肿瘤恶病质<br />
• <strong>A</strong>ge &gt;55 + smoking — dominant risk factors for gastric adenocarcinoma / 年龄&gt;55岁+吸烟——胃腺癌的主要危险因素<br />
• <strong>R</strong>ectal melena / dark stools — digested upper GI blood = endoscopy now / 黑便——消化的上消化道出血=立即内镜检查<br />
• <strong>M</strong>alignancy suspected = EGD mandatory, not empirical PPI / 怀疑恶性肿瘤=必须行EGD，而非经验性PPI</p></th>

<tr>
<td>Alarm features mandating EGD<br />
需行EGD的报警症状</td>
