</tr>
<tr>
<td>Reactive thrombocytosis vs. essential thrombocythemia<br />
反应性血小板增多vs原发性血小板增多症</td>
<td>Reactive: platelet &lt;1,000,000, no splenomegaly, normal bone marrow, resolves with treatment of underlying cause; Essential: JAK2 mutation, splenomegaly, requires cytoreductive therapy<br />
反应性：血小板&lt;100万，无脾肿大，骨髓正常，治疗原发病后缓解；原发性：JAK2突变，脾肿大，需降细胞治疗</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>When empirical H. pylori test-and-treat is acceptable<br />
经验性H. pylori检测治疗可接受的情形</td>
<td>Age &lt;55 years AND no alarm features AND new-onset uninvestigated dyspepsia; stool antigen or urea breath test preferred over serology (serology cannot distinguish active from past infection)<br />
年龄&lt;55岁且无报警症状且新发未经检查的消化不良；粪便抗原或尿素呼气试验优于血清学（血清学不能区分活动性与既往感染）</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Gastric cancer staging workup<br />
胃癌分期检查</td>
<td>CT chest/abdomen/pelvis (distant metastases) → endoscopic ultrasound EUS (T and N stage) → diagnostic laparoscopy if no distant metastases to exclude peritoneal spread before surgery<br />
胸腹盆CT（远处转移）→超声内镜（T和N分期）→若无远处转移则诊断性腹腔镜排除腹膜播散再手术</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

## 8. Extensions / 延伸扩展

- **Linitis plastica:** Diffuse infiltrating gastric cancer producing a leather-bottle stomach; presents with early satiety and weight loss with minimal bleeding; EGD may show thickened, rigid folds rather than discrete mass; worst prognosis among gastric cancer subtypes\
  **皮革胃（Linitis plastica）:** 弥漫浸润性胃癌形成皮革瓶样胃；表现为早饱和体重下降，出血较少；EGD可见增厚、僵硬黏膜皱襞而非局限性肿块；胃癌亚型中预后最差

- **NSAID-induced injury vs. malignancy coexistence:** NSAIDs plausibly cause epigastric pain and melena, but thrombocytosis, malnourishment, and unintentional weight loss cannot be attributed to NSAIDs — when unexplained systemic features coexist with GI symptoms, malignancy must be excluded before attributing everything to medications\
  **NSAIDs损伤与恶性肿瘤并存的鉴别:** NSAIDs可合理解释上腹痛和黑便，但血小板增多、营养不良和无意体重下降不能归因于NSAIDs——当不明原因的全身特征与消化道症状并存时，必须在将一切归因于药物之前排除恶性肿瘤

- **Gastric MALT lymphoma:** H. pylori–driven mucosal-associated lymphoid tissue lymphoma; early-stage disease can achieve complete remission with H. pylori eradication alone; distinguished from adenocarcinoma by EGD biopsy immunohistochemistry\
  **胃MALT淋巴瘤:** H. pylori驱动的黏膜相关淋巴组织淋巴瘤；早期病变单纯根除H. pylori即可达到完全缓解；通过EGD活检免疫组化与腺癌鉴别

- **HER2 testing in gastric cancer:** Approximately 15–20% of gastric/gastroesophageal junction adenocarcinomas are HER2-positive (IHC 3+ or FISH amplified); addition of trastuzumab to first-line chemotherapy improves survival in HER2-positive metastatic disease (ToGA trial)\
  **胃癌HER2检测:** 约15–20%的胃/胃食管结合部腺癌HER2阳性（IHC 3+或FISH扩增）；在HER2阳性转移性疾病的一线化疗中加入曲妥珠单抗可改善生存（ToGA试验）

# Question 166 — Amyotrophic Lateral Sclerosis / 肌萎缩侧索硬化症

## Question Stem / 题干

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 100%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><p>A <strong>67-year-old man</strong> comes to the physician because of a <strong>6-month history of increasing difficulty walking</strong>. He has <strong>not had pain or numbness</strong>. He has no history of serious illness or recent infection. Examination of the lower extremities shows <strong>atrophy</strong>; <strong>muscle strength is 3/5 bilaterally</strong>. <strong>Deep tendon reflexes are increased</strong> in the lower extremities. <strong>Sensation is intact</strong>. Which of the following is the most likely diagnosis?</p>
<p><strong>Q: Most likely diagnosis?</strong></p>
<p>A) Amyotrophic lateral sclerosis<br />
B) Multiple sclerosis<br />
C) Myasthenia gravis<br />
D) Polymyositis<br />
E) Transverse myelitis</p>
<p><strong>Correct Answer: A</strong></p></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
</tbody>
</table>

## 1. Key Stem Clues / 题干关键词抓考点

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 50%" />
<col style="width: 50%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Key Stem Clue</strong><br />
<strong>关键词</strong></th>
<th><strong>Why It Matters</strong><br />
<strong>为什么重要</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>67-year-old man, progressive over 6 months<br />
67岁男性，进行性加重6个月</td>
<td>ALS typically begins in midlife to late adulthood; gradual progression is characteristic<br />
ALS通常起病于中年至老年，渐进性加重是其特征</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>No pain, no numbness<br />
无疼痛，无麻木</td>
<td>Sensory sparing is the hallmark of pure motor neuron disease; rules out demyelinating and compressive etiologies<br />
感觉保留是纯运动神经元病的标志，可排除脱髓鞘性和压迫性病因</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Lower extremity muscle atrophy<br />
下肢肌肉萎缩</td>
<td>Atrophy indicates lower motor neuron (LMN) degeneration of anterior horn cells<br />
萎缩提示下运动神经元（LMN）退变，即脊髓前角细胞受累</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Muscle strength 3/5 bilaterally<br />
双侧肌力3/5级</td>
<td>Significant bilateral weakness from LMN dysfunction; bilateral involvement is consistent with ALS<br />
来自LMN功能障碍的显著双侧无力，双侧受累符合ALS表现</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Deep tendon reflexes increased<br />
深腱反射亢进</td>
<td>Hyperreflexia is an upper motor neuron (UMN) sign — coexistence of UMN + LMN signs is the ALS hallmark<br />
腱反射亢进是上运动神经元（UMN）体征——UMN与LMN体征并存是ALS的诊断标志</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Sensation intact<br />
感觉完整保留</td>
<td>ALS spares sensory neurons; this distinguishes ALS from MS, transverse myelitis, and compressive myelopathy<br />
ALS不累及感觉神经元，可与MS、横贯性脊髓炎及压迫性脊髓病相鉴别</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

## 2. Mechanism / 机制理解

**Amyotrophic lateral sclerosis** involves simultaneous degeneration of **upper motor neurons** (corticospinal tract) and **lower motor neurons** (anterior horn cells), producing a uniquely mixed motor picture:

**肌萎缩侧索硬化症**同时累及**上运动神经元**（皮质脊髓束）和**下运动神经元**（脊髓前角细胞），产生独特的混合运动表现：

- UMN degeneration → hyperreflexia, spasticity, Babinski sign\
  UMN退变 → 腱反射亢进、痉挛、Babinski征阳性

- LMN degeneration → muscle atrophy, fasciculations, weakness, flaccidity\
  LMN退变 → 肌萎缩、肌束震颤、无力、肌张力降低

- Sensory neurons and sphincters are spared → intact sensation, no bowel/bladder dysfunction\
  感觉神经元和括约肌不受累 → 感觉完整，无大小便功能障碍

- Mechanism likely involves RNA processing dysfunction and glutamate excitotoxicity, leading to gliosis\
  发病机制可能涉及RNA加工障碍和谷氨酸兴奋性毒性，最终导致胶质增生

**Anatomic rule of thumb:** "Lateral" (corticospinal tract) accounts for UMN signs; "anterior" (anterior horn) accounts for LMN signs — the name ALS literally maps to the anatomy.

**解剖小窍门:** "侧索"（皮质脊髓束）对应UMN体征；"前角"（脊髓前角）对应LMN体征——ALS这个名字本身就是解剖的地图。

## 3. Correct Answer (A) — Amyotrophic Lateral Sclerosis / 正确答案 (A) — 肌萎缩侧索硬化症

**Amyotrophic lateral sclerosis (ALS)** is the only disease that simultaneously destroys UMN and LMN pathways while completely sparing sensory function:

**肌萎缩侧索硬化症（ALS）**是唯一同时破坏UMN和LMN通路而感觉功能完全保留的疾病：

- Coexisting hyperreflexia (UMN) + atrophy/weakness (LMN) = ALS until proven otherwise\
  腱反射亢进（UMN）+肌萎缩/无力（LMN）并存 = 排除其他病因前首先考虑ALS

- Typically asymmetric onset, though bilateral presentation occurs; onset usually in upper or lower limbs\
  典型起病不对称，但双侧受累亦可见；通常起病于上肢或下肢

- No sensory involvement, no pain, no bladder dysfunction — pure motor neuron disease\
  无感觉受累，无疼痛，无大小便障碍——纯运动神经元病

- Mean age of onset ~55–65 years; slightly more common in men\
  平均起病年龄约55~65岁，男性略多见

**Diagnosis:** Primarily clinical (UMN + LMN signs, El Escorial criteria); supported by EMG showing acute/chronic denervation; nerve conduction studies showing reduced CMAP; MRI to exclude structural causes

**诊断:** 主要依靠临床（UMN+LMN体征并存，El Escorial标准）；EMG示急/慢性失神经改变可支持诊断；神经传导示复合肌肉动作电位降低；MRI排除结构性病变

**Treatment:** Riluzole (glutamate antagonist, modestly improves survival ~3 months); edaravone (free radical scavenger); supportive care including NIV/BiPAP, PEG tube, speech therapy, PT/OT

**治疗:** 利鲁唑（谷氨酸拮抗剂，约延长生存期3个月）；依达拉奉（自由基清除剂）；支持治疗包括无创通气/BiPAP、经皮胃造瘘、言语治疗、物理及职业治疗

## 4. Options Elimination / 错误选项排除逻辑

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 33%" />
<col style="width: 33%" />
<col style="width: 33%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Option</strong><br />
<strong>选项</strong></th>
<th><strong>Why Wrong</strong><br />
<strong>为什么错</strong></th>
<th><strong>Key Discriminator</strong><br />
<strong>鉴别要点</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>A — Amyotrophic lateral sclerosis ✓<br />
A — 肌萎缩侧索硬化症 ✓</td>
<td>CORRECT — Mixed UMN (hyperreflexia) + LMN (atrophy, weakness) signs with intact sensation perfectly fits ALS<br />
正确——腱反射亢进（UMN）+肌萎缩/无力（LMN）并存且感觉保留，完美符合ALS</td>
<td>Both UMN and LMN signs + no sensory loss<br />
UMN与LMN体征并存+无感觉缺损</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>B — Multiple sclerosis<br />
B — 多发性硬化</td>
<td>Wrong — MS typically presents in younger white women (3rd–4th decade); always causes sensory deficits and often optic neuritis/bladder dysfunction; does not produce LMN atrophy<br />
错误——MS多见于年轻白人女性（30~40岁），总伴感觉缺损，常有视神经炎/膀胱功能障碍；不引起LMN性肌萎缩</td>
<td>MS: sensory loss + no LMN atrophy; ALS: sensory sparing + prominent atrophy<br />
MS：有感觉缺损+无LMN萎缩；ALS：感觉保留+显著萎缩</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>C — Myasthenia gravis<br />
C — 重症肌无力</td>
<td>Wrong — MG causes fatigable weakness (worse with repetition), primarily ocular and bulbar muscles; reflexes normal or reduced; no atrophy in early disease<br />
错误——MG表现为疲劳性无力（重复运动后加重），主要累及眼肌和球部肌肉；腱反射正常或减低；早期无萎缩</td>
<td>MG: fatigable + normal reflexes; ALS: progressive non-fatigable + hyperreflexia<br />
MG：疲劳性无力+腱反射正常；ALS：进行性非疲劳性无力+腱反射亢进</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>D — Polymyositis<br />
D — 多发性肌炎</td>
<td>Wrong — Polymyositis causes symmetric proximal muscle weakness with normal reflexes, elevated CK, and no hyperreflexia; autoimmune inflammatory myopathy<br />
错误——多发性肌炎表现为对称性近端肌无力，腱反射正常，CK升高，无腱反射亢进；属于自身免疫性炎性肌病</td>
<td>Myopathy: normal reflexes + elevated CK; ALS: hyperreflexia + normal CK<br />
肌病：腱反射正常+CK升高；ALS：腱反射亢进+CK正常</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>E — Transverse myelitis<br />
E — 横贯性脊髓炎</td>
<td>Wrong — Transverse myelitis presents acutely/subacutely with BOTH motor AND sensory deficits (with a sensory level) and often bladder/bowel dysfunction; this patient has intact sensation<br />
错误——横贯性脊髓炎急性/亚急性起病，同时具有运动和感觉缺损（存在感觉平面），常伴大小便障碍；本患者感觉完整</td>
<td>Transverse myelitis: sensory level + bladder dysfunction; ALS: sensory sparing<br />
横贯性脊髓炎：感觉平面+大小便障碍；ALS：感觉保留</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

*The most tempting distractor is Multiple sclerosis (B), which also causes UMN signs with hyperreflexia — but MS never produces LMN atrophy and always causes sensory deficits, whereas ALS is defined by pure motor involvement with both UMN and LMN findings coexisting.*

多发性硬化（B）是最容易迷惑人的干扰项，因为它也可引起腱反射亢进等UMN体征——但MS从不引起LMN性肌萎缩，且总伴感觉缺损；而ALS是纯运动疾病，以UMN和LMN体征并存为定义。

## 5. High-Yield Summary Table — Upper vs. Lower Motor Neuron Signs / 上运动神经元体征与下运动神经元体征对比

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 33%" />
<col style="width: 33%" />
<col style="width: 33%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Feature</strong><br />
<strong>特征</strong></th>
<th><strong>Upper Motor Neuron (UMN)</strong><br />
<strong>上运动神经元（UMN）</strong></th>
<th><strong>Lower Motor Neuron (LMN)</strong><br />
<strong>下运动神经元（LMN）</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>Lesion location<br />
病变部位</td>
<td>Motor cortex → corticospinal tract<br />
运动皮层→皮质脊髓束</td>
<td>Anterior horn cells → peripheral nerve<br />
脊髓前角细胞→周围神经</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Muscle tone<br />
肌张力</td>
<td>Increased (spasticity)<br />
增高（痉挛性）</td>
<td>Decreased (flaccidity)<br />
降低（弛缓性）</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Deep tendon reflexes<br />
深腱反射</td>
<td>Hyperreflexia<br />
亢进</td>
<td>Hyporeflexia or absent<br />
减弱或消失</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Muscle atrophy<br />
肌萎缩</td>
<td>Late, mild (disuse only)<br />
晚期轻度（废用性）</td>
<td>Early and prominent<br />
早期且显著</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Fasciculations<br />
肌束震颤</td>
<td>Absent<br />
无</td>
<td>Present<br />
有</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Babinski sign<br />
Babinski征</td>
<td>Positive (upgoing toe)<br />
阳性（趾背伸）</td>
<td>Absent<br />
阴性</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Pure disease example<br />
纯UMN/LMN疾病举例</td>
<td>Stroke, primary lateral sclerosis<br />
卒中、原发性侧索硬化</td>
<td>Polio, GBS, progressive muscular atrophy<br />
脊髓灰质炎、GBS、进行性肌萎缩</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>ALS finding<br />
ALS中的表现</td>
<td>Hyperreflexia despite muscle weakness<br />
肌无力的同时腱反射亢进</td>
<td>Atrophy + fasciculations + weakness<br />
萎缩+肌束震颤+无力</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

## 6. One-Sentence Summary & Memory Hook / 一句话总结 & 记忆钩

**ALS is the only disease that simultaneously produces hyperreflexia (UMN) and muscle atrophy (LMN) with complete sensory sparing — this paradoxical combination is pathognomonic.**

**ALS是唯一同时引起腱反射亢进（UMN）和肌萎缩（LMN）且感觉完全保留的疾病——这种矛盾组合是其病理特征性表现。**

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 100%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><p><strong>Memory Hook — "ALS = Both Ends of the Motor Highway" / 记忆钩 — "ALS = 运动通路两端同时崩溃":</strong></p>
<p>• <strong>A</strong>trophy — LMN sign; anterior horn cells dying, muscles waste away / 萎缩——LMN体征；前角细胞凋亡，肌肉消耗<br />
• <strong>L</strong>ively reflexes — UMN sign; hyperreflexia despite profound weakness is the paradox that defines ALS / 腱反射活跃——UMN体征；严重无力却腱反射亢进，是ALS的矛盾所在<br />
• <strong>S</strong>ensation spared — the one pathway ALS never touches; if sensory loss is present, reconsider the diagnosis / 感觉保留——ALS从不累及的唯一通路；若有感觉缺损则需重新考虑诊断</p></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
</tbody>
</table>

## 7. High-Yield Topic Knowledge — Amyotrophic Lateral Sclerosis / 高频知识表 — 肌萎缩侧索硬化症

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 50%" />
<col style="width: 50%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Topic</strong><br />
<strong>考点</strong></th>
<th><strong>Key Points</strong><br />
<strong>要点</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>Pathophysiology<br />
病理生理</td>
<td>Simultaneous degeneration of UMN (lateral corticospinal tract) and LMN (anterior horn cells); mechanism involves RNA processing errors (TDP-43) and glutamate excitotoxicity; results in gliosis<br />
UMN（侧皮质脊髓束）和LMN（前角细胞）同时退变；机制涉及RNA加工异常（TDP-43）和谷氨酸兴奋性毒性；导致胶质增生</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Clinical presentation<br />
临床表现</td>
<td>Progressive motor weakness (often asymmetric onset); atrophy + fasciculations (LMN); hyperreflexia + spasticity (UMN); bulbar involvement (dysarthria, dysphagia) in ~25%; sensation and early cognition intact<br />
进行性运动无力（常不对称起病）；萎缩+肌束震颤（LMN）；腱反射亢进+痉挛（UMN）；约25%有球部受累（构音障碍、吞咽困难）；感觉和早期认知保留</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Diagnosis<br />
诊断</td>
<td>Clinical (El Escorial criteria: UMN + LMN signs in ≥2 regions); EMG: acute/chronic denervation + reinnervation; nerve conduction: reduced CMAP; MRI brain/spine to exclude structural lesions<br />
临床诊断（El Escorial标准：≥2个区域同时有UMN+LMN体征）；EMG：急/慢性失神经+再支配；神经传导：复合肌肉动作电位降低；脑/脊髓MRI排除结构性病变</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Treatment<br />
治疗</td>
<td>Riluzole (glutamate antagonist; first approved drug; extends survival ~3 months); edaravone (free radical scavenger, IV); supportive: NIV/BiPAP, PEG tube, speech/PT/OT<br />
利鲁唑（谷氨酸拮抗剂；首个获批药物；约延长生存期3个月）；依达拉奉（自由基清除剂，静脉注射）；支持治疗：无创通气/BiPAP、经皮胃造瘘、言语/物理/职业治疗</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Prognosis<br />
预后</td>
<td>Median survival 2–5 years from symptom onset; bulbar onset has worse prognosis; death most commonly from respiratory failure (diaphragm weakness)<br />
自症状出现后中位生存期2~5年；球部起病型预后更差；死亡最常见原因为呼吸衰竭（膈肌无力）</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Genetics<br />
遗传学</td>
<td>~10% familial ALS; most common mutations: SOD1, C9orf72 (also linked to FTD), FUS, TARDBP (TDP-43 protein)<br />
约10%为家族性ALS；最常见突变：SOD1、C9orf72（同时与额颞叶痴呆相关）、FUS、TARDBP（TDP-43蛋白）</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>ALS vs. Primary Lateral Sclerosis<br />
ALS vs. 原发性侧索硬化</td>
<td>Primary lateral sclerosis = pure UMN degeneration only, no LMN signs, much slower progression (decades); ALS has both UMN + LMN and is fatal within years<br />
原发性侧索硬化 = 纯UMN退变，无LMN体征，进展极缓慢（数十年）；ALS同时具备UMN+LMN，数年内致死</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

## 8. Extensions / 延伸扩展

- **Differential of mixed UMN+LMN signs:** ALS is the classic; also consider cervical spondylotic myelopathy (but has neck pain + sensory loss at level) and subacute combined degeneration from B12 deficiency (but has posterior column sensory loss)\
  **混合UMN+LMN体征的鉴别诊断:** ALS是经典病因；也需考虑颈椎病性脊髓病（但有颈痛+节段性感觉缺损）和B12缺乏性亚急性联合变性（但有后柱感觉缺损）

- **Bulbar ALS variant:** Some patients present first with dysarthria and dysphagia (bulbar onset ALS) — carries worse prognosis than limb-onset; eventually progresses to limb weakness in all patients\
  **球部起病型ALS变式:** 部分患者以构音障碍和吞咽困难为首发症状（球部起病型）——预后较肢体起病型更差；最终所有患者均进展至肢体无力

- **Key complication — respiratory failure:** Diaphragm is a LMN-innervated muscle; FVC monitoring every 3–6 months is critical; NIV introduction when FVC \< 50% predicted\
  **关键并发症——呼吸衰竭:** 膈肌由LMN支配，同样受累；每3~6个月监测用力肺活量（FVC）至关重要；当FVC \< 50%预测值时引入无创通气

- **Fasciculations rule of thumb:** Isolated fasciculations without weakness or atrophy = benign fasciculation syndrome (very common, not ALS); in ALS, fasciculations always accompany weakness and EMG-confirmed denervation\
  **肌束震颤的临床规律:** 孤立性肌束震颤（不伴无力或萎缩）= 良性肌束震颤综合征（极为常见，非ALS）；ALS中肌束震颤总伴随无力和EMG确认的失神经改变

# Question 167 — Mittelschmerz (Mid-Cycle Ovulatory Pain) / 排卵痛（月经周期中期疼痛）

## Question Stem / 题干

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 100%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><p><strong>A 14-year-old girl</strong> is brought to the physician because of an <strong>18-hour history of persistent right-sided lower abdominal pain</strong>. She has <strong>not had fever, vomiting, or diarrhea</strong>. She has no history of serious illness or operative procedures. Menarche was at the age of 12 years, and <strong>menses occur at regular 28-day intervals</strong>. Her <strong>last menstrual period was 2 weeks ago</strong>. She is <strong>not sexually active</strong>. Her <strong>temperature is 37°C (98.6°F)</strong>, pulse is 72/min, respirations are 14/min, and blood pressure is 120/80 mm Hg. Abdominal examination shows mild tenderness with guarding over the right lower quadrant. There is no distention, and bowel sounds are normal. The remainder of the examination shows no abnormalities. Her hemoglobin concentration is 13.9 g/dL, and <strong>leukocyte count is 8000/mm³</strong> with a normal differential. Urinalysis shows no abnormalities. <strong>Abdominal ultrasonography shows a small amount of fluid in the pelvis</strong>. Which of the following is the most likely diagnosis?</p>
<p><strong>Q: Which of the following is the most likely diagnosis?</strong></p>
<p>A) Appendicitis<br />
B) Ectopic pregnancy<br />
C) Mittelschmerz<br />
D) Ovarian torsion<br />
E) Pelvic inflammatory disease</p>
<p><strong>Correct Answer: C</strong></p></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
</tbody>
</table>

## 1. Key Stem Clues / 题干关键词抓考点

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 50%" />
<col style="width: 50%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Key Stem Clue</strong><br />
<strong>关键词</strong></th>
<th><strong>Why It Matters</strong><br />
<strong>为什么重要</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>Last menstrual period 2 weeks ago<br />
末次月经在2周前</td>
<td>Indicates mid-cycle timing (day ~14 of a 28-day cycle) — the classic Mittelschmerz window at ovulation<br />
提示处于月经周期中期（28天周期约第14天）——排卵痛的典型时间窗</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Regular 28-day menstrual cycles<br />
规律的28天月经周期</td>
<td>Predictable ovulation at day 14; mid-cycle pain correlates exactly with follicular rupture<br />
排卵时间可预测在第14天；周期中期疼痛与卵泡破裂时间精确吻合</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Not sexually active<br />
无性生活史</td>
<td>Immediately eliminates ectopic pregnancy and sexually transmitted PID from the differential<br />
立即排除异位妊娠和性传播性盆腔炎</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Leukocyte count 8000/mm³ (normal)<br />
白细胞计数8000/mm³（正常）</td>
<td>No leukocytosis argues against appendicitis and any infectious etiology<br />
无白细胞增多，不支持阑尾炎及任何感染性病因</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Temperature 37°C (afebrile)<br />
体温37°C（无发热）</td>
<td>Fever absent argues against appendicitis, PID, and ovarian torsion with ischemic necrosis<br />
无发热不支持阑尾炎、盆腔炎及缺血坏死性卵巢扭转</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Small amount of fluid in the pelvis on ultrasound<br />
超声显示盆腔少量积液</td>
<td>Hallmark of follicular rupture — free follicular fluid in the cul-de-sac irritates the peritoneum<br />
卵泡破裂的标志性表现——直肠子宫陷凹内游离卵泡液刺激腹膜</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Right-sided lower abdominal pain, mild<br />
右下腹轻度疼痛</td>
<td>Corresponds to right ovarian ovulation; mild intensity distinguishes from appendicitis and torsion<br />
对应右侧卵巢排卵；轻度疼痛可与阑尾炎和卵巢扭转鉴别</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

## 2. Mechanism / 机制理解

**Mittelschmerz** (German: "middle pain") results from **peritoneal irritation** caused by the enlarging **dominant follicle** or the release of **follicular fluid** upon ovulation:

**排卵痛**（德语"中期疼痛"）由**腹膜刺激**引起，来源于增大的**优势卵泡**或排卵时**卵泡液**的释放：

- The LH surge around day 14 triggers dominant follicle rupture and egg release\
  约第14天LH激增触发优势卵泡破裂并排出卵子

- Released follicular fluid accumulates in the cul-de-sac and irritates the parietal peritoneum, causing unilateral pain\
  释放的卵泡液积聚于直肠子宫陷凹，刺激壁层腹膜，引起单侧疼痛

- Pain is self-limited (hours to 2 days), localizes to the side of ovulation, and requires no treatment beyond NSAIDs\
  疼痛自限性（持续数小时至2天），局限于排卵侧，仅需NSAIDs对症处理

**Anatomic rule of thumb:** Either ovary can ovulate in any given cycle; alternation is not guaranteed, so Mittelschmerz may recur on the same side in consecutive cycles without implying pathology.

**解剖小窍门:** 任一侧卵巢均可在任意周期排卵；左右交替并非必然，因此排卵痛可连续数个周期在同侧发生，并不提示病理状态。

## 3. Correct Answer (C) — Mittelschmerz / 正确答案 (C) — 排卵痛

**Mittelschmerz** is benign mid-cycle pelvic pain caused by peritoneal irritation at ovulation, occurring in females with predictable regular menstrual cycles:

**排卵痛** 是排卵时腹膜受刺激引起的良性周期中期盆腔疼痛，发生于月经周期规律的女性：

- Presents with mild unilateral lower abdominal or pelvic pain at approximately day 14 of a regular 28-day cycle\
  表现为规律28天周期约第14天出现的轻度单侧下腹部或盆腔疼痛

- All vital signs and laboratory values (WBC, hemoglobin, urinalysis) are within normal limits — no systemic inflammation\
  所有生命体征和实验室检查（白细胞、血红蛋白、尿常规）均在正常范围——无全身性炎症

- Ultrasound shows only small amount of free pelvic fluid from ruptured follicle; no appendiceal dilation, no absent ovarian Doppler flow\
  超声仅显示来自破裂卵泡的少量盆腔游离积液；无阑尾扩张，无卵巢多普勒血流消失

**Diagnosis:** Clinical diagnosis based on mid-cycle timing in a regular-cycle patient, unilateral mild pain, absence of fever and leukocytosis; ultrasound demonstrating only free pelvic fluid (no appendiceal or ovarian pathology) confirms.

**诊断:** 临床诊断依据为规律月经患者的周期中期时机、单侧轻度疼痛、无发热及白细胞增多；超声仅显示盆腔游离积液（无阑尾或卵巢病变）可确认诊断。

**Treatment:** Reassurance and NSAIDs for pain relief; no antibiotics, no surgery, no further workup required in straightforward presentations.

**治疗:** 安抚患者并给予NSAIDs缓解疼痛；典型表现无需抗生素、手术或进一步检查。

## 4. Options Elimination / 错误选项排除逻辑

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 33%" />
<col style="width: 33%" />
<col style="width: 33%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Option</strong><br />
<strong>选项</strong></th>
<th><strong>Why Wrong</strong><br />
<strong>为什么错</strong></th>
<th><strong>Key Discriminator</strong><br />
<strong>鉴别要点</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>A — Appendicitis<br />
A — 阑尾炎</td>
<td>Appendicitis requires fever, leukocytosis, anorexia/nausea, and appendiceal pathology on imaging — none are present here<br />
阑尾炎需有发热、白细胞增多、厌食/恶心及影像学阑尾病变——本例均无</td>
<td>WBC 8000 (normal), afebrile, no nausea; US shows only free fluid with no appendiceal abnormality<br />
白细胞8000（正常）、无发热、无恶心；超声仅见游离积液，无阑尾异常</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>B — Ectopic pregnancy<br />
B — 异位妊娠</td>
<td>Requires sexual activity and a positive β-hCG; this patient explicitly is not sexually active<br />
需有性生活史且β-hCG阳性；患者明确无性生活</td>
<td>Sexual inactivity makes ectopic pregnancy physiologically impossible<br />
无性生活使异位妊娠在生理上不可能发生</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>C — Mittelschmerz ✓<br />
C — 排卵痛 ✓</td>
<td>CORRECT — Mid-cycle LMP (2 weeks ago), regular 28-day cycles, no fever, normal WBC, free pelvic fluid on US all converge on ovulatory pain<br />
正确——周期中期末次月经（2周前）、规律28天周期、无发热、白细胞正常、超声盆腔积液，均指向排卵痛</td>
<td>All four pillars align: timing + normal vitals + normal labs + small free fluid only on US<br />
四要素完全吻合：时机+生命体征正常+实验室正常+超声仅见少量游离积液</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>D — Ovarian torsion<br />
D — 卵巢扭转</td>
<td>Torsion presents with sudden severe pain, prominent nausea/vomiting, and absent ovarian blood flow on Doppler — this patient has only mild pain and normal US aside from free fluid<br />
卵巢扭转表现为突发剧烈疼痛、明显恶心/呕吐及多普勒血流消失——本例仅有轻度疼痛，超声除游离积液外均正常</td>
<td>Pain severity (mild vs. severe) and presence of ovarian Doppler flow are the critical discriminators<br />
疼痛严重程度（轻度vs.剧烈）和卵巢多普勒血流存在是关键鉴别点</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>E — Pelvic inflammatory disease<br />
E — 盆腔炎</td>
<td>PID requires sexual activity for STI transmission (Chlamydia/Gonorrhea); also presents with cervical motion tenderness, purulent discharge, and fever<br />
盆腔炎需有性生活才能传播性病（衣原体/淋球菌）；还需有宫颈举痛、脓性分泌物和发热</td>
<td>Not sexually active; no fever, no discharge, no cervical motion tenderness<br />
无性生活；无发热、无分泌物、无宫颈举痛</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

*The most tempting distractor is Appendicitis (A): both cause RLQ pain with guarding, but the mid-cycle LMP timing, normal WBC, afebrile state, and ultrasound showing only free pelvic fluid (no appendiceal pathology) lock in Mittelschmerz.*

阑尾炎（A）是最具迷惑性的干扰项：两者均可引起右下腹痛伴腹肌紧张，但末次月经2周前的周期中期时机、白细胞正常、无发热，以及超声仅显示盆腔游离积液（无阑尾病变）可确诊排卵痛。

## 6. One-Sentence Summary & Memory Hook / 一句话总结 & 记忆钩

**Mittelschmerz is benign mid-cycle unilateral pelvic pain from follicular rupture at ovulation — characterized by normal vitals, normal labs, and only small free fluid on ultrasound in a patient with regular menstrual cycles.**

**排卵痛是排卵时卵泡破裂引起的良性周期中期单侧盆腔疼痛——表现为月经规律患者生命体征正常、实验室检查正常、超声仅见少量盆腔游离积液。**

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 100%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><p><strong>Memory Hook — "MITT" Rule for Mittelschmerz / 记忆钩 — 排卵痛"MITT"四要点:</strong></p>
<p>• <strong>M</strong>id-cycle timing — LMP exactly 2 weeks ago in a regular 28-day cycle = day 14 = ovulation / 周期中期时机——规律28天周期中末次月经恰好2周前=第14天=排卵<br />
• <strong>I</strong>psilateral mild pain — unilateral dull pain on the side of the ovulating ovary, not severe / 同侧轻度疼痛——疼痛位于排卵侧卵巢，单侧钝痛，非剧烈疼痛<br />
• <strong>T</strong>emperature and labs normal — afebrile, WBC normal, urinalysis normal, no β-hCG needed if not sexually active / 体温及实验室正常——无发热、白细胞正常、尿常规正常、无性生活者无需查β-hCG<br />
• <strong>T</strong>ransient pelvic fluid on US — small free cul-de-sac fluid from ruptured follicle; no appendiceal or ovarian pathology / 超声一过性盆腔积液——来自破裂卵泡的少量直肠子宫陷凹游离积液；无阑尾或卵巢病变</p></th>
</tr>
</thead>

</tbody>
</table>

## 7. High-Yield Topic Knowledge — Mittelschmerz & Gynecologic Causes of Mid-Cycle Pelvic Pain / 高频知识表 — 排卵痛与月经周期中期盆腔疼痛的妇科病因

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 50%" />

<tr>
<th><strong>Topic</strong><br />
<strong>考点</strong></th>
<th><strong>Key Points</strong><br />

</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>Definition and etymology<br />
定义与词源</td>
<td>Mittelschmerz = German "middle pain"; benign unilateral pelvic pain at ovulation (~day 14 of a 28-day cycle) from peritoneal irritation by follicular fluid<br />
Mittelschmerz=德语"中期疼痛"；排卵时（28天周期约第14天）卵泡液刺激腹膜引起的良性单侧盆腔疼痛</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Mechanism of pain<br />
疼痛机制</td>
<td>LH surge → dominant follicle rupture → follicular fluid released into peritoneal cavity → irritates parietal peritoneum → crampy unilateral pain<br />
LH激增→优势卵泡破裂→卵泡液释放入腹腔→刺激壁层腹膜→单侧痉挛样疼痛</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Hallmark lab and imaging findings<br />
标志性实验室及影像学表现</td>
<td>All labs normal (WBC, hemoglobin, urinalysis, β-hCG negative); ultrasound shows only small free pelvic fluid — no appendiceal, ovarian, or uterine pathology<br />
所有实验室检查正常（白细胞、血红蛋白、尿常规、β-hCG阴性）；超声仅见少量盆腔游离积液——无阑尾、卵巢或子宫病变</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Key discriminators from appendicitis<br />
与阑尾炎的关键鉴别</td>
<td>Appendicitis: fever + leukocytosis + nausea + appendiceal pathology on US; Mittelschmerz: none of these, plus mid-cycle timing<br />
阑尾炎：发热+白细胞增多+恶心+超声阑尾病变；排卵痛：以上均无，且有周期中期时机</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Key discriminators from ovarian torsion<br />
与卵巢扭转的关键鉴别</td>
<td>Torsion: sudden severe pain + nausea/vomiting + absent ovarian Doppler; Mittelschmerz: mild pain + present Doppler + free fluid only<br />
卵巢扭转：突发剧烈疼痛+恶心/呕吐+卵巢多普勒血流消失；排卵痛：轻度疼痛+血流存在+仅有游离积液</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Role of sexual history in diagnosis<br />
性生活史在诊断中的作用</td>
<td>Sexual inactivity immediately eliminates ectopic pregnancy (requires fertilization) and STI-related PID (requires exposure); always ask<br />
无性生活立即排除异位妊娠（需受精）和性传播性盆腔炎（需暴露史）；始终需询问</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Management<br />
处理原则</td>
<td>Reassurance + NSAIDs for symptom relief; no antibiotics, no surgical referral, no further imaging in classic presentations; pain resolves within 24–48 hours<br />
安慰患者+NSAIDs缓解症状；典型表现无需抗生素、外科转诊或进一步影像学检查；疼痛于24–48小时内消退</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Recurrence pattern<br />
复发规律</td>
<td>May occur monthly; side of pain can alternate or recur on the same side; recurrence does not indicate pathology and requires no further workup<br />
可每月复发；疼痛侧可交替或反复在同侧；复发不提示病理状态，无需进一步检查</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

## 8. Extensions / 延伸扩展

- **Differential of RLQ pain in adolescent females:** Mittelschmerz (mid-cycle, normal labs), appendicitis (fever + leukocytosis + nausea), ovarian torsion (severe pain + absent Doppler), ruptured ovarian cyst (larger fluid, more pain, may have hemodynamic instability)\
  **青少年女性右下腹痛鉴别:** 排卵痛（周期中期、实验室正常）、阑尾炎（发热+白细胞增多+恶心）、卵巢扭转（剧烈疼痛+多普勒血流消失）、卵巢囊肿破裂（积液更多、疼痛更重、可能有血流动力学不稳定）

- **Variant — Ruptured hemorrhagic ovarian cyst:** Larger rupture with more significant bleeding produces greater free fluid, more severe pain, and possible drop in hemoglobin; management may require close monitoring or intervention\
  **题目变式——出血性卵巢囊肿破裂:** 较大破裂伴更显著出血可产生更多游离积液、更剧烈疼痛，血红蛋白可能下降；处理可能需要密切监测或干预

- **Key complication to avoid:** Misdiagnosing Mittelschmerz as appendicitis and proceeding to unnecessary surgery; the triad of mid-cycle timing + normal WBC + afebrile state + US showing only free fluid should prevent this error\
  **需避免的关键失误:** 将排卵痛误诊为阑尾炎而实施不必要的手术；周期中期时机+白细胞正常+无发热+超声仅见游离积液的四联征应能防止此类错误

- **Risk factor context:** Mittelschmerz is more noticeable in patients with thin body habitus or heightened visceral sensitivity; OCPs suppress ovulation and thus eliminate Mittelschmerz in patients who find it recurrently bothersome\
  **风险因素背景:** 排卵痛在体型消瘦或内脏敏感性增高的患者中更为明显；口服避孕药抑制排卵，从而消除反复困扰患者的排卵痛

# Question 168 — Prosthetic Socket Pressure Injury / 假肢接受腔压力性损伤

## Question Stem / 题干

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 100%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><p>A <strong>62-year-old man</strong>, who underwent <strong>right below-the-knee amputation 36 years ago</strong>, comes to the emergency department because of a <strong>1-month history of an ulcer on the end of the residual limb</strong>. His amputation was the result of injuries he sustained while serving in the military. He says his <strong>prosthetic socket has "felt loose and has been rubbing recently."</strong> During the past 6 months, he has had progressive difficulty walking because of sharp pain that radiates up his leg. The <strong>pain has been occurring earlier during his walks; it slowly improves with rest</strong>. He previously walked 1 mile daily for exercise and could walk several miles without stopping. He has not had vomiting, fever, chills, or malaise. He has <strong>type 2 diabetes mellitus</strong> treated with diet. One month ago, his <strong>hemoglobin A1c was 6%</strong>. Vital signs are within normal limits. Examination of the right lower extremity shows <strong>mild erythema</strong> and a <strong>1 × 1-cm ulcer, with a depth of 3 mm</strong>, over the anteromedial aspect of the limb. There is <strong>viable soft tissue, and margins are clear</strong>. The limb is warm. The <strong>popliteal pulse is 1+</strong>. In addition to a recommendation for non-weight bearing and avoidance of direct pressure to the site, which of the following is the most appropriate next step in management?</p>
<p><strong>Q: Most appropriate next step in management?</strong></p>
<p>A) MRI of the right lower extremity<br />
B) Recommendation for refitting of the prosthetic socket<br />
C) Surgical revision of the amputation site<br />
D) Wound culture and antibiotic therapy<br />
E) X-ray of the right lower extremity</p>
<p><strong>Correct Answer: B</strong></p></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
</tbody>
</table>

## 1. Key Stem Clues / 题干关键词抓考点

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 50%" />
<col style="width: 50%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Key Stem Clue</strong><br />
<strong>关键词</strong></th>
<th><strong>Why It Matters</strong><br />
<strong>为什么重要</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>Prosthetic socket "felt loose and has been rubbing recently"<br />
假肢接受腔"近期感觉松动并有摩擦"</td>
<td>Direct mechanical cause of the ulcer — identifies the exact intervention needed<br />
溃疡的直接机械原因——明确了所需干预方向</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>1-month ulcer, anteromedial aspect of residual limb<br />
残肢前内侧1个月溃疡史</td>
<td>Location consistent with socket friction point; timeline aligns with socket loosening<br />
位置与接受腔摩擦点吻合；时间线与接受腔松动一致</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>No fever, chills, malaise; viable tissue, clear margins<br />
无发热、寒战、全身不适；软组织存活，边缘清晰</td>
<td>No signs of infection — antibiotics and wound culture NOT indicated<br />
无感染征象——抗生素和创面培养均无指征</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Pain occurring earlier in walks, improves with rest<br />
步行时疼痛出现越来越早，休息后缓解</td>
<td>Classic intermittent claudication — suggests underlying peripheral arterial disease<br />
典型间歇性跛行——提示潜在外周动脉疾病</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Popliteal pulse 1+ (diminished)<br />
腘动脉搏动1+（减弱）</td>
<td>Confirms peripheral arterial disease; warm limb rules out acute stump ischemia<br />
证实外周动脉疾病；肢体温暖排除残肢急性缺血</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>HbA1c 6%, diet-controlled diabetes<br />
HbA1c 6%，饮食控制的2型糖尿病</td>
<td>Well-controlled diabetes — less likely to have severe infection or neuropathic complications<br />
血糖控制良好——严重感染或神经病变并发症可能性低</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

## 2. Mechanism / 机制理解

**Pressure injury** develops when sustained **mechanical forces** (shear, friction, direct pressure) exceed local capillary closing pressure, causing **tissue ischemia and skin breakdown**:

**压力性损伤**由持续的**机械力**（剪切力、摩擦力、直接压力）超过局部毛细血管闭合压，导致**组织缺血和皮肤破溃**：

- An ill-fitting prosthetic socket generates repetitive shear and friction against residual limb skin with every step\
  不合适的假肢接受腔每次步行都对残肢皮肤产生反复的剪切和摩擦

- Moisture accumulation inside the socket (sweat) increases skin maceration and fragility\
  接受腔内湿气积聚（汗液）增加皮肤浸渍和脆弱性

- Weight change, muscle atrophy, or material wear → socket loosens → increased pistoning motion → more friction\
  体重变化、肌肉萎缩或接受腔磨损 → 接受腔松动 → 活塞运动增加 → 摩擦加剧

**Anatomic rule of thumb:** The anteromedial distal tibia is a high-risk zone because bone is close to the surface with minimal subcutaneous padding — identical to heel ulcers in bedridden patients.

**解剖小窍门:** 胫骨前内侧远端是高风险区域，因为骨骼接近皮肤表面，皮下脂肪衬垫极少——与卧床患者足跟溃疡的原理相同。

## 3. Correct Answer (B) — Prosthetic Socket Refitting / 正确答案 (B) — 假肢接受腔重新适配

**Prosthetic socket refitting** is the definitive intervention because it eliminates the root mechanical cause of this pressure ulcer:

**假肢接受腔重新适配**是决定性干预，因为它消除了此压力性溃疡的根本机械原因：

- Treating the wound without fixing the socket = guaranteed recurrence\
  不纠正接受腔而只处理创面 = 必然复发

- Causes of socket loosening: weight loss, disuse muscle atrophy, limb volume fluctuations, material wear over time\
  接受腔松动的原因：体重减轻、废用性肌肉萎缩、肢体体积波动、材料随时间磨损

- Conservative management triad: non-weight bearing + pressure avoidance + socket refit\
  保守治疗三联：非负重 + 避免压迫 + 接受腔重新适配

**Diagnosis:** Stage 2 pressure injury (partial-thickness skin loss, viable base, clear margins) secondary to ill-fitting prosthetic socket, without signs of soft tissue infection.

**诊断:** 继发于不合适假肢接受腔的2期压力性损伤（部分厚度皮肤缺失，基底存活，边缘清晰），无软组织感染征象。

**Treatment:** Non-weight bearing, local wound care, referral to certified prosthetist for socket refitting. Close follow-up to monitor wound healing and watch for developing infection.

**治疗:** 非负重、局部伤口护理、转诊认证假肢技师进行接受腔重新适配。密切随访监测创面愈合及感染迹象。

## 4. Options Elimination / 错误选项排除逻辑

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 33%" />
<col style="width: 33%" />
<col style="width: 33%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Option</strong><br />
<strong>选项</strong></th>
<th><strong>Why Wrong</strong><br />
<strong>为什么错</strong></th>
<th><strong>Key Discriminator</strong><br />
<strong>鉴别要点</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>A — MRI of the right lower extremity<br />
A — 右下肢MRI</td>
<td>Not indicated without high-risk features (bone exposure, sinus tract, systemic infection signs, failed healing)<br />
无高危特征时不需要（无骨骼暴露、瘘管、全身感染征象或治疗失败）</td>
<td>MRI is reserved for suspected osteomyelitis or deep abscess — not routine for shallow pressure ulcer<br />
MRI用于怀疑骨髓炎或深部脓肿——不用于浅表压力性溃疡的常规评估</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>B — Recommendation for refitting of the prosthetic socket ✓<br />
B — 建议重新适配假肢接受腔 ✓</td>
<td>CORRECT — eliminates the root mechanical cause; patient explicitly reports socket looseness and rubbing<br />
正确——消除根本机械原因；患者明确报告接受腔松动及摩擦</td>
<td>Identifying the mechanical culprit is sufficient to direct management without further testing<br />
识别机械原因即可指导治疗，无需进一步检查</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>C — Surgical revision of the amputation site<br />
C — 手术修整截肢部位</td>
<td>Invasive; not warranted without infection, extensive necrosis, or failure of conservative management<br />
侵入性操作；无感染、大范围坏死或保守治疗失败则无指征</td>
<td>3 mm superficial ulcer with viable tissue and clear margins does not meet surgical threshold<br />
3mm浅表溃疡伴存活组织和清晰边缘未达到手术指征</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>D — Wound culture and antibiotic therapy<br />
D — 创面培养和抗生素治疗</td>
<td>No clinical signs of infection: afebrile, no malaise, no purulent discharge, no expanding erythema<br />
无临床感染征象：无发热、无全身不适、无脓性分泌物、无扩展性红斑</td>
<td>Antibiotics are indicated for soft tissue infection, not for uncomplicated pressure injury<br />
抗生素适用于软组织感染，而非无并发症的压力性损伤</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>E — X-ray of the right lower extremity<br />
E — 右下肢X线</td>
<td>Neither sensitive nor specific for soft tissue infection or early osteomyelitis<br />
对软组织感染或早期骨髓炎既不敏感也不特异</td>
<td>X-ray may detect gas (necrotizing infection) or late bony destruction, but MRI is preferred if imaging truly needed<br />
X线可检测到气体（坏死性感染）或晚期骨质破坏，但若确需影像学检查MRI更优</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

*The most tempting distractor is D — diabetes + ulcer often triggers antibiotic reflexes, but this patient has no fever, no malaise, no purulent discharge, and no expanding erythema, making infection clinically absent and antibiotics unnecessary.*

最容易误选的干扰项是D——糖尿病合并溃疡常引发开抗生素的反射，但本患者无发热、无全身不适、无脓性分泌物、无扩展性红斑，临床上无感染证据，不需要抗生素。

## 5. High-Yield Summary Table — Pressure Injury vs. Infected Wound vs. Ischemic Ulcer / 压力性损伤 vs. 感染性创面 vs. 缺血性溃疡
