## 6. One-Sentence Summary & Memory Hook / 一句话总结 & 记忆钩

**A non-infected residual limb ulcer caused by a loose, rubbing prosthetic socket requires socket refitting — not antibiotics, imaging, or surgery — because treating the wound without eliminating the mechanical cause guarantees recurrence.**

**由松动摩擦的假肢接受腔引起的无感染残肢溃疡需要重新适配接受腔——而非抗生素、影像学或手术——因为不消除机械原因而仅处理创面必然复发。**

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 100%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><p><strong>Memory Hook — R.A.F.T. for Pressure Ulcer Management / 记忆钩 — 压力性溃疡管理 "R.A.F.T.":</strong></p>
<p>• <strong>R</strong>oot cause removal — identify and eliminate the mechanical source first (refit the socket!) / <strong>R</strong> — 根本原因消除：首先识别并消除机械来源（重新适配接受腔！）<br />
• <strong>A</strong>ssess for infection — fever, purulence, and systemic signs before reaching for antibiotics / <strong>A</strong> — 评估感染：开抗生素前先检查有无发热、脓液和全身征象<br />
• <strong>F</strong>ree from pressure — non-weight bearing and offloading to allow wound healing / <strong>F</strong> — 卸除压力：非负重和压力减载以促进创面愈合<br />
• <strong>T</strong>rack healing closely — follow up for infection development and wound progression / <strong>T</strong> — 密切追踪愈合：随访监测感染发生和创面进展</p></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
</tbody>
</table>

## 7. High-Yield Topic Knowledge — Prosthetic Limb Pressure Complications / 高频知识表 — 假肢压力性并发症

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 50%" />
<col style="width: 50%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Topic</strong><br />
<strong>考点</strong></th>
<th><strong>Key Points</strong><br />
<strong>要点</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>Pressure injury staging (NPUAP/EPUAP)<br />
压力性损伤分期（NPUAP/EPUAP）</td>
<td>Stage 1: intact skin, non-blanchable erythema; Stage 2: partial-thickness loss, no slough (this patient); Stage 3: full-thickness loss; Stage 4: bone/tendon/muscle exposed; Unstageable: slough/eschar obscures base<br />
1期：皮肤完整，不可褪色红斑；2期：部分厚度缺失，无腐肉（本患者）；3期：全层皮肤缺失；4期：骨/肌腱/肌肉暴露；不可分期：腐肉/焦痂遮盖基底</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Causes of prosthetic socket ill-fit<br />
接受腔不合适的原因</td>
<td>Weight change (gain or loss), disuse muscle atrophy, limb volume fluctuations (edema), socket material wear, increased activity levels<br />
体重变化（增加或减少）、废用性肌肉萎缩、肢体体积波动（水肿）、接受腔材料磨损、活动水平变化</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>When to obtain MRI of amputation stump<br />
何时行残端MRI</td>
<td>Suspected osteomyelitis: bone exposure, sinus tract formation, systemic infection signs, or wound that fails to heal despite conservative management<br />
怀疑骨髓炎时：骨骼暴露、瘘管形成、全身感染征象或保守治疗后创面不愈合</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Intermittent claudication vs. critical limb ischemia<br />
间歇性跛行 vs. 严重肢体缺血</td>
<td>Claudication: exertional pain relieved by rest, ABI 0.4–0.9; Critical limb ischemia: rest pain (worse at night/elevation), non-healing ulcer, ABI &lt; 0.4 — requires urgent revascularization<br />
间歇性跛行：劳累时疼痛休息缓解，ABI 0.4-0.9；严重肢体缺血：静息痛（夜间/抬高加重）、不愈合溃疡，ABI &lt; 0.4——需紧急血运重建</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Soft tissue infection diagnostic criteria<br />
软组织感染诊断标准</td>
<td>At least 2 of: warmth, erythema extending beyond wound margins, induration, tenderness, purulent discharge; systemic signs (fever, leukocytosis) support diagnosis<br />
至少2项：温热感、红斑超出伤口边缘、硬结、压痛、脓性分泌物；全身征象（发热、白细胞升高）支持诊断</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Diabetic wound healing impairment<br />
糖尿病创面愈合损伤</td>
<td>Impaired angiogenesis, reduced neutrophil chemotaxis and phagocytosis, peripheral neuropathy masking pain, microvascular disease — even well-controlled diabetes warrants close wound follow-up<br />
血管新生受损、中性粒细胞趋化和吞噬功能下降、外周神经病变掩盖疼痛、微血管病变——即使控制良好的糖尿病也需要密切创面随访</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

## 8. Extensions / 延伸扩展

- **Concurrent PAD implications:** This patient's progressive claudication + diminished popliteal pulse warrants ABI measurement and potential vascular surgery referral — PAD may impair stump healing even after socket refitting\
  **合并PAD的影响:** 该患者进展性跛行+腘动脉搏动减弱需测踝臂指数并可能转诊血管外科——即使重新适配接受腔后，PAD仍可能影响残肢愈合

- **Infection escalation triggers:** If wound fails to improve: expanding erythema, fever, purulent discharge, or non-healing at 2–4 weeks → wound culture + antibiotics; bone exposure or systemic signs → MRI to rule out osteomyelitis\
  **感染升级的触发条件:** 若创面不改善：扩展性红斑、发热、脓性分泌物或2-4周不愈合 → 创面培养+抗生素；骨骼暴露或全身征象 → MRI排除骨髓炎

- **Surgical debridement indications:** Reserved for infected pressure injury with significant necrotic burden, extensive slough, or undermining — superficial viable wound like this patient's does not meet criteria\
  **手术清创指征:** 仅用于感染性压力性损伤伴大量坏死组织、广泛腐肉或潜行——本患者浅表存活创面不符合手术指征

- **Multidisciplinary team for amputees:** Optimal stump wound care requires prosthetist (socket refit), wound care nurse, physical therapist, and vascular surgery (given PAD); primary care coordinates long-term diabetes management\
  **截肢患者多学科团队:** 最佳残肢创面护理需要假肢技师（接受腔重新适配）、伤口护理护士、物理治疗师和血管外科（鉴于PAD）；初级保健协调长期糖尿病管理

# Question 169 — Hyperfunctioning Thyroid Nodule (Toxic Adenoma) / 高功能甲状腺结节（毒性腺瘤）

## Question Stem / 题干

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 100%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><p>A <strong>40-year-old man</strong> comes to the physician 6 days after noticing a <strong>nonpainful lump in his neck</strong>. He also has a <strong>2-week history of palpitations</strong>. He is otherwise asymptomatic. He has no history of serious illness and takes no medications. His temperature is 37.2°C (99°F), <strong>pulse is 110/min</strong>, respirations are 16/min, and <strong>blood pressure is 134/60 mm Hg</strong>. Examination shows a <strong>1.4-cm, firm thyroid nodule</strong>. His <strong>serum thyroid-stimulating hormone concentration is less than 0.05 mIU/L</strong>, and <strong>serum free thyroxine concentration is 3.5 ng/dL</strong> (N=0.9–1.7). Which of the following is the most appropriate next step in management?</p>
<p><strong>Q: Most appropriate next step in management?</strong></p>
<p>A) Fine-needle aspiration biopsy of the nodule<br />
B) Measurement of serum calcitonin concentration<br />
C) Operative resection of the nodule<br />
D) Radioactive iodine uptake scan<br />
E) Ultrasonography of the thyroid gland</p>
<p><strong>Correct Answer: D</strong></p></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
</tbody>
</table>

## 1. Key Stem Clues / 题干关键词抓考点

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 50%" />
<col style="width: 50%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Key Stem Clue</strong><br />
<strong>关键词</strong></th>
<th><strong>Why It Matters</strong><br />
<strong>为什么重要</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>TSH &lt; 0.05 mIU/L<br />
TSH &lt; 0.05 mIU/L</td>
<td>Suppressed TSH → hyperfunctioning nodule; radioactive iodine scan is next step<br />
TSH被抑制 → 高功能结节；下一步行放射性碘扫描</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Free T4 = 3.5 ng/dL (elevated)<br />
游离T4 = 3.5 ng/dL（升高）</td>
<td>Confirms overt hyperthyroidism; explains tachycardia and palpitations<br />
证实明显甲亢；解释心动过速和心悸症状</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Pulse 110/min<br />
脉率 110/min</td>
<td>Tachycardia — classic autonomic sign of excess thyroid hormone<br />
心动过速——过量甲状腺激素的经典自主神经表现</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>BP 134/60 mm Hg (wide pulse pressure)<br />
血压 134/60 mmHg（脉压增大）</td>
<td>Wide pulse pressure is a hallmark of hyperthyroid state (high CO, low SVR)<br />
脉压增大是甲亢的特征表现（高心排量、低体循环阻力）</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Nonpainful firm thyroid nodule, 1.4 cm<br />
无痛、质硬甲状腺结节，1.4 cm</td>
<td>Solitary nodule with suppressed TSH = "hot" autonomous nodule<br />
单发结节伴TSH受抑 = "热结节"自主功能结节</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Age 40, no radiation history, no family history<br />
40岁，无放射线暴露史，无家族史</td>
<td>Lower malignancy risk — but hot nodule itself is rarely malignant<br />
恶性风险较低——且热结节本身很少为恶性</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

## 2. Mechanism / 机制理解

A **hyperfunctioning (autonomous) thyroid nodule** produces thyroid hormone independently of TSH regulation, leading to **suppression of pituitary TSH** via negative feedback and elevated circulating **free T4 and T3**:

高功能（自主）甲状腺结节独立于TSH调节产生甲状腺激素，通过负反馈导致**垂体TSH受抑**，循环中**游离T4和T3**升高：

- The nodule's TSH receptor constitutively activates adenylyl cyclase → autonomous hormone synthesis\
  结节的TSH受体持续激活腺苷酸环化酶 → 自主合成甲状腺激素

- Elevated thyroid hormones suppress hypothalamic TRH and pituitary TSH → TSH \< 0.05\
  升高的甲状腺激素抑制下丘脑TRH和垂体TSH → TSH \< 0.05

- Excess T3/T4 increases heart rate, cardiac output, and reduces SVR → tachycardia, wide pulse pressure\
  过量T3/T4增加心率、心排量并降低体循环阻力 → 心动过速、脉压增大

- On RAI scan: hot nodule shows focal uptake; surrounding normal tissue is suppressed (cold)\
  RAI扫描上：热结节显示局灶性摄取；周围正常组织受抑制（冷区）

**Anatomic rule of thumb:** Autonomous nodules ≥1 cm in size are most likely to cause clinical hyperthyroidism because they have sufficient mass to produce supra-physiologic hormone levels.

**解剖小窍门:** 直径 ≥1 cm 的自主结节最易导致临床甲亢，因其体积足以产生超生理水平的甲状腺激素。

## 3. Correct Answer (D) — Radioactive Iodine Uptake Scan / 正确答案 (D) — 放射性碘摄取扫描

**Radioactive iodine uptake (RAIU) scan / thyroid scintigraphy** is the appropriate next step when TSH is suppressed, because it distinguishes a hot (hyperfunctioning) nodule from a cold (hypofunctioning) nodule, which determines whether FNA biopsy is needed:

**放射性碘摄取扫描/甲状腺闪烁显像**是TSH受抑时的恰当下一步，因为它可区分热（高功能）结节和冷（低功能）结节，从而决定是否需要FNA活检：

- Hot nodule (focal uptake) → autonomous functioning; malignancy risk very low → FNA NOT needed\
  热结节（局灶性摄取）→ 自主功能性；恶性风险极低 → 无需FNA

- Cold nodule (absent uptake) → higher malignancy risk → FNA is next step\
  冷结节（摄取缺失）→ 恶性风险较高 → 下一步行FNA

- RAIU scan result guides whether ultrasound-guided FNA should be added\
  RAIU扫描结果指导是否需要加做超声引导下FNA

**Diagnosis:** Suppressed TSH + elevated free T4 + firm solitary nodule = toxic adenoma until proven otherwise; scintigraphy confirms autonomous function.

**诊断:** TSH受抑 + 游离T4升高 + 单发质硬结节 = 除外其他前提下为毒性腺瘤；闪烁显像证实自主功能。

**Treatment:** For confirmed hyperfunctioning nodule — options include RAI ablation, surgical resection, or long-term antithyroid drugs; decision depends on size, symptoms, and patient preference.

**治疗:** 确诊高功能结节后——选项包括RAI消融、手术切除或长期抗甲状腺药物；决策取决于结节大小、症状及患者意愿。

## 4. Options Elimination / 错误选项排除逻辑

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 33%" />
<col style="width: 33%" />
<col style="width: 33%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Option</strong><br />
<strong>选项</strong></th>
<th><strong>Why Wrong</strong><br />
<strong>为什么错</strong></th>
<th><strong>Key Discriminator</strong><br />
<strong>鉴别要点</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>A — Fine-needle aspiration biopsy of the nodule<br />
A — 细针穿刺活检</td>
<td>FNA is premature — with suppressed TSH, RAI scan must come first; hot nodules are rarely malignant and do not require FNA<br />
FNA为时过早——TSH受抑时必须先行RAI扫描；热结节很少恶性，不需FNA</td>
<td>TSH status must direct workup before deciding on biopsy<br />
TSH状态必须在决定活检前指导检查流程</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>B — Measurement of serum calcitonin concentration<br />
B — 检测血清降钙素浓度</td>
<td>ATA does not routinely recommend calcitonin screening; it screens for medullary thyroid cancer but is not the established next step<br />
ATA不常规推荐降钙素筛查；它筛查甲状腺髓样癌，但不是既定下一步</td>
<td>Calcitonin is not in the standard TSH-guided algorithm<br />
降钙素不在以TSH为导向的标准流程中</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>C — Operative resection of the nodule<br />
C — 手术切除结节</td>
<td>Surgery before diagnosis/characterization is premature; indication depends on scan results, response to therapy, or confirmed malignancy<br />
诊断/定性之前手术为时过早；适应证取决于扫描结果、治疗反应或确认的恶性</td>
<td>Never operate before scintigraphy in a biochemically hyperthyroid patient<br />
对生化甲亢患者，闪烁显像前不应手术</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>D — Radioactive iodine uptake scan ✓<br />
D — 放射性碘摄取扫描 ✓</td>
<td>CORRECT — suppressed TSH mandates scintigraphy to determine if nodule is hyperfunctioning before deciding on FNA<br />
正确——TSH受抑要求先行闪烁显像以确定结节是否高功能，再决定是否FNA</td>
<td>RAI scan → hot nodule → FNA avoidable; cold nodule → FNA next<br />
RAI扫描→热结节→可避免FNA；冷结节→下一步FNA</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>E — Ultrasonography of the thyroid gland<br />
E — 甲状腺超声</td>
<td>Ultrasound is part of workup but should follow scintigraphy; scan data informs whether FNA is needed at time of ultrasound<br />
超声是检查的一部分，但应在闪烁显像之后进行；扫描数据决定超声时是否需要同时行FNA</td>
<td>Ultrasound alone cannot distinguish hot from cold nodules<br />
超声本身无法区分热结节与冷结节</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

*The most tempting distractor is Choice E (ultrasound) — it is part of the workup, but ordering it before scintigraphy when TSH is suppressed misses the critical sequence: RAI scan first to determine if FNA is even needed.*

Choice E（超声）是最诱人的干扰项——它确实是检查项目之一，但在TSH受抑时先做超声而非闪烁显像，忽略了关键顺序：先行RAI扫描以判断是否需要FNA。

## 5. High-Yield Summary Table — Hot vs. Cold Thyroid Nodule Workup / 热结节 vs. 冷结节检查流程对比

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 33%" />
<col style="width: 33%" />
<col style="width: 33%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Feature</strong><br />
<strong>特征</strong></th>
<th><strong>Hot Nodule (Hyperfunctioning)</strong><br />
<strong>热结节（高功能）</strong></th>
<th><strong>Cold Nodule (Hypofunctioning)</strong><br />
<strong>冷结节（低功能）</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>TSH level<br />
TSH水平</td>
<td>Suppressed (&lt; 0.05)<br />
受抑（&lt; 0.05）</td>
<td>Normal or elevated<br />
正常或升高</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>RAI scan appearance<br />
RAI扫描表现</td>
<td>Focal uptake in nodule; surrounding tissue suppressed<br />
结节局灶性摄取；周围组织受抑制</td>
<td>Absent uptake ("cold")<br />
摄取缺失（"冷区"）</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Malignancy risk<br />
恶性风险</td>
<td>Very low (&lt; 1%)<br />
极低（&lt; 1%）</td>
<td>Higher (~5–15%)<br />
较高（约5–15%）</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>FNA needed?<br />
需要FNA？</td>
<td>No — not required<br />
否——不需要</td>
<td>Yes — essential<br />
是——必要</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Management<br />
治疗方案</td>
<td>RAI ablation, surgery, or antithyroid drugs<br />
RAI消融、手术或抗甲状腺药物</td>
<td>FNA → depends on cytology<br />
FNA → 取决于细胞学结果</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>When to order RAI scan<br />
何时行RAI扫描</td>
<td>Always when TSH is low<br />
TSH低时始终需要</td>
<td>Not necessary (already cold on scan)<br />
不需要（扫描已显示冷区）</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

## 6. One-Sentence Summary & Memory Hook / 一句话总结 & 记忆钩

**When a thyroid nodule is found with suppressed TSH, the next step is always radioactive iodine uptake scan to determine if it is a "hot" autonomous nodule before proceeding to FNA.**

**发现甲状腺结节伴TSH受抑时，下一步始终是放射性碘摄取扫描，先判断是否为"热"自主结节，再决定是否行FNA。**

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 100%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><p><strong>Memory Hook — TSH-Guided Thyroid Nodule Algorithm / 记忆钩 — TSH指导甲状腺结节处理流程:</strong></p>
<p>• <strong>L</strong>ow TSH → <strong>L</strong>aunch RAI scan first (hot nodule = low malignancy, skip FNA) / TSH低 → 先做RAI扫描（热结节 = 低恶性，跳过FNA）<br />
• <strong>N</strong>ormal/high TSH → <strong>N</strong>odule needs ultrasound + FNA if indicated / TSH正常/升高 → 结节需超声 + 必要时FNA<br />
• <strong>H</strong>ot = <strong>H</strong>armless (autonomous, rarely malignant) / 热结节 = 无害（自主功能，很少恶性）<br />
• <strong>C</strong>old = <strong>C</strong>oncerning (needs cytology) / 冷结节 = 需警惕（需细胞学检查）</p></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
</tbody>
</table>

## 7. High-Yield Topic Knowledge — Thyroid Nodule Evaluation / 高频知识表 — 甲状腺结节评估

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 50%" />
<col style="width: 50%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Topic</strong><br />
<strong>考点</strong></th>
<th><strong>Key Points</strong><br />
<strong>要点</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>Initial evaluation of any thyroid nodule<br />
任何甲状腺结节的初始评估</td>
<td>Always start with serum TSH measurement — determines the entire subsequent workup<br />
始终从血清TSH检测开始——决定后续全部检查流程</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>RAI scan indications<br />
RAI扫描适应证</td>
<td>Indicated when TSH is below normal; distinguishes hyperfunctioning (hot) from hypofunctioning (cold) nodules<br />
TSH低于正常时有指征；区分高功能（热）与低功能（冷）结节</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Hot nodule characteristics<br />
热结节特征</td>
<td>Autonomous TSH receptor mutation; suppressed TSH; free T4/T3 elevated; malignancy rare; FNA not needed<br />
TSH受体自主突变；TSH受抑；游离T4/T3升高；恶性罕见；不需FNA</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Cold nodule characteristics<br />
冷结节特征</td>
<td>Poor iodine uptake; ~5–15% malignancy risk; FNA essential for diagnosis<br />
碘摄取差；约5–15%恶性风险；FNA是诊断必需</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Calcitonin in thyroid nodule workup<br />
降钙素在甲状腺结节检查中的地位</td>
<td>ATA does not routinely recommend; elevated calcitonin suggests medullary thyroid carcinoma (C-cell origin)<br />
ATA不常规推荐；降钙素升高提示甲状腺髓样癌（C细胞来源）</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Hyperthyroid nodule treatment options<br />
甲亢结节的治疗选择</td>
<td>RAI ablation (most common), thyroidectomy, or long-term methimazole/PTU; choice based on nodule size, severity, patient factors<br />
RAI消融（最常见）、甲状腺切除术或长期甲巯咪唑/PTU；取决于结节大小、严重程度及患者因素</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Malignancy risk factors for thyroid nodules<br />
甲状腺结节恶性风险因素</td>
<td>Young age, male sex, prior head/neck radiation, family history of thyroid cancer, MEN2, rapid growth, cervical lymphadenopathy<br />
年龄小、男性、头颈部放疗史、甲状腺癌家族史、MEN2、快速增长、颈部淋巴结肿大</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

## 8. Extensions / 延伸扩展

- **Cause of tachycardia/palpitations here:** Excess thyroid hormone increases beta-adrenergic sensitivity → sinus tachycardia; AF risk increases with prolonged hyperthyroidism\
  **本题心动过速/心悸的原因:** 过量甲状腺激素增加β肾上腺素能敏感性 → 窦性心动过速；长期甲亢增加房颤风险

- **Toxic multinodular goiter vs. toxic adenoma:** Both present with suppressed TSH; scintigraphy shows multiple hot foci in TMNG vs. single focus in toxic adenoma; both require RAI scan\
  **毒性多结节性甲状腺肿 vs. 毒性腺瘤:** 两者均表现为TSH受抑；闪烁显像示TMNG多发热区 vs. 毒性腺瘤单发热区；两者均需RAI扫描

- **Wide pulse pressure mechanism:** Hyperthyroidism → increased cardiac output + decreased systemic vascular resistance → systolic BP up, diastolic BP down\
  **脉压增大机制:** 甲亢 → 心排量增加 + 体循环阻力降低 → 收缩压升高、舒张压降低

- **NBME exam trap:** If TSH is normal and a nodule is found → go straight to ultrasound + FNA based on ultrasound features; RAI scan is only relevant when TSH is suppressed\
  **NBME考试陷阱:** 若TSH正常且发现结节 → 直接行超声 + 根据超声特征决定FNA；RAI扫描仅在TSH受抑时相关

# Question 170 — Myopericarditis / 病毒性心肌心包炎

## Question Stem / 题干

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 100%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><p>A <strong>previously healthy 24-year-old man</strong> comes to the emergency department because of a <strong>12-hour history of increasing pain to the left of the center of his chest</strong>. Initially, the pain was mild and occurred only when he breathed deeply. Now, the pain is more severe and constant. He rates the pain as an <strong>8 on a 10-point scale</strong>. The <strong>pain increases when he lies on his back, decreases when he leans forward</strong>, and does not radiate. He has not had palpitations, shortness of breath, nausea, vomiting, or sweating. He says that he is <strong>"recovering from a head cold," which he has had for 14 days</strong>. He appears moderately uncomfortable but is in no respiratory distress. His temperature is 37.6°C (99.6°F), pulse is 66/min and regular, respirations are 20/min, and blood pressure is 152/88 mm Hg. Examination, including cardiovascular examination, shows no abnormalities. His <strong>serum creatine kinase activity is 420 mg/dL with an MB fraction of 12% (N&lt;5%)</strong>. An ECG is shown. Which of the following is the most appropriate next step in diagnosis?</p>
<p><strong>Q: Most appropriate next step in diagnosis?</strong></p>
<p>A) Echocardiography<br />
B) CT scan of the chest<br />
C) Cardiac MRI<br />
D) Coronary angiography<br />
E) Pericardiocentesis</p>
<p><strong>Correct Answer: A</strong></p></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
</tbody>
</table>

---

## 1. Key Stem Clues / 题干关键词抓考点

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 50%" />
<col style="width: 50%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Key Stem Clue</strong><br />
<strong>关键词</strong></th>
<th><strong>Why It Matters</strong><br />
<strong>为什么重要</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>24-year-old healthy male<br />
24岁既往健康男性</td>
<td>Young age makes atherosclerotic ACS unlikely; shifts differential toward inflammatory/infectious etiologies<br />
年轻男性使粥样硬化性ACS概率极低，诊断方向指向炎症/感染病因</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Pain worsens supine, improves leaning forward<br />
仰卧位加重、前倾位减轻</td>
<td>Pathognomonic positional relief of pericarditis — inflamed pericardial layers separate when leaning forward<br />
心包炎的病理特征性体位性缓解——前倾时两层发炎的心包分离</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>14-day viral URI prodrome ("head cold")<br />
14天病毒性上呼吸道感染前驱期（"感冒"）</td>
<td>Supports viral etiology (Coxsackievirus B, echovirus); pericarditis typically follows URI by 1–3 weeks<br />
支持病毒性病因（柯萨奇B病毒、埃可病毒）；心包炎通常在上呼吸道感染后1-3周出现</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>CK-MB fraction 12% (N&lt;5%)<br />
CK-MB分数12%（正常&lt;5%）</td>
<td>Elevated CK-MB indicates myocardial involvement → myopericarditis; changes management and prognosis<br />
CK-MB升高提示心肌受累→心肌心包炎，改变诊疗策略和预后</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>No radiation, no diaphoresis, no nausea<br />
无放射痛、无出汗、无恶心</td>
<td>Absence of typical ACS features argues against STEMI/NSTEMI<br />
缺乏典型ACS特征，不支持STEMI/NSTEMI</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>ECG shown (diffuse ST elevation + PR depression implied)<br />
ECG提示弥漫性ST抬高+PR段压低</td>
<td>Saddle-shaped ST elevation in multiple leads + PR depression is the hallmark of pericarditis on ECG<br />
多导联马鞍形ST抬高+PR段压低是心包炎的ECG标志性表现</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

---

## 2. Mechanism / 机制理解

**Pericarditis** is inflammation of the pericardial sac, most commonly triggered by **viral infection** (Coxsackievirus B, echovirus, adenovirus). When the **visceral and parietal pericardial layers** become inflamed and rub against each other, characteristic **pleuritic-positional chest pain** results. Concurrent myocardial inflammation (**myopericarditis**) is evidenced by elevated **CK-MB and troponin**:

病毒性**心包炎**是心包囊的炎症，最常由**病毒感染**（柯萨奇B病毒、埃可病毒、腺病毒）触发。当**脏层和壁层心包**发炎相互摩擦时，出现特征性的**胸膜炎样-体位性胸痛**。伴随的心肌炎症（**心肌心包炎**）通过**CK-MB和肌钙蛋白升高**得以证实：

- Viral replication in pericardial tissue → cytokine release → pericardial inflammation → fibrinous exudate on pericardial surfaces\
  病毒在心包组织复制→细胞因子释放→心包炎症→心包表面纤维素性渗出

- Inflamed layers rub → friction rub (harsh diastolic sound) + pleuritic pain that responds to position\
  发炎的心包层摩擦→摩擦音（粗糙舒张期杂音）+对体位有反应的胸膜炎样疼痛

- Fluid accumulation (effusion) may follow → if rapidly accumulating, can compress cardiac chambers → **tamponade**\
  随后可出现积液→若快速积聚，可压迫心腔→**心脏压塞**

- Myocardial extension → cardiomyocyte necrosis → elevated **CK-MB/troponin** → risk of arrhythmia or reduced EF\
  心肌受累延伸→心肌细胞坏死→**CK-MB/肌钙蛋白**升高→心律失常或EF降低风险

**Anatomic rule of thumb:** The pericardium wraps the heart in two layers (visceral = epicardium, parietal = outer fibrous layer) with only ~50 mL of fluid normally. Rapid accumulation of even 150–200 mL can cause tamponade.

**解剖小窍门:** 心包将心脏包裹在两层结构中（脏层=心外膜，壁层=外层纤维层），正常情况下只有约50 mL液体。即使快速积聚150-200 mL也可引起心脏压塞。

---

## 3. Correct Answer (A) — Echocardiography / 正确答案 (A) — 超声心动图

**Echocardiography** is the first-line imaging modality in suspected pericarditis/myopericarditis because it rapidly and non-invasively provides critical information:

**超声心动图**是疑似心包炎/心肌心包炎时的一线影像学检查，因为它能快速无创地提供关键信息：

- Detects pericardial effusion (size, location, hemodynamic significance)\
  检测心包积液（大小、位置、血流动力学意义）

- Identifies signs of cardiac tamponade (right ventricular diastolic collapse, respiratory variation in mitral/tricuspid inflow)\
  识别心脏压塞征象（右心室舒张期塌陷、二尖瓣/三尖瓣血流随呼吸变化）

- Assesses left ventricular ejection fraction (LVEF) — critical given elevated CK-MB suggesting myocarditis\
  评估左心室射血分数（LVEF）——CK-MB升高提示心肌炎，此步骤至关重要

- Rules out other structural causes (wall motion abnormalities suggesting ACS, valvular disease)\
  排除其他结构性原因（提示ACS的室壁运动异常、瓣膜病）

**Diagnosis:** Myopericarditis in a young man following viral URI; positional chest pain + elevated CK-MB + ECG changes make this diagnosis. Echo confirms effusion and assesses myocardial function.

**诊断:** 病毒性上呼吸道感染后年轻男性心肌心包炎；体位性胸痛+CK-MB升高+ECG改变确立诊断。超声心动图确认积液并评估心肌功能。

**Treatment:** NSAIDs (aspirin or ibuprofen) + colchicine for 3 months; restrict strenuous exercise for 3–6 months; if myocarditis component present, add consideration for LVEF monitoring and potentially ACE inhibitor/beta-blocker.

**治疗:** NSAIDs（阿司匹林或布洛芬）+秋水仙碱持续3个月；限制剧烈运动3-6个月；若存在心肌炎成分，需监测LVEF，必要时考虑ACEI/β受体阻滞剂。

---

## 4. Options Elimination / 错误选项排除逻辑

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 33%" />
<col style="width: 33%" />
<col style="width: 33%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Option</strong><br />
<strong>选项</strong></th>
<th><strong>Why Wrong</strong><br />
<strong>为什么错</strong></th>
<th><strong>Key Discriminator</strong><br />
<strong>鉴别要点</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>A — Echocardiography ✓<br />
A — 超声心动图 ✓</td>
<td>CORRECT — First-line imaging to evaluate effusion, tamponade, and LVEF in myopericarditis<br />
正确——心肌心包炎中评估积液、压塞和LVEF的一线影像检查</td>
<td>Provides real-time functional + structural cardiac assessment non-invasively<br />
无创提供实时心脏功能和结构评估</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>B — CT scan of the chest<br />
B — 胸部CT扫描</td>
<td>Provides structural information (pericardial thickness, calcification) but limited functional data; cannot assess EF or tamponade hemodynamics<br />
提供结构信息（心包厚度、钙化）但功能数据有限；无法评估EF或压塞血流动力学</td>
<td>Echo superior for hemodynamic/functional assessment; CT used for constrictive pericarditis workup<br />
超声在血流动力学/功能评估上更优；CT用于缩窄性心包炎检查</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>C — Cardiac MRI<br />
C — 心脏MRI</td>
<td>Gold standard for myocarditis characterization (late gadolinium enhancement) but limited availability, high cost, and time-consuming; not first-line in acute setting<br />
心肌炎表征的金标准（延迟钆增强）但可及性有限、费用高、耗时；急性期不作为一线检查</td>
<td>MRI used after echo establishes diagnosis and stability is confirmed; not for acute triage<br />
MRI在超声确立诊断且稳定性确认后使用；不用于急性分诊</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>D — Coronary angiography<br />
D — 冠状动脉造影</td>
<td>Invasive test for coronary artery anatomy; indicated for ACS (STEMI, NSTEMI with high-risk features), not inflammatory pericarditis<br />
冠状动脉解剖的有创检查；适用于ACS（STEMI、高危特征的NSTEMI），不适用于炎症性心包炎</td>
<td>No ischemic ECG pattern (no reciprocal ST depression, no Q waves); positional pain pattern inconsistent with ACS<br />
无缺血性ECG表现（无对应性ST压低、无Q波）；体位性疼痛与ACS不一致</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>E — Pericardiocentesis<br />
E — 心包穿刺引流</td>
<td>Therapeutic/diagnostic procedure for confirmed pericardial effusion or tamponade; should NOT be performed before imaging confirms the effusion exists<br />
针对已确认心包积液或压塞的治疗/诊断操作；在影像确认积液存在之前不应进行</td>
<td>No imaging confirmation of effusion yet; no clinical signs of tamponade (no hypotension, no JVD, no paradoxus)<br />
尚无积液影像确认；无心脏压塞临床征象（无低血压、无颈静脉怒张、无奇脉）</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

*The most tempting distractor is E (Pericardiocentesis) — students may jump to drainage because of the elevated CK-MB, but the key principle is: confirm effusion with echo BEFORE any invasive procedure.*

心包穿刺（E选项）是最容易出错的干扰选项——因为CK-MB升高，考生可能直接想到引流操作，但关键原则是：任何有创操作前必须先通过超声心动图确认积液存在。

---

## 5. High-Yield Summary Table — Pericarditis vs. Myocarditis vs. STEMI / 心包炎 vs. 心肌炎 vs. STEMI 鉴别

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 25%" />
<col style="width: 25%" />
<col style="width: 25%" />
<col style="width: 25%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Feature</strong><br />
<strong>特征</strong></th>
<th><strong>Pericarditis</strong><br />
<strong>心包炎</strong></th>
<th><strong>Myocarditis</strong><br />
<strong>心肌炎</strong></th>
<th><strong>STEMI</strong><br />
<strong>ST段抬高心肌梗死</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>Age / demographics<br />
年龄/人群</td>
<td>Young adults, post-viral<br />
年轻成人，病毒感染后</td>
<td>Young adults, post-viral<br />
年轻成人，病毒感染后</td>
<td>Older adults, CV risk factors<br />
老年人，心血管危险因素</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Pain character<br />
疼痛特征</td>
<td>Pleuritic, positional<br />
胸膜炎样，体位相关</td>
<td>Dull ache, less positional<br />
钝痛，体位相关性差</td>
<td>Pressure/crushing, radiation<br />
压榨性，可放射</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>ECG pattern<br />
ECG表现</td>
<td>Diffuse ST↑, PR depression (saddle)<br />
弥漫性ST↑，PR段压低（马鞍形）</td>
<td>Non-specific ST/T changes, arrhythmias<br />
非特异性ST/T改变，心律失常</td>
<td>Focal ST↑ + reciprocal ST↓<br />
局限性ST↑+对应导联ST↓</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Troponin / CK-MB<br />
肌钙蛋白/CK-MB</td>
<td>Mildly elevated if myopericarditis<br />
心肌心包炎时轻中度升高</td>
<td>Markedly elevated<br />
显著升高</td>
<td>Markedly elevated<br />
显著升高</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Friction rub<br />
摩擦音</td>
<td>Present (classic)<br />
存在（经典表现）</td>
<td>Usually absent<br />
通常缺失</td>
<td>Absent (unless post-MI pericarditis)<br />
缺失（除非MI后心包炎）</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Echo finding<br />
超声心动图表现</td>
<td>Effusion ± normal wall motion<br />
积液±室壁运动正常</td>
<td>Reduced EF, wall motion abnormality<br />
EF降低，室壁运动异常</td>
<td>Regional wall motion abnormality<br />
节段性室壁运动异常</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Treatment<br />
治疗</td>
<td>NSAIDs + colchicine<br />
NSAIDs+秋水仙碱</td>
<td>Supportive, restrict activity<br />
支持治疗，限制活动</td>
<td>Reperfusion (PCI/thrombolytics)<br />
再灌注治疗（PCI/溶栓）</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

---

## 6. One-Sentence Summary & Memory Hook / 一句话总结 & 记忆钩

**In a young patient with post-viral pleuritic chest pain that improves leaning forward and elevated CK-MB, diagnose myopericarditis and order echocardiography first to assess for effusion and cardiac function.**

**在病毒感染后出现前倾位缓解的胸膜炎样胸痛且CK-MB升高的年轻患者中，诊断心肌心包炎，并首先行超声心动图评估积液和心脏功能。**

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 100%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><p><strong>Memory Hook — PERI Clues / 记忆钩 — 心包炎 "PERI" 四线索:</strong></p>
<p>• <strong>P</strong>ositional relief (lean forward) — pain better sitting up / 前倾位（前倾减轻）——坐起时疼痛缓解<br />
• <strong>E</strong>CG: saddle-shaped diffuse ST↑ + PR depression — "every lead lit up" / ECG：马鞍形弥漫ST↑+PR压低——"每个导联都亮了"<br />
• <strong>R</strong>ub (friction rub in diastole) — leathery scratch / 摩擦音（舒张期摩擦音）——皮革样摩擦感<br />
• <strong>I</strong>nfection antecedent (viral URI 1–3 weeks prior) — always ask about recent illness / 感染前驱（1-3周前病毒性上呼吸道感染）——务必追问近期病史</p></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
</tbody>
</table>

---

## 7. High-Yield Topic Knowledge — Pericarditis & Myopericarditis / 高频知识表 — 心包炎与心肌心包炎

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 50%" />
<col style="width: 50%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Topic</strong><br />
<strong>考点</strong></th>
<th><strong>Key Points</strong><br />
<strong>要点</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>Most common cause of pericarditis<br />
心包炎最常见病因</td>
<td>Viral (idiopathic): Coxsackievirus B, echovirus, adenovirus, EBV, CMV; accounts for ~90% of cases<br />
病毒性（特发性）：柯萨奇B病毒、埃可病毒、腺病毒、EBV、CMV；约占90%病例</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>ECG stages of pericarditis<br />
心包炎ECG分期</td>
<td>Stage 1: diffuse ST↑ + PR↓; Stage 2: ST normalizes; Stage 3: T-wave inversion; Stage 4: ECG normalizes<br />
第1期：弥漫ST↑+PR↓；第2期：ST正常化；第3期：T波倒置；第4期：ECG正常化</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Cardiac tamponade signs (Beck's triad)<br />
心脏压塞体征（Beck三联征）</td>
<td>Hypotension + muffled heart sounds + jugular venous distension; plus pulsus paradoxus &gt;10 mmHg<br />
低血压+心音低钝+颈静脉怒张；加上奇脉&gt;10 mmHg</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>CK-MB vs. Troponin in myopericarditis<br />
心肌心包炎中CK-MB与肌钙蛋白</td>
<td>Both may be elevated; troponin more sensitive for myocardial injury; elevated markers indicate myocarditis component and worse prognosis<br />
两者均可升高；肌钙蛋白对心肌损伤更敏感；标志物升高提示心肌炎成分及预后较差</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Treatment of pericarditis<br />
心包炎治疗</td>
<td>Aspirin 750–1000 mg TID or ibuprofen 600 mg TID + colchicine 0.5 mg BID for 3 months; avoid NSAIDs if STEMI (impair healing); restrict strenuous activity<br />
阿司匹林750-1000 mg TID或布洛芬600 mg TID+秋水仙碱0.5 mg BID持续3个月；STEMI时避免NSAIDs（影响愈合）；限制剧烈运动</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Dressler syndrome<br />
Dressler综合征</td>
<td>Post-MI or post-cardiac surgery pericarditis (weeks to months later); autoimmune mechanism; treat with NSAIDs/colchicine<br />
MI后或心脏手术后数周至数月出现的心包炎；自身免疫机制；NSAIDs/秋水仙碱治疗</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Constrictive pericarditis<br />
缩窄性心包炎</td>
<td>Late complication of pericarditis (TB most common worldwide); fibrotic pericardium restricts diastolic filling; presents with right heart failure signs; treat with pericardiectomy<br />
心包炎晚期并发症（全球以结核最常见）；纤维化心包限制舒张期充盈；表现为右心衰体征；心包剥脱术治疗</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

---

## 8. Extensions / 延伸扩展

- **Differential of chest pain in young adults:** Consider myopericarditis, spontaneous pneumothorax, pulmonary embolism, aortic dissection (Marfan), costochondritis — age and positional features help narrow\
  **年轻成人胸痛鉴别:** 考虑心肌心包炎、自发性气胸、肺栓塞、主动脉夹层（Marfan综合征）、肋软骨炎——年龄和体位特征有助于缩窄诊断

- **Key complication — Cardiac tamponade:** Occurs when pericardial fluid accumulates faster than pericardium can stretch; physiology is equalization of diastolic pressures in all chambers; echo shows RV diastolic collapse\
  **关键并发症——心脏压塞:** 当心包积液积聚速度超过心包伸展能力时发生；生理机制为所有心腔舒张压均等化；超声表现为右心室舒张期塌陷

- **Variant — Purulent pericarditis:** Bacterial (Staph, Strep, gram-negatives); presents with high fever, toxic appearance, rapid tamponade; requires urgent pericardiocentesis + IV antibiotics; high mortality\
  **变式——化脓性心包炎:** 细菌性（金葡菌、链球菌、革兰阴性菌）；表现为高热、中毒面容、快速压塞；需紧急心包穿刺+静脉抗生素；高死亡率

- **Recurrent pericarditis:** ~15–30% of patients; colchicine reduces recurrence by 50%; refractory cases may require immunosuppression (anakinra) or pericardiectomy\
  **复发性心包炎:** 约15-30%患者复发；秋水仙碱使复发率降低50%；难治性病例可能需要免疫抑制（anakinra）或心包剥脱术

# Question 171 — Salicylate Toxicity / 水杨酸（阿司匹林）中毒

## Question Stem / 题干

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 100%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><p>A <strong>21-year-old man</strong> is brought to the emergency department by paramedics because of a <strong>10-hour history of altered mental status</strong>. The mother says the patient was "fine" last night. This morning, he did not wake up at his usual time; when she went to check on him, she could not get him to wake up. He has no history of serious medical or psychiatric illness and takes no medications. His mother says he does not smoke cigarettes, drink alcohol, or use illicit drugs. On arrival, he is lethargic but is not in respiratory distress. He is responsive to painful stimuli. His temperature is 36.7°C (98.0°F), pulse is 120/min, respirations are <strong>26/min</strong>, and blood pressure is 135/85 mm Hg. Pulse oximetry on room air shows an oxygen saturation of 100%. Physical examination shows no other abnormalities. Laboratory studies are shown: Serum Na+ 143 mEq/L, K+ 3.8 mEq/L, <strong>Cl- 110 mEq/L</strong>, <strong>HCO3- 13 mEq/L</strong>, Urea nitrogen 14 mg/dL, Glucose 120 mg/dL, <strong>Osmolality 290 mOsmol/kg H2O</strong>; Urine Glucose none, <strong>Ketones 3+</strong>. Arterial blood gas: <strong>pH 7.43</strong>, <strong>PCO2 22 mm Hg</strong>, PO2 96 mm Hg. Which of the following is the most likely diagnosis?</p>
<p><strong>Q: Which of the following is the most likely diagnosis?</strong></p>
<p>A) Alcoholic ketoacidosis<br />
B) Diabetic ketoacidosis<br />
C) Ethylene glycol toxicity<br />
D) Methanol toxicity<br />
E) Salicylate toxicity</p>
<p><strong>Correct Answer: E</strong></p></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
</tbody>
</table>

## 1. Key Stem Clues / 题干关键词抓考点

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 50%" />
<col style="width: 50%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Key Stem Clue</strong><br />
<strong>关键词</strong></th>
<th><strong>Why It Matters</strong><br />
<strong>为什么重要</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>Anion gap = Na⁺ − (Cl⁻ + HCO₃⁻) = 143 − (110 + 13) = 20 mEq/L<br />
阴离子间隙 = 143 − (110 + 13) = 20 mEq/L</td>
<td>Elevated AG (normal 8–12) → high-AG metabolic acidosis; drives differential toward MUDPILES causes<br />
阴离子间隙升高（正常 8–12）→ 高 AG 代谢性酸中毒；鉴别方向指向 MUDPILES</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>pH 7.43 (alkalotic) despite HCO₃⁻ only 13 mEq/L<br />
pH 7.43（碱性），但 HCO₃⁻ 仅 13 mEq/L</td>
<td>Alkalotic pH with low bicarbonate = concurrent respiratory alkalosis must be present and dominating; this "mixed disorder" pattern narrows the diagnosis sharply<br />
碱性 pH 伴低碳酸氢盐 = 同时存在呼吸性碱中毒且占主导；此"混合型"模式极大缩窄诊断范围</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>PCO₂ 22 mmHg — lower than Winter's formula predicts<br />
PCO₂ 22 mmHg — 低于 Winter 公式预测值</td>
<td>Expected PCO₂ = 1.5 × 13 + 8 = 27.5 ± 2 mmHg (range 25.5–29.5); actual 22 &lt; expected → independent respiratory alkalosis superimposed on metabolic acidosis<br />
预期 PCO₂ = 27.5 ± 2 mmHg（范围 25.5–29.5）；实际 22 &lt; 预期 → 独立叠加的呼吸性碱中毒，而非单纯代偿</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Serum osmolality 290 mOsmol/kg (within normal limits)<br />
血清渗透压 290 mOsmol/kg（在正常范围内）</td>
<td>No osmolar gap → effectively excludes ethylene glycol and methanol, which produce osmotically active toxic metabolites<br />
无渗透压差 → 有效排除乙二醇和甲醇中毒——二者产生渗透活性有毒代谢产物</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Urine ketones 3+ with blood glucose only 120 mg/dL; urine glucose negative<br />
尿酮体 3+，但血糖仅 120 mg/dL；尿糖阴性</td>
<td>Ketonuria without significant hyperglycemia or glucosuria → not DKA; salicylate uncouples oxidative phosphorylation → excess ketone production independent of insulin deficiency<br />
酮尿症不伴明显高血糖或葡萄糖尿 → 排除 DKA；水杨酸盐解偶联氧化磷酸化 → 不依赖胰岛素缺乏的酮体过量生成</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Mother specifically denies alcohol use and all medications<br />
母亲明确否认饮酒及任何用药史</td>
<td>Alcoholic KA requires alcohol; "no medications" is a classic red herring — aspirin is OTC and easy to conceal; covert ingestion must be considered in unexplained mixed acid-base disorders<br />
酒精性 KA 需要饮酒史；"未服药"是经典误导——阿司匹林无需处方且易于隐瞒；不明原因混合型酸碱紊乱时必须考虑隐性摄入</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Tachypnea (RR 26/min) in a young man with no pulmonary findings<br />
呼吸急促（RR 26/min），年轻男性，无肺部体征</td>
<td>Physiologic hyperventilation without respiratory distress → primary CNS respiratory center stimulation; SpO₂ 100% confirms no hypoxic drive<br />
生理性过度通气且无呼吸窘迫 → 中枢呼吸中枢原发性受刺激；SpO₂ 100% 确认无低氧驱动</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

## 2. Mechanism / 机制理解

**Salicylate** (aspirin) toxicity produces a characteristic **mixed acid-base disorder** through two simultaneous but temporally offset mechanisms that act on different physiologic targets:

**水杨酸盐**（阿司匹林）中毒通过两条同时但时间错开的机制产生特征性**混合型酸碱紊乱**，分别作用于不同生理靶点：

- Salicylate directly stimulates medullary respiratory centers → hyperventilation → CO₂ blown off → **respiratory alkalosis** (early onset, dominant in adults)\
  水杨酸盐直接刺激延髓呼吸中枢 → 过度通气 → CO₂ 大量排出 → **呼吸性碱中毒**（早期出现，成人中占主导）

- Salicylate uncouples mitochondrial **oxidative phosphorylation** → cells shift to anaerobic glycolysis → lactic acid + ketoacids accumulate → **high anion gap metabolic acidosis** (delayed, hours later)\
  水杨酸盐解偶联线粒体**氧化磷酸化** → 细胞转向无氧糖酵解 → 乳酸 + 酮酸堆积 → **高 AG 代谢性酸中毒**（延迟出现，数小时后）

- Net result in adults: respiratory alkalosis dominates → **alkalotic or near-normal pH** despite metabolic acidosis and low HCO₃⁻\
  成人净结果：呼吸性碱中毒占主导 → 尽管存在代谢性酸中毒和低 HCO₃⁻，pH **仍偏碱或接近正常**

- Salicylate does NOT produce osmotically active metabolites → **no osmolar gap**, unlike ethylene glycol and methanol\
  水杨酸盐**不**产生渗透活性代谢产物 → **无渗透压差**，与乙二醇和甲醇不同

- CNS penetration is pH-dependent: unionized (lipid-soluble) salicylate crosses the blood-brain barrier; acidic blood → more unionized drug → more CNS penetration → worsens encephalopathy\
  CNS 渗透具有 pH 依赖性：非电离（脂溶性）水杨酸盐穿过血脑屏障；血液酸性 → 更多非电离药物 → 更多 CNS 渗透 → 脑病加重

**Therapeutic pearl:** Sodium bicarbonate alkalinizes both blood (trapping drug as ionized form, reducing CNS entry) and urine (trapping ionized drug in tubular lumen, increasing excretion)

**治疗要点:** 碳酸氢钠同时碱化血液（使药物以电离形式存在，减少进入 CNS）和尿液（使电离药物滞留于肾小管，增加排泄）

## 3. Correct Answer (E) — Salicylate Toxicity / 正确答案 (E) — 水杨酸（阿司匹林）中毒

**Salicylate toxicity** is the only condition among the choices that simultaneously produces respiratory alkalosis + high-AG metabolic acidosis with normal serum osmolality and urine ketones:

**水杨酸中毒**是选项中唯一能同时引起呼吸性碱中毒 + 高 AG 代谢性酸中毒、且血清渗透压正常、尿酮体阳性的疾病：

- Mixed acid-base: respiratory alkalosis (medullary stimulation, early) superimposed on high-AG metabolic acidosis (ETC uncoupling, late) → net alkalotic pH = 7.43\
  混合型酸碱紊乱：呼吸性碱中毒（延髓受刺激，早期）叠加高 AG 代谢性酸中毒（ETC 解偶联，晚期）→ 净 pH 偏碱 = 7.43

- Urine ketones 3+ with glucose only 120 mg/dL and negative urine glucose → ETC uncoupling, not insulin deficiency\
  尿酮体 3+ 但血糖仅 120 mg/dL 且尿糖阴性 → ETC 解偶联所致，非胰岛素缺乏

- Normal osmolality (290 mOsmol/kg) → no osmolar gap → effectively excludes ethylene glycol and methanol\
  渗透压正常（290 mOsmol/kg）→ 无渗透压差 → 有效排除乙二醇和甲醇

- Clinical syndrome: tachypnea, tinnitus, hyperthermia, agitation, delirium, GI upset — all absent in the other toxic ingestions in the differential\
  临床综合征：呼吸急促、耳鸣、发热、烦躁、谵妄、胃肠道不适——鉴别诊断中其他中毒均不具备全部这些特征

**Diagnosis:** Calculate anion gap + apply Winter's formula in any patient with unexplained altered mental status; alkalotic pH with high AG + low PCO₂ below expected compensation = salicylate until proven otherwise; order serum salicylate level

**诊断:** 对任何不明原因意识改变患者计算阴离子间隙 + 应用 Winter 公式；碱性 pH 伴高 AG + PCO₂ 低于预期代偿值 = 水杨酸中毒，直到排除为止；应检测血清水杨酸盐浓度

**Treatment:** IV sodium bicarbonate infusion (urinary alkalinization + systemic alkalinization); hemodialysis for severe altered mental status, end-stage kidney disease, pulmonary edema, or clinical deterioration

**治疗:** 静脉碳酸氢钠输注（尿液碱化 + 全身碱化）；重度意识障碍、终末期肾病、肺水肿或临床恶化时行血液透析

## 4. Options Elimination / 错误选项排除逻辑

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 33%" />
<col style="width: 33%" />
<col style="width: 33%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Option</strong><br />
<strong>选项</strong></th>
<th><strong>Why Wrong</strong><br />
<strong>为什么错</strong></th>
<th><strong>Key Discriminator</strong><br />
<strong>鉴别要点</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>A — Alcoholic ketoacidosis<br />
A — 酒精性酮症酸中毒</td>
<td>History explicitly denies alcohol use; AKA causes high-AG metabolic acidosis but does NOT produce respiratory alkalosis; pH would be acidotic, not 7.43<br />
病史明确否认饮酒；AKA 引起高 AG 代谢性酸中毒但<strong>不</strong>产生呼吸性碱中毒；pH 应偏酸，而非 7.43</td>
<td>AKA: requires alcohol history, low/normal glucose, pH acidotic, no independent respiratory alkalosis<br />
AKA：需有饮酒史、血糖低/正常、pH 偏酸、无独立呼吸性碱中毒</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>B — Diabetic ketoacidosis<br />
B — 糖尿病酮症酸中毒</td>
<td>Glucose only 120 mg/dL (DKA typically &gt;250); urine glucose negative (DKA should be positive); no known diabetes; DKA produces metabolic acidosis without respiratory alkalosis → pH would be acidotic<br />
血糖仅 120 mg/dL（DKA 通常 &gt;250）；尿糖阴性（DKA 应为阳性）；无糖尿病史；DKA 产生代谢性酸中毒而无呼吸性碱中毒 → pH 应偏酸</td>
<td>DKA: glucose &gt;250 mg/dL, urine glucose 3+, pH acidotic (not 7.43), no independent respiratory alkalosis<br />
DKA：血糖 &gt;250 mg/dL，尿糖 3+，pH 偏酸（非 7.43），无独立呼吸性碱中毒</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>C — Ethylene glycol toxicity<br />
C — 乙二醇中毒</td>
<td>Serum osmolality 290 is normal — EG is osmotically active and creates a significant osmolar gap (&gt;10 mOsmol/kg); also presents with acute kidney injury and oxalate crystals on urinalysis<br />
血清渗透压 290 正常——乙二醇具有渗透活性，会产生显著渗透压差（&gt;10 mOsmol/kg）；还伴有急性肾损伤和尿草酸钙结晶</td>
<td>EG: elevated osmolality with osmolar gap &gt;10, AKI, urinary calcium oxalate crystals, no urine ketones<br />
乙二醇：渗透压升高且渗透压差 &gt;10，AKI，尿草酸钙结晶，无尿酮体</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>D — Methanol toxicity<br />
D — 甲醇中毒</td>
<td>Normal osmolality rules out methanol (also osmotically active → osmolar gap &gt;10); methanol's hallmark is visual disturbances and optic neuropathy from formic acid, absent here<br />
渗透压正常排除甲醇（同样具有渗透活性 → 渗透压差 &gt;10）；甲醇的标志性表现是甲酸引起的视觉障碍和视神经病变，本例无此表现</td>
<td>MeOH: osmolar gap &gt;10, visual disturbances, optic disc hyperemia, putaminal hemorrhage, no ketones<br />
甲醇：渗透压差 &gt;10，视觉障碍，视盘充血，豆状核出血，无尿酮体</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>E — Salicylate toxicity ✓<br />
E — 水杨酸中毒 ✓</td>
<td>CORRECT — only cause of mixed respiratory alkalosis + high-AG metabolic acidosis with alkalotic pH, normal osmolality, and positive urine ketones in a young patient with unexplained altered mental status<br />
正确——唯一可引起混合型呼吸性碱中毒 + 高 AG 代谢性酸中毒、pH 偏碱、渗透压正常、尿酮体阳性的病因，见于不明原因意识改变的年轻患者</td>
<td>Mixed acid-base (respiratory alkalosis dominant) + normal osmolality + urine ketones + no hyperglycemia = salicylate<br />
混合型酸碱紊乱（呼吸性碱中毒主导）+ 渗透压正常 + 尿酮体 + 无高血糖 = 水杨酸中毒</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

*The most dangerous distractor is DKA (Choice B) due to the 3+ urine ketones — the pivot clues are the blood glucose (only 120, not \>250), negative urine glucose, and the alkalotic pH 7.43 (DKA is acidotic), which decisively rule it out.*

DKA（B 选项）因尿酮体 3+ 最具迷惑性——关键鉴别点是血糖（仅 120，而非 \>250）、尿糖阴性、以及碱性 pH 7.43（DKA 应为酸性），三点合并可决定性排除 DKA。

## 5. High-Yield Summary Table — Salicylate Toxicity vs DKA/AKA vs Toxic Alcohols / 水杨酸中毒 vs DKA/酒精性KA vs 有毒醇类中毒

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 25%" />
<col style="width: 25%" />
<col style="width: 25%" />
<col style="width: 25%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Feature</strong><br />
<strong>特征</strong></th>
<th><strong>Salicylate Toxicity</strong><br />
<strong>水杨酸中毒</strong></th>
<th><strong>DKA / Alcoholic KA</strong><br />
<strong>DKA / 酒精性酮症酸中毒</strong></th>
<th><strong>Ethylene Glycol / Methanol</strong><br />
<strong>乙二醇 / 甲醇</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>Acid-base pattern<br />
酸碱模式</td>
<td>Mixed: respiratory alkalosis + high-AG metabolic acidosis<br />
混合型：呼吸性碱中毒 + 高 AG 代谢性酸中毒</td>
<td>Pure high-AG metabolic acidosis<br />
单纯高 AG 代谢性酸中毒</td>
<td>High-AG metabolic acidosis<br />
高 AG 代谢性酸中毒</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Serum pH<br />
血清 pH</td>
<td>Alkalotic or near-normal (adults, early)<br />
偏碱或接近正常（成人，早期）</td>
<td>Acidotic (typically &lt; 7.3)<br />
偏酸（通常 &lt; 7.3）</td>
<td>Acidotic<br />
偏酸</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Osmolar gap<br />
渗透压差</td>
<td>None (normal osmolality)<br />
无（渗透压正常）</td>
<td>None<br />
无</td>
<td>Present (&gt; 10 mOsmol/kg)<br />
存在（&gt; 10 mOsmol/kg）</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Blood glucose<br />
血糖</td>
<td>Normal or mildly elevated<br />
正常或轻度升高</td>
<td>DKA: markedly elevated (&gt;250); AKA: normal or low<br />
DKA：显著升高（&gt;250）；AKA：正常或低</td>
<td>Normal<br />
正常</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Urine ketones<br />
尿酮体</td>
<td>Positive (ETC uncoupling)<br />
阳性（ETC 解偶联）</td>
<td>Positive (DKA and AKA)<br />
阳性（DKA 和 AKA 均阳性）</td>
<td>Negative<br />
阴性</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Classic distinguishing feature<br />
经典鉴别特征</td>
<td>Tinnitus, alkalotic pH, mixed acid-base pattern<br />
耳鸣、碱性 pH、混合型酸碱紊乱</td>
<td>DKA: polyuria/polydipsia, hyperglycemia; AKA: alcohol history, low glucose<br />
DKA：多尿/多饮、高血糖；AKA：饮酒史、低血糖</td>
<td>EG: oxalate crystals, AKI; MeOH: visual disturbances, optic neuropathy<br />
乙二醇：草酸钙结晶、AKI；甲醇：视觉障碍、视神经病变</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Treatment<br />
治疗</td>
<td>NaHCO₃ infusion ± hemodialysis<br />
碳酸氢钠输注 ± 血液透析</td>
<td>DKA: insulin + IV fluids; AKA: glucose + thiamine<br />
DKA：胰岛素 + 补液；AKA：葡萄糖 + 维生素 B₁</td>
<td>Fomepizole (ADH inhibitor) + hemodialysis<br />
甲吡唑（醇脱氢酶抑制剂）+ 血液透析</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

## 6. One-Sentence Summary & Memory Hook / 一句话总结 & 记忆钩

**A young patient with altered mental status, tachypnea, alkalotic pH, high anion gap metabolic acidosis, normal serum osmolality, and positive urine ketones without hyperglycemia has salicylate toxicity until proven otherwise.**

**意识改变的年轻患者，伴呼吸急促、碱性 pH、高阴离子间隙代谢性酸中毒、血清渗透压正常、无高血糖但尿酮体阳性，水杨酸中毒在排除前应首先考虑。**

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 100%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><p><strong>Memory Hook — THANE for Salicylate Toxicity Clinical Features / 记忆钩 — "THANE" 记忆水杨酸中毒临床特征:</strong></p>
<p>• <strong>T</strong>innitus — hallmark symptom; virtually absent in DKA, AKA, and toxic alcohols / 耳鸣——标志性症状；DKA、AKA 及有毒醇类中毒几乎不出现<br />
• <strong>H</strong>yperventilation (respiratory alkalosis) — direct medullary respiratory center stimulation / 过度通气（呼吸性碱中毒）——直接刺激延髓呼吸中枢<br />
• <strong>A</strong>ltered mental status / Agitation — encephalopathy, delirium, hallucinations / 意识改变/烦躁——脑病、谵妄、幻觉<br />
• <strong>N</strong>ausea / GI upset — direct gastric irritation by salicylate / 恶心/胃肠道不适——水杨酸盐直接刺激胃黏膜<br />
• <strong>E</strong>levated anion gap (metabolic acidosis) — delayed ETC uncoupling effect, appears hours after ingestion / 阴离子间隙升高（代谢性酸中毒）——ETC 解偶联的延迟效应，摄入数小时后出现</p></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
</tbody>
</table>

## 7. High-Yield Topic Knowledge — Salicylate Toxicity & Mixed Acid-Base Disorders / 高频知识表 — 水杨酸中毒与混合型酸碱紊乱

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 50%" />
<col style="width: 50%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Topic</strong><br />
<strong>考点</strong></th>
<th><strong>Key Points</strong><br />
<strong>要点</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>Salicylate acid-base signature<br />
水杨酸盐酸碱标志</td>
<td>Mixed respiratory alkalosis + high-AG metabolic acidosis; adults → alkalotic or near-normal pH (respiratory dominates); children → acidotic pH (metabolic dominates); this "double disorder" is essentially pathognomonic<br />
混合型呼吸性碱中毒 + 高 AG 代谢性酸中毒；成人 → pH 偏碱或接近正常（呼吸占主导）；儿童 → pH 偏酸（代谢占主导）；此"双重紊乱"几乎具有诊断特异性</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Winter's formula for compensation check<br />
Winter 公式核查代偿</td>
<td>Expected PCO₂ = 1.5 × HCO₃⁻ + 8 ± 2; if actual PCO₂ &lt; expected lower bound → additional independent respiratory alkalosis; this case: expected 25.5–29.5, actual 22 → confirms superimposed respiratory alkalosis<br />
预期 PCO₂ = 1.5 × HCO₃⁻ + 8 ± 2；若实际 PCO₂ &lt; 预期下限 → 存在额外的独立呼吸性碱中毒；本题：预期 25.5–29.5，实际 22 → 确认叠加性呼吸性碱中毒</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Osmolar gap interpretation<br />
渗透压差解读</td>
<td>Measured − calculated osmolality; calculated = 2×Na + glucose/18 + BUN/2.8; normal gap &lt; 10 mOsmol/kg; gap &gt; 10 → toxic alcohols (EG, MeOH, isopropanol, ethanol); salicylate does NOT cause osmolar gap<br />
实测 − 计算渗透压；计算值 = 2×Na + 血糖/18 + BUN/2.8；正常差值 &lt; 10 mOsmol/kg；差值 &gt; 10 → 有毒醇类（乙二醇、甲醇、异丙醇、乙醇）；水杨酸盐<strong>不</strong>引起渗透压差</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Salicylate treatment: NaHCO₃ rationale<br />
水杨酸中毒治疗：碳酸氢钠的原理</td>
<td>(1) Alkaline blood → more ionized (charged) salicylate → cannot cross blood-brain barrier → less CNS toxicity; (2) Alkaline urine → ionized drug trapped in tubule → increased renal excretion; target urine pH 7.5–8.0<br />
（1）碱性血液 → 更多电离型水杨酸盐 → 无法穿过血脑屏障 → CNS 毒性减少；（2）碱性尿液 → 电离药物滞留于肾小管 → 增加肾脏排泄；目标尿液 pH 7.5–8.0</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Dialysis indications in salicylate toxicity<br />
水杨酸中毒血液透析指征</td>
<td>Severe altered mental status, end-stage kidney disease, pulmonary edema, clinical deterioration despite treatment; dialysis effectively removes salicylate directly<br />
严重意识障碍、终末期肾病、肺水肿、治疗后临床恶化；血液透析可直接有效清除水杨酸盐</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Covert ingestion in history<br />
病史中的隐性摄入问题</td>
<td>Aspirin is OTC; young adults may ingest for self-harm without disclosing; family members may not know; "no medications" does not exclude salicylate; always check serum salicylate level in unexplained mixed acid-base disorders<br />
阿司匹林无需处方；年轻人可能因自伤目的而隐瞒摄入；家属可能不知情；"未服药"不能排除水杨酸盐摄入；不明原因混合型酸碱紊乱应常规检测血清水杨酸盐浓度</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Pitfall: acetazolamide contraindicated<br />
陷阱：乙酰唑胺禁忌</td>
<td>Acetazolamide inhibits carbonic anhydrase → alkaline urine (good) but acidic blood (bad) → more unionized salicylate in blood → increased CNS penetration → worsens toxicity; avoid in salicylate poisoning<br />
乙酰唑胺抑制碳酸酐酶 → 碱性尿（有益）但酸性血（有害）→ 血液中更多非电离型水杨酸盐 → CNS 渗透增加 → 加重中毒；水杨酸中毒时禁用</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

## 8. Extensions / 延伸扩展

- **Differential of mixed respiratory alkalosis + high-AG metabolic acidosis:** Salicylate toxicity is the classic and most testable cause; also consider sepsis (lactic acidosis + reflex hyperventilation) and severe hepatic failure (hyperammonemia stimulates breathing + lactic acidosis)\
  **呼吸性碱中毒 + 高 AG 代谢性酸中毒混合型鉴别:** 水杨酸中毒是经典且最常考的病因；也需考虑脓毒症（乳酸酸中毒 + 反射性过度通气）和严重肝衰竭（高氨血症刺激呼吸 + 乳酸酸中毒）

- **Pediatric vs adult salicylate toxicity pattern:** Children predominantly develop metabolic acidosis (pH acidotic) due to immature respiratory compensation; adults show respiratory alkalosis dominance early (pH alkalotic); do not be reassured by alkalotic pH — it does not exclude severe poisoning\
  **儿童 vs 成人水杨酸中毒模式:** 儿童因呼吸代偿不成熟，主要表现为代谢性酸中毒（pH 偏酸）；成人早期以呼吸性碱中毒为主（pH 偏碱）；碱性 pH 不能让人放松警惕——不能排除严重中毒

- **Key complication — non-cardiogenic pulmonary edema:** Salicylate increases capillary permeability; pulmonary edema can develop without cardiac dysfunction; presence of pulmonary edema is an absolute indication for hemodialysis regardless of other parameters\
  **关键并发症——非心源性肺水肿:** 水杨酸盐增加毛细血管通透性；可在无心脏功能障碍的情况下发生肺水肿；肺水肿的出现是血液透析的绝对指征，无论其他参数如何

- **Toxic alcohol differentiation mnemonic:** Osmolar gap present → think EG/MeOH/isopropanol; osmolar gap absent + high AG → think salicylate, lactic acidosis, DKA, uremia; osmolar gap present + high AG → late EG/MeOH (toxic metabolites formed, parent compound metabolized)\
  **有毒醇类鉴别助记:** 渗透压差存在 → 考虑乙二醇/甲醇/异丙醇；渗透压差不存在 + 高 AG → 考虑水杨酸盐、乳酸酸中毒、DKA、尿毒症；渗透压差存在 + 高 AG → 乙二醇/甲醇晚期（有毒代谢产物已形成，母体化合物已代谢）

# Question 172 — Delayed Primary Closure for Contaminated Abdominal Wound / 污染腹部伤口的延迟一期闭合

## Question Stem / 题干

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 100%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><p>A <strong>25-year-old man</strong> is brought to the emergency department <strong>1 hour</strong> after sustaining a <strong>gunshot wound to the abdomen</strong>. He has pain at the bullet entry site. He is awake, alert, and appropriately conversant. His temperature is <strong>38.8°C (101.8°F)</strong>, pulse is 85/min, respirations are 18/min, and blood pressure is 128/70 mm Hg. Abdominal examination shows a bullet wound <strong>5 cm to the right of the umbilicus</strong>. There is moderate tenderness over the entry site. The remainder of the examination shows no abnormalities. During operative exploration, <strong>250 mL of succus entericus</strong> and <strong>eight small bowel holes</strong> are found in the abdomen; the bowel holes are treated by resection of 12 cm of proximal ileum. The intestine is reconstructed with a stapled anastomosis. The midline abdominal fascia is sutured closed. Which of the following methods of skin and soft tissue wound management at this point is most likely to decrease the risk for postoperative wound infection?</p>
<p><strong>Q: Which wound management method is most likely to decrease postoperative infection risk?</strong></p>
<p>A) Delayed primary closure<br />
B) Hand-sewn suture closure of the skin<br />
C) Use of skin staples<br />
D) Application of cyanoacrylate adhesive to the wound<br />
E) Split-thickness skin graft</p>
<p><strong>Correct Answer: A</strong></p></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
</tbody>
</table>

## 1. Key Stem Clues / 题干关键词抓考点

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 50%" />
<col style="width: 50%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Key Stem Clue</strong><br />
<strong>关键词</strong></th>
<th><strong>Why It Matters</strong><br />
<strong>为什么重要</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>Gunshot wound to abdomen<br />
腹部枪伤</td>
<td>Traumatic mechanism → high contamination risk, classifies as Class IV wound<br />
外伤性机制 → 高污染风险，归为IV类伤口</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Temperature 38.8°C pre-operatively<br />
术前体温 38.8°C</td>
<td>Pre-op fever signals active infection already underway, not just contamination risk<br />
术前发热提示感染已经存在，而非仅有污染风险</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>250 mL succus entericus<br />
250 mL 肠液</td>
<td>Small bowel contents spilled into peritoneum → gross intraperitoneal contamination<br />
小肠内容物溢入腹腔 → 严重腹腔内污染</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Eight small bowel holes<br />
8 个小肠破口</td>
<td>Multiple perforations = extensive fecal/enteric contamination of wound layers<br />
多处穿孔 = 伤口各层受到广泛肠道污染</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Fascia already sutured closed<br />
筋膜已缝合关闭</td>
<td>Question targets only skin/subcutaneous tissue management, not abdominal re-entry<br />
问题专指皮肤和皮下组织处理，不涉及腹腔再次进入</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Resection of proximal ileum, stapled anastomosis<br />
近端回肠切除，钉合器吻合</td>
<td>Bowel surgery + contamination = dirty operative field even after irrigation<br />
肠道手术+污染 = 即使冲洗后术野仍为污染环境</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

## 2. Mechanism / 机制理解

**Wound classification** drives the closure decision: Class IV **dirty/infected** wounds (traumatic injuries with devitalized tissue or **fecal/enteric contamination**) carry SSI rates of 10–40% with immediate closure:

**伤口分级**决定闭合策略：IV类**污染/感染**伤口（含坏死组织或**粪便/肠道污染**的外伤性伤口）若立即缝合，SSI发生率高达10-40%：

- Immediate skin closure → seals bacteria into subcutaneous tissue → oxygen-poor environment favors anaerobic growth → abscess\
  立即缝合皮肤 → 细菌封锁于皮下组织 → 低氧环境有利于厌氧菌生长 → 脓肿形成

- Delayed primary closure (DPC): skin/subcutaneous left open 3–5 days with moist packing or NPWT → allows exudate drainage and daily debridement\
  延迟一期闭合（DPC）：皮肤/皮下组织留开3-5天，湿纱布填塞或负压治疗 → 允许渗液引流和每日清创

- At day 3–5 reassessment: if no purulence, erythema, or fever → wound closed primarily; bacterial load has decreased sufficiently\
  3-5天后复评：若无脓液、红斑或发热 → 行一期缝合；细菌负荷已充分降低

- NPWT (−125 mmHg): removes fluid, promotes granulation tissue, reduces edema in wound edges\
  负压治疗（-125 mmHg）：去除液体，促进肉芽组织形成，减轻伤口边缘水肿

**Anatomic rule of thumb:** Even in grossly contaminated wounds, the deep fascia can be closed to protect abdominal viscera; the skin and subcutaneous tissue (superficial layers) must be left open to drain in Class III–IV wounds.

**解剖小窍门:** 即使在严重污染的伤口中，深筋膜也可缝合以保护腹腔脏器；但皮肤和皮下组织（浅层）在III-IV类伤口中必须留开以引流。

## 3. Correct Answer (A) — Delayed Primary Closure / 正确答案 (A) — 延迟一期闭合

**Delayed primary closure (DPC)** intentionally leaves the skin and subcutaneous tissue open at initial surgery, creating a managed open wound that drains bacterial contamination before definitive closure at 3–5 days:

**延迟一期闭合（DPC）**在初次手术时有意将皮肤和皮下组织留开，形成可管理的开放伤口，在3-5天后的最终缝合前引流细菌污染：

- Wound packed with moist saline gauze (or NPWT device placed) immediately after fascial closure\
  筋膜缝合后立即用湿盐水纱布填塞伤口（或放置负压治疗装置）

- Daily wound checks: assess for purulence, cellulitis, necrosis; debride as needed\
  每日伤口检查：评估脓液、蜂窝织炎、坏死；必要时清创

- Re-closure at day 3–5 if wound appears clean: sutures or staples placed at bedside or in OR\
  3-5天后若伤口清洁则重新缝合：在床旁或手术室缝合

- SSI rate significantly lower than immediate closure for Class IV wounds\
  IV类伤口的SSI率显著低于立即缝合

**Diagnosis:** This patient has a textbook Class IV wound: traumatic gunshot injury + 250 mL succus entericus + 8 bowel holes + pre-operative fever of 38.8°C — all criteria for DPC over immediate skin closure.

**诊断:** 该患者为典型的IV类伤口：外伤性枪伤 + 250 mL肠液 + 8个肠穿孔 + 术前体温38.8°C — 这些均支持DPC而非立即缝合皮肤。

**Treatment:** Close fascia → leave skin/subcutaneous open → pack with moist gauze or apply NPWT → return to OR or bedside at 3–5 days for delayed closure once wound is clean and patient afebrile.

**治疗:** 缝合筋膜 → 皮肤/皮下留开 → 湿纱布填塞或负压治疗 → 3-5天后返回手术室或床旁，待伤口清洁、患者退热后行延迟缝合。

## 4. Options Elimination / 错误选项排除逻辑

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 33%" />
<col style="width: 33%" />
<col style="width: 33%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Option</strong><br />
<strong>选项</strong></th>
<th><strong>Why Wrong</strong><br />
<strong>为什么错</strong></th>
<th><strong>Key Discriminator</strong><br />
<strong>鉴别要点</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>A — Delayed primary closure ✓<br />
A — 延迟一期闭合 ✓</td>
<td>CORRECT — Standard of care for Class IV contaminated wounds; allows drainage and reassessment before closure<br />
正确——IV类污染伤口的标准治疗；允许缝合前引流和重新评估</td>
<td>Only method that fully opens wound to environment; maximally reduces SSI by drainage<br />
唯一使伤口完全开放的方法；通过引流最大程度降低SSI</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>B — Hand-sewn suture closure<br />
B — 手工缝合皮肤</td>
<td>Completely seals wound → traps bacteria in contaminated subcutaneous tissue → abscess or wound dehiscence<br />
完全封闭伤口 → 细菌封锁于污染的皮下组织 → 脓肿或伤口裂开</td>
<td>No drainage possible with complete closure in infected field<br />
感染环境中完全缝合后无法引流</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>C — Use of skin staples<br />
C — 皮肤钉合器</td>
<td>Allows some drainage between staples (better than sutures), but gaps are insufficient for grossly contaminated wounds; DPC remains superior<br />
钉合器间允许少量引流（优于缝合），但对严重污染伤口引流不足；DPC仍更优</td>
<td>Incomplete drainage vs. fully open wound in Class IV scenario<br />
IV类场景中引流不充分，不及完全开放伤口</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>D — Cyanoacrylate adhesive<br />
D — 氰基丙烯酸酯粘合剂</td>
<td>Absolutely contraindicated in contaminated/infected tissue; approved only for small, clean, superficial lacerations under low tension<br />
污染/感染组织绝对禁忌；仅用于小型、清洁、低张力浅表撕裂伤</td>
<td>Contamination = absolute contraindication to tissue adhesive<br />
污染 = 组织粘合剂的绝对禁忌证</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>E — Split-thickness skin graft<br />
E — 断层皮片移植</td>
<td>No significant tissue loss in this case; grafts contraindicated in infected beds; used for burns or large traumatic tissue defects<br />
此例无明显组织缺损；植皮禁用于感染创面；用于烧伤或大面积外伤组织缺损</td>
<td>Tissue present and viable — graft is overtreatment and would fail in contaminated field<br />
组织存在且有活力——植皮为过度治疗，且在污染创面会失败</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

*The most tempting distractor is C (staples) — students recall that staples reduce SSI vs. sutures in clean wounds, but fail to recognize that DPC (leaving the wound entirely open) is the appropriate strategy when gross contamination precludes any immediate closure.*

最诱人的干扰项是C（钉合器）——学生记得清洁伤口中钉合器比缝合更能降低SSI，但未能认识到在严重污染时，DPC（完全开放伤口）才是正确策略，任何形式的立即缝合均不适用。

## 5. High-Yield Summary Table — Wound Classification & Closure Strategy / 伤口分级与皮肤闭合策略

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 33%" />
<col style="width: 33%" />
<col style="width: 33%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Feature</strong><br />
<strong>特征</strong></th>
<th><strong>Class I–II (Clean / Clean-contaminated)</strong><br />
<strong>I-II类（清洁/清洁-污染）</strong></th>
<th><strong>Class III–IV (Contaminated / Dirty-infected)</strong><br />
<strong>III-IV类（污染/感染）</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>Examples<br />
代表性例子</td>
<td>Elective hernia repair, cholecystectomy without spillage<br />
择期疝修补、无溢漏胆囊切除术</td>
<td>Gunshot + bowel perforation, fecal spillage, drained abscess<br />
枪伤+肠穿孔、粪便溢漏、脓肿引流</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>SSI rate (without prophylaxis)<br />
SSI率（无预防措施）</td>
<td>1–5%<br />
1-5%</td>
<td>10–40%<br />
10-40%</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Fascia management<br />
筋膜处理</td>
<td>Close primarily<br />
一期缝合</td>
<td>Close primarily (protect viscera)<br />
一期缝合（保护脏器）</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Skin/subcutaneous management<br />
皮肤/皮下处理</td>
<td>Primary closure (sutures or staples)<br />
一期缝合（缝线或钉合器）</td>
<td>Leave OPEN → delayed primary closure at day 3–5<br />
留开 → 第3-5天延迟一期缝合</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Interim wound dressing<br />
暂时性伤口敷料</td>
<td>Standard sterile dressing<br />
标准无菌敷料</td>
<td>Moist saline gauze packing or NPWT<br />
湿盐水纱布填塞或负压治疗</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Closure timing<br />
缝合时机</td>
<td>Immediate (at time of surgery)<br />
即刻（术中）</td>
<td>Delayed 3–5 days after confirming clean wound<br />
确认伤口清洁后延迟3-5天</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

## 6. One-Sentence Summary & Memory Hook / 一句话总结 & 记忆钩

**For Class IV (dirty/contaminated) abdominal wounds, close the fascia but leave the skin and subcutaneous tissue open for delayed primary closure at 3–5 days to allow bacterial drainage and minimize surgical site infection.**

**对于IV类（污染/感染）腹部伤口，缝合筋膜，但皮肤和皮下组织留开，3-5天后行延迟一期缝合，以允许细菌引流并最大程度降低手术部位感染。**

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 100%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><p><strong>Memory Hook — D.R.A.I.N. Rule for Dirty Wounds / 记忆钩 — 污染伤口的 D.R.A.I.N. 法则:</strong></p>
<p>• <strong>D</strong>irty wound (Class IV) → delay skin closure, never seal immediately / 污染伤口（IV类）→ 延迟缝合皮肤，切勿立即封闭<br />
• <strong>R</strong>eassess at day 3–5 → close only if clean, afebrile, no pus / 第3-5天复评 → 清洁、退热、无脓方可缝合<br />
• <strong>A</strong>bdominal fascia → close even in contaminated field (protects viscera) / 腹腔筋膜 → 即使污染也缝合（保护脏器）<br />
• <strong>I</strong>nfection prevented → by open drainage between dressing changes / 预防感染 → 通过换药期间开放引流实现<br />
• <strong>N</strong>PWT or moist gauze → the packing method of choice during the open interval / 负压治疗或湿纱布 → 开放期间首选填塞方式</p></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
</tbody>
</table>

## 7. High-Yield Topic Knowledge — Surgical Site Infection (SSI) / 高频知识表 — 手术部位感染（SSI）

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 50%" />
<col style="width: 50%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Topic</strong><br />
<strong>考点</strong></th>
<th><strong>Key Points</strong><br />
<strong>要点</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>Wound classification (Altemeier)<br />
伤口分级（Altemeier分类）</td>
<td>Class I clean → II clean-contaminated → III contaminated (fresh GI spillage) → IV dirty (pre-existing infection, perforated viscus, fecal contamination); drives closure and prophylaxis decisions<br />
I类清洁 → II类清洁-污染 → III类污染（新鲜胃肠溢漏）→ IV类感染（预存感染、脏器穿孔、粪便污染）；决定缝合和预防用药</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Delayed primary closure (DPC) mechanism<br />
延迟一期闭合机制</td>
<td>Wound left open allows drainage of bacteria and exudate; repeated debridement possible; closure once wound is visually clean and patient afebrile (day 3–5)<br />
伤口留开允许细菌和渗液引流；可反复清创；待伤口肉眼清洁且患者退热后缝合（第3-5天）</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>NPWT indications<br />
负压治疗适应证</td>
<td>Open wounds after DPC decision; applies −125 mmHg; removes exudate, reduces edema, promotes granulation; speeds wound readiness for closure<br />
DPC决策后的开放伤口；施加-125 mmHg负压；去除渗液、减轻水肿、促进肉芽生长；加速伤口准备好缝合</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>SSI risk factors<br />
SSI危险因素</td>
<td>Patient factors: DM, obesity, immunosuppression, smoking, malnutrition; operative factors: prolonged surgery &gt;2 hrs, blood transfusion, hypothermia, contaminated wound class<br />
患者因素：糖尿病、肥胖、免疫抑制、吸烟、营养不良；手术因素：手术&gt;2小时、输血、低体温、污染伤口分级</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>SSI presentation<br />
SSI的临床表现</td>
<td>Typically day 5–10 post-op; fever, wound erythema, induration, purulent drainage; deep SSI (organ/space) may present later with pain + systemic sepsis<br />
通常术后第5-10天；发热、伤口红斑、硬结、脓性引流；深部SSI（器官/间隙）可能更晚出现，伴疼痛和全身脓毒症</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Primary vs. secondary vs. tertiary intention<br />
一期/二期/三期愈合</td>
<td>Primary: immediate closure, heals fast, minimal scar; secondary: open wound granulates and epithelializes (months, large scar); tertiary (DPC): delayed closure after open period → best of both for contaminated wounds<br />
一期：立即缝合，愈合快，瘢痕小；二期：开放伤口肉芽化上皮化（数月，大瘢痕）；三期（DPC）：开放后延迟缝合 → 污染伤口的最佳选择</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

## 8. Extensions / 延伸扩展

- **Damage control surgery context:** in hemodynamically unstable trauma patients, the abdomen may be left entirely open (open abdomen) with a Bogota bag or mesh — DPC of the skin is a separate decision from fascial management\
  **损伤控制手术背景:** 血流动力学不稳定的创伤患者，腹腔可能完全留开（开放腹腔），用Bogota袋或补片覆盖——皮肤DPC是独立于筋膜处理的单独决策

- **Antibiotic prophylaxis timing:** given within 60 minutes of incision; for contaminated/dirty wounds, therapeutic (not just prophylactic) antibiotics continued post-op; does NOT replace DPC\
  **抗生素预防时机:** 切皮前60分钟内给药；对于污染/感染伤口，术后继续治疗性（非仅预防性）抗生素；不能替代DPC

- **Succus entericus vs. fecal matter:** succus (proximal small bowel content) is less bacterially dense than colonic feces but still causes significant SSI risk; the 8 holes + 250 mL volume = high inoculum regardless\
  **肠液vs粪便:** 肠液（近端小肠内容物）细菌密度低于结肠粪便，但仍有显著SSI风险；8个破口+250mL量 = 无论如何细菌接种量均高

- **Skin staples vs. sutures evidence:** RCTs show staples have modestly lower SSI rates than subcuticular sutures in clean orthopedic/obstetric wounds; this advantage does NOT extend to contaminated wounds where DPC dominates both\
  **钉合器vs缝线证据:** RCT显示在清洁骨科/产科伤口中钉合器SSI率略低于皮内缝合；该优势在污染伤口中不适用，DPC均优于两者

# Question 173 — Diabetic Ketoacidosis: Hormonal Profile / 糖尿病酮症酸中毒：激素谱变化

## Question Stem / 题干

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 100%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><p>A <strong>32-year-old woman</strong> comes to the physician because of a <strong>2-week history of fatigue and increased urination</strong>. She has had a <strong>2.3-kg (5-lb) weight loss</strong> despite eating more during this time. She has had two urinary tract infections in the past. She takes no medications. She does not smoke cigarettes, drink alcohol, or use illicit drugs. The patient is alert and fully oriented. She is 165 cm (5 ft 5 in) tall and weighs 52 kg (115 lb); <strong>BMI is 19 kg/m²</strong>. Her temperature is 36.5°C (97.7°F), <strong>pulse is 100/min</strong>, respirations are 20/min, and <strong>blood pressure is 90/60 mm Hg</strong>. Pulse oximetry on room air shows an oxygen saturation of 100%. The oropharynx is dry. The remainder of the examination shows no abnormalities. Laboratory studies show: Serum Na+ 142 mEq/L, K+ 5.4 mEq/L, Cl- 104 mEq/L, <strong>HCO3- 16 mEq/L</strong>, <strong>Glucose 800 mg/dL</strong>, Creatinine 1.3 mg/dL; Urine specific gravity 1.030, Bilirubin none, Protein none, RBC 0–5/hpf, WBC 25–50/hpf, Nitrites positive, Leukocyte esterase positive, Glucose &gt;1000 mg/24 h. Which of the following serum hormonal profiles is most consistent with this patient's presentation?</p>
<p><strong>Q: Which of the following serum hormonal profiles is most consistent with this patient's presentation?</strong></p>
<p>A) Insulin: Decreased, Glucagon: decreased, Catecholamines: decreased<br />
B) Insulin: Decreased, Glucagon: increased, Catecholamines: decreased<br />
C) Insulin: Decreased, Glucagon: decreased, Catecholamines: increased<br />
D) Insulin: Decreased, Glucagon: increased, Catecholamines: increased<br />
E) Insulin: Increased, Glucagon: increased, Catecholamines: decreased<br />
F) Insulin: Increased, Glucagon: decreased, Catecholamines: increased<br />
G) Insulin: Increased, Glucagon: decreased, Catecholamines: decreased<br />
H) Insulin: Increased, Glucagon: increased, Catecholamines: increased</p>
<p><strong>Correct Answer: D</strong></p></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
</tbody>
</table>

## 1. Key Stem Clues / 题干关键词抓考点

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 50%" />
<col style="width: 50%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Key Stem Clue</strong><br />
<strong>关键词</strong></th>
<th><strong>Why It Matters</strong><br />
<strong>为什么重要</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>32-year-old woman, BMI 19 kg/m² (thin), no medications<br />
32岁女性，BMI 19 kg/m²（偏瘦），无服药史</td>
<td>Thin young patient with new-onset hyperglycemia → Type 1 DM (autoimmune beta-cell destruction), not T2DM; T1DM = absolute insulin deficiency<br />
偏瘦年轻患者新发高血糖 → 1型糖尿病（自身免疫β细胞破坏），而非2型；1型糖尿病=绝对胰岛素缺乏</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Polyuria + weight loss despite eating more (polyphagia)<br />
多尿+进食增多却体重下降（多食）</td>
<td>Classic DM triad (polyuria, polydipsia, polyphagia + weight loss); without insulin, cells cannot uptake glucose → perceived starvation → counterregulatory hormones activated<br />
糖尿病经典三联征（多尿、多饮、多食+体重下降）；无胰岛素则细胞无法摄取葡萄糖→感知性饥饿→反调节激素激活</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Glucose 800 mg/dL; Urine glucose &gt;1000 mg/24h<br />
血糖800 mg/dL；尿糖&gt;1000 mg/24h</td>
<td>Severe hyperglycemia confirms DM; glucose spills into urine when serum exceeds renal threshold (~180 mg/dL); glucagon-driven gluconeogenesis and glycogenolysis contribute<br />
严重高血糖确诊糖尿病；血糖超过肾阈值（~180 mg/dL）时葡萄糖溢入尿液；胰高糖素驱动的糖异生和糖原分解加剧高血糖</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>HCO3- 16 mEq/L; Anion gap = 142 − (104 + 16) = 22<br />
HCO3- 16 mEq/L；阴离子间隙 = 22</td>
<td>High anion gap metabolic acidosis → ketoacidosis from accumulation of beta-hydroxybutyrate and acetoacetate; bicarbonate consumed buffering ketoacids<br />
高阴离子间隙代谢性酸中毒 → 酮症酸中毒（β羟丁酸和乙酰乙酸积累）；碳酸氢盐被消耗于缓冲酮酸</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Tachycardia (100/min), hypotension (90/60 mmHg), dry oropharynx<br />
心动过速（100次/分），低血压（90/60 mmHg），口咽干燥</td>
<td>Severe dehydration from osmotic diuresis; also reflects acute physiologic stress → catecholamine surge (sympathoadrenal axis activation)<br />
渗透性利尿导致严重脱水；同时反映急性生理应激 → 儿茶酚胺激增（交感-肾上腺轴激活）</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>WBC 25–50/hpf, nitrites positive, leukocyte esterase positive<br />
尿WBC 25–50/hpf，亚硝酸盐阳性，白细胞酯酶阳性</td>
<td>Active UTI is the precipitating factor for DKA; infection triggers catecholamine release and induces insulin resistance, worsening ketogenesis<br />
活动性UTI是DKA的诱发因素；感染触发儿茶酚胺释放并诱导胰岛素抵抗，加重酮体生成</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>K+ 5.4 mEq/L (mildly elevated)<br />
K+ 5.4 mEq/L（轻度升高）</td>
<td>Transcellular K+ shift out of cells due to acidosis (H+/K+ exchange) and insulin deficiency; apparent hyperkalemia masks total body K+ depletion — critical for management<br />
因酸中毒（H+/K+交换）和胰岛素缺乏导致K+从细胞内外移；表面高钾掩盖体内总K+耗竭——对处理至关重要</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

## 2. Mechanism / 机制理解

In **Type 1 DM**, autoimmune destruction of pancreatic **beta cells** eliminates **insulin** production. Without insulin, cells cannot uptake glucose and enter **perceived starvation**, triggering a cascade of counterregulatory responses:

在**1型糖尿病**中，胰腺**β细胞**遭自身免疫性破坏，**胰岛素**分泌丧失。无胰岛素时细胞无法摄取葡萄糖，进入**感知性饥饿**状态，触发一系列反调节响应：

- **Glucagon** rises because insulin normally tonically suppresses alpha-cell glucagon secretion — without insulin, glucagon is disinhibited; perceived starvation further stimulates alpha cells to mobilize fuel\
  **胰高糖素**升高：胰岛素正常情况下持续抑制α细胞的胰高糖素分泌——胰岛素缺失后去抑制；感知性饥饿进一步刺激α细胞动员燃料

- **Glucagon** promotes glycogenolysis, gluconeogenesis, and critically **lipolysis** → free fatty acids flood to liver → β-oxidation → acetyl-CoA overflow → **ketogenesis** (beta-hydroxybutyrate, acetoacetate, acetone)\
  **胰高糖素**促进糖原分解、糖异生，关键的是促进**脂肪分解** → 游离脂肪酸大量流向肝脏 → β氧化 → 乙酰辅酶A溢出 → **酮体生成**（β羟丁酸、乙酰乙酸、丙酮）

- **Catecholamines** (epinephrine, norepinephrine) surge from acute physiologic stress: hypotension, dehydration, acidosis, and concurrent UTI; they independently stimulate lipolysis via beta-adrenergic receptors on adipocytes, amplifying ketone production\
  **儿茶酚胺**（肾上腺素、去甲肾上腺素）因急性生理应激激增：低血压、脱水、酸中毒和并发UTI；通过脂肪细胞β肾上腺素受体独立刺激脂肪分解，放大酮体生成

**Pathophysiologic rule of thumb:** In DKA, two counterregulatory hormones go UP (glucagon, catecholamines) and one goes DOWN (insulin) — the "2-up, 1-down" pattern driven by starvation + stress.

**病理生理小窍门:** DKA中两种反调节激素升高（胰高糖素、儿茶酚胺），一种降低（胰岛素）——由饥饿+应激共同驱动的"2升1降"模式。

## 3. Correct Answer (D) — DKA Counterregulatory Hormonal Profile / 正确答案 (D) — DKA反调节激素谱

**Diabetic Ketoacidosis (DKA)** arises from absolute insulin deficiency in T1DM, producing the triad of hyperglycemia, ketonemia, and high anion gap metabolic acidosis with a characteristic three-hormone pattern:

**糖尿病酮症酸中毒（DKA）**源于1型糖尿病的绝对胰岛素缺乏，产生高血糖、酮血症和高阴离子间隙代谢性酸中毒三联征，伴有特征性三激素模式：

- Insulin: decreased — autoimmune beta-cell destruction in T1DM leaves no insulin-secreting cells\
  胰岛素：降低——1型糖尿病自身免疫性β细胞破坏，无胰岛素分泌细胞残余

- Glucagon: increased — insulin removal disinhibits alpha cells; perceived cellular starvation drives glucagon-mediated lipolysis and ketogenesis\
  胰高糖素：升高——胰岛素去除解除对α细胞的抑制；细胞感知性饥饿驱动胰高糖素介导的脂肪分解和酮体生成

- Catecholamines: increased — sympathoadrenal response to acute stress (dehydration, hypotension, acidosis, UTI); also directly promotes lipolysis synergistically with glucagon\
  儿茶酚胺：升高——对急性应激的交感-肾上腺反应（脱水、低血压、酸中毒、UTI）；也与胰高糖素协同直接促进脂肪分解

**Diagnosis:** Young thin patient (T1DM risk) + new-onset DM triad + glucose 800 + HCO3 16 + anion gap 22 + concurrent UTI as precipitant → DKA as first presentation of T1DM

**诊断:** 年轻偏瘦患者（1型糖尿病风险）+ 新发糖尿病三联征 + 血糖800 + HCO3 16 + 阴离子间隙22 + UTI作为诱因 → 1型糖尿病首次发作DKA

**Treatment:** IV 0.9% NaCl bolus → insulin drip (regular insulin 0.1 units/kg/hr) → potassium replacement (before insulin if K+ \< 3.5; concurrently if 3.5–5.5) → antibiotics for UTI → monitor glucose, AG, and electrolytes every 1–2 hours

**治疗:** 静脉0.9% NaCl快速输注 → 胰岛素滴注（普通胰岛素0.1单位/kg/小时）→ 钾替代（K+\<3.5时先补钾再用胰岛素；K+3.5–5.5时同步）→ 抗生素治疗UTI → 每1–2小时监测血糖、阴离子间隙和电解质

## 4. Options Elimination / 错误选项排除逻辑

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 33%" />
<col style="width: 33%" />
<col style="width: 33%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Option</strong><br />
<strong>选项</strong></th>
<th><strong>Why Wrong</strong><br />
<strong>为什么错</strong></th>
<th><strong>Key Discriminator</strong><br />
<strong>鉴别要点</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>A — Insulin ↓, Glucagon ↓, Catecholamines ↓<br />
A — 胰岛素↓，胰高糖素↓，儿茶酚胺↓</td>
<td>Both counterregulatory hormones are down — impossible; absent insulin disinhibits glucagon, and severe stress (hypotension, infection) must activate the sympathoadrenal axis<br />
两种反调节激素均降低——不可能；胰岛素缺失解除对胰高糖素的抑制，严重应激（低血压、感染）必然激活交感-肾上腺轴</td>
<td>Cannot have ↓ glucagon when insulin is absent<br />
胰岛素缺失时胰高糖素不可能降低</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>B — Insulin ↓, Glucagon ↑, Catecholamines ↓<br />
B — 胰岛素↓，胰高糖素↑，儿茶酚胺↓</td>
<td>Glucagon is correctly elevated, but catecholamines cannot be down; this patient has hypotension (90/60), tachycardia, acidosis, and active infection — all potent sympathoadrenal triggers<br />
胰高糖素正确升高，但儿茶酚胺不可能降低；患者有低血压（90/60）、心动过速、酸中毒和活动性感染——均是强力交感-肾上腺触发因素</td>
<td>Physiologic stress always elevates catecholamines<br />
生理应激必然升高儿茶酚胺</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>C — Insulin ↓, Glucagon ↓, Catecholamines ↑<br />
C — 胰岛素↓，胰高糖素↓，儿茶酚胺↑</td>
<td>Glucagon is decreased — incorrect; insulin normally suppresses glucagon; when insulin disappears, glucagon is released from tonic inhibition and must rise<br />
胰高糖素降低——不正确；胰岛素正常情况下抑制胰高糖素；胰岛素消失后，胰高糖素从持续抑制中释放必然升高</td>
<td>Absent insulin = disinhibited glucagon = glucagon ↑<br />
胰岛素缺失=胰高糖素去抑制=胰高糖素升高</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>D — Insulin ↓, Glucagon ↑, Catecholamines ↑ ✓<br />
D — 胰岛素↓，胰高糖素↑，儿茶酚胺↑ ✓</td>
<td>CORRECT — beta-cell destruction → absent insulin; disinhibited alpha cells + perceived starvation → glucagon ↑ drives ketogenesis; dehydration + hypotension + UTI → catecholamines ↑ amplify lipolysis<br />
正确——β细胞破坏→胰岛素缺失；α细胞去抑制+感知性饥饿→胰高糖素↑驱动酮体生成；脱水+低血压+UTI→儿茶酚胺↑放大脂肪分解</td>
<td>Only combination consistent with T1DM DKA physiology<br />
唯一与1型糖尿病DKA病理生理一致的组合</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>E — Insulin ↑, Glucagon ↑, Catecholamines ↓<br />
E — 胰岛素↑，胰高糖素↑，儿茶酚胺↓</td>
<td>Insulin is elevated — wrong; T1DM has autoimmune destruction of beta cells with no insulin production; elevated insulin with elevated glucagon is also physiologically contradictory<br />
胰岛素升高——错误；1型糖尿病自身免疫破坏β细胞，无胰岛素产生；胰岛素升高同时胰高糖素升高在生理上也自相矛盾</td>
<td>T1DM = no beta cells = no insulin<br />
1型糖尿病=无β细胞=无胰岛素</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>F — Insulin ↑, Glucagon ↓, Catecholamines ↑<br />
F — 胰岛素↑，胰高糖素↓，儿茶酚胺↑</td>
<td>Insulin is elevated — wrong for T1DM; this pattern could represent a non-diabetic stress state (e.g., sepsis in a euglycemic patient) but cannot explain glucose 800 and ketoacidosis<br />
胰岛素升高——1型糖尿病不正确；此模式可能代表非糖尿病应激状态（如正常血糖患者脓毒症），但无法解释血糖800和酮症酸中毒</td>
<td>Glucose 800 + ketoacidosis requires insulin deficiency, not excess<br />
血糖800+酮症酸中毒需要胰岛素缺乏，而非过多</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>G — Insulin ↑, Glucagon ↓, Catecholamines ↓<br />
G — 胰岛素↑，胰高糖素↓，儿茶酚胺↓</td>
<td>Insulin elevated — wrong; this profile resembles the post-prandial anabolic state of a healthy person; opposite of what occurs in DKA<br />
胰岛素升高——错误；此谱系类似健康人餐后合成代谢状态；与DKA中发生的完全相反</td>
<td>This is the fed-state profile — DKA is the opposite of fed state<br />
这是进食状态激素谱——DKA与进食状态完全相反</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>H — Insulin ↑, Glucagon ↑, Catecholamines ↑<br />
H — 胰岛素↑，胰高糖素↑，儿茶酚胺↑</td>
<td>Insulin elevated — wrong; also, simultaneous elevation of insulin and glucagon is contradictory (insulin suppresses glucagon); this combination does not represent any coherent physiologic state<br />
胰岛素升高——错误；同时升高胰岛素和胰高糖素在生理上矛盾（胰岛素抑制胰高糖素）；此组合不代表任何连贯的生理状态</td>
<td>T1DM has absolute insulin deficiency — no scenario produces elevated insulin<br />
1型糖尿病为绝对胰岛素缺乏——任何情况下胰岛素都不会升高</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

*The most tempting distractor is B (insulin ↓, glucagon ↑, catecholamines ↓) — it correctly identifies glucagon elevation but forgets that severe physiologic stress (hypotension, dehydration, active infection) always triggers the sympathoadrenal axis, making catecholamine elevation mandatory in this clinical context.*

最容易出错的干扰项是B（胰岛素↓，胰高糖素↑，儿茶酚胺↓）——正确识别了胰高糖素升高，但忽视了严重生理应激（低血压、脱水、活动性感染）必然激活交感-肾上腺轴，在此临床情境下儿茶酚胺升高是必然的。

</tr>
