</tr>
<tr>
<td>D — Renal biopsy ✓<br />
D — 肾活检 ✓</td>
<td>CORRECT — Identifies ISN/RPS histologic class, which is essential for determining whether aggressive immunosuppression is warranted in this patient with urinary protein + blood<br />
正确——明确ISN/RPS组织学分类，对于决定该尿蛋白+血尿患者是否需要积极免疫抑制治疗至关重要</td>
<td>Direct determination of treatment intensity; UA alone cannot distinguish Class I/II from III/IV<br />
直接决定治疗强度；单凭尿检无法区分I/II类与III/IV类</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>E — X-rays of the knees<br />
E — 膝关节X线</td>
<td>SLE arthritis is nonerosive and nondeforming; x-rays will be normal and do not change management (NSAIDs/hydroxychloroquine/steroids are used regardless)<br />
SLE关节炎无侵蚀性和变形性；X线正常，且不改变管理（无论如何均用NSAIDs/羟氯喹/激素）</td>
<td>SLE joint disease is managed clinically, not radiographically; bone erosions on x-ray would suggest RA instead<br />
SLE关节病临床管理而非影像指导；X线骨侵蚀提示RA而非SLE</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

*The most tempting distractor is echocardiography given pleuritic chest pain, but the normal cardiac exam and pressing urinary findings make renal biopsy the management-determining investigation.*

胸膜炎性胸痛最容易使人选超声心动图，但正常心脏查体和突出的尿液异常使肾活检成为决定管理的关键检查。

## 6. One-Sentence Summary & Memory Hook / 一句话总结 & 记忆钩

**In a young woman with multiple SLE criteria and urinary protein + blood, renal biopsy is required to classify lupus nephritis (ISN/RPS Class I–VI) and determine whether aggressive immunosuppression is warranted.**

**对于满足多项SLE诊断标准并出现尿蛋白+血尿的年轻女性，必须行肾活检对狼疮性肾炎进行ISN/RPS I-VI类分型，以决定是否需要积极免疫抑制治疗。**

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 100%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><p><strong>Memory Hook — SLE SOAP criteria + Biopsy Rule / 记忆钩 — SLE"SOAP"诊断标准+活检法则:</strong></p>
<p>• <strong>S</strong>erositis (pleuritis/pericarditis) — chest pain with breathing = SLE serositis / 浆膜炎（胸膜/心包）——深呼吸胸痛=SLE浆膜炎<br />
• <strong>O</strong>ral ulcers (painless) — soft palate ulcers = classic SLE criterion / 口腔溃疡（无痛）——软腭溃疡=经典SLE标准<br />
• <strong>A</strong>rthritis (nonerosive) + <strong>A</strong>ntibodies (anti-dsDNA, anti-Sm) — joints swell but x-rays normal / 关节炎（无侵蚀性）+抗体——关节肿胀但X线正常<br />
• <strong>P</strong>roteinuria/hematuria → <strong>P</strong>erform biopsy — UA alone cannot determine class or treatment / 蛋白尿/血尿→必须<strong>活检</strong>——尿检无法决定分类或治疗</p></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
</tbody>
</table>

## 7. High-Yield Topic Knowledge — Lupus Nephritis Workup and Management / 高频知识表 — 狼疮性肾炎检查与管理

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 50%" />
<col style="width: 50%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Topic</strong><br />
<strong>考点</strong></th>
<th><strong>Key Points</strong><br />
<strong>要点</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>Indication for renal biopsy in SLE<br />
SLE肾活检指征</td>
<td>Any proteinuria &gt;500 mg/day or active urinary sediment (RBC casts, hematuria) in SLE patient; biopsy required to classify<br />
SLE患者蛋白尿&gt;500mg/天或活动性尿沉渣（RBC管型、血尿）均需活检分型</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>ISN/RPS Classification<br />
ISN/RPS分型</td>
<td>I: minimal mesangial; II: mesangial proliferative; III: focal (&lt;50% glomeruli); IV: diffuse (≥50%); V: membranous; VI: advanced sclerosing<br />
I类：轻微系膜性；II类：系膜增殖性；III类：局灶（&lt;50%肾小球）；IV类：弥漫（≥50%）；V类：膜性；VI类：硬化性</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Why biopsy changes management<br />
活检为何改变管理</td>
<td>Class I/II: no cytotoxic therapy; Class III/IV: mandatory induction immunosuppression; Class V: MMF + RAAS blockade; Class VI: consider dialysis planning<br />
I/II类：不用细胞毒药物；III/IV类：必须诱导免疫抑制；V类：MMF+RAAS阻断；VI类：考虑透析准备</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>SLE diagnostic criteria (SLICC 2012)<br />
SLE诊断标准（SLICC 2012）</td>
<td>≥4 of 11 criteria OR biopsy-proven lupus nephritis + ANA or anti-dsDNA; criteria include malar rash, oral ulcers, arthritis, serositis, renal, neuro, heme, immunologic, ANA<br />
满足11条中≥4条，或活检证实狼疮性肾炎+ANA或抗dsDNA；标准包括蝶形红斑、口腔溃疡、关节炎、浆膜炎、肾脏、神经、血液、免疫学、ANA</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Monitoring lupus nephritis activity<br />
监测狼疮性肾炎活动</td>
<td>Urinalysis + creatinine q3months; anti-dsDNA titers and C3/C4 complement levels (↓C3/C4 + ↑anti-dsDNA = flare); 24-hr urine protein or protein:creatinine ratio<br />
每3个月尿检+肌酐；抗dsDNA滴度和C3/C4补体（↓C3/C4+↑抗dsDNA=复发）；24小时尿蛋白或蛋白/肌酐比值</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Hydroxychloroquine role in all SLE<br />
羟氯喹在所有SLE中的作用</td>
<td>Background therapy for all SLE patients regardless of class; reduces flares, thrombotic events, and organ damage; monitor for retinal toxicity annually<br />
所有SLE患者的基础治疗，不分分类；减少复发、血栓事件和脏器损伤；每年监测视网膜毒性</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>SLE arthritis vs RA<br />
SLE关节炎vs类风湿关节炎</td>
<td>SLE: nonerosive, nondeforming, x-rays normal, anti-dsDNA/anti-Sm positive; RA: erosive, deforming, x-rays show erosions, RF/anti-CCP positive<br />
SLE：无侵蚀性、无变形，X线正常，抗dsDNA/抗Sm阳性；RA：侵蚀性、变形，X线有侵蚀，RF/抗CCP阳性</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

## 8. Extensions / 延伸扩展

- **Neuropsychiatric SLE (NPSLE):** Presents with seizures, psychosis, cognitive dysfunction, or stroke — evaluated with MRI brain and cerebral angiography; no NPSLE symptoms in this patient justify those tests\
  **神经精神性SLE（NPSLE）:** 表现为癫痫、精神症状、认知障碍或卒中——通过脑部MRI和脑血管造影评估；该患者无NPSLE症状，不支持相关检查

- **Pleuritis vs. Pericarditis in SLE:** Pleuritic chest pain + clear lungs = pleuritis (serositis); pericarditis presents with friction rub and diffuse ST elevation on ECG — echocardiography reserved for suspected effusion with cardiac findings\
  **SLE胸膜炎vs心包炎:** 胸膜炎性胸痛+肺清 = 胸膜炎（浆膜炎）；心包炎表现为摩擦音和ECG弥漫性ST段抬高——超声心动图用于有心脏查体异常时怀疑积液的情况

- **Anti-phospholipid syndrome (APS) complication:** SLE patients with antiphospholipid antibodies at risk for arterial/venous thrombosis, recurrent miscarriage — treat with anticoagulation (warfarin for thrombotic APS)\
  **抗磷脂综合征（APS）并发症:** 有抗磷脂抗体的SLE患者易发动静脉血栓、反复流产——用抗凝治疗（血栓性APS用华法林）

- **Key complication — End-stage renal disease (ESRD):** Class IV proliferative lupus nephritis carries ~20% 10-year risk of ESRD; aggressive induction followed by maintenance therapy (MMF) is the cornerstone of renal preservation\
  **重要并发症——终末期肾病（ESRD）:** IV类增殖性狼疮性肾炎10年ESRD风险约20%；积极诱导后MMF维持治疗是保护肾功能的核心策略

- **Exam variant — When to choose echocardiography:** If the same patient had a pericardial friction rub, muffled heart sounds, or pulsus paradoxus, echocardiography (not biopsy) would be the priority to rule out tamponade\
  **考题变式——何时选超声心动图:** 若同一患者出现心包摩擦音、心音低钝或奇脉，超声心动图（而非活检）才是首选，以排除心脏压塞

# Question 180 — Chronic Venous Insufficiency / 慢性静脉功能不全

## Question Stem / 题干

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 100%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><p>A <strong>67-year-old woman</strong> comes to the physician because of a <strong>6-month history of mild pain in her legs</strong> with walking and at rest. Her pain is <strong>somewhat relieved when she elevates her legs</strong>. She has a <strong>3-year history of intermittent swelling of her legs</strong>. She has no history of serious illness and takes no medications. She has smoked <strong>one-half pack of cigarettes daily for 18 years</strong>. She has been able to perform her normal daily activities. Cardiopulmonary examination shows <strong>no abnormalities</strong>. There is <strong>nonpitting edema of the lower extremities</strong>. A photograph of the right lower extremity is shown. Which of the following is the most appropriate next step in diagnosis of the lower extremity findings?</p>
<p><strong>Q: Most appropriate next step in diagnosis?</strong></p>
<p>A) Echocardiography<br />
B) Lymphangiography<br />
C) Skin biopsy<br />
D) Angiography of the lower extremities<br />
E) No further evaluation is indicated</p>
<p><strong>Correct Answer: E</strong></p></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
</tbody>
</table>

## 1. Key Stem Clues / 题干关键词抓考点

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 50%" />
<col style="width: 50%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Key Stem Clue</strong><br />
<strong>关键词</strong></th>
<th><strong>Why It Matters</strong><br />
<strong>为什么重要</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>67-year-old woman<br />
67 岁女性</td>
<td>Elderly age is a primary risk factor for chronic venous insufficiency (CVI)<br />
高龄是慢性静脉功能不全（CVI）的主要危险因素</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Pain relieved with leg elevation<br />
抬腿后疼痛缓解</td>
<td>Elevation reduces venous hydrostatic pressure; this directly distinguishes venous from arterial pain (arterial worsens with elevation)<br />
抬腿降低静脉流体静压；这是静脉性与动脉性疼痛的关键鉴别（动脉性疼痛抬腿加重）</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>3-year history of intermittent leg swelling<br />
3 年间歇性腿部肿胀史</td>
<td>Chronic, progressive course points to venous insufficiency rather than an acute process<br />
慢性进行性病程提示静脉功能不全，而非急性病变</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Nonpitting edema of the lower extremities<br />
下肢非凹陷性水肿</td>
<td>Characteristic of CVI; pitting edema suggests cardiac, hepatic, or renal etiology<br />
CVI 的典型体征；凹陷性水肿更提示心脏、肝脏或肾脏病因</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Smoking one-half pack daily for 18 years<br />
每日半包烟，持续 18 年</td>
<td>Tobacco use is a recognized independent risk factor for venous disease<br />
吸烟是静脉疾病已确认的独立危险因素</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>No cardiopulmonary abnormalities<br />
心肺检查无异常</td>
<td>Rules out heart failure as the cause of bilateral leg edema<br />
排除心力衰竭作为双侧腿部水肿的病因</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Photograph of right lower extremity<br />
右下肢照片所示</td>
<td>Implies visible varicose veins, completing the classic clinical triad of CVI<br />
暗示可见静脉曲张，完成 CVI 典型临床三联征</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

## 2. Mechanism / 机制理解

**Chronic venous insufficiency** develops when **venous valvular incompetence** leads to retrograde blood flow, causing **sustained venous hypertension** in the lower extremity:

**慢性静脉功能不全**由**静脉瓣膜功能不全**导致血液逆流，引起下肢**持续性静脉高压**所致：

- Incompetent perforator and superficial vein valves allow blood to pool in superficial venous system\
  穿通静脉和浅静脉瓣膜功能不全导致血液淤积于浅静脉系统

- Sustained venous hypertension causes plasma extravasation into the interstitium → nonpitting edema and hemosiderin deposition\
  持续静脉高压导致血浆渗漏至组织间隙 → 非凹陷性水肿及含铁血黄素沉积

- Dilated, tortuous varicose veins form as vein walls stretch under chronic pressure\
  在持续压力下静脉壁扩张，形成迂曲扩张的静脉曲张

- Leg elevation reduces hydrostatic pressure → promotes venous return → relieves pain and swelling\
  抬高患肢降低流体静压 → 促进静脉回流 → 缓解疼痛和肿胀

**Key distinguishing pearl:** Pain improved by elevation = venous etiology; pain worsened by elevation = arterial etiology.

**关键鉴别要点:** 抬腿缓解 = 静脉性；抬腿加重 = 动脉性。

## 3. Correct Answer (E) — No Further Evaluation Indicated / 正确答案 (E) — 无需进一步评估

**Chronic venous insufficiency** is a clinical diagnosis established by history and physical examination alone — no imaging or laboratory workup is required when the presentation is classic:

**慢性静脉功能不全**是仅凭病史和体格检查即可确立的临床诊断——当表现典型时，无需影像学或实验室检查：

- Classic triad: varicose veins + nonpitting edema + leg pain relieved by elevation\
  典型三联征：静脉曲张 + 非凹陷性水肿 + 抬腿缓解的腿部疼痛

- Absent cardiac findings on exam excludes heart failure, making further cardiac workup unnecessary\
  体检无心脏异常排除心力衰竭，无需进一步心脏评估

- Venous duplex ultrasonography is reserved for atypical presentations or pre-procedural planning, not routine diagnosis\
  静脉双功超声仅用于不典型病例或术前规划，不作为常规诊断手段

**Diagnosis:** Clinical — varicose veins, nonpitting edema, pain relieved with elevation, normal cardiopulmonary exam; duplex US only if presentation is unclear

**诊断:** 临床诊断——静脉曲张、非凹陷性水肿、抬腿缓解的疼痛、心肺检查正常；仅在表现不典型时行双功超声

**Treatment:** First-line conservative measures — compression stockings (20–30 mmHg), leg elevation, regular exercise; refractory cases may undergo sclerotherapy or endovenous ablation

**治疗:** 首选保守治疗——弹力袜（20–30 mmHg）、抬高患肢、规律运动；难治性病例可行硬化治疗或腔内静脉消融术

## 4. Options Elimination / 错误选项排除逻辑

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 33%" />
<col style="width: 33%" />
<col style="width: 33%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Option</strong><br />
<strong>选项</strong></th>
<th><strong>Why Wrong</strong><br />
<strong>为什么错</strong></th>
<th><strong>Key Discriminator</strong><br />
<strong>鉴别要点</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>A — Echocardiography<br />
A — 超声心动图</td>
<td>Wrong — evaluates cardiac structure; this patient has no cardiac symptoms, no JVD, no S3, and a normal cardiopulmonary exam<br />
错误——评估心脏结构；本患者无心脏症状、无颈静脉怒张、无第三心音、心肺检查正常</td>
<td>Heart failure causes pitting edema bilaterally with signs of systemic venous congestion; absent here<br />
心衰引起双侧凹陷性水肿伴全身静脉充血体征；本例均无</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>B — Lymphangiography<br />
B — 淋巴管造影</td>
<td>Wrong — used for lymphatic system evaluation (cancer metastasis, lymphedema); patient has CVI, not lymphedema<br />
错误——用于淋巴系统评估（癌症转移、淋巴水肿）；本患者为 CVI，非淋巴水肿</td>
<td>Lymphedema lacks varicose veins and is associated with cancer, radiation, or infection history — none present here<br />
淋巴水肿无静脉曲张，与肿瘤、放疗或感染史相关——本例均无</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>C — Skin biopsy<br />
C — 皮肤活检</td>
<td>Wrong — used for skin cancer or vasculitis; no atypical or suspicious skin lesions are described<br />
错误——用于皮肤癌或血管炎诊断；题目未描述非典型或可疑皮肤病变</td>
<td>Varicose veins and nonpitting edema are classic CVI findings, not suspicious lesions requiring histologic evaluation<br />
静脉曲张和非凹陷性水肿是典型 CVI 体征，非需要组织学评估的可疑病变</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>D — Angiography of the lower extremities<br />
D — 下肢血管造影</td>
<td>Wrong — evaluates the arterial system; indicated for PAD or aneurysms, not venous disease<br />
错误——评估动脉系统；用于外周动脉病或动脉瘤，不适用于静脉疾病</td>
<td>No signs of arterial disease: claudication worsens with walking (not here), elevation relieves symptoms (opposite of PAD), no pulse deficits described<br />
无动脉疾病体征：间歇性跛行行走加重（本例不符）、抬腿缓解（与 PAD 相反）、无脉搏消失描述</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>E — No further evaluation is indicated ✓<br />
E — 无需进一步评估 ✓</td>
<td>CORRECT — CVI is a clinical diagnosis; the classic history and physical exam are sufficient for diagnosis<br />
正确——CVI 为临床诊断；典型病史与体格检查足以确诊</td>
<td>Varicose veins + nonpitting edema + elevation relieves pain + normal cardiac exam = clinical CVI, no workup required<br />
静脉曲张 + 非凹陷性水肿 + 抬腿缓解 + 心脏检查正常 = 临床 CVI 诊断，无需检查</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

*The most tempting distractor is (D) Angiography — leg pain and smoking history may prompt concern for peripheral arterial disease, but pain relief with elevation and the presence of varicose veins firmly establish a venous rather than arterial etiology.*

最容易混淆的干扰项是（D）血管造影——腿部疼痛和吸烟史可能引发对外周动脉疾病的考量，但抬腿缓解疼痛以及静脉曲张的存在，明确指向静脉性而非动脉性病因。

## 5. High-Yield Summary Table — Chronic Venous Insufficiency vs. Peripheral Arterial Disease vs. Lymphedema / 慢性静脉功能不全 vs. 外周动脉疾病 vs. 淋巴水肿

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 25%" />
<col style="width: 25%" />
<col style="width: 25%" />
<col style="width: 25%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Feature</strong><br />
<strong>特征</strong></th>
<th><strong>Chronic Venous Insufficiency</strong><br />
<strong>慢性静脉功能不全</strong></th>
<th><strong>Peripheral Arterial Disease</strong><br />
<strong>外周动脉疾病</strong></th>
<th><strong>Lymphedema</strong><br />
<strong>淋巴水肿</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>Pain character<br />
疼痛特点</td>
<td>Aching heaviness, may occur at rest and with walking<br />
酸胀沉重感，静息和行走时均可出现</td>
<td>Cramping claudication with walking; rest pain in severe cases<br />
行走时痉挛性跛行；严重时出现静息痛</td>
<td>Usually painless or mild aching<br />
通常无痛或轻度酸痛</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Effect of elevation<br />
抬腿效果</td>
<td>Relieved — promotes venous drainage<br />
缓解——促进静脉引流</td>
<td>Worsened — reduces arterial perfusion pressure<br />
加重——降低动脉灌注压</td>
<td>Minimal change<br />
改变不明显</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Edema type<br />
水肿类型</td>
<td>Nonpitting (chronic); bilateral<br />
非凹陷性（慢性）；双侧</td>
<td>Usually absent<br />
通常无水肿</td>
<td>Early pitting → later nonpitting (brawny induration)<br />
早期凹陷性 → 晚期非凹陷性（橡皮肿）</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Skin findings<br />
皮肤表现</td>
<td>Varicose veins, hemosiderin hyperpigmentation, stasis dermatitis, medial malleolus ulcers<br />
静脉曲张、含铁血黄素色素沉着、淤积性皮炎、内踝溃疡</td>
<td>Shiny hairless skin, dependent rubor, pallor on elevation, punched-out ulcers at toes/heels<br />
皮肤光亮无毛、垂足红斑、抬腿苍白、趾尖/足跟穿凿样溃疡</td>
<td>Peau d'orange texture, hyperkeratosis, fibrosis<br />
橘皮征、角化过度、皮下纤维化</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Key risk factors<br />
主要危险因素</td>
<td>Elderly age, prolonged standing, obesity, prior DVT, smoking<br />
高龄、久站、肥胖、既往深静脉血栓、吸烟</td>
<td>Smoking, diabetes, hypertension, dyslipidemia<br />
吸烟、糖尿病、高血压、血脂异常</td>
<td>Cancer, radiation, lymph node surgery, filariasis, congenital<br />
肿瘤、放疗、淋巴结手术、丝虫病、先天性</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Diagnosis<br />
诊断方法</td>
<td>Clinical; duplex US if atypical or pre-procedural<br />
临床诊断；不典型或术前行双功超声</td>
<td>ABI (&lt; 0.9 abnormal), duplex US, CT/conventional angiography<br />
踝肱指数（&lt; 0.9 异常）、双功超声、CT/常规血管造影</td>
<td>Clinical; lymphoscintigraphy if needed<br />
临床诊断；必要时行淋巴闪烁显像</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>First-line treatment<br />
一线治疗</td>
<td>Compression stockings, leg elevation, exercise; ablation or sclerotherapy if refractory<br />
弹力袜、抬腿、运动；难治时消融或硬化治疗</td>
<td>Risk factor modification, cilostazol, supervised walking; revascularization if severe<br />
危险因素控制、西洛他唑、监督下步行训练；严重时血运重建</td>
<td>Manual lymphatic drainage, compression garments, decongestive therapy<br />
手法淋巴引流、弹力衣、综合消肿治疗</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

## 6. One-Sentence Summary & Memory Hook / 一句话总结 & 记忆钩

**Chronic venous insufficiency is a clinical diagnosis — varicose veins, nonpitting edema, and leg pain relieved by elevation in an elderly patient with risk factors requires no further workup.**

**慢性静脉功能不全是临床诊断——有危险因素的老年患者出现静脉曲张、非凹陷性水肿及抬腿缓解的腿部疼痛，无需进一步检查。**

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 100%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><p><strong>Memory Hook — LEGS for Chronic Venous Insufficiency / 记忆钩 — LEGS 慢性静脉功能不全四要点:</strong></p>
<p>• <strong>L</strong>eg elevation relieves pain — the single most important differentiator from arterial disease / 抬腿减轻疼痛——与动脉疾病最重要的单一鉴别点<br />
• <strong>E</strong>dema nonpitting + varicose veins — classic physical exam pair for CVI / 非凹陷性水肿 + 静脉曲张——CVI 体检的经典组合<br />
• <strong>G</strong>o clinical only — no imaging needed when presentation is classic / 仅凭临床即可——表现典型时无需影像检查<br />
• <strong>S</strong>moking, standing, senility (age) — the three main modifiable and non-modifiable risk factors / 吸烟、久站、高龄——三大主要可变与不可变危险因素</p></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
</tbody>
</table>

## 7. High-Yield Topic Knowledge — Chronic Venous Insufficiency / 高频知识表 — 慢性静脉功能不全

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 50%" />
<col style="width: 50%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Topic</strong><br />
<strong>考点</strong></th>
<th><strong>Key Points</strong><br />
<strong>要点</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>Pathophysiology<br />
病理生理</td>
<td>Valvular incompetence → venous reflux → sustained venous hypertension → plasma leakage into interstitium → nonpitting edema, hemosiderin deposition, skin changes<br />
瓣膜功能不全 → 静脉反流 → 持续静脉高压 → 血浆渗漏至组织间隙 → 非凹陷性水肿、含铁血黄素沉积、皮肤改变</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Risk factors<br />
危险因素</td>
<td>Elderly age, prolonged standing, obesity, prior DVT, tobacco use, female sex, family history of venous disease; CVI is the most common chronic venous disorder<br />
高龄、久站、肥胖、既往深静脉血栓、吸烟、女性、静脉疾病家族史；CVI 是最常见的慢性静脉疾病</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Classic physical findings<br />
典型体格检查发现</td>
<td>Varicose veins, nonpitting edema, brownish hemosiderin hyperpigmentation, stasis dermatitis; venous ulcers (shallow, irregular, medial malleolus) in advanced disease<br />
静脉曲张、非凹陷性水肿、棕褐色含铁血黄素色素沉着、淤积性皮炎；晚期可见静脉溃疡（浅表、边界不规则、位于内踝）</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Diagnosis approach<br />
诊断策略</td>
<td>Clinical diagnosis when presentation is classic; venous duplex ultrasonography reserved for atypical cases, pre-procedural mapping, or DVT exclusion — not routinely indicated<br />
表现典型时为临床诊断；静脉双功超声仅用于不典型病例、术前定位或排除 DVT——不常规推荐</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Conservative treatment<br />
保守治疗</td>
<td>Compression stockings (20–30 mmHg for mild, 30–40 mmHg for severe), regular leg elevation above heart level, aerobic exercise to enhance calf muscle pump<br />
弹力袜（轻度 20–30 mmHg，重度 30–40 mmHg）、定期将腿抬高至心脏以上、有氧运动增强腓肠肌泵功能</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Interventional options<br />
介入选择</td>
<td>Endovenous thermal ablation (laser/radiofrequency), ultrasound-guided sclerotherapy, surgical great saphenous vein stripping for refractory symptomatic patients<br />
腔内热消融（激光/射频）、超声引导硬化治疗、难治性症状患者行大隐静脉手术剥脱</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Venous vs. arterial ulcer<br />
静脉性 vs. 动脉性溃疡</td>
<td>Venous: medial malleolus, shallow, irregular borders, surrounding lipodermatosclerosis, painless or mildly painful; Arterial: toes/heels, deep punched-out, painful, associated with PAD signs<br />
静脉性：内踝、浅表、边界不规则、周围脂肪皮肤硬化、无痛或轻度疼痛；动脉性：趾尖/足跟、深部穿凿样、疼痛明显、伴 PAD 体征</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Post-thrombotic syndrome<br />
血栓后综合征</td>
<td>CVI variant following DVT due to permanent valve destruction; same clinical presentation as CVI but with prior DVT history; adequate anticoagulation during DVT reduces long-term risk<br />
DVT 后因瓣膜永久性破坏导致的 CVI 变体；与 CVI 临床表现相同但有 DVT 病史；DVT 期间充分抗凝可降低远期风险</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

## 8. Extensions / 延伸扩展

- **Differential of bilateral leg edema:** Heart failure (pitting, JVD, S3 gallop), nephrotic syndrome (pitting, periorbital edema, heavy proteinuria), hepatic cirrhosis (pitting, ascites, jaundice), hypothyroidism (nonpitting, diffuse myxedema), CVI (nonpitting, varicose veins, relieved by elevation)\
  **双侧腿部水肿鉴别:** 心力衰竭（凹陷性、颈静脉怒张、奔马律）、肾病综合征（凹陷性、眶周水肿、大量蛋白尿）、肝硬化（凹陷性、腹水、黄疸）、甲状腺功能减退（非凹陷性、弥漫性黏液水肿）、CVI（非凹陷性、静脉曲张、抬腿缓解）

- **Key complication:** Venous stasis ulcers at the medial malleolus are the most serious CVI complication — slow-healing, prone to secondary bacterial infection, requiring wound care plus compression\
  **关键并发症:** 内踝静脉淤血性溃疡是 CVI 最严重的并发症——愈合缓慢、易继发细菌感染，需伤口护理联合压迫治疗

- **Variant — when duplex ultrasound IS indicated:** Atypical presentation (unilateral edema without varicose veins), pre-ablation mapping, suspected concurrent DVT, or recurrence after prior treatment — these scenarios justify imaging\
  **题目变式——何时需要双功超声:** 不典型表现（单侧水肿无静脉曲张）、消融术前定位、疑似合并深静脉血栓或既往治疗后复发——这些情况需要影像检查

- **Mnemonic review — elevation test:** If elevating the leg relieves pain → venous (increased venous return); if elevation worsens pain → arterial (gravity no longer assists perfusion to ischemic tissue); this single maneuver is the highest-yield bedside differentiator on NBME\
  **助记复习——抬腿试验:** 抬腿缓解疼痛 → 静脉性（促进静脉回流）；抬腿加重疼痛 → 动脉性（重力不再辅助缺血组织灌注）；这一单一操作是 NBME 中最高频的床边鉴别手段

# Question 181 — Palliative Care: Anticholinergic Management of Death Rattle / 姑息治疗：抗胆碱药物管理临终喉鸣

## Question Stem / 题干

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 100%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><p>Ten days after undergoing <strong>left above-the-knee amputation</strong> for <strong>severe diabetic soft-tissue infection</strong>, a <strong>78-year-old man</strong> in the intensive care unit has <strong>noisy, labored breathing</strong>. His postoperative course has been complicated by <strong>sepsis, delirium, and respiratory insufficiency</strong>. His temperature is 37.5°C (99.5°F), pulse is 72/min, <strong>respirations are 9/min</strong>, and blood pressure is 100/50 mm Hg. Pulse oximetry on 3 L of oxygen by nasal cannula shows an <strong>oxygen saturation of 92%</strong>. He is not oriented to person, place, or time. Breath sounds are coarse and distant bilaterally. The extremities are cool to the touch and mottled. After discussions with the patient's family, and consistent with the patient's wishes, the family has chosen to provide <strong>comfort care</strong>. The family remains concerned about the patient's <strong>current loud breathing and secretions</strong>.</p>
<p><strong>Q: Which of the following is the most appropriate next step in management?</strong></p>
<p>A) Administration of humidified oxygen<br />
B) Administration of morphine<br />
C) Administration of scopolamine<br />
D) Intubation and mechanical ventilation<br />
E) Placement of a nasogastric tube</p>
<p><strong>Correct Answer: C</strong></p></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
</tbody>
</table>

## 1. Key Stem Clues / 题干关键词抓考点

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 50%" />
<col style="width: 50%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Key Stem Clue</strong><br />
<strong>关键词</strong></th>
<th><strong>Why It Matters</strong><br />
<strong>为什么重要</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>Comfort care chosen / 已选择舒适护理</td>
<td>Excludes all invasive or curative interventions; management goal shifts entirely to symptom relief<br />
排除所有侵入性或治疗性干预；管理目标完全转向症状缓解</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Noisy, labored breathing / 嘈杂、费力的呼吸</td>
<td>Classic "death rattle" — pooling of secretions in upper airway as patient loses ability to clear them<br />
经典"临终喉鸣"——患者失去清除分泌物能力，分泌物在上气道积聚</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Family concerned about loud breathing and secretions / 家属担忧响亮呼吸和分泌物</td>
<td>The primary management target is secretion reduction, not oxygenation or pain control<br />
主要管理目标是减少分泌物，而非改善氧合或控制疼痛</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Respirations 9/min, O2 sat 92% / 呼吸9次/分，血氧92%</td>
<td>Indicates impending death; supplemental O2 or mechanical support will not change trajectory<br />
提示濒死状态；补充氧气或机械支持不会改变病程</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Delirium, not oriented / 谵妄，定向力丧失</td>
<td>Patient cannot cooperate with oral medications; a transdermal patch route is particularly advantageous<br />
患者无法配合口服药物；经皮贴剂给药途径尤为有利</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Extremities cool and mottled / 四肢冰冷、花斑</td>
<td>Hallmark of impending death (circulatory failure); supports comfort-only approach<br />
即将死亡的标志（循环衰竭）；支持仅限舒适护理的决定</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

## 2. Mechanism / 机制理解

The **death rattle** arises because dying patients lose the **conscious drive to swallow or cough**, allowing **upper airway secretions** to pool and vibrate with each breath:

临终喉鸣源于濒死患者失去**有意识的吞咽或咳嗽驱动力**，致使**上气道分泌物**积聚并随每次呼吸振动：

- Secretions are produced by salivary glands and bronchial mucosa via **muscarinic M3 receptor** stimulation\
  分泌物由唾液腺和支气管黏膜通过**毒蕈碱M3受体**刺激产生

- **Anticholinergic agents** block M3 receptors → reduce secretion production at the source, rather than merely suctioning them away\
  **抗胆碱能药物**阻断M3受体→从源头减少分泌物产生，而非仅靠吸痰清除

- **Scopolamine** crosses the blood-brain barrier; available as a **transdermal patch** — ideal when the oral route is unavailable\
  **东莨菪碱**可穿越血脑屏障；有**经皮贴剂**剂型——口服途径不可用时的理想选择

- **Glycopyrrolate** does NOT cross the blood-brain barrier → fewer CNS side effects (less agitation/delirium), but only available as injectable or oral\
  **格隆溴铵**不穿越血脑屏障→较少CNS副作用（减少激越/谵妄），但仅有注射或口服剂型

**Anatomic rule of thumb:** Upper airway pooling → anticholinergic (dry it up); lower airway bronchospasm → bronchodilator (open it up). Don't confuse the two targets.

**解剖小窍门:** 上气道积液→抗胆碱能药物（干燥分泌物）；下气道支气管痉挛→支气管扩张剂（扩张气道）。不要混淆两个治疗靶点。

## 3. Correct Answer (C) — Scopolamine for End-of-Life Secretion Management / 正确答案 (C) — 东莨菪碱用于临终分泌物管理

**Scopolamine** is a muscarinic antagonist that reduces secretion production, directly addressing the family's stated concern:

**东莨菪碱**是一种毒蕈碱拮抗剂，减少分泌物产生，直接解决家属明确表达的关切：

- Reduces salivary and bronchial secretions by blocking M3 receptors throughout the airway\
  通过阻断气道中的M3受体减少唾液和支气管分泌物

- Available as a **transdermal patch** (placed behind the ear) — works well when patient cannot swallow\
  有**经皮贴剂**剂型（贴于耳后）——患者无法吞咽时效果良好

- Patch onset ~4 hours; start early in the anticipated dying process to stay ahead of secretion buildup\
  贴剂起效约4小时；应在预期死亡过程早期开始使用，以提前控制分泌物积聚

- Does cross BBB → may cause CNS sedation/confusion, but patient is already delirious and comfort is the overriding goal\
  可穿越血脑屏障→可能引起CNS镇静/意识混乱，但患者已有谵妄且舒适是首要目标

**Diagnosis:** Death rattle in a comfort care patient — a symptom of the normal dying process, not a pathology to reverse.

**诊断:** 舒适护理患者的临终喉鸣——正常死亡过程的症状，而非需要逆转的病理状态。

**Treatment:** Scopolamine transdermal patch (1.5 mg/72 h) or glycopyrrolate (0.2 mg IV/SC q4h); avoid routine suctioning unless secretions cause obvious patient distress.

**治疗:** 东莨菪碱经皮贴剂（1.5 mg/72小时）或格隆溴铵（0.2 mg静脉/皮下注射，每4小时一次）；除非分泌物明显引起患者痛苦，否则避免常规吸痰。

## 4. Options Elimination / 错误选项排除逻辑

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 33%" />
<col style="width: 33%" />
<col style="width: 33%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Option</strong><br />
<strong>选项</strong></th>
<th><strong>Why Wrong</strong><br />
<strong>为什么错</strong></th>
<th><strong>Key Discriminator</strong><br />
<strong>鉴别要点</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>A — Administration of humidified oxygen<br />
A — 给予加湿氧气</td>
<td>Humidification adds moisture to the airway, worsening secretion pooling; does not address the root cause<br />
加湿向气道增加水分，加重分泌物积聚；不解决根本原因</td>
<td>Secretion problem requires drying (anticholinergic), not humidification<br />
分泌物问题需要干燥（抗胆碱能），而非加湿</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>B — Administration of morphine<br />
B — 给予吗啡</td>
<td>Addresses pain and dyspnea sensation (air hunger) but does NOT reduce secretion volume or the noisy breathing the family finds distressing<br />
解决疼痛和呼吸困难感觉（空气饥渴感），但不减少分泌物量或引起家属痛苦的嘈杂呼吸</td>
<td>Morphine = pain/air hunger; scopolamine = secretions — match the drug to the specific symptom<br />
吗啡=疼痛/空气饥渴；东莨菪碱=分泌物——将药物与具体症状匹配</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>C — Administration of scopolamine ✓<br />
C — 给予东莨菪碱 ✓</td>
<td>CORRECT — Anticholinergic directly reduces secretion production via M3 blockade; patch formulation ideal for this patient<br />
正确——抗胆碱能药物通过M3阻断直接减少分泌物产生；贴剂剂型对该患者理想</td>
<td>Matches both the target symptom (secretions) and the route challenge (cannot swallow)<br />
同时匹配目标症状（分泌物）和给药途径挑战（无法吞咽）</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>D — Intubation and mechanical ventilation<br />
D — 插管和机械通气</td>
<td>Directly contradicts the family's decision for comfort care; invasive, prolongs dying without improving quality of life<br />
直接违背家属选择舒适护理的决定；侵入性，延长死亡过程而不改善生活质量</td>
<td>Comfort care = no escalation of life-sustaining treatment under any circumstance<br />
舒适护理=任何情况下均不升级维持生命的治疗</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>E — Placement of a nasogastric tube<br />
E — 放置鼻胃管</td>
<td>Invasive; death rattle secretions arise from loss of swallowing/cough reflex — NOT from gastric reflux — so NG tube is both harmful and ineffective<br />
侵入性；临终喉鸣分泌物源于吞咽/咳嗽反射丧失——而非胃食管反流——因此鼻胃管既有害又无效</td>
<td>Misidentification of secretion origin; NG tube cannot address salivary or bronchial secretions<br />
错误识别分泌物来源；鼻胃管无法解决唾液或支气管分泌物</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

*The most tempting distractor is (B) morphine — entirely appropriate in palliative care, but it targets dyspnea and pain, not the specific complaint of noisy secretions that prompted this question.*

最具迷惑性的干扰项是（B）吗啡——在姑息治疗中完全适当，但它针对呼吸困难和疼痛，而非引发本题的嘈杂分泌物这一具体主诉。

## 5. High-Yield Summary Table — Scopolamine vs. Glycopyrrolate for End-of-Life Secretion Management / 东莨菪碱与格隆溴铵在临终分泌物管理中的比较

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 33%" />
<col style="width: 33%" />
<col style="width: 33%" />

<tr>
<th><strong>Feature</strong><br />

<th><strong>Scopolamine</strong><br />
<strong>东莨菪碱</strong></th>
<th><strong>Glycopyrrolate</strong><br />
<strong>格隆溴铵</strong></th>
</tr>

<tbody>
<tr>
<td>Mechanism / 机制</td>
<td>Muscarinic (M1/M2/M3) antagonist<br />
毒蕈碱受体（M1/M2/M3）拮抗剂</td>
<td>Muscarinic (M1/M2/M3) antagonist<br />
毒蕈碱受体（M1/M2/M3）拮抗剂</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>BBB crossing / 穿越血脑屏障</td>
<td>Yes → sedation, confusion possible<br />
可以→可能有镇静、意识混乱</td>
<td>No → minimal CNS side effects<br />
不可以→CNS副作用极少</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Available routes / 给药途径</td>
<td>Transdermal patch, IV, SC, oral<br />
经皮贴剂、静脉、皮下、口服</td>
<td>IV, SC, oral (no patch)<br />
静脉、皮下、口服（无贴剂）</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Patch availability / 贴剂可用性</td>
<td>Yes — 1.5 mg/72 h (key advantage when oral unavailable)<br />
有——1.5 mg/72小时（口服不可用时的关键优势）</td>
<td>No patch formulation<br />
无贴剂剂型</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Preferred clinical scenario / 首选临床场景</td>
<td>Patient cannot swallow; transdermal route needed<br />
患者无法吞咽；需要经皮给药途径</td>
<td>Minimize CNS effects; CNS sedation undesired<br />
最小化CNS效应；不希望CNS镇静时</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Patch onset / 贴剂起效时间</td>
<td>~4 hours; apply early<br />
约4小时；宜早期应用</td>
<td>No patch (N/A)<br />
无贴剂，不适用</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

## 6. One-Sentence Summary & Memory Hook / 一句话总结 & 记忆钩

**In a dying patient under comfort care, the death rattle (noisy breathing from pooled upper airway secretions) is best managed with an anticholinergic agent such as scopolamine, which reduces secretion production via M3 receptor blockade and is available as a transdermal patch when oral intake is impossible.**

**对于舒适护理目标的临终患者，临终喉鸣（因上气道分泌物积聚导致的嘈杂呼吸）最佳处理是使用抗胆碱能药物（如东莨菪碱），通过M3受体阻断减少分泌物产生，且在无法口服时可使用经皮贴剂。**

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 100%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><p><strong>Memory Hook — SCOPE of Scopolamine / 记忆钩 — 东莨菪碱的 "SCOPE":</strong></p>
<p>• <strong>S</strong>ecretions — the target: blocks M3 to dry them at the source / 分泌物——治疗靶点：阻断M3从源头干燥分泌物<br />
• <strong>C</strong>omfort care — only appropriate in palliative/dying context / 舒适护理——仅适用于姑息/临终情境<br />
• <strong>O</strong>ral route unavailable — patch solves the delivery problem / 口服不可用——贴剂解决给药问题<br />
• <strong>P</strong>atch = behind the ear, 72-hour duration, onset 4 hours / 贴剂=贴于耳后，持续72小时，起效4小时<br />
• <strong>E</strong>xtra CNS effect (vs. glycopyrrolate which does NOT cross BBB) / 额外CNS效应（而格隆溴铵不穿越血脑屏障）</p></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
</tbody>
</table>

## 7. High-Yield Topic Knowledge — Palliative and End-of-Life Care Pharmacology / 高频知识表 — 姑息与临终护理药理学

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 50%" />
<col style="width: 50%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Topic</strong><br />
<strong>考点</strong></th>
<th><strong>Key Points</strong><br />
<strong>要点</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>Death rattle definition / 临终喉鸣定义</td>
<td>Noisy, moist breathing in dying patients from pooled secretions; caused by loss of cough/swallow reflex, NOT gastric reflux<br />
临终患者因分泌物积聚产生的嘈杂、湿润呼吸声；由咳嗽/吞咽反射丧失导致，而非胃食管反流</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>First-line pharmacotherapy / 一线药物治疗</td>
<td>Scopolamine patch (1.5 mg/72 h) or glycopyrrolate (0.2 mg IV/SC q4h) — both reduce secretion production via M3 blockade<br />
东莨菪碱贴剂（1.5 mg/72小时）或格隆溴铵（0.2 mg静脉/皮下，每4小时）——均通过M3阻断减少分泌物产生</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Morphine role in palliative care / 吗啡在姑息治疗中的作用</td>
<td>Indicated for pain and dyspnea (air hunger sensation); does NOT reduce secretions; can be used alongside anticholinergics<br />
适用于疼痛和呼吸困难（空气饥渴感）；不减少分泌物；可与抗胆碱能药物联合使用</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Nonpharmacologic measures / 非药物措施</td>
<td>Lateral positioning (gravity-assisted drainage), reducing IV fluids, gentle oropharyngeal suctioning only if causing obvious distress<br />
侧卧位（重力辅助引流）、减少静脉补液、仅在引起明显痛苦时轻柔口咽部吸痰</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Glycopyrrolate advantage / 格隆溴铵优势</td>
<td>Does not cross BBB → less CNS agitation/delirium; preferred when CNS side effects are a concern but patch not required<br />
不穿越血脑屏障→较少CNS激越/谵妄；当关注CNS副作用但不需要贴剂时首选</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Signs of imminent death / 即将死亡的体征</td>
<td>Mottled extremities, cool skin, Cheyne-Stokes breathing, decreased urine output, death rattle — indicate hours to days remaining<br />
四肢花斑、皮肤冰冷、陈-施呼吸、尿量减少、临终喉鸣——提示剩余数小时至数天</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Comfort care contraindications / 舒适护理禁忌</td>
<td>No intubation, no NG tube, no aggressive IV hydration, no CPR — all contraindicated once comfort care goals established<br />
无插管、无鼻胃管、无积极静脉补液、无心肺复苏——一旦确立舒适护理目标均为禁忌</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

## 8. Extensions / 延伸扩展

- **Differential of noisy breathing in ICU:** Stridor (upper airway obstruction — laryngeal edema, foreign body), death rattle (secretions), pulmonary edema (crackles), or bronchospasm (wheeze) — each has a different management approach\
  **ICU嘈杂呼吸的鉴别:** 喘鸣（上气道梗阻——喉头水肿、异物）、临终喉鸣（分泌物）、肺水肿（湿啰音）或支气管痉挛（哮鸣音）——各有不同处理方法

- **Variant — glycopyrrolate preferred:** When family requests minimal sedation and CNS side effects are a concern, glycopyrrolate is preferred over scopolamine; requires IV/SC access\
  **题目变式——格隆溴铵优先:** 当家属要求最小化镇静且关注CNS副作用时，格隆溴铵优于东莨菪碱；需要静脉/皮下通路

- **Key complication of anticholinergics:** Urinary retention, constipation, dry mouth, blurred vision, tachycardia — important for recognizing anticholinergic toxidrome on USMLE ("hot as a hare, dry as a bone, mad as a hatter")\
  **抗胆碱能药物的关键并发症:** 尿潴留、便秘、口干、视力模糊、心动过速——对于识别USMLE抗胆碱能毒综合征很重要（"热如野兔、干如枯骨、疯如疯帽匠"）

- **Ethics pearl — surrogate decision-making:** When patient's previously expressed wishes align with family's comfort care decision, this is valid surrogate decision-making; the physician supports symptom management within that scope and does not override it\
  **伦理要点——代理决策:** 当患者之前表达的意愿与家属的舒适护理决定一致时，这是有效的代理决策；医生在该范围内支持症状管理，而不应凌驾于其上

# Question 182 — Foreign Body Aspiration / 异物吸入

## Question Stem / 题干

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 100%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><p>A <strong>previously healthy 4-year-old boy</strong> is brought to the emergency department by his mother on a <strong>winter evening</strong> because of the <strong>sudden onset of coughing</strong> and <strong>mild difficulty breathing</strong>. His symptoms began <strong>late this afternoon when he was playing with other children at a party</strong>. His brother has asthma. The patient's temperature is <strong>37.2°C (99°F)</strong>, pulse is 92/min, and <strong>respirations are 36/min</strong>. Physical examination shows <strong>intense intermittent coughing</strong> and <strong>mild intercostal retractions</strong>. <strong>Wheezes are heard bilaterally but are greater on the right</strong>. An x-ray of the chest is shown. Which of the following is the most likely diagnosis?</p>
<p><strong>Q: Most likely diagnosis?</strong></p>
<p>A) Asthma<br />
B) Congenital lobar emphysema<br />
C) Foreign body aspiration<br />
D) Laryngotracheitis<br />
E) Pneumonia</p>
<p><strong>Correct Answer: C</strong></p></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
</tbody>
</table>

---

## 1. Key Stem Clues / 题干关键词抓考点

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 50%" />
<col style="width: 50%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Key Stem Clue</strong><br />
<strong>关键词</strong></th>
<th><strong>Why It Matters</strong><br />
<strong>为什么重要</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>Previously healthy 4-year-old, playing at a party<br />
既往健康的4岁男孩，在派对上与其他孩子玩耍</td>
<td>Classic scenario for foreign body aspiration — toddlers and preschoolers commonly aspirate small objects/food during play<br />
典型异物吸入场景——学步儿和学龄前儿童在玩耍时常吸入小物件或食物</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Sudden onset of symptoms<br />
症状突然发作</td>
<td>Abrupt onset without prodrome suggests mechanical obstruction, not infection<br />
无前驱症状的突然发作提示机械性梗阻而非感染</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Wheezes greater on the right<br />
右侧哮鸣音更明显</td>
<td>Right main bronchus is wider and more vertical — aspirated objects lodge preferentially on the right<br />
右主支气管更宽且更垂直——吸入的异物优先嵌顿于右侧</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Afebrile (37.2°C)<br />
无发热（37.2°C）</td>
<td>Absence of fever argues against pneumonia, viral croup, or other infectious etiology<br />
无发热不支持肺炎、病毒性哮喘或其他感染性病因</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Tachypnea (RR 36/min) with intercostal retractions<br />
呼吸急促（RR 36次/分）伴肋间凹陷</td>
<td>Signs of increased work of breathing due to partial bronchial obstruction<br />
部分支气管梗阻导致呼吸做功增加的体征</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Brother has asthma (family history)<br />
兄弟患哮喘（家族史）</td>
<td>Red herring — asthma is a distractor given family history, but unilateral wheezing and acute context favor aspiration<br />
红鲱鱼干扰——家族史使哮喘成为干扰项，但单侧哮鸣音和急性发作背景更支持异物吸入</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

---

## 2. Mechanism / 机制理解

**Foreign body aspiration** causes **partial or complete bronchial obstruction**, triggering a cascade of **air-trapping**, **ball-valve effect**, and **hyperinflation** distal to the obstruction:

**异物吸入**导致**部分或完全支气管梗阻**，在梗阻远端引发**气体潴留**、**活瓣效应**和**过度充气**的级联反应：

- Air enters during inspiration (bronchus dilates) but cannot fully exit during expiration (bronchus narrows around object) → progressive hyperinflation\
  吸气时气体进入（支气管扩张），但呼气时无法完全排出（支气管收缩压迫异物）→进行性过度充气

- Hyperinflated ipsilateral lung pushes mediastinum toward the contralateral side (mediastinal shift away from lesion)\
  同侧肺过度充气将纵隔推向对侧（纵隔偏移远离病变侧）

- Right main bronchus branches off trachea at ~25° angle vs left at ~45° → aspirated objects deposit in the right lung more commonly\
  右主支气管与气管成约25°夹角，左侧约45°→吸入的异物更常沉积于右肺

**Anatomic rule of thumb:** Right bronchus = straighter, wider, shorter = the "highway" for aspirated objects; left bronchus = sharper turn = natural defense

**解剖小窍门:** 右主支气管=更直、更宽、更短=吸入异物的"高速公路"；左主支气管=转角更急=天然防御屏障

---

## 3. Correct Answer (C) — Foreign Body Aspiration / 正确答案 (C) — 异物吸入

**Foreign body aspiration** is a pediatric emergency characterized by **sudden-onset respiratory symptoms** following a choking episode, classically in children under 5 years of age:

**异物吸入**是一种儿科急症，特征为窒息发作后**突发呼吸道症状**，典型见于5岁以下儿童：

- Sudden onset during play/eating; may be witnessed or unwitnessed\
  玩耍/进食时突然发作；可能被目击或未被目击

- Triad: coughing + wheezing (unilateral) + decreased breath sounds on affected side\
  三联征：咳嗽 + 哮鸣音（单侧）+ 患侧呼吸音降低

- CXR: unilateral hyperinflation + mediastinal shift toward contralateral side; radiolucent objects (food, plastic) often NOT visible\
  胸片：单侧过度充气 + 纵隔向对侧偏移；透X线异物（食物、塑料）通常不可见

- Objects lodged in larynx/trachea cause stridor, rapid hypoxia, cyanosis → life-threatening\
  嵌顿于喉/气管的异物导致喘鸣、快速缺氧、紫绀→危及生命

**Diagnosis:** Clinical suspicion (acute onset + unilateral findings in a toddler) + CXR showing unilateral hyperinflation with mediastinal shift; bronchoscopy is confirmatory and therapeutic

**诊断:** 临床疑诊（学步儿急性发作+单侧体征）+ 胸片显示单侧过度充气伴纵隔偏移；支气管镜检查具有确诊和治疗双重价值

**Treatment:** Rigid bronchoscopy for foreign body removal; if complete obstruction causing acute hypoxia, back blows and abdominal thrusts (Heimlich) as immediate maneuver

**治疗:** 硬质支气管镜取出异物；若完全梗阻导致急性缺氧，立即行背部叩击和腹部冲击（海姆立克手法）

---

## 4. Options Elimination / 错误选项排除逻辑

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 33%" />
<col style="width: 33%" />
<col style="width: 33%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Option</strong><br />
<strong>选项</strong></th>
<th><strong>Why Wrong</strong><br />
<strong>为什么错</strong></th>
<th><strong>Key Discriminator</strong><br />
<strong>鉴别要点</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>A — Asthma<br />
A — 哮喘</td>
<td>Bilateral symmetric hyperinflation; chronic/recurrent pattern; not typically sudden-onset at a party<br />
双侧对称性过度充气；慢性/反复发作模式；不典型表现为在派对上突然发作</td>
<td>Asthma = bilateral wheezes + bilateral hyperinflation; FBA = unilateral wheezes + unilateral hyperinflation<br />
哮喘=双侧哮鸣音+双侧过度充气；异物吸入=单侧哮鸣音+单侧过度充气</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>B — Congenital lobar emphysema<br />
B — 先天性大叶性肺气肿</td>
<td>Typically presents within first 6 months of life; would not present acutely at age 4<br />
通常在出生后6个月内出现；不会在4岁时急性发作</td>
<td>Age of presentation is the key discriminator — congenital = neonatal/infant; FBA = toddler/preschool<br />
发病年龄是关键鉴别点——先天性=新生儿/婴儿期；异物吸入=幼儿/学龄前期</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>C — Foreign body aspiration ✓<br />
C — 异物吸入 ✓</td>
<td>CORRECT — sudden onset during play, unilateral greater wheezing, afebrile, consistent age group and context<br />
正确——玩耍时突然发作，单侧哮鸣音更重，无发热，年龄和背景均符合</td>
<td>Acute onset + unilateral CXR findings + afebrile toddler at play = pathognomonic constellation<br />
急性发作+单侧胸片改变+无发热的玩耍中幼儿=特征性综合征</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>D — Laryngotracheitis<br />
D — 喉气管炎（哮吼）</td>
<td>Presents with barking cough, stridor, rhinorrhea, fever; "steeple sign" on CXR (subglottic narrowing); no barking cough or stridor here<br />
表现为犬吠样咳嗽、喘鸣、流涕、发热；胸片示"尖塔征"（声门下狭窄）；本例无犬吠咳嗽或喘鸣</td>
<td>Croup = barking cough + inspiratory stridor + steeple sign; FBA = intermittent cough + expiratory wheeze + unilateral hyperinflation<br />
哮吼=犬吠咳+吸气性喘鸣+尖塔征；异物吸入=间歇性咳嗽+呼气性哮鸣+单侧过度充气</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>E — Pneumonia<br />
E — 肺炎</td>
<td>Fever typically present; productive cough; CXR shows lobar consolidation/infiltrates, not hyperinflation<br />
通常有发热；咳嗽有痰；胸片示大叶性实变/浸润影，而非过度充气</td>
<td>Pneumonia = fever + consolidation on CXR; FBA = afebrile + hyperinflation + mediastinal shift<br />
肺炎=发热+胸片实变；异物吸入=无发热+过度充气+纵隔偏移</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

*The most tempting distractor is Asthma (Choice A): the family history of asthma in the brother and the bilateral wheezing can mislead — but the unilateral predominance of wheezing and the acute onset during play at a party are the pivotal clues that shift the diagnosis to foreign body aspiration.*

哮喘（选项A）是最具迷惑性的干扰项：兄弟的哮喘家族史和双侧哮鸣音容易误导——但右侧为主的单侧哮鸣音以及在派对玩耍时的急性发作，是将诊断转向异物吸入的关键线索。

---

</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

## 6. One-Sentence Summary & Memory Hook / 一句话总结 & 记忆钩

**A toddler with sudden-onset unilateral wheezing and respiratory distress at a social event has foreign body aspiration until proven otherwise — unilateral hyperinflation on CXR with contralateral mediastinal shift confirms the diagnosis, and rigid bronchoscopy is both diagnostic and curative.**

**幼儿在社交场合突发单侧哮鸣音和呼吸窘迫，在排除之前应视为异物吸入——胸片上的单侧过度充气伴对侧纵隔偏移证实诊断，硬质支气管镜兼具诊断和治疗双重作用。**

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 100%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><p><strong>Memory Hook — "RIGHT SIDE RULES" for FBA / 记忆钩 — 异物吸入"右侧法则":</strong></p>
<p>• <strong>R</strong>ight bronchus — wider, straighter → aspirated objects land here most often / 右主支气管——更宽更直→异物最常在此嵌顿<br />
• <strong>I</strong>nstant onset — no prodrome, no fever, just sudden choke / 即刻发作——无前驱症状，无发热，只是突然窒息<br />
• <strong>G</strong>reater wheeze on affected side (unilateral asymmetry is the key clue) / 患侧哮鸣音更重（单侧不对称是关键线索）<br />
• <strong>H</strong>yperinflation ipsilateral + mediastinal shift to opposite side on CXR / 同侧过度充气+胸片示纵隔偏向对侧<br />
• <strong>T</strong>reat with bronchoscopy (rigid) for removal / 用（硬质）支气管镜取出治疗</p></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
</tbody>
</table>

---

## 7. High-Yield Topic Knowledge — Pediatric Foreign Body Aspiration / 高频知识表 — 儿科异物吸入

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 50%" />
<col style="width: 50%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Topic</strong><br />
<strong>考点</strong></th>
<th><strong>Key Points</strong><br />
<strong>要点</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>Epidemiology &amp; risk<br />
流行病学与危险因素</td>
<td>Most common in children &lt;3 years; peak at 1–2 years; boys &gt; girls; food (peanuts, grapes, hot dogs) and small objects (coins, toys)<br />
最常见于&lt;3岁儿童；高峰1–2岁；男&gt;女；食物（花生、葡萄、热狗）和小物件（硬币、玩具）</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Location preference<br />
解剖好发部位</td>
<td>Right lung &gt; left lung (right bronchus: wider, shorter, more vertical ~25° from trachea); tracheal/laryngeal objects = more dangerous (stridor, cyanosis)<br />
右肺&gt;左肺（右主支气管：更宽、更短、与气管成角约25°）；气管/喉部异物=更危险（喘鸣、紫绀）</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>CXR findings<br />
胸片表现</td>
<td>Ipsilateral hyperinflation + contralateral mediastinal shift (ball-valve effect); expiratory or bilateral decubitus films increase sensitivity; most objects are radiolucent<br />
同侧过度充气+对侧纵隔偏移（活瓣效应）；呼气相或双侧卧位片可提高敏感性；大多数异物为透X线</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Inspiratory vs. expiratory films<br />
吸气相 vs. 呼气相胸片</td>
<td>On expiratory film, normal lung deflates but hyperinflated (obstructed) lung stays inflated → makes asymmetry more obvious; useful when inspiration film looks equivocal<br />
呼气相正常肺缩小但过度充气（梗阻）肺保持充气→使不对称更明显；当吸气相不确定时有用</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Diagnosis &amp; workup<br />
诊断与检查</td>
<td>High clinical suspicion is essential (CXR normal in up to 30%); rigid bronchoscopy is gold standard for diagnosis AND treatment<br />
高度临床怀疑至关重要（高达30%胸片正常）；硬质支气管镜是诊断和治疗的金标准</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Complications of delayed diagnosis<br />
延迟诊断并发症</td>
<td>Recurrent pneumonia (post-obstructive), bronchiectasis, lung abscess, atelectasis, chronic cough<br />
反复肺炎（梗阻后性）、支气管扩张、肺脓肿、肺不张、慢性咳嗽</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>First aid for complete obstruction<br />
完全梗阻的急救</td>
<td>&lt;1 year: back blows + chest thrusts; ≥1 year: abdominal thrusts (Heimlich maneuver); blind finger sweeps are contraindicated (can push object deeper)<br />
&lt;1岁：背部叩击+胸部冲击；≥1岁：腹部冲击（海姆立克手法）；禁止盲目手指清扫（可将异物推深）</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

---

## 8. Extensions / 延伸扩展

- **Differential of unilateral wheeze in children:** Foreign body aspiration (most common acute), endobronchial tumor (rare, older children), extrinsic compression by lymphadenopathy, mucus plug\
  **儿童单侧哮鸣音鉴别:** 异物吸入（最常见急性病因）、支气管内肿瘤（罕见，较大儿童）、淋巴结病外压、黏液栓

- **Variant — tracheal vs. bronchial location:** Objects at the trachea/larynx cause bilateral wheeze + stridor + rapidly progressive hypoxia + cyanosis; bronchial objects (like this case) cause unilateral wheeze with preserved oxygenation initially\
  **题目变式——气管 vs. 支气管位置:** 气管/喉部异物导致双侧哮鸣+喘鸣+快速进行性低氧+紫绀；支气管异物（如本例）最初导致单侧哮鸣，氧合尚可

- **Radiolucent vs. radiopaque objects:** Most aspirated objects in children are radiolucent (organic material: food, plastic) → NOT seen on CXR; only ~10–20% are radiopaque (metal, glass); indirect CXR signs (hyperinflation, mediastinal shift) are the actual diagnostic clues\
  **透X线 vs. 不透X线异物:** 儿童大多数吸入异物为透X线（有机物：食物、塑料）→胸片不可见；仅约10–20%不透X线（金属、玻璃）；胸片间接征象（过度充气、纵隔偏移）才是真正的诊断线索

- **Key complication — post-obstructive pneumonia:** Recurrent or persistent pneumonia in the same lobe should always raise suspicion for an undiagnosed retained foreign body, especially in young children\
  **关键并发症——梗阻后肺炎:** 同一肺叶反复或持续性肺炎应始终引起对未诊断滞留异物的怀疑，尤其是幼儿

# Question 183 — Adjustment Disorder Post-Myocardial Infarction / 心肌梗死后适应障碍

## Question Stem / 题干

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 100%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><p>A <strong>62-year-old man</strong> comes to the office with his wife for a follow-up examination <strong>4 weeks after</strong> he was hospitalized for management of an <strong>acute myocardial infarction</strong> that required cardiac catheterization. He has had a <strong>1.4-kg (3-lb) weight gain</strong> since discharge. He has not had shortness of breath or chest pain on exertion. He has been <strong>sleeping well</strong>. His medications are losartan and atorvastatin; he is <strong>intermittently adherent</strong> to his regimen. He has had <strong>irregular attendance at an outpatient cardiac rehabilitation program</strong>; he says he sometimes skips sessions because he is tired. His wife says he is <strong>irritable</strong> and often talks of his father who died of a heart attack at the age of 65 years. The couple has <strong>not resumed sexual activity because of the patient's fear of having another heart attack</strong>. The patient enjoys seeing his grandchildren but is <strong>no longer interested in playing poker with his friends</strong>. He is 168 cm (5 ft 6 in) tall and weighs 85 kg (187 lb); BMI is 30 kg/m². His pulse is 90/min, respirations are 16/min, and blood pressure is 130/84 mm Hg. Physical examination shows no pedal edema. On mental status examination, he describes his mood as <strong>"blah"</strong> and has a <strong>constricted affect</strong>. He reports <strong>no suicidal ideation or suicide plan</strong>. Which of the following is the most likely diagnosis?</p>
<p><strong>Q: Most likely diagnosis?</strong></p>
<p>A) Adjustment disorder<br />
B) Generalized anxiety disorder<br />
C) Hypoactive sexual desire disorder<br />
D) Major depressive disorder<br />
E) Post-traumatic stress disorder</p>
<p><strong>Correct Answer: A</strong></p></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
</tbody>
</table>

## 1. Key Stem Clues / 题干关键词抓考点

</tr>

情绪"平淡"，情感受限</td>
<td>Subclinical depressive features — distress present but below MDD diagnostic threshold<br />
亚临床抑郁特征——存在痛苦但低于 MDD 诊断阈值</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Skipping cardiac rehab, intermittent medication adherence<br />
不规律参加心脏康复，间歇性服药依从性差</td>
<td>Conduct disturbance / functional impairment — required component for adjustment disorder diagnosis<br />
行为紊乱/功能受损——适应障碍诊断的必要成分</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

## 2. Mechanism / 机制理解

The diagnosis of **adjustment disorder** requires an identifiable **psychosocial stressor** followed by a maladaptive emotional or behavioral response within **3 months**, causing distress **disproportionate** to the stressor and/or significant **functional impairment**, without meeting full criteria for another established Axis I disorder:

适应障碍的诊断需要一个可识别的**心理社会压力源**，在 **3 个月内**出现适应不良的情绪或行为反应，引起与压力源**不相称**的明显痛苦和/或显著的**功能损害**，且不满足其他精神障碍的完整诊断标准：

- **Stressor:** acute MI + fear of recurrence → triggers anxiety, behavioral avoidance, irritability\
  **压力源:** 急性心肌梗死 + 复发恐惧 → 触发焦虑、行为回避、易激惹

- **Subthreshold symptoms:** partial anhedonia (poker), dysphoric mood ("blah"), without full MDD/GAD/PTSD criteria\
  **亚阈值症状:** 部分快感缺失（打牌）、心境不悦（"平淡"），不满足完整的 MDD/GAD/PTSD 标准

- **Functional impairment:** skipping rehab, poor medication adherence, avoiding sexual activity, social withdrawal\
  **功能受损:** 跳过心脏康复、服药依从性差、回避性生活、社交退缩

- **Self-limiting nature:** adjustment disorder typically resolves within 6 months of stressor termination\
  **自限性:** 适应障碍通常在压力源消除后 6 个月内自行缓解

**Diagnostic rule of thumb:** Adjustment disorder is a "diagnosis of exclusion from below" — rule OUT MDD, GAD, PTSD by counting symptoms and checking duration; if criteria aren't fully met but distress + functional impairment are present, adjustment disorder fits.

**诊断小窍门:** 适应障碍是"从下往上的排除性诊断"——通过数症状和核查持续时间排除 MDD、GAD、PTSD；若不完全满足标准但存在痛苦 + 功能受损，则适应障碍成立。

## 3. Correct Answer (A) — Adjustment Disorder / 正确答案 (A) — 适应障碍

**Adjustment disorder** is defined as an emotional and/or behavioral response to an identifiable stressor, occurring within 3 months, causing marked distress disproportionate to the stressor, with significant functional impairment, and not meeting criteria for another psychiatric disorder:

**适应障碍**定义为对可识别压力源的情绪和/或行为反应，在 3 个月内发生，引起与压力源不相称的明显痛苦，伴有显著功能受损，且不满足其他精神障碍的诊断标准：

- Stressor: acute MI (4 weeks ago) — onset within 3-month window ✓\
  压力源：急性心肌梗死（4 周前）——在 3 个月时间窗内发生 ✓

- Distress out of proportion: irritability, fear of death, behavioral avoidance beyond typical cardiac recovery\
  痛苦不成比例：易激惹、死亡恐惧、超出典型心脏康复范围的行为回避

- Functional impairment: nonadherence to medications, irregular rehab, social withdrawal (poker), sexual avoidance\
  功能受损：服药不依从、不规律康复、社交退缩（打牌）、性生活回避

- Does NOT meet MDD criteria (lacks ≥5 symptoms for ≥2 weeks), GAD criteria (anxiety not generalized), or PTSD criteria (no intrusive re-experiencing or hyperarousal)\
  不满足 MDD 标准（缺乏持续 ≥2 周的 ≥5 条症状）、GAD 标准（焦虑非泛化）或 PTSD 标准（无侵入性再体验或高觉醒）

**Diagnosis:** Clinical — identify stressor, count symptoms against MDD/GAD/PTSD criteria, confirm functional impairment; adjustment disorder if subthreshold but distress + impairment present

**诊断:** 临床诊断——识别压力源，对照 MDD/GAD/PTSD 标准盘点症状，确认功能受损；若亚阈值但存在痛苦 + 功能受损则诊断适应障碍

**Treatment:** Brief supportive psychotherapy is first-line; address cardiac rehab adherence and medication compliance; sexual counseling (gradual return to sexual activity is safe ~4 weeks post-MI for stable patients)

**治疗:** 短程支持性心理治疗为一线；解决心脏康复依从性和服药依从性问题；性咨询（稳定患者心肌梗死后约 4 周可安全逐渐恢复性活动）

<col style="width: 33%" />
<col style="width: 33%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Option</strong><br />
<strong>选项</strong></th>
<th><strong>Why Wrong</strong><br />
<strong>为什么错</strong></th>
<th><strong>Key Discriminator</strong><br />
<strong>鉴别要点</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>A — Adjustment disorder ✓<br />
A — 适应障碍 ✓</td>
<td>CORRECT — identifiable stressor (MI) within 3 months, disproportionate distress + functional impairment, subthreshold for MDD/GAD/PTSD<br />
正确——3 个月内可识别压力源（MI），不成比例的痛苦 + 功能受损，低于 MDD/GAD/PTSD 诊断阈值</td>
<td>Onset within 3 months of stressor; does not meet full criteria for any other disorder<br />
在压力源 3 个月内发病；不满足任何其他障碍的完整标准</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>B — Generalized anxiety disorder<br />
B — 广泛性焦虑障碍</td>
<td>Requires excessive, uncontrollable worry across multiple domains (work, health, finances, etc.) for ≥6 months — this patient's anxiety is specific to MI recurrence only, and duration is only 4 weeks<br />
需要对多个领域（工作、健康、财务等）过度、难以控制的担忧持续 ≥6 个月——此患者焦虑仅特定于 MI 复发，且持续时间仅 4 周</td>
<td>GAD = worry across ≥3 domains for ≥6 months; this patient has 1 specific fear for 4 weeks<br />
GAD = 跨 ≥3 个领域担忧持续 ≥6 个月；此患者仅 1 个特定恐惧持续 4 周</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>C — Hypoactive sexual desire disorder<br />
C — 性欲减退障碍</td>
<td>Requires ≥6 months of reduced sexual desire NOT attributable to another cause — here, the avoidance is explicitly attributable to fear of MI recurrence (i.e., a specific anxiety), and duration is only 4 weeks<br />
需要 ≥6 个月的性欲减退且不归因于其他原因——此处回避明确归因于 MI 复发恐惧（即特定焦虑），且持续时间仅 4 周</td>
<td>HSDD requires duration ≥6 months AND no attributable cause; both criteria fail here<br />
HSDD 需要持续 ≥6 个月且无可归因原因；此处两项标准均不满足</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>D — Major depressive disorder<br />
D — 重性抑郁障碍</td>
<td>Requires ≥5 of 9 DSM symptoms for ≥2 weeks — patient has irritability, partial anhedonia (poker), and "blah" mood (~3 symptoms); he sleeps well, no guilt/worthlessness, no concentration impairment, no suicidality, no psychomotor changes<br />
需要 9 条 DSM 症状中 ≥5 条持续 ≥2 周——患者有易激惹、部分快感缺失（打牌）和"平淡"情绪（约 3 条）；睡眠良好，无内疚/无价值感，无注意力障碍，无自杀意念，无精神运动改变</td>
<td>Count the symptoms: ≤3 present vs. 5 required for MDD; preserved sleep is the key disqualifier<br />
数症状：现有 ≤3 条 vs. MDD 需要 5 条；睡眠保留是关键排除标志</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>E — Post-traumatic stress disorder<br />
E — 创伤后应激障碍</td>
<td>Requires ≥1 month of intrusive re-experiencing (flashbacks, nightmares), hyperarousal, and avoidance of trauma reminders — patient has no intrusive symptoms, no hyperarousal; talking about father represents fear/worry, not flashback re-experiencing<br />
需要 ≥1 个月的侵入性再体验（闪回、噩梦）、高觉醒和对创伤提醒物的回避——患者无侵入性症状，无高觉醒；谈论父亲代表恐惧/担忧，而非闪回再体验</td>
<td>PTSD requires intrusion cluster + arousal cluster; absence of flashbacks/nightmares rules it out<br />
PTSD 需要侵入症状群 + 觉醒症状群；无闪回/噩梦可排除</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

*The trickiest distractor is D (MDD) — count symptoms carefully: irritability, partial anhedonia, and dysphoric mood total ~3, falling short of the 5-symptom threshold; preserved sleep and absent suicidality are the decisive disqualifiers.*

最容易误选的干扰项是 D（MDD）——仔细数症状：易激惹、部分快感缺失和心境不悦共约 3 条，低于 5 条阈值；睡眠保留和无自杀意念是决定性排除标志。

## 6. One-Sentence Summary & Memory Hook / 一句话总结 & 记忆钩

**Adjustment disorder = identifiable stressor → disproportionate distress + functional impairment within 3 months, subthreshold for MDD, GAD, and PTSD — treated with brief supportive psychotherapy.**

**适应障碍 = 可识别压力源 → 3 个月内不成比例的痛苦 + 功能受损，低于 MDD、GAD 和 PTSD 的诊断阈值——以短程支持性心理治疗为首选。**

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 100%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><p><strong>Memory Hook — "SAD" Triad for Adjustment Disorder / 记忆钩 — 适应障碍"SAD"三要素:</strong></p>
<p>• <strong>S</strong>tressor — specific identifiable psychosocial event, onset within 3 months / 特定可识别心理社会压力源，3 个月内起病<br />
• <strong>A</strong>bnormal response — disproportionate distress AND/OR significant functional impairment / 异常反应——不成比例的痛苦和/或显著功能受损<br />
• <strong>D</strong>oesn't qualify — subthreshold; does NOT meet full criteria for MDD, GAD, PTSD, or conduct disorder / 不够格——亚阈值；不满足 MDD、GAD、PTSD 或品行障碍的完整标准</p></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
</tbody>
</table>

## 7. High-Yield Topic Knowledge — Adjustment Disorder Criteria & Post-MI Psychiatric Complications / 高频知识表 — 适应障碍诊断标准 & 心肌梗死后精神并发症

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 50%" />
<col style="width: 50%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Topic</strong><br />
<strong>考点</strong></th>
<th><strong>Key Points</strong><br />
<strong>要点</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>Adjustment disorder subtypes<br />
适应障碍亚型</td>
<td>With depressed mood; with anxiety; with mixed anxiety and depressed mood; with disturbance of conduct; with mixed disturbance of emotions and conduct; unspecified<br />
伴抑郁情绪型；伴焦虑型；伴混合焦虑抑郁情绪型；伴行为紊乱型；伴情绪和行为混合紊乱型；未特定型</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>3-month onset rule<br />
3 个月起病规则</td>
<td>Symptoms must begin within 3 months of stressor; if they persist &gt;6 months after stressor resolution, reconsider the diagnosis (may have evolved into MDD)<br />
症状必须在压力源后 3 个月内开始；若压力源消除后持续 &gt;6 个月，需重新考虑诊断（可能已演变为 MDD）</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Post-MI depression prevalence<br />
心肌梗死后抑郁发生率</td>
<td>~20% of MI patients develop MDD; post-MI depression independently associated with 2–3× increased cardiac mortality<br />
约 20% 的心肌梗死患者发展为 MDD；心肌梗死后抑郁独立与心脏死亡率增加 2–3 倍相关</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Sexual activity post-MI<br />
心肌梗死后性活动</td>
<td>Safe to resume ~4 weeks post-MI for stable patients (metabolic equivalent ≈ climbing 2 flights of stairs); fear is common and addressable with reassurance and counseling<br />
稳定患者约 4 周后可恢复性活动（代谢当量 ≈ 爬 2 层楼梯）；恐惧很常见，可通过保证和咨询解决</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>MDD symptom checklist (SIG E CAPS)<br />
MDD 症状清单 (SIG E CAPS)</td>
<td>Sleep disturbance, Interest loss (anhedonia), Guilt/worthlessness, Energy loss, Concentration difficulty, Appetite/weight change, Psychomotor change, Suicidal ideation — need ≥5 for ≥2 weeks including depressed mood or anhedonia<br />
睡眠障碍、兴趣丧失（快感缺失）、内疚/无价值感、精力丧失、注意力下降、食欲/体重改变、精神运动改变、自杀意念——需 ≥5 条持续 ≥2 周，包括抑郁情绪或快感缺失</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Treatment of adjustment disorder<br />
适应障碍的治疗</td>
<td>Brief supportive psychotherapy is first-line; pharmacotherapy (SSRIs) reserved for severe/persistent cases; typically self-limiting with stressor resolution<br />
短程支持性心理治疗为一线；SSRIs 仅用于严重/持续病例；通常随压力源消除而自限</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Cardiac rehab as psychiatric barometer<br />
心脏康复作为精神健康晴雨表</td>
<td>Poor attendance at cardiac rehab is a red flag for underlying psychological distress post-MI; always screen for depression and anxiety in nonadherent patients<br />
心脏康复出勤率低是心肌梗死后心理痛苦的危险信号；应对所有不依从患者筛查抑郁和焦虑</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

## 8. Extensions / 延伸扩展

- **Differential of post-MI low mood:** Adjustment disorder (most common, subthreshold symptoms), MDD (≥5 symptoms ≥2 weeks), demoralization syndrome (hopelessness + passive death wish without full depressive episode), grief reaction (mourning loss of pre-MI identity/function)\
  **心肌梗死后情绪低落的鉴别:** 适应障碍（最常见，亚阈值症状）、MDD（≥5 条症状 ≥2 周）、士气低落综合征（无望感 + 被动死亡意愿，无完整抑郁发作）、悲伤反应（哀悼心肌梗死前身份/功能的丧失）

- **Variant — conduct disturbance subtype:** When behavioral features dominate (medication nonadherence, skipping rehab, reckless driving) with minimal mood symptoms — still requires identifiable stressor within 3 months and functional impairment\
  **题目变式——行为紊乱亚型:** 当行为特征占主导（服药不依从、跳过康复、鲁莽驾驶），情绪症状极少时——仍需 3 个月内可识别压力源和功能受损

- **Key complication:** Untreated post-MI adjustment disorder increases risk of progression to MDD and worsens cardiac outcomes via behavioral pathways (medication nonadherence, physical inactivity, social isolation)\
  **关键并发症:** 未治疗的心肌梗死后适应障碍增加进展为 MDD 的风险，并通过行为途径（服药不依从、体力不活动、社交孤立）恶化心脏结局

- **Screening tool — PHQ-9:** PHQ-9 score 5–9 = subthreshold depression (consistent with adjustment disorder); score ≥10 = probable MDD warranting pharmacotherapy; routinely used at post-MI follow-up visits\
  **筛查工具——PHQ-9:** PHQ-9 分数 5–9 = 亚阈值抑郁（与适应障碍一致）；≥10 分 = 可能 MDD，需要药物治疗；常规用于心肌梗死后随访

# Question 184 — Appendicitis in Pregnancy / 妊娠期阑尾炎

## Question Stem / 题干

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 100%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><p>A <strong>17-year-old primigravid</strong> patient at <strong>22 weeks' gestation</strong> comes to the physician because of a <strong>12-hour history of fever, nausea, and vomiting</strong>. She has <strong>abdominal tenderness on the right side when she coughs</strong>. Her temperature is <strong>38.3°C (101°F)</strong>. Pelvic and rectal examinations show <strong>right-sided tenderness</strong>. Fetal heart tones are normal. Her <strong>leukocyte count is 18,000/mm³ with a shift to the left</strong>. Her <strong>serum amylase activity is within the reference range</strong>. During the next 8 hours, vomiting, fever, and abdominal pain continue. <strong>Ultrasonography of the gallbladder shows no abnormalities</strong>. Which of the following is the most appropriate next step in diagnosis?</p>
<p><strong>Q: Most appropriate next step in diagnosis?</strong></p>
<p>A) Barium enema<br />
B) Gallium scan<br />
C) Laparoscopy<br />
D) Peritoneal lavage<br />
E) Amniocentesis</p>
<p><strong>Correct Answer: C</strong></p></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
</tbody>
</table>

## 1. Key Stem Clues / 题干关键词抓考点

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 50%" />
<col style="width: 50%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Key Stem Clue</strong><br />
<strong>关键词</strong></th>
<th><strong>Why It Matters</strong><br />
<strong>为什么重要</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>17-year-old primigravid at 22 weeks' gestation<br />
17岁初产妇，妊娠22周</td>
<td>Pregnancy displaces the appendix superiorly, shifting classic RLQ pain location upward<br />
妊娠使阑尾向上移位，经典右下腹痛位置随之改变</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Fever + nausea + vomiting × 12 hours<br />
发热+恶心+呕吐12小时</td>
<td>Classic triad of appendicitis; duration indicates no spontaneous resolution<br />
阑尾炎典型三联征；病程提示症状持续进展未自行缓解</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Abdominal tenderness on right side when coughing<br />
咳嗽时右侧腹部压痛</td>
<td>Dunphy sign — cough-provoked pain indicates peritoneal irritation, pointing toward appendicitis<br />
Dunphy征——咳嗽诱发疼痛提示腹膜刺激，指向阑尾炎</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Leukocyte count 18,000/mm³ with left shift<br />
白细胞18,000/mm³伴核左移</td>
<td>Marked leukocytosis exceeding physiologic pregnancy range (≤16,000) + left shift = pathologic bacterial infection<br />
白细胞显著超过妊娠生理上限（≤16,000）+核左移=病理性细菌感染</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Serum amylase within reference range<br />
血清淀粉酶正常</td>
<td>Excludes acute pancreatitis as the cause of abdominal pain<br />
排除急性胰腺炎作为腹痛原因</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Gallbladder ultrasound shows no abnormalities<br />
胆囊超声无异常</td>
<td>Rules out cholecystitis and cholelithiasis; narrows the differential to appendicitis<br />
排除胆囊炎和胆石症；将鉴别诊断收窄至阑尾炎</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Symptoms persist and progress over 8 hours<br />
症状在随后8小时持续进展</td>
<td>Clinical deterioration despite conservative management mandates definitive invasive diagnosis<br />
保守处理后病情持续恶化，需要有创手段明确诊断</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

## 2. Mechanism / 机制理解

The **gravid uterus** progressively displaces the **cecum and appendix cephalad** throughout pregnancy, fundamentally altering the clinical presentation of appendicitis:

妊娠期**增大的子宫**持续将**盲肠和阑尾头侧推移**，从根本上改变阑尾炎的临床表现：

- Normally the appendix lies at **McBurney's point** (RLQ); by 22 weeks it may lie at the umbilical level or even the RUQ, mimicking cholecystitis\
  正常阑尾位于**麦氏点**（右下腹）；妊娠22周时可上移至脐水平甚至右上腹，模拟胆囊炎

- Displaced appendix → **parietal peritoneal irritation** occurs at atypical locations → classic RLQ guarding and rebound may be absent\
  阑尾移位→**壁腹膜刺激**发生在非典型位置→经典右下腹肌卫和反跳痛可能缺如

- Omentum is also displaced upward → reduced ability to **wall off** a perforated appendix → higher risk of diffuse peritonitis in pregnancy\
  大网膜同样上移→**包裹**穿孔阑尾的能力降低→妊娠期更易发生弥漫性腹膜炎

- Physiologic **leukocytosis** (up to 16,000/mm³) is normal in pregnancy; WBC of 18,000 with left shift crosses into pathologic range\
  妊娠期生理性**白细胞增多**（可达16,000/mm³）属正常；18,000伴核左移已超入病理范围

**Anatomic rule of thumb:** The appendix migrates approximately 1 cm per month superiorly after the first trimester, reaching the RUQ by the third trimester.

**解剖小窍门:** 孕早期后阑尾每月约上移1厘米，至孕晚期可达右上腹水平。

## 3. Correct Answer (C) — Laparoscopy / 正确答案 (C) — 腹腔镜检查

**Laparoscopy** is the most appropriate next step when clinical suspicion for appendicitis remains high yet noninvasive imaging has been non-diagnostic:

**腹腔镜检查**在临床高度怀疑阑尾炎而无创影像无法明确诊断时，是最合适的下一步：

- Provides **direct visualization** of the appendix, cecum, and pelvis — simultaneously allowing diagnosis and immediate surgical treatment\
  可**直接观察**阑尾、盲肠和盆腔——同时实现诊断和即刻手术治疗

- **No ionizing radiation** to the fetus, unlike barium enema, CT scan, or gallium scan\
  **无电离辐射**暴露给胎儿，有别于钡剂灌肠、CT或镓扫描

- Safe in pregnancy up to approximately **26–28 weeks**; second trimester is the preferred operative window\
  妊娠**约26–28周**内腹腔镜安全可行；妊娠中期是首选手术窗口

- In this patient, gallbladder ultrasound was normal, amylase was normal, yet fever and leukocytosis persist — laparoscopy is the logical definitive step\
  该患者胆囊超声正常、淀粉酶正常，但发热和白细胞增多持续——腹腔镜是合乎逻辑的确诊步骤

**Diagnosis:** Appendicitis in pregnancy is clinically unreliable due to uterine displacement of the appendix; when ultrasound and MRI are non-diagnostic and suspicion persists, laparoscopy provides the definitive answer.

**诊断:** 妊娠期阑尾位置改变使临床诊断不可靠；当超声/MRI无法确诊而临床持续高度怀疑时，腹腔镜是明确诊断的手段。

**Treatment:** Urgent laparoscopic appendectomy to prevent perforation, sepsis, preterm labor, and fetal or maternal mortality.

**治疗:** 紧急腹腔镜阑尾切除术，防止穿孔、脓毒症、早产及母胎死亡。

## 4. Options Elimination / 错误选项排除逻辑

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 33%" />
<col style="width: 33%" />
<col style="width: 33%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Option</strong><br />
<strong>选项</strong></th>
<th><strong>Why Wrong</strong><br />
<strong>为什么错</strong></th>
<th><strong>Key Discriminator</strong><br />
<strong>鉴别要点</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>A — Barium enema<br />
A — 钡剂灌肠</td>
<td>WRONG — evaluates colonic pathology (IBD, cancer); uses radiation, which is contraindicated in pregnancy; not relevant to suspected appendicitis<br />
错误——评估结肠病变（炎症性肠病、肿瘤）；使用辐射，妊娠期禁忌；与疑似阑尾炎无关</td>
<td>Wrong anatomical target + radiation risk in pregnancy<br />
靶器官不对+妊娠期辐射风险</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>B — Gallium scan<br />
B — 镓扫描</td>
<td>WRONG — detects infection/inflammation broadly but uses radiation (contraindicated in pregnancy) and lacks specificity for appendicitis<br />
错误——可广泛检测感染/炎症，但使用辐射（妊娠期禁忌），且对阑尾炎无特异性</td>
<td>Radiation-based; non-specific; cannot simultaneously treat<br />
放射性检查；缺乏特异性；无法同时治疗</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>C — Laparoscopy ✓<br />
C — 腹腔镜 ✓</td>
<td>CORRECT — direct visualization, simultaneous surgical treatment, no radiation, safe in second trimester<br />
正确——直接可视化，可同时手术治疗，无辐射，妊娠中期安全</td>
<td>Gold standard when noninvasive workup is non-diagnostic<br />
无创检查无法确诊时的金标准</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>D — Peritoneal lavage<br />
D — 腹腔灌洗</td>
<td>WRONG — used for diagnosing intra-abdominal hemorrhage in trauma; nonspecific for infection; requires supraumbilical incision in pregnancy<br />
错误——用于外伤性腹腔内出血诊断；对感染无特异性；妊娠期需脐上切口</td>
<td>Trauma indication, not infection; invasive without diagnostic specificity<br />
外伤适应证，非感染；有创但缺乏诊断特异性</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>E — Amniocentesis<br />
E — 羊膜穿刺</td>
<td>WRONG — evaluates fetal chromosomal abnormalities; fetal heart tones are normal here; no obstetric indication<br />
错误——评估胎儿染色体异常；该患者胎心正常；无产科适应证</td>
<td>Completely irrelevant to maternal abdominal infection<br />
与母体腹腔感染完全无关</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

*The most tempting distractor is B (gallium scan) — it seems relevant because it detects infection — but radiation is contraindicated in pregnancy, it cannot treat, and laparoscopy is both diagnostic and therapeutic.*

镓扫描（B）是最具迷惑性的干扰项——看似相关因为可检测感染——但妊娠期辐射禁忌、无法同时治疗，而腹腔镜兼具诊断与治疗双重价值。

## 6. One-Sentence Summary & Memory Hook / 一句话总结 & 记忆钩

**In a pregnant patient with fever, marked leukocytosis, right-sided abdominal tenderness, normal gallbladder ultrasound, and normal amylase, suspect appendicitis displaced by the gravid uterus — laparoscopy is the definitive next diagnostic and therapeutic step.**

**妊娠患者出现发热、明显白细胞增多、右侧腹压痛、胆囊超声正常、淀粉酶正常时，应高度怀疑因增大子宫移位的阑尾炎——腹腔镜是兼具诊断与治疗价值的确定性下一步。**

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 100%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><p><strong>Memory Hook — GRAPE for Pregnancy Appendicitis / 记忆钩 — 妊娠期阑尾炎 "GRAPE":</strong></p>
<p>• <strong>G</strong>ravid uterus displaces appendix cephalad — pain migrates RLQ → RUQ / 增大子宫使阑尾头侧移位——疼痛从右下腹移向右上腹<br />
• <strong>R</strong>ight-sided tenderness + leukocytosis &gt;16,000 = suspect appendicitis / 右侧压痛+白细胞&gt;16,000=怀疑阑尾炎<br />
• <strong>A</strong>mylase normal + gallbladder US normal → not pancreatitis or cholecystitis / 淀粉酶正常+胆囊超声正常→排除胰腺炎和胆囊炎<br />
• <strong>P</strong>rogressing symptoms → no more delay → proceed to laparoscopy / 症状持续进展→不再等待→行腹腔镜检查<br />
• <strong>E</strong>mergent laparoscopic appendectomy prevents rupture, sepsis, preterm labor, death / 紧急腹腔镜阑尾切除术防止穿孔、脓毒症、早产和死亡</p></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
</tbody>
</table>

## 7. High-Yield Topic Knowledge — Appendicitis in Pregnancy / 高频知识表 — 妊娠期阑尾炎

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 50%" />
<col style="width: 50%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Topic</strong><br />
<strong>考点</strong></th>
<th><strong>Key Points</strong><br />
<strong>要点</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>Appendix position by trimester<br />
各孕期阑尾位置</td>
<td>1st trimester: RLQ (McBurney's point); 2nd trimester: near umbilicus; 3rd trimester: RUQ — may mimic cholecystitis or hepatitis<br />
孕早期：右下腹（麦氏点）；孕中期：脐周；孕晚期：右上腹——可模拟胆囊炎或肝炎</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Most common surgical emergency in pregnancy<br />
妊娠期最常见外科急症</td>
<td>Appendicitis is the most common non-obstetric surgical emergency in pregnancy, occurring in ~1/1500 pregnancies<br />
阑尾炎是妊娠期最常见的非产科外科急症，发生率约1/1500次妊娠</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Preferred imaging (radiation-free)<br />
首选影像（无辐射）</td>
<td>Ultrasound first; MRI second (best soft-tissue detail, no radiation); CT only if MRI unavailable and clinical urgency is high<br />
超声优先；MRI次之（软组织分辨率最佳，无辐射）；仅在MRI不可及且临床紧迫时使用CT</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Physiologic leukocytosis in pregnancy<br />
妊娠期生理性白细胞增多</td>
<td>Normal WBC upper limit in pregnancy: ~16,000/mm³; during labor: up to 20,000–30,000; leukocytosis alone is not diagnostic<br />
妊娠期白细胞正常上限约16,000/mm³；产程中可达20,000–30,000；单独白细胞增多不能诊断</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Fetal loss risk by stage<br />
不同阶段胎儿丢失风险</td>
<td>Uncomplicated appendicitis: ~1.5% fetal loss; perforated appendicitis: ~20–35% fetal loss — early intervention is critical<br />
单纯阑尾炎：胎儿丢失率约1.5%；穿孔性阑尾炎：约20–35%——早期干预至关重要</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Safe laparoscopic window in pregnancy<br />
妊娠期腹腔镜安全窗口</td>
<td>2nd trimester (weeks 14–26) is preferred; 1st trimester risks organogenesis; 3rd trimester — enlarged uterus limits visualization<br />
孕中期（14–26周）首选；孕早期有器官形成风险；孕晚期子宫过大影响腹腔镜视野</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Negative appendectomy rate in pregnancy<br />
妊娠期阴性阑尾切除率</td>
<td>Acceptable negative appendectomy rate in pregnancy is 20–35%; risk of missed perforation outweighs risk of negative exploration<br />
妊娠期可接受的阴性手术率为20–35%；漏诊穿孔的风险大于阴性探查的手术风险</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

## 8. Extensions / 延伸扩展

- **Differential of right-sided abdominal pain in pregnancy:** Appendicitis, cholecystitis, round ligament pain, ovarian torsion, placental abruption, preterm labor — the gravid uterus makes clinical differentiation especially challenging\
  **妊娠期右侧腹痛鉴别:** 阑尾炎、胆囊炎、圆韧带痛、卵巢扭转、胎盘早剥、早产——增大子宫使临床鉴别尤为困难

- **Complication cascade of delayed diagnosis:** Appendiceal perforation → diffuse peritonitis (omentum cannot wall off) → sepsis → preterm labor → fetal demise; delay even hours worsens maternal and fetal outcomes\
  **延误诊断的并发症链:** 阑尾穿孔→弥漫性腹膜炎（大网膜无法包裹）→脓毒症→早产→胎儿死亡；哪怕数小时延误均会恶化母胎预后

- **Radiation avoidance principle in pregnancy:** CT (~35 mGy fetal dose) is teratogenic above 50–100 mGy; even below threshold, cumulative risk is avoided — always prefer ultrasound or MRI first\
  **妊娠期辐射规避原则:** CT（胎儿剂量约35 mGy）在50–100 mGy以上有致畸性；即便低于阈值也应避免累积风险——始终优先选择超声或MRI

- **McBurney's point unreliability in pregnancy:** Classic two-thirds distance from umbilicus to ASIS is only reliable in non-pregnant adults; do not use as a landmark for tenderness assessment in 2nd or 3rd trimester\
  **妊娠期麦氏点不可靠性:** 经典脐至髂前上棘外1/3定位仅在非妊娠成人可靠；孕中晚期不应将其作为压痛评估的定位依据

# Question 185 — Traumatic Hyphema with Sickle Cell Disease / 外伤性前房积血合并镰状细胞病

## Question Stem / 题干

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 100%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><p><strong>An 18-year-old man</strong> comes to the clinic because of a <strong>3-hour history of right eye pain</strong> with <strong>mild light sensitivity</strong> and <strong>blurry vision</strong> that have been present since he awakened this morning. He has had no symptoms in his left eye. He reports being <strong>struck in the face by a soccer ball</strong> last night but having no symptoms at that time. Medical history is remarkable for admission to the hospital 2 years ago for acute chest syndrome <strong>secondary to sickle cell disease</strong>; he has taken <strong>hydroxyurea</strong> since that time. He takes no other medications and does not wear corrective lenses. Family history is remarkable for glaucoma in his maternal grandfather. The patient's vital signs are within normal limits. Examination of the right eye shows <strong>blood filling the lower 20% of the anterior chamber</strong>. Pupils are equal and reactive to light and accommodation bilaterally, and visual fields are intact. Visual acuity is <strong>20/60 in the right eye</strong> and 20/20 in the left eye. <strong>Intraocular pressure is 27 mm Hg</strong> in the right eye and 18 mm Hg in the left eye (N=12–22). Which of the following factors in this patient most strongly increases his risk for complications of his current condition?</p>
<p><strong>Q: Which of the following factors most strongly increases his risk for complications of his current condition?</strong></p>
<p>A) Age<br />
B) Family history<br />
C) Hydroxyurea use<br />
D) Sickle cell disease</p>
<p><strong>Correct Answer: D</strong></p></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
</tbody>
</table>

## 1. Key Stem Clues / 题干关键词抓考点

<table>
<colgroup>

<strong>为什么重要</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>Blunt trauma from soccer ball<br />
足球击中面部（钝性外伤）</td>
<td>Classic mechanism for traumatic hyphema via damage to AC angle, iris root, or ciliary body<br />
典型前房积血机制：前房角、虹膜根部或睫状体受损出血</td>
</tr>

<td>Hydroxyurea use<br />
羟基脲使用</td>
<td>Increases fetal hemoglobin (HbF) to reduce sickling crises, but does NOT reduce intraocular complication risk from hyphema<br />
增加胎儿血红蛋白（HbF）以减少镰变危象，但不能降低前房积血的眼内并发症风险</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Family history of glaucoma<br />
青光眼家族史</td>
<td>Distractor; relevant to long-term open-angle glaucoma risk but does not significantly increase acute hyphema complication risk<br />
干扰项；与长期开角型青光眼风险相关，但不显著增加急性前房积血并发症风险</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

## 2. Mechanism / 机制理解

**Traumatic hyphema** occurs when blunt force damages richly **vascularized structures** in the anterior segment — the **AC angle**, **iris root**, or **ciliary body** — causing hemorrhage into the anterior chamber:

**外伤性前房积血**发生于钝性外力损伤前节**富含血管结构**——**前房角**、**虹膜根部**或**睫状体**——导致出血进入前房：

- Blood accumulates inferiorly by gravity, producing the classic layered hyphema appearance\
  血液因重力沉积于下方，形成典型的分层前房积血外观

- Red blood cells obstruct the trabecular meshwork → reduced aqueous outflow → elevated IOP\
  红细胞堵塞小梁网 → 房水流出减少 → 眼压升高

- In sickle cell disease, **sickled RBCs** are rigid and deformed — they cannot traverse the trabecular meshwork, causing far more severe and persistent IOP elevation than normal RBCs\
  镰状细胞病患者，**镰状红细胞**僵硬变形——无法通过小梁网，造成比正常红细胞严重得多的持续性眼压升高

- Elevated IOP → retinal ischemia → triggers further sickling in **retinal arterioles and venules** → retinal arterial or venous occlusion → rapid, irreversible vision loss\
  眼压升高 → 视网膜缺血 → 诱发**视网膜小动脉和小静脉**内进一步镰变 → 视网膜动静脉闭塞 → 迅速、不可逆的视力丧失

**Anatomic rule of thumb:** The trabecular meshwork is the "drain filter" of the anterior chamber — anything that clogs it (blood cells, sickled cells, inflammatory debris) raises IOP downstream.

**解剖小窍门:** 小梁网是前房的"排水过滤器"——任何堵塞它的物质（血细胞、镰状细胞、炎性碎屑）都会导致眼压升高。

## 3. Correct Answer (D) — Sickle Cell Disease / 正确答案 (D) — 镰状细胞病

**Sickle cell disease** creates a unique vicious cycle that dramatically amplifies hyphema complications beyond what other listed factors can produce:

**镰状细胞病**产生独特的恶性循环，使前房积血并发症的严重程度远超其他所列因素：

- Sickled RBCs are rigid and cannot be filtered through the trabecular meshwork, causing disproportionate, refractory IOP elevation\
  镰状红细胞僵硬，无法被小梁网过滤，导致不成比例、难治性的眼压升高

- Elevated IOP → retinal ischemia → triggers sickling in retinal arterioles and venules\
  眼压升高 → 视网膜缺血 → 诱发视网膜小动脉和小静脉内镰变

- Retinal vascular occlusions (arterial or venous) cause rapid, irreversible vision loss — a catastrophic outcome not shared by non-sickle patients\
  视网膜血管闭塞（动脉或静脉）导致迅速、不可逆视力丧失——非镰状细胞患者不存在此灾难性结局

**Diagnosis:** Hyphema with elevated IOP in a known sickle cell disease patient — the combination mandates urgent, aggressive management with a compressed timeline

**诊断:** 已知镰状细胞病患者发生前房积血伴眼压升高——该组合需要紧急、积极的处理，且时间窗口大幅压缩

**Treatment:** Topical IOP-lowering agents first (prefer topical CAIs over systemic acetazolamide, which worsens sickling); surgical anterior chamber washout is indicated if IOP is not controlled within 24 hours — compared to 5 days for patients without sickle cell disease

**治疗:** 首选局部降眼压药（优先局部碳酸酐酶抑制剂而非全身性乙酰唑胺，后者会加重镰变）；若 24 小时内眼压未控制，需手术前房冲洗——而非镰状细胞患者可等待 5 天

<strong>为什么错</strong></th>

<strong>鉴别要点</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>A — Age<br />
A — 年龄</td>
<td>Young age increases hyphema incidence (higher rate of ocular trauma in adolescents) but does NOT increase the rate of complications once hyphema has already occurred<br />
年龄小增加前房积血发生率（青少年眼外伤更多），但一旦发生前房积血，不增加并发症发生率</td>

<tr>

外祖父青光眼史与长期开角型青光眼风险相关，与急性前房积血并发症无关；间接风险远不及患者自身的系统性疾病</td>

间接家族风险 vs. 直接系统性病理生理</td>
