<tr>
<td>C — Hydroxyurea use<br />
C — 羟基脲使用</td>
<td>Hydroxyurea increases HbF and reduces sickling crises; it does not cause increased intraocular bleeding and does not worsen hyphema complication risk — it is a treatment, not a risk factor<br />
羟基脲增加 HbF、减少镰变危象；不增加眼内出血，不加重前房积血并发症风险——是治疗药物，不是危险因素</td>
<td>Treatment for sickle cell disease ≠ complication risk factor<br />
镰状细胞病治疗药物 ≠ 并发症危险因素</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>D — Sickle cell disease ✓<br />
D — 镰状细胞病 ✓</td>
<td>CORRECT — Sickled RBCs cause disproportionate trabecular meshwork obstruction → refractory IOP elevation → retinal vascular sickling → irreversible vision loss; unique vicious cycle absent in other options<br />
正确——镰状红细胞造成不成比例的小梁网梗阻 → 难治性眼压升高 → 视网膜血管镰变 → 不可逆视力丧失；其他选项均无此独特恶性循环</td>
<td>Only factor that triggers a pathophysiologic cascade unique to hyphema in this disease<br />
唯一触发该病特有前房积血病理生理级联的因素</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

*The most tempting distractor is (B) family history of glaucoma — it seems relevant because this patient already has elevated IOP, but glaucoma family history affects lifetime open-angle glaucoma risk, not the acute complication profile of traumatic hyphema.*

最强干扰项是（B）青光眼家族史——因患者已有眼压升高而显得相关，但青光眼家族史影响的是终身开角型青光眼风险，而非急性外伤性前房积血的并发症。

## 5. High-Yield Summary Table — Hyphema Management: General Population vs. Sickle Cell Disease / 前房积血处理对比：普通患者 vs. 镰状细胞病患者

## 6. One-Sentence Summary & Memory Hook / 一句话总结 & 记忆钩

**In traumatic hyphema, sickle cell disease is the most dangerous comorbidity because rigid sickled RBCs obstruct the trabecular meshwork causing refractory IOP elevation, which then triggers retinal vascular sickling and irreversible vision loss — mandating surgical washout if IOP is not controlled within 24 hours.**

**外伤性前房积血中，镰状细胞病是最危险的合并症，因为僵硬的镰状红细胞堵塞小梁网导致难治性眼压升高，继而诱发视网膜血管镰变和不可逆视力丧失——若 24 小时内眼压未控制则须手术冲洗。**

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 100%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><p><strong>Memory Hook — SICK Eye Rule / 记忆钩 — "SICK 眼"规则:</strong></p>
<p>• <strong>S</strong>ickled RBCs — rigid, clog the trabecular meshwork / 镰状红细胞——僵硬，堵塞小梁网<br />
• <strong>I</strong>OP spikes — refractory, disproportionately high / 眼压骤升——难治性，不成比例地高<br />
• <strong>C</strong>ascade — retinal ischemia → further sickling → vascular occlusion / 级联反应——视网膜缺血 → 进一步镰变 → 血管闭塞<br />
• <strong>K</strong>ey clock: 24 hours to surgical washout (not 5 days!) / 关键时钟：24 小时内手术冲洗（不是 5 天！）</p></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
</tbody>
</table>

## 7. High-Yield Topic Knowledge — Hyphema: Etiology, Complications & Sickle Cell Implications / 高频知识表 — 前房积血：病因、并发症与镰状细胞病关联

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 50%" />
<col style="width: 50%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Topic</strong><br />
<strong>考点</strong></th>
<th><strong>Key Points</strong><br />
<strong>要点</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>Definition and grading<br />
定义与分级</td>
<td>Hyphema = blood in anterior chamber; graded 0–4 by percentage filling; blood pools inferiorly by gravity<br />
前房积血 = 血液积聚于前房；按充填比例分 0–4 级；血液因重力沉积于下方</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Common etiologies<br />
常见病因</td>
<td>Blunt ocular trauma (most common); post-surgical; spontaneous (von Willebrand disease, hemophilia, leukemia, anticoagulants)<br />
眼球钝性外伤（最常见）；术后；自发性（vWD、血友病、白血病、抗凝药）</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Acute complications<br />
急性并发症</td>
<td>Elevated IOP → glaucomatous optic nerve damage; rebleeding (peaks day 3–5 post-trauma); corneal blood staining with prolonged high IOP<br />
眼压升高 → 青光眼性视神经损伤；再出血（外伤后第 3–5 天高峰）；长期高眼压致角膜血染</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Sickle cell — unique danger<br />
镰状细胞病——特殊危险</td>
<td>Sickled RBCs irreversibly obstruct trabecular meshwork → severe IOP spike → retinal ischemia → sickling in retinal vessels → retinal arterial/venous occlusion → irreversible vision loss<br />
镰状红细胞不可逆地堵塞小梁网 → 眼压急剧升高 → 视网膜缺血 → 视网膜血管内镰变 → 视网膜动静脉闭塞 → 不可逆视力丧失</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Hydroxyurea pharmacology<br />
羟基脲药理</td>
<td>Induces HbF synthesis → dilutes HbS → reduces polymerization and sickling crises; does not affect intraocular bleeding risk or hyphema complication rates<br />
诱导 HbF 合成 → 稀释 HbS → 减少聚合与镰变危象；不影响眼内出血风险或前房积血并发症发生率</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Medical management principles<br />
药物处理原则</td>
<td>Topical beta-blockers or alpha-2 agonists to lower IOP; avoid miotics (worsen inflammation); avoid aspirin/NSAIDs (increase rebleeding risk); avoid systemic acetazolamide in sickle cell patients<br />
局部β阻断剂或α2激动剂降低眼压；避免缩瞳剂（加重炎症）；避免阿司匹林/NSAID（增加再出血风险）；镰状细胞患者避免全身性乙酰唑胺</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Chronic complication: angle recession<br />
慢性并发症：角度后退性青光眼</td>
<td>Up to 10% of traumatic hyphema patients develop late angle recession glaucoma months to years post-injury due to trabecular meshwork scarring; lifelong IOP monitoring required<br />
高达 10% 的外伤性前房积血患者因小梁网瘢痕化在伤后数月至数年发生迟发性角度后退性青光眼；需终身监测眼压</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

## 8. Extensions / 延伸扩展

- **Rebleeding risk:** Rebleeding peaks at day 3–5 post-injury due to clot retraction exposing friable new vessels; it is typically more severe than the initial bleed and is the rationale for activity restriction and avoiding antiplatelet agents\
  **再出血风险:** 再出血高峰在伤后第 3–5 天，因血凝块收缩暴露脆弱新生血管；通常比初次出血更严重，这是限制活动和禁用抗血小板药的依据

- **Sickle cell trait (HbAS) also at risk:** Both sickle cell disease (HbSS) and trait (HbAS) confer elevated hyphema complication risk; HbAS can sickle under the hypoxic, acidic microenvironment of the anterior chamber even without systemic crisis\
  **镰状细胞特征（HbAS）同样高风险:** 镰状细胞病（HbSS）和特征（HbAS）均增加前房积血并发症风险；HbAS 在前房低氧、酸性微环境中可发生镰变，即使无全身性危象

- **Systemic acetazolamide contraindication:** In sickle cell patients, systemic acetazolamide causes metabolic acidosis and hyperosmolarity that worsen RBC sickling — topical dorzolamide or brinzolamide are the preferred alternatives\
  **全身性乙酰唑胺禁忌:** 镰状细胞患者使用全身性乙酰唑胺可致代谢性酸中毒和高渗透压，加重红细胞镰变——首选局部多佐胺或布林唑胺替代

- **Differential of spontaneous hyphema:** Unlike traumatic hyphema, spontaneous hyphema in the absence of trauma should prompt workup for coagulopathy (hemophilia, vWD), hematologic malignancy (leukemia), or anticoagulant overdose\
  **自发性前房积血鉴别:** 与外伤性前房积血不同，无外伤史的自发性前房积血应排查凝血障碍（血友病、vWD）、血液系统恶性肿瘤（白血病）或抗凝药过量

# Question 186 — Sexually Transmitted Epididymitis / 性传播感染性附睾炎

## Question Stem / 题干

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 100%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><p>A <strong>previously healthy 16-year-old boy</strong> comes to the physician because of <strong>constant right-sided scrotal pain for 36 hours</strong>. He had <strong>sexual intercourse with a new partner 1 week ago</strong>. His temperature is <strong>38°C (100.4°F)</strong>. Abdominal examination shows no abnormalities. There is a <strong>scant penile discharge</strong>. The <strong>right scrotum is swollen and tender, especially posteriorly</strong>. The <strong>pain is less severe when the scrotum is elevated</strong>. Urinalysis and Gram stain of the urethral discharge show <strong>leukocytes</strong>. Which of the following is the most appropriate next step in management?</p>
<p><strong>Q: Most appropriate next step in management?</strong></p>
<p>A) Semen analysis<br />
B) Transillumination of the scrotum<br />
C) Doppler ultrasonography<br />
D) CT scan<br />
E) Antibiotic therapy<br />
F) Operative procedure</p>
<p><strong>Correct Answer: E</strong></p></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
</tbody>
</table>

## 1. Key Stem Clues / 题干关键词抓考点

<tr>
<td>16-year-old, new sexual partner 1 week ago<br />

<td>Points to sexually transmitted etiology (Chlamydia trachomatis or Neisseria gonorrhoeae) rather than enteric organisms<br />

</tr>
<tr>

疼痛持续 36 小时</td>
<td>Subacute onset favors epididymitis; testicular torsion typically presents more acutely (hours)<br />
亚急性起病倾向附睾炎；睾丸扭转通常更急（数小时内）</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

---

## 2. Mechanism / 机制理解

**Epididymitis** in sexually active adolescents is most commonly caused by **ascending infection** from urethritis: **Chlamydia trachomatis** (most common) or **Neisseria gonorrhoeae**. The organism travels from the urethra to the vas deferens and into the **epididymis**, producing an acute inflammatory response with hypervascularity, edema, and purulent exudate:

**附睾炎**在性活跃青少年中最常由**上行性感染**引起，源自尿道炎：**沙眼衣原体**（最常见）或**淋病奈瑟菌**。病原体从尿道经输精管上行至**附睾**，引发急性炎症反应，伴充血、水肿和脓性渗出：

- Urethral colonization → retrograde ascent via vas deferens → epididymal inflammation\
  尿道定植 → 经输精管逆行上行 → 附睾炎症

- Posterior epididymal swelling compresses surrounding structures → scrotal fullness and pain\
  附睾后部肿胀压迫周围组织 → 阴囊胀满感和疼痛

- Cremasteric reflex is **preserved** (unlike torsion) because the nerve is not compromised\
  提睾反射**保留**（与扭转不同），因为神经未受影响

- Prehn sign positive: elevating testis reduces venous congestion and stretch → pain relief\
  Prehn 征阳性：托举睾丸减少静脉淤血和牵拉 → 疼痛缓解

**Anatomic rule of thumb:** The epididymis sits posterior and superior to the testis — posterior tenderness on palpation = epididymitis until proven otherwise.

**解剖小窍门:** 附睾位于睾丸后上方——触诊时后部压痛 = 附睾炎，直到排除其他诊断为止。

---

## 3. Correct Answer (E) — Antibiotic Therapy for STI Epididymitis / 正确答案 (E) — STI 性附睾炎的抗生素治疗

**Antibiotic therapy** is the immediate treatment of choice when clinical features clearly support **infectious epididymitis** caused by a sexually transmitted pathogen:

**抗生素治疗**是临床表现明确支持**性传播病原体感染性附睾炎**时的首选即刻治疗：

- Ceftriaxone 500 mg IM single dose (covers N. gonorrhoeae) + Doxycycline 100 mg PO BID × 10 days (covers C. trachomatis)\
  头孢曲松 500 mg 肌注单次（覆盖淋球菌）+ 多西环素 100 mg 口服 BID × 10 天（覆盖衣原体）

- Azithromycin 1 g single dose is an alternative when doxycycline compliance is a concern\
  阿奇霉素 1 g 单次是依从性存疑时的替代方案

- Adjuncts: NSAIDs, bed rest, scrotal support, ice packs for symptom relief\
  辅助措施：NSAIDs、卧床休息、阴囊托举、冰敷以缓解症状

- Follow-up NAAT (nucleic acid amplification testing) to identify specific organism and screen for co-infections (syphilis, HIV)\
  随访 NAAT（核酸扩增检测）以明确病原体并筛查合并感染（梅毒、HIV）

**Diagnosis:** Classic triad of posterior scrotal tenderness + positive Prehn sign + leukocytes in discharge in a sexually active young male = STI epididymitis; initiate treatment empirically without waiting for culture results.

**诊断:** 性活跃年轻男性出现阴囊后部压痛 + Prehn 征阳性 + 分泌物白细胞的经典三联征 = STI 附睾炎；经验性治疗，无需等待培养结果。

**Treatment:** Ceftriaxone + doxycycline (or azithromycin); treat partner(s) concurrently; report to public health if gonorrhea confirmed.

**治疗:** 头孢曲松 + 多西环素（或阿奇霉素）；同时治疗性伴侣；确认淋病后向公共卫生部门报告。

---

## 4. Options Elimination / 错误选项排除逻辑

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 33%" />
<col style="width: 33%" />
<col style="width: 33%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Option</strong><br />
<strong>选项</strong></th>
<th><strong>Why Wrong</strong><br />
<strong>为什么错</strong></th>
<th><strong>Key Discriminator</strong><br />
<strong>鉴别要点</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>A — Semen analysis<br />
A — 精液分析</td>
<td>Wrong — used for infertility evaluation, not acute scrotal pain or infection workup<br />
错误——用于不育症评估，与急性阴囊痛或感染无关</td>
<td>No role in acute infectious scrotal pathology<br />
在急性感染性阴囊病变中无适应证</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>B — Transillumination of the scrotum<br />
B — 阴囊透光试验</td>
<td>Wrong — used to diagnose hydrocele (painless, transilluminates); this patient has painful, swollen scrotum from infection<br />
错误——用于诊断鞘膜积液（无痛，透光阳性）；本患者阴囊疼痛肿胀源于感染</td>
<td>Hydrocele presents painlessly without fever or discharge<br />
鞘膜积液无疼痛，无发热和分泌物</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>C — Doppler ultrasonography<br />
C — 多普勒超声</td>
<td>Wrong — most useful when testicular torsion is suspected (shows absent blood flow); this presentation is classic epididymitis, so Doppler would not change management<br />
错误——最适用于疑似睾丸扭转（显示血流缺失）；本例表现为经典附睾炎，超声不会改变处理方案</td>
<td>Use Doppler when diagnosis is uncertain (torsion vs. epididymitis), not when clinical features are already classic<br />
仅在诊断不确定时（扭转 vs. 附睾炎）使用超声，不适用于临床表现已经典型时</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>D — CT scan<br />
D — CT 扫描</td>
<td>Wrong — CT evaluates pelvic/abdominal pathology but is inadequate for acute scrotal conditions; radiation without diagnostic benefit here<br />
错误——CT 评估盆腔/腹腔病变，不适用于急性阴囊疾病；此处辐射暴露无诊断获益</td>
<td>Ultrasound (not CT) is the imaging modality of choice for scrotal pathology<br />
超声（非 CT）是阴囊疾病的首选影像学方法</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>E — Antibiotic therapy ✓<br />
E — 抗生素治疗 ✓</td>
<td>CORRECT — classic STI epididymitis with positive Prehn sign, posterior tenderness, penile discharge, and leukocytes; empiric antibiotics are the immediate next step<br />
正确——经典 STI 附睾炎，Prehn 征阳性、后部压痛、阴茎分泌物及白细胞；经验性抗生素治疗是立即下一步</td>
<td>All other options are either irrelevant workup or appropriate only for torsion/other diagnoses<br />
其他选项均为无关检查或仅适用于扭转/其他诊断</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>F — Operative procedure<br />
F — 手术操作</td>
<td>Wrong — surgery (orchiopexy) is indicated for testicular torsion to prevent infarction; this patient lacks torsion features (no absent cremasteric reflex, Prehn sign positive)<br />
错误——手术（睾丸固定术）用于睾丸扭转以防止梗死；本患者无扭转特征（提睾反射保留、Prehn 征阳性）</td>
<td>Absent cremasteric reflex + sudden onset + NO discharge would favor torsion requiring surgery<br />
提睾反射消失 + 突然发作 + 无分泌物才支持需要手术的扭转</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

*The most tempting distractor is C (Doppler ultrasound) — test-takers may reflexively order imaging to "rule out torsion," but when clinical features clearly point to epididymitis (positive Prehn, discharge, leukocytes, fever), empiric antibiotics come first.*

Doppler 超声是最容易混淆的干扰项——考生可能条件反射地选择影像学"排除扭转"，但当临床表现已明确指向附睾炎（Prehn 征阳性、分泌物、白细胞、发热）时，经验性抗生素才是第一步。

## 5. High-Yield Summary Table — Epididymitis vs. Testicular Torsion / 附睾炎 vs. 睾丸扭转鉴别对比

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 33%" />
<col style="width: 33%" />
<col style="width: 33%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Feature</strong><br />
<strong>特征</strong></th>
<th><strong>Epididymitis</strong><br />
<strong>附睾炎</strong></th>
<th><strong>Testicular Torsion</strong><br />
<strong>睾丸扭转</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>Age / peak<br />
年龄/高峰</td>
<td>Sexually active adolescents &amp; adults (15–35 y)<br />
性活跃青少年和成人（15–35 岁）</td>
<td>Bimodal: neonates and adolescents (12–18 y)<br />
双峰：新生儿和青少年（12–18 岁）</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Onset<br />
起病方式</td>
<td>Subacute (hours to days)<br />
亚急性（数小时至数天）</td>
<td>Sudden, acute (minutes to hours)<br />
突然、急性（数分钟至数小时）</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Fever<br />
发热</td>
<td>Common (38–39°C)<br />
常见（38–39°C）</td>
<td>Absent (typically afebrile)<br />
无（通常无发热）</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Penile/urethral discharge<br />
阴茎/尿道分泌物</td>
<td>Present (STI etiology)<br />
有（STI 病因）</td>
<td>Absent<br />
无</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Prehn sign (elevation)<br />
Prehn 征（托举）</td>
<td>Positive — pain relieved<br />
阳性——疼痛缓解</td>
<td>Negative — pain unchanged or worse<br />
阴性——疼痛不变或加重</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Cremasteric reflex<br />
提睾反射</td>
<td>Preserved<br />
保留</td>
<td>Absent (highly specific for torsion)<br />
消失（高度特异性提示扭转）</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Tenderness location<br />
压痛部位</td>
<td>Posterior scrotal (epididymis)<br />
阴囊后部（附睾）</td>
<td>Diffuse testicular; may have transverse lie<br />
弥漫性睾丸；可有睾丸横位</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Doppler ultrasound<br />
多普勒超声</td>
<td>Normal or increased flow (hypervascularity)<br />
正常或血流增多（充血）</td>
<td>Absent or decreased blood flow<br />
血流缺失或减少</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Treatment<br />
治疗</td>
<td>Antibiotics (ceftriaxone + doxycycline)<br />
抗生素（头孢曲松 + 多西环素）</td>
<td>Emergency surgery — orchiopexy within 6 hours<br />
急诊手术——6 小时内睾丸固定术</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

## 6. One-Sentence Summary & Memory Hook / 一句话总结 & 记忆钩

**A sexually active adolescent with subacute scrotal pain, posterior epididymal tenderness, penile discharge, fever, and a positive Prehn sign has epididymitis caused by C. trachomatis or N. gonorrhoeae, and should be treated immediately with ceftriaxone plus doxycycline.**

**性活跃青少年出现亚急性阴囊疼痛、附睾后部压痛、阴茎分泌物、发热及 Prehn 征阳性，诊断为衣原体或淋球菌性附睾炎，应立即给予头孢曲松联合多西环素治疗。**

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 100%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><p><strong>Memory Hook — PRED Distinguishes Epididymitis / 记忆钩 — PRED 四字诀鉴别附睾炎:</strong></p>
<p>• <strong>P</strong>rehn sign positive — elevation relieves pain (epididymitis) / Prehn 征阳性——托举缓解疼痛（附睾炎）<br />
• <strong>R</strong>eflex cremasteric preserved — no torsion / 提睾反射保留——排除扭转<br />
• <strong>E</strong>tiologic agents: Chlamydia trachomatis #1, N. gonorrhoeae #2 / 病原体：衣原体第一，淋球菌第二<br />
• <strong>D</strong>ischarge present + leukocytes = STI → empiric antibiotics NOW / 分泌物 + 白细胞 = STI → 立即经验性抗生素</p></th>
</tr>

## 7. High-Yield Topic Knowledge — Epididymitis: Diagnosis & Management / 高频知识表 — 附睾炎：诊断与处理

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 50%" />
<col style="width: 50%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Topic</strong><br />
<strong>考点</strong></th>
<th><strong>Key Points</strong><br />
<strong>要点</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>Most common organisms by age<br />
按年龄分组的最常见病原体</td>
<td>Age &lt;35 / sexually active: C. trachomatis &gt; N. gonorrhoeae; Age &gt;35 or anal insertive sex: E. coli and other enteric organisms<br />
35 岁以下/性活跃：衣原体 &gt; 淋球菌；35 岁以上或肛交插入方：大肠杆菌等肠道菌群</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Prehn sign<br />
Prehn 征</td>
<td>Scrotal elevation relieves pain in epididymitis; does NOT relieve (or worsens) pain in testicular torsion<br />
托举阴囊可缓解附睾炎疼痛；睾丸扭转时无法缓解甚至加重</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Cremasteric reflex<br />
提睾反射</td>
<td>Preserved in epididymitis; ABSENT in testicular torsion (most sensitive/specific sign for torsion in adolescents)<br />
附睾炎中保留；睾丸扭转中消失（青少年扭转最敏感/特异的体征）</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>First-line treatment (STI epididymitis)<br />
一线治疗（STI 性附睾炎）</td>
<td>Ceftriaxone 500 mg IM × 1 dose + Doxycycline 100 mg PO BID × 10 days; treat sexual partner(s) concurrently<br />
头孢曲松 500 mg 肌注单次 + 多西环素 100 mg 口服 BID × 10 天；同时治疗性伴侣</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Role of Doppler ultrasound<br />
多普勒超声的作用</td>
<td>Indicated when diagnosis is uncertain to distinguish torsion (absent flow) from epididymitis (normal/increased flow); NOT needed when clinical picture is classic<br />
当诊断不确定时用于鉴别扭转（血流缺失）与附睾炎（正常/增多）；临床表现典型时无需进行</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Epididymo-orchitis<br />
附睾睾丸炎</td>
<td>Extension of epididymitis to the testis; presents with even more severe swelling; Doppler may show global hypervascularity; same antibiotic regimen<br />
附睾炎累及睾丸；肿胀更严重；多普勒可见全面充血；抗生素方案相同</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Follow-up<br />
随访</td>
<td>NAAT for C. trachomatis and N. gonorrhoeae; screen for HIV, syphilis, hepatitis B/C; partner notification and treatment mandatory<br />
衣原体和淋球菌 NAAT 检测；筛查 HIV、梅毒、乙/丙型肝炎；强制伴侣通知和治疗</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

---

## 8. Extensions / 延伸扩展

- **Differential of acute scrotum:** Epididymitis, testicular torsion, torsion of testicular appendage (blue dot sign in prepubertal boys), incarcerated inguinal hernia, orchitis (often mumps in unvaccinated)\
  **急性阴囊的鉴别诊断:** 附睾炎、睾丸扭转、睾丸附件扭转（青春期前男孩蓝点征）、嵌顿性腹股沟疝、睾丸炎（未接种疫苗者常为腮腺炎）

- **Torsion window:** Testicular salvage rate is \>90% if detorsion occurs within 6 hours, drops to ~50% at 12 hours, and near 0% at 24 hours — distinguishing torsion from epididymitis is a time-sensitive priority\
  **扭转时间窗:** 6 小时内复位睾丸挽救率 \>90%，12 小时降至约 50%，24 小时接近 0%——鉴别扭转与附睾炎是时间敏感的优先事项

- **Key complication of untreated epididymitis:** Abscess formation, infertility (bilateral scarring), chronic epididymitis, and spread to adjacent testis (epididymo-orchitis)\
  **未治疗附睾炎的关键并发症:** 脓肿形成、不育症（双侧瘢痕）、慢性附睾炎、累及邻近睾丸（附睾睾丸炎）

- **Variant — enteric epididymitis:** Men \>35 years or those practicing receptive anal intercourse: treat with levofloxacin 500 mg PO daily × 10 days (covers E. coli and other Gram-negative organisms)\
  **题目变式——肠道菌群性附睾炎:** 35 岁以上男性或肛交接受方：左氧氟沙星 500 mg 口服每日一次 × 10 天（覆盖大肠杆菌等革兰阴性菌）

# Question 187 — Acute Pseudogout (CPPD Disease) / 急性假性痛风（焦磷酸钙沉积病）

## Question Stem / 题干

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 100%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><p>A <strong>52-year-old woman</strong> comes to the physician because of a <strong>1-week history</strong> of increasingly severe <strong>pain and swelling of her right knee</strong>. She now is <strong>unable to walk</strong> because of the symptoms. Five years ago, she fell and hit the knee on the bathroom floor. She has hypertension treated with lisinopril. Her temperature is 36.9°C (98.4°F), pulse is 84/min, respirations are 20/min, and blood pressure is 132/76 mm Hg. The right knee is <strong>erythematous, swollen, and warm</strong>. There is diffuse tenderness to light touch; passive and active range of motion is limited by pain. There is no crepitus, but ballottement shows <strong>moderate knee effusion</strong>. Arthrocentesis is performed, and joint fluid analysis shows a <strong>leukocyte count of 50,000/mm³</strong>. A Gram stain is negative; <strong>rhomboid-shaped crystals</strong> are present. An x-ray of the knee is shown.</p>
<p><strong>Q: Which of the following is the most appropriate pharmacotherapy?</strong></p>
<p>A) Febuxostat<br />
B) Ibuprofen<br />
C) Infliximab<br />
D) Methotrexate<br />
E) Penicillamine</p>
<p><strong>Correct Answer: B</strong></p></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
</tbody>
</table>

## 1. Key Stem Clues / 题干关键词抓考点

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 50%" />
<col style="width: 50%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Key Stem Clue</strong><br />
<strong>关键词</strong></th>
<th><strong>Why It Matters</strong><br />
<strong>为什么重要</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>Rhomboid-shaped crystals<br />
菱形晶体</td>
<td>Pathognomonic for CPPD (pseudogout); needle-shaped crystals indicate gout instead<br />
假性痛风的病理诊断特征；针状晶体则提示痛风</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Gram stain negative<br />
革兰染色阴性</td>
<td>Rules out septic arthritis, the most dangerous and urgent mimic requiring antibiotics<br />
排除化脓性关节炎，后者是最危险、最紧迫的鉴别诊断，需立即抗生素治疗</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Leukocyte count 50,000/mm³<br />
白细胞计数 50,000/mm³</td>
<td>Confirms inflammatory arthritis; septic arthritis typically pushes WBC &gt;100,000 with positive culture<br />
确认炎症性关节炎；化脓性关节炎白细胞通常超过100,000且培养阳性</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Right knee monoarthritis<br />
右膝单关节炎</td>
<td>Knee is the most common joint affected by pseudogout; podagra (1st MTP) favors gout<br />
膝关节是假性痛风最常受累部位；痛风足（第一跖趾关节）更提示痛风</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>History of knee trauma 5 years ago<br />
5年前膝关节外伤史</td>
<td>Trauma is a recognized precipitating factor for acute CPPD crystal shedding and flares<br />
外伤是急性 CPPD 晶体脱落和发作的已知诱发因素</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Afebrile (36.9°C), no systemic toxicity<br />
无发热（36.9°C），无全身中毒表现</td>
<td>Lowers suspicion for septic arthritis (typically febrile); supports crystal-driven arthritis<br />
降低化脓性关节炎可能性（通常伴发热）；支持晶体性关节炎诊断</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

## 2. Mechanism / 机制理解

**Calcium pyrophosphate dihydrate (CPPD)** crystals deposit in articular cartilage and fibrocartilage over years due to **elevated inorganic pyrophosphate** in the synovial microenvironment. Acute flares occur when crystals shed into the joint space, where they are phagocytosed by neutrophils, triggering an **IL-1β–mediated inflammatory cascade**:

**焦磷酸钙二水合物（CPPD）**晶体因滑液微环境中**无机焦磷酸盐浓度升高**而在关节软骨和纤维软骨中多年积累。当晶体脱落进入关节腔时，中性粒细胞将其吞噬，触发 **IL-1β 介导的炎症级联反应**：

- CPPD crystals accumulate silently over years → shed acutely with trauma, surgery, or acute illness\
  CPPD 晶体多年静默积累 → 在外伤、手术或急性疾病时急性脱落

- Neutrophils phagocytose crystals → lysosomal rupture → release of IL-1β, IL-6, TNF-α\
  中性粒细胞吞噬晶体 → 溶酶体破裂 → 释放 IL-1β、IL-6、TNF-α

- Cytokine surge → synovial inflammation → erythema, warmth, severe effusion, limited ROM\
  细胞因子骤增 → 滑膜炎 → 红斑、局部发热、明显积液、活动受限

- X-ray hallmark: **chondrocalcinosis** (linear calcification of hyaline cartilage and fibrocartilage)\
  X线特征：**软骨钙化症**（透明软骨和纤维软骨线性钙化）

**Anatomic rule of thumb:** Pseudogout favors large joints (knee \> wrist \> hip); gout favors small joints (1st MTP "podagra" \> ankle).

**解剖小窍门:** 假性痛风好发于大关节（膝关节 \> 腕关节 \> 髋关节）；痛风好发于小关节（第一跖趾关节"痛风足" \> 踝关节）。

## 3. Correct Answer (B) — NSAIDs for Acute Crystal Arthritis / 正确答案 (B) — NSAIDs 治疗急性晶体性关节炎

**Ibuprofen (NSAID)** targets COX-1/COX-2–mediated prostaglandin synthesis, directly suppressing the inflammatory response triggered by CPPD crystal phagocytosis:

**布洛芬（NSAID）**靶向 COX-1/COX-2 介导的前列腺素合成，直接抑制 CPPD 晶体吞噬所触发的炎症反应：

- NSAIDs inhibit COX-1/COX-2 → reduce prostaglandin E2 synthesis → decrease inflammation, pain, and fever\
  NSAIDs 抑制 COX-1/COX-2 → 减少前列腺素 E2 合成 → 减轻炎症、疼痛和发热

- Colchicine (alternative first-line) disrupts microtubule polymerization → inhibits neutrophil chemotaxis and crystal phagocytosis\
  秋水仙碱（替代一线药物）破坏微管聚合 → 抑制中性粒细胞趋化和晶体吞噬

- Intra-articular or systemic corticosteroids reserved for contraindications to NSAIDs/colchicine (e.g., renal failure, GI bleed)\
  关节内或全身糖皮质激素用于 NSAIDs/秋水仙碱禁忌时（如肾衰竭、胃肠道出血）

**Diagnosis:** Acute CPPD arthritis (pseudogout) confirmed by rhomboid-shaped weakly positively birefringent crystals on compensated polarized light microscopy, negative Gram stain ruling out septic arthritis, and chondrocalcinosis on knee x-ray.

**诊断:** 急性 CPPD 关节炎（假性痛风），由补偿偏振光显微镜下菱形弱正性双折射晶体、排除化脓性关节炎的革兰染色阴性，及膝关节 X 线软骨钙化症确诊。

**Treatment:** NSAIDs (ibuprofen, indomethacin) or colchicine for acute flares; intra-articular corticosteroid injection for refractory or contraindicated cases; no urate-lowering equivalent (no febuxostat/allopurinol) for CPPD.

**治疗:** 急性发作用 NSAIDs（布洛芬、吲哚美辛）或秋水仙碱；难治性或禁忌患者用关节内糖皮质激素注射；CPPD 无类似降尿酸的特异性长期治疗方案（无非布司他/别嘌醇）。

## 4. Options Elimination / 错误选项排除逻辑

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 33%" />
<col style="width: 33%" />
<col style="width: 33%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Option</strong><br />
<strong>选项</strong></th>
<th><strong>Why Wrong</strong><br />
<strong>为什么错</strong></th>
<th><strong>Key Discriminator</strong><br />
<strong>鉴别要点</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>A — Febuxostat<br />
A — 非布司他</td>
<td>Xanthine oxidase inhibitor that lowers uric acid synthesis — indicated for gout, not pseudogout<br />
黄嘌呤氧化酶抑制剂，减少尿酸合成——用于痛风而非假性痛风</td>
<td>Pseudogout involves CPPD crystals, not uric acid; febuxostat has no effect on pyrophosphate metabolism<br />
假性痛风涉及 CPPD 晶体而非尿酸；非布司他对焦磷酸代谢无任何作用</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>B — Ibuprofen ✓<br />
B — 布洛芬 ✓</td>
<td>CORRECT — NSAIDs are first-line for acute pseudogout; directly inhibits prostaglandin-mediated inflammation<br />
正确——NSAIDs 是急性假性痛风一线治疗，直接抑制前列腺素介导的炎症</td>
<td>COX inhibition addresses the acute crystal-triggered inflammatory cascade effectively<br />
COX 抑制有效针对晶体触发的急性炎症级联反应</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>C — Infliximab<br />
C — 英夫利西单抗</td>
<td>Anti-TNF-α monoclonal antibody for RA, IBD, psoriasis — no indication in crystal arthritis<br />
抗 TNF-α 单克隆抗体，用于类风湿关节炎、炎症性肠病、银屑病——在晶体性关节炎中无适应症</td>
<td>Biological DMARDs target chronic autoimmune inflammation; pseudogout is an acute crystal-driven process not requiring biologic therapy<br />
生物 DMARDs 针对慢性自身免疫性炎症；假性痛风是急性晶体驱动过程，不需要生物制剂治疗</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>D — Methotrexate<br />
D — 甲氨蝶呤</td>
<td>Dihydrofolate reductase inhibitor used as DMARD for RA, psoriasis, and certain lymphomas — not for CPPD<br />
二氢叶酸还原酶抑制剂，作为 DMARD 用于类风湿关节炎、银屑病和某些淋巴瘤——不用于 CPPD</td>
<td>Methotrexate targets chronic autoimmune pathways; pseudogout requires acute anti-inflammatory treatment, not immunosuppression<br />
甲氨蝶呤靶向慢性自身免疫通路；假性痛风需要急性抗炎治疗而非免疫抑制</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>E — Penicillamine<br />
E — 青霉胺</td>
<td>Chelating agent primarily for Wilson disease (copper); also used in RA — unrelated to CPPD pathophysiology<br />
螯合剂，主要用于 Wilson 病（铜蓄积）；也用于类风湿关节炎——与 CPPD 病理生理无关</td>
<td>No mechanism to address CPPD crystal deposition, pyrophosphate metabolism, or associated acute joint inflammation<br />
对 CPPD 晶体沉积、焦磷酸代谢或相关急性关节炎症均无任何治疗机制</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

*The most tempting distractor is (A) Febuxostat — examinees may conflate pseudogout with gout; the key discriminator is crystal morphology (rhomboid CPPD vs. needle-shaped monosodium urate) and the mechanistic point that febuxostat targets uric acid synthesis, not pyrophosphate.*

最容易混淆的干扰项是（A）非布司他——考生可能将假性痛风与痛风混淆；关键鉴别在于晶体形态（菱形 CPPD vs. 针状尿酸钠）以及非布司他靶向尿酸合成而非焦磷酸盐代谢这一机制要点。

## 6. One-Sentence Summary & Memory Hook / 一句话总结 & 记忆钩

**Pseudogout presents with acute large-joint inflammation (especially knee) due to rhomboid CPPD crystal shedding, diagnosed by arthrocentesis, and treated acutely with NSAIDs or colchicine — febuxostat and urate-lowering agents have no role.**

**假性痛风表现为菱形 CPPD 晶体脱落导致的大关节急性炎症（尤以膝关节为主），经关节穿刺确诊，急性期用 NSAIDs 或秋水仙碱治疗——非布司他等降尿酸药物无效。**

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 100%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><p><strong>Memory Hook — "RKCK for Pseudogout" / 记忆钩 — 假性痛风四要素 "RKCK":</strong></p>
<p>• <strong>R</strong>homboid crystals — CPPD morphology (vs. needle-shaped urate in gout) / 菱形晶体——CPPD 形态（vs. 痛风针状尿酸盐）<br />
• <strong>K</strong>nee is #1 joint — most common site for pseudogout, not the big toe / 膝关节最常受累——假性痛风最好发部位，而非大脚趾<br />
• <strong>C</strong>hondrocalcinosis on x-ray — linear cartilage calcification = CPPD fingerprint / X线软骨钙化症——线性软骨钙化是 CPPD 指纹特征<br />
• <strong>K</strong>eep NSAIDs/colchicine — same acute Rx as gout, but NO febuxostat/allopurinol / 保留 NSAIDs/秋水仙碱——急性期治疗与痛风相同，但无需非布司他/别嘌醇</p></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
</tbody>
</table>

## 7. High-Yield Topic Knowledge — Pseudogout (CPPD Disease) / 高频知识表 — 假性痛风（CPPD 病）

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 50%" />
<col style="width: 50%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Topic</strong><br />
<strong>考点</strong></th>
<th><strong>Key Points</strong><br />
<strong>要点</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>Crystal characteristics<br />
晶体特征</td>
<td>Rhomboid-shaped CPPD; weakly positively birefringent (blue parallel to slow axis of compensator); contrast with gout's needle-shaped negatively birefringent MSU (yellow parallel)<br />
菱形 CPPD 晶体；弱正性双折射（平行补偿器慢轴时蓝色）；与痛风针状负性双折射尿酸钠（平行时黄色）相对比</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Most common joint and distribution<br />
最常见关节及分布</td>
<td>Knee (most common), wrist, hip, shoulder, ankle; large joints predominate; contrast with gout's predilection for 1st MTP and distal joints<br />
膝关节（最常见）、腕关节、髋关节、肩关节、踝关节；以大关节为主；与痛风偏好第一跖趾关节和远端小关节相对比</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Synovial fluid analysis<br />
滑液分析</td>
<td>WBC typically 2,000–50,000/mm³; rhomboid crystals under compensated polarized light; Gram stain and culture negative (distinguishes from septic arthritis); arthrocentesis mandatory to exclude septic joint<br />
白细胞通常 2,000–50,000/mm³；补偿偏振光下见菱形晶体；革兰染色和培养阴性（区别于化脓性关节炎）；必须行关节穿刺排除化脓性关节</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>X-ray hallmark<br />
X线特征</td>
<td>Chondrocalcinosis — linear radiodense calcification within articular hyaline cartilage and fibrocartilage (knee menisci, wrist triangular fibrocartilage complex); may coexist with degenerative joint changes<br />
软骨钙化症——关节透明软骨和纤维软骨内线性高密度钙化（膝关节半月板、腕关节三角纤维软骨复合体）；可与退行性关节改变并存</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Associated metabolic conditions<br />
相关代谢疾病</td>
<td>Hyperparathyroidism, hemochromatosis, hypomagnesemia, hypothyroidism, hypophosphatasia — screen with PTH, calcium, ferritin/transferrin saturation, magnesium, TSH; especially in patients &lt;60 years old<br />
甲状旁腺功能亢进、血色病、低镁血症、甲状腺功能减退、低磷酸酯酶症——用 PTH、钙、铁蛋白/转铁蛋白饱和度、镁、TSH 筛查；尤其在&lt;60岁患者中</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Acute treatment hierarchy<br />
急性期治疗层次</td>
<td>First-line: NSAIDs (ibuprofen, indomethacin) or colchicine; Second-line: intra-articular corticosteroid injection; Third-line: systemic corticosteroids — choice depends on comorbidities (renal failure, GI risk, thrombocytopenia)<br />
一线：NSAIDs（布洛芬、吲哚美辛）或秋水仙碱；二线：关节内糖皮质激素注射；三线：全身糖皮质激素——选择取决于合并症（肾衰竭、胃肠道风险、血小板减少症）</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Chronic CPPD arthropathy<br />
慢性 CPPD 关节病</td>
<td>Can mimic osteoarthritis (chronic joint degeneration) or RA (polyarticular symmetric pattern); no disease-modifying equivalent to urate-lowering therapy; management is symptomatic<br />
可模仿骨关节炎（慢性关节退变）或类风湿关节炎（多关节对称模式）；无类似降尿酸治疗的病情改善药物；治疗以对症为主</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

## 8. Extensions / 延伸扩展

- **Differential of acute monoarthritis with effusion:** Septic arthritis (WBC \>100,000, Gram stain +, fever, unwell), gout (needle MSU, 1st MTP), pseudogout (rhomboid CPPD, knee), reactive arthritis (recent infection, asymmetric oligoarthritis), hemarthrosis (trauma, coagulopathy)\
  **伴积液的急性单关节炎鉴别诊断:** 化脓性关节炎（白细胞\>100,000，革兰染色阳性，发热，病情重），痛风（针状尿酸钠，第一跖趾关节），假性痛风（菱形 CPPD，膝关节），反应性关节炎（近期感染，不对称少关节炎），关节积血（外伤，凝血功能障碍）

- **Metabolic workup triggers:** CPPD in a patient \<60 years old or with recurrent flares warrants screening for hyperparathyroidism, hemochromatosis, hypomagnesemia, and hypothyroidism — correcting the underlying cause may reduce flare frequency\
  **代谢筛查触发条件:** \<60岁患者出现 CPPD 或反复发作者，需筛查甲状旁腺功能亢进、血色病、低镁血症和甲状腺功能减退——纠正潜在病因可降低发作频率

- **Variant — Crowned dens syndrome:** CPPD deposition around the odontoid process (C2 dens) causes acute neck pain, stiffness, and fever; can mimic meningitis or cervical spine infection on presentation\
  **变体——冠状齿突综合征:** CPPD 沉积于齿突（C2）周围，引起急性颈痛、颈项强直和发热；临床表现可类似脑膜炎或颈椎感染

- **Key exam trap — Lisinopril as a trigger:** Thiazide diuretics (not ACE inhibitors like lisinopril) precipitate gout by decreasing uric acid excretion; lisinopril in this stem is a red herring for gout—the rhomboid crystals and knee involvement confirm CPPD regardless of the medication history\
  **考试陷阱——赖诺普利作为诱因:** 噻嗪类利尿剂（而非赖诺普利等 ACE 抑制剂）通过减少尿酸排泄诱发痛风；本题中赖诺普利是提示痛风的"烟雾弹"——菱形晶体和膝关节受累无论用药史如何均确认 CPPD

# Question 188 — Post-thyroidectomy Hypoparathyroidism with Hypocalcemia / 甲状腺切除术后甲状旁腺功能减退伴低钙血症

## Question Stem / 题干

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 100%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><p>A <strong>28-year-old woman</strong> comes to the office for a follow-up examination <strong>2 weeks after undergoing a total thyroidectomy</strong> because of a thyroid nodule. Immediately after the operation, the patient had the onset of <strong>marked hypocalcemia</strong> and was admitted to the intensive care unit. During her hospital stay, intravenous calcium and calcitriol were administered. Today, she has had <strong>recurrent numbness around her mouth</strong> and <strong>muscle cramping</strong>. Current medications are <strong>calcium carbonate</strong> three times daily with meals and <strong>calcitriol</strong> twice daily. Vital signs are within normal limits. Physical examination shows <strong>spasm of the ipsilateral facial muscles when tapping 2 cm anterior to the ears on the zygomatic arch</strong> bilaterally. The remainder of the examination shows no abnormalities. Laboratory studies are most likely to show an increase in which of the following in this patient?</p>
<p><strong>Q: Laboratory studies are most likely to show an increase in which of the following in this patient?</strong></p>
<p>A) Serum calcium concentration<br />
B) Serum magnesium concentration<br />
C) Serum parathyroid hormone concentration<br />
D) Serum parathyroid hormone-related protein concentration<br />
E) Urinary 24-hour calcium excretion<br />
F) Urine potassium excretion</p>
<p><strong>Correct Answer: E</strong></p></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
</tbody>
</table>

## 2. Mechanism / 机制理解

**Parathyroid hormone (PTH)** is the master regulator of calcium homeostasis, exerting its effects at **three organ targets** to raise serum calcium:

**甲状旁腺激素 (PTH)** 是钙稳态的主调节激素，通过作用于**三个靶器官**来升高血钙：

- Bone: PTH activates osteoclasts → bone resorption → releases calcium and phosphate into serum\
  骨骼：PTH激活破骨细胞 → 骨吸收 → 钙和磷酸盐释放入血

- Kidney (DCT): PTH stimulates calcium reabsorption and phosphate excretion in the distal convoluted tubule\
  肾脏（远曲小管）：PTH刺激远曲小管钙重吸收并促进磷酸盐排泄

- Gut: PTH stimulates renal 1α-hydroxylase → converts 25-OH VitD to calcitriol → increases intestinal calcium absorption\
  肠道：PTH刺激肾脏1α-羟化酶 → 将25-羟维生素D转化为骨化三醇 → 增加肠道钙吸收

**Anatomic rule of thumb:** Without PTH, the renal DCT "calcium gate" closes — calcium filtered at the glomerulus cannot be reabsorbed. So even when serum calcium is low, urinary calcium excretion paradoxically rises.

**解剖小窍门:** 没有PTH，肾脏远曲小管的"钙闸门"关闭——肾小球滤过的钙无法被重吸收。因此，即使血钙偏低，尿钙排泄仍矛盾性升高。

## 3. Correct Answer (E) — Increased Urinary Calcium Excretion in Hypoparathyroidism / 正确答案 (E) — 甲状旁腺功能减退导致尿钙排泄增加

**Urinary 24-hour calcium excretion** is paradoxically elevated in hypoparathyroidism despite low serum calcium:

**24小时尿钙排泄** 在甲状旁腺功能减退时，尽管血钙偏低，尿钙却矛盾性升高：

- Loss of PTH → loss of PTH-stimulated calcium reabsorption in the DCT → more calcium escapes into urine\
  PTH缺乏 → 失去PTH介导的远曲小管钙重吸收 → 更多钙流失至尿液

- Calcium carbonate supplementation increases the filtered calcium load at the glomerulus → more calcium presented to an unresponsive tubule\
  碳酸钙补充增加肾小球滤过钙负荷 → 更多钙进入无法重吸收的肾小管

- Calcitriol supplementation enhances intestinal absorption → further raises serum and filtered calcium load\
  骨化三醇补充增强肠道吸收 → 进一步升高血钙和滤过钙负荷

- Net result: despite low serum calcium, the urine contains excess calcium (hypercalciuria) — a key long-term monitoring concern\
  净效果：尽管血钙低，尿液中仍含过多钙（高钙尿症）——这是长期监测的关键问题

**Diagnosis:** Post-thyroidectomy hypoparathyroidism with persistent hypocalcemic symptoms (Chvostek sign, perioral numbness) and hypercalciuria despite calcium/calcitriol therapy.

**诊断:** 甲状腺切除术后甲状旁腺功能减退，尽管已接受钙和骨化三醇治疗，仍有持续性低钙血症症状（Chvostek征、口周麻木）及高钙尿症。

**Treatment:** Continue oral calcium carbonate + calcitriol; monitor 24-hour urinary calcium to prevent nephrocalcinosis; thiazide diuretics can be added to reduce hypercalciuria by enhancing DCT calcium reabsorption independent of PTH.

**治疗:** 继续口服碳酸钙 + 骨化三醇；监测24小时尿钙以预防肾钙质沉着；可加用噻嗪类利尿剂，通过不依赖PTH的机制增强远曲小管钙重吸收来降低高钙尿症。

<tr>
<td>A — Serum calcium concentration<br />
A — 血清钙浓度</td>
<td>Serum Ca is LOW — patient has ongoing hypocalcemic symptoms and Chvostek sign at this visit<br />
血清钙偏低——患者此次就诊时仍有低钙血症症状和Chvostek征</td>

<tr>

<tr>
<td>C — Serum parathyroid hormone concentration<br />
C — 血清甲状旁腺激素浓度</td>
<td>PTH is DECREASED — parathyroid glands were removed or devascularized during thyroidectomy; this is the root cause<br />
PTH降低——甲状旁腺在甲状腺切除术中被切除或去血管化；这是根本原因</td>
<td>Low PTH is the primary abnormality; the question asks what is INCREASED<br />
PTH降低是原发性异常；题目询问哪项"升高"</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>D — Serum parathyroid hormone-related protein concentration<br />
D — 血清甲状旁腺激素相关蛋白浓度</td>
<td>PTHrP is associated with hypercalcemia of malignancy — this patient has hypocalcemia, not hypercalcemia<br />
PTHrP与恶性肿瘤相关性高钙血症有关——此患者为低钙血症，非高钙血症</td>
<td>PTHrP elevation = elevated serum Ca + suppressed PTH in cancer workup<br />
PTHrP升高 = 癌症排查中血钙升高 + PTH受抑</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>E — Urinary 24-hour calcium excretion ✓<br />
E — 24小时尿钙排泄 ✓</td>
<td>CORRECT — absent PTH removes DCT calcium reabsorption → hypercalciuria despite low serum calcium<br />
正确——PTH缺失导致远曲小管钙重吸收消失 → 尽管血钙低仍出现高钙尿症</td>
<td>Paradoxical hypercalciuria in hypoparathyroidism is a classic exam pearl<br />
甲状旁腺功能减退时的矛盾性高钙尿症是经典考点</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>F — Urine potassium excretion<br />
F — 尿钾排泄</td>
<td>Increased urinary K is caused by diuretics, mineralocorticoid excess, or gastric fluid losses — none apply here<br />
尿钾增多由利尿剂、盐皮质激素过多或胃液丢失引起——此处均不适用</td>
<td>No history of diuretic use, hypertension, or vomiting to suggest renal K wasting<br />
无利尿剂使用、高血压或呕吐史提示肾性钾丢失</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

*The most tempting distractor is Choice C — many students confuse "what is the primary abnormality" with "what is increased." PTH is decreased in hypoparathyroidism; only urinary calcium rises paradoxically.*

最容易选错的干扰项是C选项——很多学生将"原发性异常"与"升高的指标"混淆。甲状旁腺功能减退时PTH是降低的；只有尿钙出现矛盾性升高。

饮食缺乏、吸收不良、慢性肾衰竭</td>
</tr>

## 6. One-Sentence Summary & Memory Hook / 一句话总结 & 记忆钩

**In post-thyroidectomy hypoparathyroidism, absent PTH eliminates renal calcium reabsorption in the DCT, causing paradoxically elevated urinary calcium excretion despite persistent hypocalcemia.**

**甲状腺切除术后甲状旁腺功能减退中，PTH缺失消除了远曲小管的肾脏钙重吸收，导致尽管持续低钙血症，尿钙排泄仍矛盾性升高。**

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 100%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><p><strong>Memory Hook — PTH's "BKG" Triple Rule / 记忆钩 — PTH的"BKG"三靶规则:</strong></p>
<p>• <strong>B</strong>one — PTH activates osteoclasts → releases calcium from bone / PTH激活破骨细胞 → 从骨骼释放钙<br />
• <strong>K</strong>idney (DCT) — PTH reabsorbs calcium, excretes phosphate / PTH重吸收钙、排泄磷酸盐<br />
• <strong>G</strong>ut — PTH triggers calcitriol → intestinal calcium absorption / PTH触发骨化三醇产生 → 肠道吸收钙<br />
• <strong>No PTH = No K</strong>idney reabsorption → urine Ca goes UP even as serum Ca goes DOWN / <strong>无PTH = 无肾脏</strong>重吸收 → 尿钙升高，血钙下降</p></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
</tbody>
</table>

## 7. High-Yield Topic Knowledge — Post-thyroidectomy Complications & Calcium Homeostasis / 高频知识表 — 甲状腺切除术后并发症与钙稳态

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 50%" />
<col style="width: 50%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Topic</strong><br />
<strong>考点</strong></th>
<th><strong>Key Points</strong><br />
<strong>要点</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>Chvostek sign<br />
Chvostek征</td>
<td>Tapping 2 cm anterior to ear over CN VII (zygomatic arch) → ipsilateral facial muscle spasm; indicates hypocalcemia; specificity ~90%, sensitivity ~25%<br />
在耳前2cm处叩击面神经（颧弓）→ 同侧面肌痉挛；提示低钙血症；特异性约90%，敏感性约25%</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Trousseau sign<br />
Trousseau征</td>
<td>BP cuff inflated above systolic for 3 minutes → carpal spasm (wrist flexion + MCP extension + finger adduction); more sensitive than Chvostek for hypocalcemia<br />
血压袖带充气高于收缩压3分钟 → 腕痉挛（腕屈曲 + 掌指关节伸展 + 手指内收）；对低钙血症的敏感性高于Chvostek征</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>PTH's 3 target actions<br />
PTH的3个靶器官作用</td>
<td>Bone: osteoclast activation → Ca release; Kidney DCT: Ca reabsorption + PO4 excretion; Kidney PCT: 1α-hydroxylase activation → calcitriol → gut Ca absorption<br />
骨骼：破骨细胞激活 → 钙释放；肾脏远曲小管：钙重吸收 + 磷酸盐排泄；肾脏近曲小管：1α-羟化酶激活 → 骨化三醇 → 肠道钙吸收</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Hypoparathyroidism lab pattern<br />
甲状旁腺功能减退实验室特征</td>
<td>Low PTH, Low Ca, High PO4, High urinary Ca, Low calcitriol — the combination distinguishes it from VitD deficiency<br />
PTH低、钙低、磷酸盐高、尿钙高、骨化三醇低——此组合将其与维生素D缺乏区分开来</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Why calcitriol (not cholecalciferol) in hypoparathyroidism<br />
为什么甲状旁腺功能减退用骨化三醇而非普通维生素D</td>
<td>PTH is required to activate 25-OH VitD via renal 1α-hydroxylase; without PTH, plain vitamin D cannot be converted to active calcitriol → must supplement calcitriol directly<br />
PTH是经肾脏1α-羟化酶将25-羟维生素D活化为骨化三醇所必需的；无PTH则普通维生素D无法转化 → 必须直接补充骨化三醇</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Nephrocalcinosis risk in treated hypoparathyroidism<br />
治疗中的甲状旁腺功能减退的肾钙质沉着风险</td>
<td>Hypercalciuria persists despite hypocalcemia → calcium deposits in renal tubules → nephrolithiasis and progressive CKD; monitor 24-hr urine Ca regularly<br />
高钙尿症在低钙血症时持续存在 → 钙在肾小管沉积 → 肾结石和进展性CKD；定期监测24小时尿钙</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Thiazide diuretics in hypoparathyroidism<br />
噻嗪类利尿剂在甲状旁腺功能减退中的应用</td>
<td>Thiazides increase DCT calcium reabsorption independent of PTH (by reducing intracellular Na → activating Na/Ca exchanger) → useful to reduce hypercalciuria and nephrolithiasis risk<br />
噻嗪类通过降低细胞内Na（激活Na/Ca交换体）增加远曲小管钙重吸收，不依赖PTH → 有助于降低高钙尿症和肾结石风险</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

## 8. Extensions / 延伸扩展

- **Differential of hypocalcemia:** Hypoparathyroidism (post-surgical, autoimmune, DiGeorge), pseudohypoparathyroidism (PTH resistance), vitamin D deficiency, hypomagnesemia, pancreatitis, hungry bone syndrome after parathyroidectomy\
  **低钙血症鉴别:** 甲状旁腺功能减退（术后、自身免疫、DiGeorge综合征）、假性甲状旁腺功能减退（PTH抵抗）、维生素D缺乏、低镁血症、胰腺炎、甲状旁腺切除术后"骨饥渴综合征"

- **Variant — Pseudohypoparathyroidism:** PTH is HIGH (end-organ resistance), serum Ca is LOW, serum PO4 is HIGH — same labs as hypoparathyroidism except PTH is elevated; features of Albright hereditary osteodystrophy (short 4th metacarpal, short stature, intellectual disability)\
  **题目变式——假性甲状旁腺功能减退:** PTH高（末端器官抵抗），血钙低，血磷高——实验室结果与甲状旁腺功能减退相同，但PTH升高；伴Albright遗传性骨营养不良特征（第四掌骨短、矮身材、智力残疾）

- **Key complication — nephrocalcinosis and nephrolithiasis:** Chronic hypercalciuria in treated hypoparathyroidism leads to calcium oxalate/phosphate stones; target 24-hr urine Ca \<300 mg/day; thiazide diuretics and adequate hydration are the main interventions\
  **关键并发症——肾钙质沉着和肾结石:** 治疗中甲状旁腺功能减退的慢性高钙尿症导致草酸钙/磷酸钙结石；目标24小时尿钙\<300 mg/天；噻嗪类利尿剂和充分补水是主要干预措施

- **Hypomagnesemia as functional hypoparathyroidism:** Severe hypomagnesemia impairs PTH secretion AND PTH end-organ response → refractory hypocalcemia that does not improve with calcium/calcitriol alone; must correct Mg first\
  **低镁血症作为功能性甲状旁腺功能减退:** 严重低镁血症既损害PTH分泌又损害PTH末端器官反应 → 顽固性低钙血症，单独补钙/骨化三醇无效；必须先纠正镁

# Question 189 — Drug-Induced Neutropenia (TMP-SMX) / 药物性粒细胞减少症（复方磺胺甲噁唑）

## Question Stem / 题干

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 100%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><p>A <strong>previously healthy 27-year-old woman</strong> comes to the physician because of a <strong>rash over her chest and back</strong> for 5 days. She has a 10-day history of <strong>pain with urination, urinary frequency, and nocturia</strong> two to three times nightly. She took <strong>her father's trimethoprim-sulfamethoxazole for 7 days</strong>, and her urinary symptoms improved. She currently takes no medications. She does not smoke cigarettes. Her temperature is 37.5°C (99.5°F), <strong>pulse is 110/min</strong>, respirations are 16/min, and blood pressure is 110/70 mm Hg. Examination of the skin shows an <strong>erythematous, maculopapular rash</strong> over the trunk. There are no oral lesions. There is no splenomegaly. Laboratory studies show: Hemoglobin 12.8 g/dL, <strong>Leukocyte count 3000/mm³</strong>, <strong>Segmented neutrophils 15%</strong>, <strong>Eosinophils 5%</strong>, Basophils 1%, Lymphocytes 54%, Monocytes 25%, Platelet count 200,000/mm³. Which of the following is the most appropriate next step in management?</p>
<p><strong>Q: Most appropriate next step in management?</strong></p>
<p>A) Repeat examination in 1 week<br />
B) Granulocyte colony-stimulating factor therapy<br />
C) Prednisone therapy<br />
D) Vitamin B12 (cyanocobalamin) supplementation<br />
E) Skin biopsy</p>
<p><strong>Correct Answer: A</strong></p></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
</tbody>
</table>

## 1. Key Stem Clues / 题干关键词抓考点

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 50%" />
<col style="width: 50%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Key Stem Clue</strong><br />
<strong>关键词</strong></th>
<th><strong>Why It Matters</strong><br />
<strong>为什么重要</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>Trimethoprim-sulfamethoxazole for 7 days<br />
服用复方磺胺甲噁唑 7 天</td>
<td>TMP-SMX is a classic cause of idiosyncratic drug-induced neutropenia<br />
TMP-SMX 是药物性粒细胞减少症的经典致病药物</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Leukocyte count 3000/mm³ with segmented neutrophils 15%<br />
白细胞计数 3000/mm³，分叶核粒细胞 15%</td>
<td>ANC = 3000 × 0.15 = 450/mm³ — severe neutropenia (ANC &lt;500); high infection risk<br />
绝对中性粒细胞计数（ANC）= 450/mm³，属于重度粒细胞减少，感染风险高</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Eosinophils 5%<br />
嗜酸性粒细胞 5%</td>
<td>Relative eosinophilia suggests drug hypersensitivity reaction<br />
相对性嗜酸性粒细胞增多提示药物超敏反应</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Erythematous maculopapular rash over trunk<br />
躯干红斑丘疹性皮疹</td>
<td>Classic cutaneous manifestation of drug hypersensitivity; TMP-SMX rash is well-recognized<br />
TMP-SMX 超敏反应的经典皮肤表现</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Currently takes no medications (drug already stopped)<br />
目前未服用任何药物（致病药物已停用）</td>
<td>Offending agent already discontinued — expectant management is appropriate<br />
致病药物已停用，期待治疗（观察等待）是合理选择</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>No oral lesions, no splenomegaly<br />
无口腔溃疡，无脾大</td>
<td>Rules out Stevens-Johnson syndrome and Felty's syndrome as alternative diagnoses<br />
排除 Stevens-Johnson 综合征及 Felty 综合征作为替代诊断</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Previously healthy, no personal or family hematologic history<br />
既往健康，无血液病个人/家族史</td>
<td>Supports acquired drug reaction over congenital or chronic bone marrow disorder<br />
支持后天性药物反应，而非先天性或慢性骨髓疾病</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

## 2. Mechanism / 机制理解

**Drug-induced neutropenia** occurs via two major mechanisms: **immune-mediated destruction** (hapten or drug-antibody complex targeting neutrophil surface antigens) or **direct myelosuppression** of granulocyte precursors. **TMP-SMX** inhibits **dihydrofolate reductase**, impairing folate metabolism and **DNA synthesis** in rapidly dividing cells including granulocyte precursors:

**药物性粒细胞减少症**通过两种主要机制发生：**免疫介导的破坏**（半抗原或药物-抗体复合物靶向中性粒细胞表面抗原）或对粒细胞前体的**直接骨髓抑制**。**TMP-SMX** 抑制**二氢叶酸还原酶**，损害包括粒细胞前体在内的快速分裂细胞的叶酸代谢及 **DNA 合成**：

- TMP-SMX blocks folate pathway → impaired granulocyte production (direct myelosuppression mechanism)\
  TMP-SMX 阻断叶酸代谢通路 → 粒细胞生成障碍（直接骨髓抑制机制）

- Idiosyncratic immune reaction: drug-antibody complexes bind neutrophil surface → complement-mediated or phagocytic destruction\
  特异质免疫反应：药物-抗体复合物结合中性粒细胞表面 → 补体介导或吞噬性破坏

- ANC \<1500/mm³ = neutropenia; ANC \<500/mm³ = severe neutropenia (life-threatening infection risk)\
  ANC \<1500/mm³ = 粒细胞减少；ANC \<500/mm³ = 重度粒细胞减少（危及生命的感染风险）

- After drug discontinuation, neutrophil recovery typically occurs within days to weeks\
  停药后，中性粒细胞通常在数天至数周内恢复正常

**Anatomic rule of thumb:** Mature neutrophils circulate for only 6–10 hours; once the bone marrow recovers after toxin removal, new cells appear rapidly in the peripheral blood.

**解剖小窍门:** 成熟中性粒细胞在血液中仅循环 6–10 小时；一旦骨髓在去除毒性因素后恢复，新生细胞会迅速出现在外周血中。

## 3. Correct Answer (A) — Watchful Waiting with Repeat CBC / 正确答案 (A) — 期待观察 + 复查血常规

**Repeat examination in 1 week** is the most appropriate next step because the offending drug (TMP-SMX) has already been discontinued, and drug-induced neutropenia is expected to resolve spontaneously without further intervention in a hemodynamically stable, afebrile patient:

**一周后复诊** 是最合适的下一步，因为致病药物（TMP-SMX）已停用，且在血流动力学稳定、无发热的患者中，药物性粒细胞减少症预期无需进一步干预即可自行缓解：

- Patient is stable with no fever \>38.3°C and no evidence of active infection or sepsis\
  患者病情稳定，无 \>38.3°C 发热，无活动性感染或脓毒症证据

- Drug already discontinued → removal of the offending agent is the definitive treatment step\
  药物已停用 → 去除致病因素即为关键治疗步骤

- Follow-up CBC in 1 week confirms neutrophil recovery and rules out persistent or worsening cytopenias\
  1 周后复查血常规，确认中性粒细胞恢复，排除持续或进展性血细胞减少

**Diagnosis:** Drug-induced neutropenia from TMP-SMX; ANC ≈ 450/mm³ (severe), but patient is clinically stable with no active infection

**诊断:** TMP-SMX 所致药物性粒细胞减少症；ANC ≈ 450/mm³（重度），但患者临床稳定，无活动性感染

**Treatment:** Discontinue offending drug (already done); watchful waiting with repeat CBC; topical corticosteroids or antihistamines for symptomatic rash relief only

**治疗:** 停用致病药物（已完成）；期待观察并复查血常规；仅在皮疹症状明显时局部使用皮质类固醇或抗组胺药

## 4. Options Elimination / 错误选项排除逻辑

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 33%" />
<col style="width: 33%" />
<col style="width: 33%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Option</strong><br />
<strong>选项</strong></th>
<th><strong>Why Wrong</strong><br />
<strong>为什么错</strong></th>
<th><strong>Key Discriminator</strong><br />
<strong>鉴别要点</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>A — Repeat examination in 1 week ✓<br />
A — 一周后复诊 ✓</td>
<td>CORRECT — Drug stopped; stable outpatient needs follow-up CBC to confirm neutrophil recovery<br />
正确——药物已停，病情稳定的门诊患者需复查血常规确认粒细胞恢复</td>
<td>Drug-induced neutropenia resolves after drug discontinuation; expectant management appropriate in stable patients<br />
药物性粒细胞减少症停药后可自行缓解；病情稳定患者适合期待治疗</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>B — Granulocyte colony-stimulating factor therapy<br />
B — 粒细胞集落刺激因子治疗</td>
<td>G-CSF is reserved for unstable or hospitalized patients with active infection, not stable outpatients whose drug has been stopped<br />
G-CSF 适用于不稳定/住院且有活动性感染的患者，不适用于已停药的稳定门诊患者</td>
<td>Patient is hemodynamically stable with no fever; drug already stopped; G-CSF provides no benefit here and is not cost-effective<br />
患者血流动力学稳定，无发热；药物已停；此时使用 G-CSF 无益且不符合成本效益</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>C — Prednisone therapy<br />
C — 泼尼松治疗</td>
<td>Systemic corticosteroids are not the primary treatment for drug-induced neutropenia; drug withdrawal is definitive<br />
全身皮质类固醇不是药物性粒细胞减少症的主要治疗；停药才是根本</td>
<td>Topical steroids or antihistamines can treat rash symptomatically; systemic prednisone not indicated for stable drug-induced neutropenia<br />
局部类固醇或抗组胺药可对症处理皮疹；稳定的药物性粒细胞减少症不需全身使用泼尼松</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>D — Vitamin B12 (cyanocobalamin) supplementation<br />
D — 维生素 B12 补充</td>
<td>B12 deficiency causes megaloblastic anemia ± neuropathy, NOT a maculopapular rash or isolated neutropenia following antibiotic use<br />
B12 缺乏导致巨幼细胞性贫血 ± 神经系统症状，而非服用抗生素后出现的斑丘疹或孤立性粒细胞减少</td>
<td>B12 deficiency hallmarks: macrocytic anemia, hypersegmented neutrophils, glossitis — none present here; rash pattern is inconsistent<br />
B12 缺乏标志：大细胞性贫血、中性粒细胞过度分叶、舌炎——本例均无；皮疹表现也不符合</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>E — Skin biopsy<br />
E — 皮肤活检</td>
<td>Mildly invasive procedure reserved for unexplained persistent symptoms; here the temporal relationship of TMP-SMX → rash + neutropenia is clinically clear<br />
轻度侵入性操作，用于原因不明的持续症状；本例 TMP-SMX → 皮疹 + 粒细胞减少的时间关系临床上已明确</td>
<td>When drug exposure clearly precedes and explains both the rash and CBC changes, observation is preferred over biopsy in a stable patient<br />
当药物暴露明确早于并可解释皮疹及血常规改变时，稳定患者应首选观察而非活检</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

*The most tempting distractor is (B) G-CSF — students may equate severe neutropenia (ANC \<500) with an automatic indication for G-CSF, but in drug-induced cases where the drug is already stopped and the patient is stable, G-CSF is not indicated; reserve it for febrile neutropenia, active infection, or failure to recover.*

最容易误选的干扰项是（B）G-CSF——学生可能将重度粒细胞减少（ANC \<500）与 G-CSF 的绝对使用指征混淆，但在药物已停用且患者病情稳定的药物性病例中，G-CSF 并无指征；应将其保留用于粒细胞减少性发热、活动性感染或停药后恢复失败的情况。

## 5. High-Yield Summary Table — Drug-Induced Neutropenia vs Aplastic Anemia vs Vitamin B12 Deficiency / 药物性粒细胞减少症 vs 再生障碍性贫血 vs 维生素 B12 缺乏症

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 25%" />
<col style="width: 25%" />
<col style="width: 25%" />
<col style="width: 25%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Feature</strong><br />
<strong>特征</strong></th>
<th><strong>Drug-Induced Neutropenia</strong><br />
<strong>药物性粒细胞减少症</strong></th>
<th><strong>Aplastic Anemia</strong><br />
<strong>再生障碍性贫血</strong></th>
<th><strong>Vitamin B12 Deficiency</strong><br />
<strong>维生素 B12 缺乏症</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>CBC pattern<br />
血常规模式</td>
<td>Isolated neutropenia (↓WBC, normal Hgb and Plt)<br />
孤立性粒细胞减少（↓WBC，Hgb 及血小板正常）</td>
<td>Pancytopenia (↓WBC, ↓Hgb, ↓Plt)<br />
全血细胞减少（↓WBC、↓Hgb、↓Plt）</td>
<td>Macrocytic anemia ± leukopenia; hypersegmented neutrophils<br />
大细胞性贫血 ± 白细胞减少；中性粒细胞过度分叶</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Common causes<br />
常见病因</td>
<td>TMP-SMX, β-lactams, clozapine, antithyroid drugs (PTU/carbimazole)<br />
TMP-SMX、β-内酰胺类、氯氮平、抗甲状腺药（PTU/卡比马唑）</td>
<td>Idiosyncratic reaction (chloramphenicol, benzene), autoimmune T-cell destruction<br />
特异质反应（氯霉素、苯）、自身免疫性 T 细胞破坏</td>
<td>Pernicious anemia (anti-IF Ab), dietary deficiency, metformin, nitrous oxide<br />
恶性贫emia（抗内因子抗体）、饮食缺乏、二甲双胍、笑气</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Bone marrow findings<br />
骨髓表现</td>
<td>Myeloid hypoplasia (granulocyte precursors ↓) or normal<br />
髓系增生低下（粒细胞前体↓）或正常</td>
<td>Hypocellular marrow with fat replacement (all lineages ↓)<br />
骨髓增生低下伴脂肪替代（所有系别均↓）</td>
<td>Hypercellular marrow; megaloblastic changes in all lineages<br />
骨髓增生活跃；所有系别均有巨幼样改变</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Skin / mucosal clues<br />
皮肤/黏膜线索</td>
<td>Drug rash (maculopapular), eosinophilia<br />
药物性皮疹（斑丘疹）、嗜酸性粒细胞增多</td>
<td>Petechiae, purpura, easy bruising (thrombocytopenia)<br />
瘀点、紫癜、易出血（血小板减少）</td>
<td>Glossitis, angular cheilitis, no rash<br />
舌炎、口角炎，无皮疹</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Neurologic involvement<br />
神经系统受累</td>
<td>None<br />
无</td>
<td>None (unless CNS bleeding from thrombocytopenia)<br />
无（除非血小板减少导致颅内出血）</td>
<td>Subacute combined degeneration: posterior + lateral columns (B12 only, not folate)<br />
亚急性联合变性：后索 + 侧索（仅 B12，叶酸缺乏不引起）</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Treatment and prognosis<br />
治疗与预后</td>
<td>Stop drug → recovery in days to weeks; G-CSF if febrile/unstable<br />
停药 → 数天至数周恢复；发热/不稳定时用 G-CSF</td>
<td>Hematopoietic stem cell transplant (young) or ATG + cyclosporine (older)<br />
造血干细胞移植（年轻患者）或 ATG + 环孢素（年长患者）</td>
<td>IM B12 (pernicious anemia) or oral supplementation (dietary); hematologic recovery faster than neurologic<br />
肌注 B12（恶性贫血）或口服补充（饮食缺乏）；血液学恢复快于神经功能</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

## 6. One-Sentence Summary & Memory Hook / 一句话总结 & 记忆钩

**In a stable patient with TMP-SMX-induced neutropenia who has already stopped the drug, the correct next step is watchful waiting with repeat CBC in 1 week — not G-CSF, systemic steroids, or biopsy.**

**对于已停用 TMP-SMX、病情稳定的药物性粒细胞减少症患者，正确的下一步是期待观察 + 1 周后复查血常规，而非 G-CSF、全身皮质类固醇或皮肤活检。**

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 100%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><p><strong>Memory Hook — WAIT: Managing Drug-Induced Neutropenia / 记忆钩 — "WAIT"口诀：药物性粒细胞减少症的处理:</strong></p>
<p>• <strong>W</strong>atch and wait (stable outpatient → observe, not act) / <strong>等</strong>待观察（病情稳定的门诊患者 → 观察而非立即干预）<br />
• <strong>A</strong>gent (drug) already stopped → recovery expected / <strong>药</strong>物已停用 → 预期自行恢复<br />
• <strong>I</strong>nfection absent → G-CSF NOT needed / <strong>感</strong>染不存在 → 无需 G-CSF<br />
• <strong>T</strong>imer: repeat CBC in 1 week to confirm recovery / <strong>时</strong>间节点：1 周后复查血常规确认恢复</p></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
</tbody>
</table>

## 7. High-Yield Topic Knowledge — Drug-Induced Neutropenia / 高频知识表 — 药物性粒细胞减少症

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 50%" />
<col style="width: 50%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Topic</strong><br />
<strong>考点</strong></th>
<th><strong>Key Points</strong><br />
<strong>要点</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>ANC thresholds<br />
ANC 分级阈值</td>
<td>Mild: ANC 1000–1500/mm³; Moderate: 500–1000/mm³; Severe: &lt;500/mm³; Agranulocytosis: &lt;100/mm³<br />
轻度：1000–1500/mm³；中度：500–1000/mm³；重度：&lt;500/mm³；粒细胞缺乏：&lt;100/mm³</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Classic neutropenia-causing drugs<br />
经典致粒细胞减少药物</td>
<td>TMP-SMX, β-lactam antibiotics, clozapine (antipsychotic), propylthiouracil / carbimazole (antithyroid), cytotoxic chemotherapy<br />
TMP-SMX、β-内酰胺类抗生素、氯氮平（抗精神病药）、丙硫氧嘧啶/卡比马唑（抗甲状腺药）、细胞毒性化疗药</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>TMP-SMX mechanism of myelosuppression<br />
TMP-SMX 骨髓抑制机制</td>
<td>Inhibits dihydrofolate reductase → impaired folate synthesis → reduced DNA synthesis in myeloid precursors<br />
抑制二氢叶酸还原酶 → 叶酸合成受损 → 髓系前体细胞 DNA 合成减少</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Indications for G-CSF in neutropenia<br />
粒细胞减少症使用 G-CSF 的指征</td>
<td>Febrile neutropenia (ANC &lt;500 + fever &gt;38.3°C), hemodynamically unstable, hospitalized, or failure to recover after drug cessation<br />
粒细胞减少性发热（ANC &lt;500 + 发热 &gt;38.3°C）、血流动力学不稳定、住院患者，或停药后恢复失败</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Expected recovery after drug withdrawal<br />
停药后预期恢复时间</td>
<td>Most drug-induced cases resolve within 1–3 weeks of discontinuing the offending agent<br />
大多数药物性粒细胞减少症在停用致病药物后 1–3 周内恢复</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Eosinophilia as a drug-reaction marker<br />
嗜酸性粒细胞增多作为药物反应标志</td>
<td>Relative eosinophilia (&gt;5% or absolute &gt;500/mm³) in the setting of drug exposure suggests immune-mediated hypersensitivity<br />
药物暴露背景下相对性嗜酸性粒细胞增多（&gt;5% 或绝对值 &gt;500/mm³）提示免疫介导的超敏反应</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>When to hospitalize for neutropenia<br />
粒细胞减少何时需住院</td>
<td>Fever &gt;38.3°C, signs of sepsis, mucositis, ANC &lt;100/mm³ with any infection symptom — these require IV antibiotics and inpatient monitoring<br />
发热 &gt;38.3°C、脓毒症征象、黏膜炎、伴任何感染症状的 ANC &lt;100/mm³——需静脉抗生素及住院监测</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

## 8. Extensions / 延伸扩展

- **Clozapine monitoring requirement:** Clozapine (atypical antipsychotic) requires mandatory CBC weekly for 6 months, then biweekly due to high agranulocytosis risk (ANC \<100); drug must be permanently discontinued if agranulocytosis develops\
  **氯氮平强制监测要求:** 氯氮平（非典型抗精神病药）因粒细胞缺乏风险高，前 6 个月须每周强制查血常规，之后每两周一次；一旦发生粒细胞缺乏必须永久停药

- **Febrile neutropenia is a medical emergency:** ANC \<500/mm³ + fever \>38.3°C → empiric broad-spectrum IV antibiotics (e.g., piperacillin-tazobactam or cefepime) must be started within 1 hour regardless of clinical stability\
  **粒细胞减少性发热是内科急症:** ANC \<500/mm³ + 发热 \>38.3°C → 无论临床是否稳定，均须在 1 小时内启动经验性广谱静脉抗生素（如哌拉西林-他唑巴坦或头孢吡肟）

- **TMP-SMX other adverse effects:** Hyperkalemia (blocks Na⁺/K⁺ transporters in collecting duct), false elevation of serum creatinine (competes with tubular creatinine secretion), Stevens-Johnson syndrome (distinguished by mucosal involvement — absent here)\
  **TMP-SMX 其他不良反应:** 高钾血症（阻断集合管 Na⁺/K⁺ 转运体）、血清肌酐假性升高（竞争肾小管肌酐分泌）、Stevens-Johnson 综合征（以黏膜受累为区别特征——本例无此表现）

- **DRESS syndrome differential:** Drug Reaction with Eosinophilia and Systemic Symptoms — also presents with eosinophilia and rash but additionally features fever \>38.5°C, lymphadenopathy, and visceral organ involvement (hepatitis, nephritis); this case lacks those features\
  **DRESS 综合征鉴别:** 药物反应伴嗜酸性粒细胞增多和全身症状——同样表现为嗜酸性粒细胞增多和皮疹，但另有 \>38.5°C 高热、淋巴结肿大及内脏器官受累（肝炎、肾炎）；本例不具备这些特征

# Question 190 — Drug-Induced Acute Interstitial Nephritis / 药物性急性间质性肾炎

## Question Stem / 题干

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 100%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><p>A <strong>57-year-old woman</strong> who was admitted to the hospital because of pneumonia has had an <strong>increase in her serum creatinine concentration from 1 mg/dL to 2.4 mg/dL during the past 3 days</strong>. On admission 7 days ago, she had severe shortness of breath and hypotension; she was intubated and mechanically ventilated for 2 days. Six days ago, a CT scan of the chest with <strong>contrast</strong> showed pneumonia at both lung bases. She also has <strong>type 2 diabetes mellitus</strong>. Current medications are <strong>ceftriaxone</strong>, azithromycin, albuterol, insulin, and lisinopril. She is now breathing 3 L/min of oxygen via nasal cannula and has mild shortness of breath. Her blood pressure has been stable for 6 days. Her urine output has been <strong>1 L/24 h during the past 2 days</strong>. Her pulse is 70/min, and blood pressure is 150/90 mm Hg. Pulse oximetry on 3 L/min of oxygen via nasal cannula shows an oxygen saturation of 94%. Crackles are heard at both lung bases. Urinalysis shows: Protein 1+, <strong>RBC 10/hpf, WBC 9/hpf</strong>, Casts none. A <strong>Wright stain of urine shows eosinophils</strong>. Which of the following is the most appropriate next step in management?</p>
<p><strong>Q: Which of the following is the most appropriate next step in management?</strong></p>
<p>A) Add acetylcysteine to the regimen<br />
B) Add nifedipine to the regimen<br />
C) Add prednisone to the regimen<br />
D) Administer a 1-L bolus of 0.9% saline<br />
E) Discontinue ceftriaxone<br />
F) No intervention is indicated</p>
<p><strong>Correct Answer: E</strong></p></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
</tbody>
</table>

## 1. Key Stem Clues / 题干关键词抓考点

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 50%" />
<col style="width: 50%" />

<tr>
<th><strong>Key Stem Clue</strong><br />
<strong>关键词</strong></th>
<th><strong>Why It Matters</strong><br />
<strong>为什么重要</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>Creatinine 1→2.4 mg/dL in 3 days<br />
肌酐 3 天内从 1 升至 2.4 mg/dL</td>
<td>Defines AKI — triggers the need to identify the etiology<br />
确认急性肾损伤——需鉴别病因</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Ceftriaxone in current medications<br />
当前用药中含头孢曲松</td>
<td>Beta-lactam antibiotics are a classic cause of drug-induced AIN<br />
β-内酰胺类是药物性 AIN 的经典病因</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>CT with contrast 6 days ago<br />
6 天前使用造影剂 CT</td>
<td>Potential distractor for contrast nephropathy; timing &gt;48h makes CIN unlikely<br />
造影剂肾病干扰项；超过 48 小时发病可能性低</td>
</tr>
<tr>

AIN 特征性表现——反映 IV 型超敏反应间质浸润</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>WBC 9/hpf, no infection worsening<br />
WBC 9/hpf，无感染加重迹象</td>
<td>Sterile pyuria in the context of AKI strongly supports AIN<br />
急性肾损伤背景下的无菌性脓尿强烈支持 AIN</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>RBC 10/hpf, casts none<br />
RBC 10/hpf，无管型</td>
<td>Absence of RBC casts rules out glomerulonephritis; intrinsic tubulo-interstitial disease<br />
无红细胞管型排除肾小球肾炎；符合肾小管间质疾病</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>BP stable for 6 days, UO 1 L/day<br />
血压稳定 6 天，尿量 1 L/天</td>
<td>Hemodynamically stable excludes prerenal AKI as primary cause<br />
血流动力学稳定排除肾前性 AKI 为主要病因</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

## 2. Mechanism / 机制理解

**Acute interstitial nephritis (AIN)** is an immune-mediated **type IV hypersensitivity reaction** in which the **renal interstitium** becomes infiltrated with T-lymphocytes and eosinophils, impairing tubular function:

**急性间质性肾炎（AIN）**是一种免疫介导的**IV 型超敏反应**，**肾间质**被 T 淋巴细胞和嗜酸性粒细胞浸润，导致肾小管功能受损：

- Drug (ceftriaxone) acts as a hapten → binds tubular antigens → activates CD4+ T cells → interstitial inflammatory cascade\
  药物（头孢曲松）作为半抗原→与肾小管抗原结合→激活 CD4+ T 细胞→间质炎症级联反应

- Tubular dysfunction → impaired reabsorption → sterile pyuria, hematuria, low-grade proteinuria\
  肾小管功能障碍→重吸收受损→无菌性脓尿、血尿、轻度蛋白尿

- Eosinophil infiltration is the histologic hallmark → shed into urine → detectable by Wright stain\
  嗜酸性粒细胞浸润是组织学标志→脱落入尿液→可通过 Wright 染色检出

**Anatomic rule of thumb:** AIN targets the interstitium and tubules — NOT the glomerulus. This explains the absence of RBC casts and the sub-nephrotic proteinuria.

**解剖小窍门:** AIN 累及间质和肾小管，而非肾小球。这解释了为何无红细胞管型，蛋白尿也不达肾病综合征范围。

## 3. Correct Answer (E) — Discontinue Ceftriaxone / 正确答案 (E) — 停用头孢曲松

**Discontinuing the offending drug** is the cornerstone of drug-induced AIN management — removing the antigenic stimulus halts the hypersensitivity cascade and allows renal recovery:

**停用致病药物**是药物性 AIN 治疗的基石——去除抗原刺激可终止超敏反应级联，使肾功能得以恢复：

- Ceftriaxone is a 3rd-generation cephalosporin; all beta-lactams carry the risk of AIN\
  头孢曲松是第三代头孢菌素；所有 β-内酰胺类均有引起 AIN 的风险

- Drug discontinuation alone leads to renal recovery in the majority of cases\
  单独停药即可使大多数患者肾功能恢复

- Corticosteroids are reserved as a second step if creatinine does not improve within 3–5 days after stopping the drug\
  类固醇作为第二步，仅在停药后 3-5 天肌酐仍无改善时才考虑使用

**Diagnosis:** Rising creatinine + beta-lactam use + sterile pyuria + urine eosinophils = drug-induced AIN. Contrast nephropathy excluded because CIN peaks at 24–48h and the CT was 6 days ago.

**诊断:** 肌酐升高 + β-内酰胺类用药史 + 无菌性脓尿 + 尿液嗜酸性粒细胞 = 药物性 AIN。造影剂肾病已排除，因 CIN 在 24-48 小时达峰，而本患者造影已过 6 天。

**Treatment:** Discontinue ceftriaxone → substitute a non-beta-lactam antibiotic for continued pneumonia coverage → monitor creatinine daily → add prednisone if no improvement in 3–5 days.

**治疗:** 停用头孢曲松→改用非 β-内酰胺类抗生素继续覆盖肺炎→每日监测肌酐→若 3-5 天无改善则加用泼尼松。

## 4. Options Elimination / 错误选项排除逻辑

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 33%" />
<col style="width: 33%" />
<col style="width: 33%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Option</strong><br />
<strong>选项</strong></th>
<th><strong>Why Wrong</strong><br />
<strong>为什么错</strong></th>
<th><strong>Key Discriminator</strong><br />
<strong>鉴别要点</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>A — Add acetylcysteine to the regimen<br />
A — 加用乙酰半胱氨酸</td>
<td>No role in AIN — used for acetaminophen overdose or pre-procedure contrast prophylaxis, not post-exposure treatment<br />
对 AIN 无效——用于对乙酰氨基酚过量或造影前预防，不用于造影后处理</td>
<td>Acetylcysteine prevents oxidative injury, not immune-mediated interstitial inflammation<br />
乙酰半胱氨酸预防氧化损伤，对免疫介导的间质炎症无效</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>B — Add nifedipine to the regimen<br />
B — 加用硝苯地平</td>
<td>No role in AIN — nifedipine is a dihydropyridine CCB for hypertension; BP is not the primary management target here<br />
对 AIN 无效——硝苯地平是二氢吡啶类 CCB 用于降压；血压并非此处首要处理目标</td>
<td>BP 150/90 is elevated but is not causing the AKI; treating AIN removes the root cause<br />
血压 150/90 偏高但并非 AKI 病因；治疗 AIN 才是解决根本</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>C — Add prednisone to the regimen<br />
C — 加用泼尼松</td>
<td>Premature — steroids have a role in AIN but ONLY after the offending drug is stopped first<br />
操之过急——类固醇在 AIN 中有作用，但必须先停用致病药物</td>
<td>Adding steroids while ceftriaxone continues perpetuates antigen exposure and undermines treatment<br />
在继续使用头孢曲松时加用类固醇，抗原暴露持续，治疗适得其反</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>D — Administer a 1-L bolus of 0.9% saline<br />
D — 给予 1 升生理盐水推注</td>
<td>Prerenal AKI excluded — BP is stable for 6 days, urine output is 1 L/day, no signs of volume depletion<br />
肾前性 AKI 已排除——血压稳定 6 天，尿量 1 L/天，无容量不足体征</td>
<td>Fluids correct prerenal causes; AIN is intrinsic renal disease unresponsive to volume loading<br />
补液纠正肾前性病因；AIN 是肾实质疾病，补液无效</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>E — Discontinue ceftriaxone ✓<br />
E — 停用头孢曲松 ✓</td>
<td>CORRECT — removes the causative antigen, which is the essential and immediate first step in drug-induced AIN<br />
正确——移除致病抗原，是药物性 AIN 最关键的即时第一步</td>
<td>Urine eosinophils + rising Cr + beta-lactam use = classic drug-induced AIN; stop the drug first<br />
尿液嗜酸粒细胞 + 肌酐升高 + β-内酰胺类用药 = 经典药物性 AIN；停药优先</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>F — No intervention is indicated<br />
F — 无需干预</td>
<td>Untreated AIN → progressive AKI → risk of permanent renal damage and CKD<br />
未治疗的 AIN→进行性 AKI→有永久肾损伤和慢性肾脏病风险</td>
<td>Active drug-induced AIN with rising creatinine always requires drug discontinuation at minimum<br />
肌酐持续升高的活动性药物性 AIN 至少需要停药处理</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

*The most tempting distractor is Choice C (prednisone) — steroids genuinely improve renal recovery in AIN, but the sequence matters: stop the drug first, then escalate to steroids only if needed.*

最具诱惑性的干扰项是 C（泼尼松）——类固醇确实能改善 AIN 的肾功能恢复，但顺序至关重要：先停药，仅在必要时才升阶梯至类固醇。

## 6. One-Sentence Summary & Memory Hook / 一句话总结 & 记忆钩

**When a hospitalized patient on a beta-lactam develops AKI with urine eosinophils and sterile pyuria, drug-induced AIN is the diagnosis and discontinuing the offending drug is the essential first step — steroids come only if needed afterward.**

**当住院患者在使用 β-内酰胺类抗生素期间出现 AKI，伴尿液嗜酸性粒细胞及无菌性脓尿时，诊断为药物性 AIN，停用致病药物是首要步骤——类固醇仅在停药后仍无改善时才考虑使用。**

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 100%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><p><strong>Memory Hook — "RASH" for AIN Recognition / 记忆钩 — "RASH" 记忆 AIN 识别要点:</strong></p>
<p>• <strong>R</strong>ising Cr + drug exposure → think AIN first / 肌酐上升 + 用药史→首先想到 AIN<br />
• <strong>A</strong>bnormal UA: eosinophils + WBCs + no RBC casts = interstitial, not glomerular / 异常尿检：嗜酸粒细胞 + WBC + 无红细胞管型 = 间质而非肾小球病变<br />
• <strong>S</strong>top the drug BEFORE adding steroids — sequence matters / 先停药再考虑类固醇——顺序至关重要<br />
• <strong>H</strong>allmark triggers: beta-lactams, NSAIDs, PPIs, sulfonamides, rifampin / 经典触发药物：β-内酰胺类、NSAIDs、PPIs、磺胺类、利福平</p></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
</tbody>
</table>

## 7. High-Yield Topic Knowledge — Acute Interstitial Nephritis (AIN) / 高频知识表 — 急性间质性肾炎

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 50%" />
<col style="width: 50%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Topic</strong><br />
<strong>考点</strong></th>
<th><strong>Key Points</strong><br />
<strong>要点</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>Classic drug causes<br />
经典药物病因</td>
<td>Beta-lactams (penicillins, cephalosporins), NSAIDs, thiazide/loop diuretics, PPIs, sulfonamides, rifampin<br />
β-内酰胺类（青霉素、头孢菌素）、NSAIDs、噻嗪类/袢利尿剂、PPIs、磺胺类、利福平</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Classic triad (present in ~10% only)<br />
经典三联征（仅约 10% 患者出现）</td>
<td>Fever + rash + eosinophilia — absence does NOT exclude AIN; do not wait for all three<br />
发热 + 皮疹 + 嗜酸性粒细胞增多——三联征缺失不能排除 AIN；不要等三联征齐全才诊断</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Urine findings<br />
尿液检查特征</td>
<td>Eosinophiluria (Wright or Hansel stain), sterile pyuria, hematuria, proteinuria &lt;3.5 g/day; NO RBC casts<br />
嗜酸粒细胞尿（Wright 或 Hansel 染色）、无菌性脓尿、血尿、蛋白尿 &lt;3.5 g/天；无红细胞管型</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Gold standard diagnosis<br />
诊断金标准</td>
<td>Renal biopsy: interstitial edema + inflammatory infiltrate (lymphocytes + eosinophils + plasma cells)<br />
肾活检：间质水肿 + 炎性浸润（淋巴细胞 + 嗜酸粒细胞 + 浆细胞）</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Management sequence<br />
处理步骤顺序</td>
<td>Step 1: Discontinue offending drug → Step 2: Supportive care → Step 3: Prednisone 1 mg/kg/day if no improvement in 3–5 days<br />
第一步：停用致病药物→第二步：支持治疗→第三步：若 3-5 天无改善，泼尼松 1 mg/kg/天</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Non-drug causes of AIN<br />
非药物性 AIN 病因</td>
<td>Infections (pyelonephritis, EBV, CMV, legionella), autoimmune (SLE, sarcoidosis, Sjögren syndrome, IgG4-RD)<br />
感染（肾盂肾炎、EBV、CMV、军团菌）、自身免疫（SLE、结节病、干燥综合征、IgG4 相关疾病）</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Contrast nephropathy timing rule<br />
造影剂肾病时间规律</td>
<td>CIN peaks at 24–48h post-contrast; creatinine normalizes within 1–2 weeks; onset &gt;48h argues against CIN<br />
CIN 于造影后 24-48h 达峰；肌酐在 1-2 周内恢复；发病超过 48 小时不支持 CIN</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Prognosis<br />
预后</td>
<td>Most recover fully with drug discontinuation ± steroids; delayed treatment → risk of irreversible CKD<br />
停药 ± 类固醇后大多数完全恢复；治疗延迟→有不可逆慢性肾脏病风险</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

## 8. Extensions / 延伸扩展

- **Differential of eosinophiluria:** AIN (most important), atheroembolism, drug reactions, urinary schistosomiasis — eosinophiluria is not specific but is highly suggestive of AIN in the appropriate clinical context\
  **嗜酸粒细胞尿的鉴别:** AIN（最重要）、胆固醇栓塞、药物反应、尿路血吸虫病——嗜酸粒细胞尿不具特异性，但在适当临床背景下高度提示 AIN

- **Contrast nephropathy vs. AIN in this case:** Patient has diabetes (heightened CIN risk) and received contrast 6 days ago — but the 6-day gap and urine eosinophils definitively shift the diagnosis to AIN over CIN\
  **本题中造影剂肾病 vs. AIN:** 患者合并糖尿病（CIN 高风险）且 6 天前使用造影剂——但 6 天间隔及尿液嗜酸粒细胞明确将诊断指向 AIN 而非 CIN

- **Lisinopril and AKI:** ACE inhibitors impair glomerular efferent arteriole constriction and can exacerbate AKI in renal hypoperfusion states, but they do not cause AIN — lisinopril is a contributing factor to monitor, not the primary culprit here\
  **赖诺普利与 AKI:** ACEI 影响出球小动脉收缩，在肾灌注不足时可加重 AKI，但不导致 AIN——赖诺普利是需监测的加重因素，不是此次主要病因

- **Step-up therapy rule:** If creatinine continues rising 3–5 days after drug cessation, add oral prednisone (1 mg/kg/day, taper over 4–6 weeks); renal biopsy before steroid initiation if diagnosis is uncertain\
  **升阶梯治疗原则:** 停药后 3-5 天肌酐仍持续升高，加用口服泼尼松（1 mg/kg/天，4-6 周减量）；若诊断不确定，在启动类固醇前行肾活检

# Question 191 — Cannabis Hyperemesis Syndrome / 大麻素性剧吐综合征

## Question Stem / 题干

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 100%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><p>A <strong>40-year-old man</strong> comes to the emergency department because of a <strong>1-day history of nausea and vomiting</strong>. He has not had fever, chills, abdominal pain, or diarrhea. He says <strong>taking a hot shower alleviates his symptoms</strong>. He has no history of serious illness and takes no medications. He says he <strong>occasionally uses illicit drugs</strong> but refuses to provide any additional information. His temperature is 36.7°C (98°F), pulse is <strong>100/min</strong>, respirations are 18/min, and blood pressure is <strong>130/90 mm Hg</strong>. Examination shows no other abnormalities. Intoxication from which of the following is the most likely cause of this patient's current condition?</p>
<p><strong>Q: Intoxication from which of the following is the most likely cause of this patient's current condition?</strong></p>
<p>A) Cannabis<br />
B) Cocaine<br />
C) Heroin<br />
D) LSD<br />
E) Methamphetamine<br />
F) PCP (phencyclidine)</p>
<p><strong>Correct Answer: A</strong></p></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
</tbody>
</table>

## 1. Key Stem Clues / 题干关键词抓考点

不支持阿片类中毒（瞳孔缩小、嗜睡）及兴奋剂精神病</td>
</tr>

## 2. Mechanism / 机制理解

**Cannabis hyperemesis syndrome (CHS)** arises from paradoxical **cannabinoid receptor** dysregulation in the setting of **chronic, high-dose cannabis use**:

**大麻素性剧吐综合征（CHS）**源于**长期、高剂量大麻使用**背景下矛盾性的**大麻素受体**功能失调：

- Chronic cannabis exposure leads to **CB1 receptor downregulation** in the gut and hypothalamus, impairing normal emesis suppression\
  长期大麻暴露导致肠道及下丘脑**CB1受体下调**，正常止吐机制受损

- Cannabinoids accumulate in adipose tissue and are slowly released, prolonging dysregulation\
  大麻素蓄积于脂肪组织并缓慢释放，延长调节紊乱的时间

- The **thermoregulatory mechanism** of hot-water bathing is hypothesized to activate cutaneous TRPV1 receptors, overriding central emetic signals\
  热水洗浴缓解症状的**体温调节机制**，推测通过激活皮肤TRPV1受体来抑制中枢性呕吐信号

- Episodes are cyclical and typically resolve within **48 hours of cannabis cessation**\
  发作呈周期性，通常在**停止使用大麻48小时内**缓解

**Anatomic rule of thumb:** The enteric nervous system is rich in CB1 receptors; chronic overstimulation paradoxically reverses their antiemetic effect.

**解剖小窍门:** 肠神经系统富含CB1受体；长期过度刺激会矛盾性地逆转其止吐效果。

## 3. Correct Answer (A) — Cannabis Hyperemesis Syndrome / 正确答案 (A) — 大麻素性剧吐综合征

**Cannabis hyperemesis syndrome** is a paradoxical complication of chronic cannabis use characterized by cyclic vomiting that is uniquely relieved by hot showers or baths:

**大麻素性剧吐综合征**是慢性大麻使用的矛盾性并发症，以周期性呕吐为特征，热水淋浴或泡浴可独特地缓解症状：

- Occurs in the setting of prolonged, frequent, high-dose recreational cannabis use\
  发生于长期、频繁、高剂量娱乐性大麻使用背景下

- Classic triad: cyclic vomiting + hot bathing relief + chronic cannabis use\
  经典三联征：周期性呕吐 + 热浴缓解 + 长期大麻使用史

- Acute cannabis intoxication can also cause tachycardia, mild hypertension, and conjunctival injection\
  急性大麻中毒还可引起心动过速、轻度高血压及结膜充血

**Diagnosis:** Cyclic vomiting with hot-shower compulsive bathing behavior in a chronic cannabis user; exclude other causes (pregnancy, obstruction, metabolic)

**诊断:** 慢性大麻使用者出现周期性呕吐伴强迫性热浴行为；需排除其他原因（妊娠、梗阻、代谢异常）

**Treatment:** Acute: antiemetics (haloperidol, ondansetron), capsaicin cream (TRPV1 agonist); Definitive: complete cannabis cessation

**治疗:** 急性期：止吐药（氟哌啶醇、昂丹司琼）、辣椒素乳膏（TRPV1激动剂）；根本治疗：完全停止使用大麻

<td>Isolated vomiting without psychotic features argues against meth<br />
单纯呕吐而无精神病特征，不支持甲基苯丙胺</td>

<td>No nystagmus, ataxia, or aggression present<br />
无眼球震颤、共济失调或攻击行为</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

*The trickiest distractor is cocaine or methamphetamine because this patient has tachycardia and hypertension — however, the pathognomonic hot-shower relief and isolated vomiting without psychotic or nasal features locks in cannabis hyperemesis syndrome.*

最容易误选的干扰项是可卡因或甲基苯丙胺，因为本患者有心动过速和高血压；但热水淋浴缓解的特征性表现，以及单纯呕吐而无精神病或鼻部症状，可锁定大麻素性剧吐综合征的诊断。

## 6. One-Sentence Summary & Memory Hook / 一句话总结 & 记忆钩

**A patient with chronic cannabis use presenting with cyclic vomiting relieved by compulsive hot bathing has cannabis hyperemesis syndrome, which resolves with cannabis cessation.**

**慢性大麻使用者出现周期性呕吐，强迫性热水淋浴可缓解，诊断为大麻素性剧吐综合征，戒断大麻后可缓解。**

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 100%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><p><strong>Memory Hook — CHS "HOT" Triad / 记忆钩 — CHS "HOT"三联征:</strong></p>
<p>• <strong>H</strong>ot shower relief — the pathognomonic sign / 热浴缓解——特征性体征<br />
• <strong>O</strong>ngoing (chronic) cannabis use — high-dose, long-term / 持续（慢性）大麻使用——高剂量、长期<br />
• <strong>T</strong>hrows up cyclically — episodic vomiting without other GI cause / 周期性呕吐——无其他消化道病因的间歇性呕吐</p></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
</tbody>

<tr>
<td>CHS definition<br />
CHS定义</td>
<td>Episodic nausea/vomiting in chronic heavy cannabis users; compulsive hot bathing is pathognomonic; resolves with cessation<br />
慢性重度大麻使用者的间歇性恶心/呕吐；强迫性热浴为特征性表现；戒断后缓解</td>
