旋转性眼球震颤+共济失调+攻击性（经典三联征）；解离性麻醉药；慢性：抑郁、记忆丧失、构音障碍</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Cannabis acute intoxication vs. CHS<br />
急性大麻中毒 vs. CHS</td>
<td>Acute: euphoria, conjunctival injection, increased appetite, cognitive slowing, paranoia; CHS requires chronic use + emesis pattern<br />
急性：欣快、结膜充血、食欲增加、认知减慢、偏执；CHS需慢性使用+呕吐模式</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

## 8. Extensions / 延伸扩展

- **Differential of cyclic vomiting:** Other conditions to consider include cyclic vomiting syndrome (CVS), Addison's disease (adrenal insufficiency), gastroparesis, and Wernicke's encephalopathy in substance users\
  **周期性呕吐鉴别:** 其他需考虑的疾病包括周期性呕吐综合征（CVS）、Addison病（肾上腺皮质功能不全）、胃轻瘫以及物质使用者中的Wernicke脑病

- **Capsaicin mechanism:** Topical capsaicin activates TRPV1 receptors in skin, mimicking the thermogenic relief of hot showers; used as an ED adjunct for acute CHS\
  **辣椒素机制:** 外用辣椒素激活皮肤TRPV1受体，模拟热水淋浴的热疗缓解效果；用于急性CHS的急诊辅助治疗

- **Key complication:** Severe dehydration and electrolyte imbalances (hypokalemia, hyponatremia) from prolonged vomiting; compulsive hot bathing can also cause scalding injuries\
  **主要并发症:** 长期呕吐导致严重脱水及电解质紊乱（低钾血症、低钠血症）；强迫性热浴还可导致烫伤

- **Step 2 CK exam tip:** Any patient with cyclic vomiting + hot shower relief = cannabis hyperemesis syndrome until proven otherwise; always ask about drug use even when patients are evasive — the hot-bath clue is the giveaway\
  **Step 2 CK 考试提示:** 任何出现周期性呕吐+热浴缓解的患者，在排除其他原因前应首先考虑大麻素性剧吐综合征；即使患者回避，也应询问药物使用史——热浴缓解是关键线索

# Question 192 — Breast Cancer Workup: Excisional Biopsy After Negative FNA / 乳腺癌检查：细针穿刺阴性后的切除活检

## Question Stem / 题干

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 100%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><p>A <strong>62-year-old woman</strong> comes to the physician because of a 4-month history of a <strong>painless mass</strong> in her left breast; the mass has <strong>not changed in size</strong>. Ten years ago, she had a total abdominal hysterectomy and <strong>bilateral salpingo-oophorectomy</strong>. She has hypertension treated with hydrochlorothiazide. Her <strong>maternal aunt was diagnosed with breast cancer at the age of 55 years</strong>. The patient's vital signs are within normal limits. Examination shows a <strong>2.5-cm hard, immobile mass</strong> in the <strong>upper outer quadrant</strong> of the left breast. <strong>Mammography and fine-needle aspiration biopsy specimen show no abnormalities.</strong></p>
<p><strong>Q: Which of the following is the most appropriate next step in management?</strong></p>
<p>A) Follow-up examination in 3 months<br />
B) Repeat mammography in 6 months<br />
C) MRI of the left breast<br />
D) Tamoxifen therapy<br />
E) Excisional biopsy</p>
<p><strong>Correct Answer: E</strong></p></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
</tbody>
</table>

## 1. Key Stem Clues / 题干关键词抓考点

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 50%" />
<col style="width: 50%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Key Stem Clue</strong><br />
<strong>关键词</strong></th>
<th><strong>Why It Matters</strong><br />
<strong>为什么重要</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>62-year-old woman<br />
62岁女性</td>
<td>Age &gt;50 is a major breast cancer risk factor; postmenopausal status amplifies risk<br />
年龄&gt;50岁是乳腺癌主要危险因素；绝经后状态进一步增加风险</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Hard, immobile 2.5-cm mass<br />
坚硬、固定的2.5厘米肿块</td>
<td>Hard + immobile = classic malignancy features; benign lesions (fibroadenoma, cyst) are typically soft and mobile<br />
坚硬+不可移动=经典恶性肿瘤特征；良性病变（纤维腺瘤、囊肿）通常质软且可移动</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Upper outer quadrant<br />
外上象限</td>
<td>Most common location for breast cancer (~50% of cases); drains to axillary Level I nodes<br />
乳腺癌最常见部位（约50%的病例）；淋巴引流至腋窝I级淋巴结</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Maternal aunt with breast cancer at 55<br />
母亲的姐妹55岁确诊乳腺癌</td>
<td>Second-degree family history raises cancer risk; suggests possible hereditary component (BRCA)<br />
二级亲属家族史增加癌症风险；提示可能存在遗传因素（BRCA基因）</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Mammography and FNA both negative<br />
乳腺钼靶和细针穿刺均阴性</td>
<td>FNA sensitivity only ~74%; mammography false-negative rate 10–15%; negative results do NOT exclude malignancy when exam is suspicious<br />
细针穿刺敏感性仅约74%；乳腺钼靶假阴性率10–15%；当体检高度可疑时，阴性结果不能排除恶性肿瘤</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Bilateral salpingo-oophorectomy<br />
双侧输卵管卵巢切除术</td>
<td>Surgical menopause reduces endogenous estrogen exposure (partially protective), but does not eliminate breast cancer risk<br />
手术性绝经减少内源性雌激素暴露（部分保护作用），但不能消除乳腺癌风险</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

## 2. Mechanism / 机制理解

**Breast cancer** is the most common nondermatologic malignancy in women. The central principle in this question is that **physical examination findings override negative imaging** when clinical suspicion is high:

**乳腺癌**是女性最常见的非皮肤科恶性肿瘤。本题的核心原则是：当临床高度怀疑时，**体格检查结果优先于阴性影像学**：

- Mammography detects calcifications and masses, but has 10–15% false-negative rate, especially in dense breast tissue\
  乳腺钼靶可发现钙化灶和肿块，但假阴性率为10–15%，尤其在致密型乳腺中更明显

- FNA provides cytology only (no tissue architecture); ~26% of samples are non-diagnostic or falsely negative\
  细针穿刺仅提供细胞学检查（无组织结构）；约26%的标本不具诊断性或为假阴性

- A hard, immobile breast mass is a "red flag" finding that mandates tissue diagnosis regardless of imaging results\
  坚硬、不可移动的乳房肿块是"危险信号"，无论影像学结果如何，均须进行组织学诊断

- Excisional biopsy removes the entire lesion for histopathology and may be curative if disease is localized\
  切除活检切除整个病变进行组织病理学检查，若病变局限则可能具有治愈性

**Anatomic rule of thumb:** The upper outer quadrant drains to axillary lymph nodes (Level I → II → III); sentinel lymph node biopsy samples Level I first to stage axillary involvement.

**解剖小窍门:** 外上象限淋巴引流至腋窝淋巴结（I级→II级→III级）；前哨淋巴结活检首先对I级淋巴结取样以进行腋窝分期。

## 3. Correct Answer (E) — Excisional Biopsy / 正确答案 (E) — 切除活检

**Excisional biopsy** is the appropriate next step when a breast mass remains clinically suspicious despite negative FNA and normal mammography:

**切除活检**是当乳房肿块在细针穿刺阴性和乳腺钼靶正常情况下仍高度临床可疑时的恰当下一步：

- Removes the entire mass for histopathologic analysis — eliminates the sampling error inherent to FNA\
  切除整个肿块进行组织病理学分析——消除了细针穿刺固有的取样误差

- Sensitivity approaches 100%, far superior to FNA (~74%) or core needle biopsy (~90–97%)\
  敏感性接近100%，远优于细针穿刺（约74%）或空芯针穿刺活检（约90–97%）

- May be curative if the cancer is entirely confined within the excised specimen (wide local excision)\
  若癌症完全局限于切除标本内（局部扩大切除术），则可能具有治愈性

**Diagnosis:** The clinical triad of hard + immobile + upper outer quadrant mass in a postmenopausal woman with family history compels definitive tissue diagnosis, not more imaging.

**诊断:** 绝经后女性合并家族史出现"坚硬+固定+外上象限"肿块的三联征，要求进行确定性组织学诊断，而非更多影像学检查。

**Treatment:** Lumpectomy ± radiation or mastectomy; adjuvant hormonal therapy (tamoxifen/aromatase inhibitor) for ER+ disease; all require confirmed histologic diagnosis first.

**治疗:** 乳房肿瘤切除术±放疗或乳房切除术；ER阳性者需辅助内分泌治疗（他莫昔芬/芳香化酶抑制剂）；所有治疗均须先有组织学确诊。

## 4. Options Elimination / 错误选项排除逻辑

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 33%" />
<col style="width: 33%" />
<col style="width: 33%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Option</strong><br />
<strong>选项</strong></th>
<th><strong>Why Wrong</strong><br />
<strong>为什么错</strong></th>
<th><strong>Key Discriminator</strong><br />
<strong>鉴别要点</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>A — Follow-up examination in 3 months<br />
A — 3个月后随访检查</td>
<td>Wrong — dangerous delay for a highly suspicious lesion; allows time for metastatic spread<br />
错误——高度可疑病变危险性延误诊断；给转移扩散留出时间</td>
<td>Watchful waiting is appropriate only for clearly benign lesions (young woman, soft mobile mass, classic fibroadenoma features)<br />
等待观察仅适用于明确良性病变（年轻女性、质软可移动肿块、典型纤维腺瘤特征）</td>

<tr>
<td>B — Repeat mammography in 6 months<br />
B — 6个月后重复乳腺钼靶</td>
<td>Wrong — mammography already negative; repeating the same test yields the same false-negative result<br />
错误——乳腺钼靶已为阴性；重复同一检查只会得到相同的假阴性结果</td>
<td>Imaging is supplementary to physical exam; a suspicious palpable mass demands tissue diagnosis, not repeat imaging<br />
影像学是体格检查的辅助手段；可疑可触及肿块需要组织学诊断，而非重复影像学</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>C — MRI of the left breast<br />
C — 左侧乳房MRI</td>
<td>Wrong — MRI cannot provide tissue diagnosis; its role is staging known cancer or screening high-risk patients<br />
错误——MRI不能提供组织学诊断；其作用是已知乳腺癌的分期或高危患者筛查</td>
<td>MRI is used post-diagnosis for extent-of-disease evaluation, not as workup for a palpable suspicious mass<br />
MRI在诊断后用于疾病范围评估，不用于可触及可疑肿块的检查</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>D — Tamoxifen therapy<br />
D — 他莫昔芬治疗</td>
<td>Wrong — treatment cannot begin without histologic diagnosis; empirical tamoxifen is inappropriate<br />
错误——未经组织学诊断不能开始治疗；经验性他莫昔芬使用不当</td>
<td>Tamoxifen is ER+ breast cancer treatment/chemoprevention — requires confirmed diagnosis or confirmed high-risk status first<br />
他莫昔芬用于ER阳性乳腺癌治疗/化学预防——须先有确诊或确认的高风险状态</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>E — Excisional biopsy ✓<br />
E — 切除活检 ✓</td>
<td>CORRECT — definitive tissue diagnosis with ~100% sensitivity; may be curative if lesion is localized<br />
正确——确定性组织学诊断，敏感性约100%；若病变局限则可能具有治愈性</td>
<td>Suspicious exam (hard, immobile) + failed FNA → excisional biopsy is the mandatory next step<br />
体检可疑（坚硬、固定）+ 细针穿刺失败 → 切除活检是必须的下一步</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

*Choice C (MRI) is the most tempting distractor because it seems more thorough than repeat mammography — but remember that MRI provides no tissue diagnosis and is not indicated as initial workup for a palpable suspicious mass.*

选项C（MRI）是最具迷惑性的干扰项，因为它看起来比重复乳腺钼靶更全面——但要记住MRI不能提供组织学诊断，且不适合作为可触及可疑肿块的初始检查。

## 6. One-Sentence Summary & Memory Hook / 一句话总结 & 记忆钩

**When physical examination reveals a hard, immobile breast mass, excisional biopsy is mandatory even if mammography and FNA are both negative, because FNA sensitivity is only ~74%.**

**当体格检查发现坚硬、固定的乳房肿块时，即使乳腺钼靶和细针穿刺均阴性，也必须进行切除活检，因为细针穿刺的敏感性仅约74%。**

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 100%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><p><strong>Memory Hook — The "EXAM" Rule for Suspicious Breast Mass / 记忆钩 — 可疑乳房肿块的"EXAM"法则:</strong></p>
<p>• <strong>E</strong>xam suspicion (hard + immobile) → always demands tissue biopsy / 体检可疑（坚硬+固定）→ 始终需要组织活检<br />
• <strong>X</strong>-ray (mammography) negative ≠ benign — 10–15% false-negative rate / 乳腺钼靶阴性 ≠ 良性——假阴性率10–15%<br />
• <strong>A</strong>spiration (FNA) negative ≠ benign — only ~74% sensitive / 细针穿刺阴性 ≠ 良性——敏感性仅约74%<br />
• <strong>M</strong>andatory excisional biopsy when exam is suspicious despite negative workup / 体检可疑而检查阴性时必须切除活检</p></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>

</table>

<tr>
<td>First imaging step in women &gt;30 with breast mass<br />
&gt;30岁女性乳房肿块的一线影像学检查</td>
<td>Mammography — false-negative rate 10–15%; ultrasound added if lesion may be cystic or for biopsy guidance<br />

年龄、家族史、BRCA1/2突变、初潮早、绝经晚、未产妇、外源性雌激素、肥胖、放射线暴露</td>

<tr>
<td>Upper outer quadrant<br />
外上象限</td>
<td>Most common breast cancer location (~50%); axillary lymph node drainage (Level I first); sentinel node biopsy samples Level I<br />
乳腺癌最常见部位（约50%）；腋窝淋巴结引流（I级最先）；前哨淋巴结活检取样I级</td>
</tr>
<tr>

他莫昔芬适应证</td>
<td>ER+ breast cancer treatment (pre- and postmenopausal); chemoprevention in high-risk women — never empirical without diagnosis<br />
ER阳性乳腺癌治疗（绝经前后均可）；高危女性化学预防——未经诊断绝不经验性使用</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

## 8. Extensions / 延伸扩展

- **Differential of palpable breast mass:** Fibroadenoma (young, rubbery, mobile), fibrocystic change (cyclically tender, multiple), abscess (warm, erythematous, lactating), fat necrosis (trauma history), carcinoma (hard, immobile, painless)\
  **乳房可触及肿块鉴别:** 纤维腺瘤（年轻、橡皮样、可移动）、纤维囊性变（周期性压痛、多发）、脓肿（温热、红斑、哺乳期）、脂肪坏死（外伤史）、癌（坚硬、固定、无痛）

- **BRCA testing indications:** Family history of breast cancer \<50 years, bilateral breast cancer, male breast cancer, ovarian cancer in first/second-degree relatives, Ashkenazi Jewish ancestry\
  **BRCA检测适应证:** 乳腺癌家族史\<50岁、双侧乳腺癌、男性乳腺癌、一级/二级亲属卵巢癌、德系犹太人血统

- **Inflammatory breast cancer (T4d):** Peau d'orange + breast erythema + rapid onset — dermal lymphatic invasion; no discrete mass; treated with neoadjuvant chemo first, then surgery\
  **炎性乳腺癌（T4d）:** 橘皮征+乳腺红斑+快速起病——真皮淋巴管侵犯；无明确肿块；先行新辅助化疗，后手术

- **Mammographic screening guidelines:** USPSTF: biennial mammography ages 50–74; ACR/ACS: annual starting at 40; women with \>20% lifetime risk should add annual breast MRI\
  **乳腺钼靶筛查指南:** USPSTF：50–74岁每两年筛查；ACR/ACS：从40岁开始每年筛查；终生风险\>20%的女性应加做年度乳房MRI

# Question 193 — Tympanic Membrane Perforation Secondary to Acute Otitis Media / 鼓膜穿孔（急性中耳炎继发）

## Question Stem / 题干

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 100%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><p>A <strong>2-year-old girl</strong> is brought to the office by her mother because of <strong>bloody drainage from her right ear</strong> that the mother first noticed last night when the patient <strong>woke up screaming and holding her right ear</strong>. The pain improved after the mother cleaned the ear with a cotton swab and gave the patient ibuprofen, but the mother noted <strong>dried, crusted blood</strong> on the patient's right ear lobe and pillow when she awoke this morning. The patient also has a <strong>3-day history of cough, congestion, and runny nose</strong>. She has no history of serious illness and receives no routine medications. She is at the 25th percentile for height and weight and 50th percentile for BMI. Vital signs are within normal limits. The <strong>right tympanic membrane cannot be visualized because of seropurulent fluid</strong> in the right external auditory canal. The remainder of the examination, including examination of the left tympanic membrane, discloses no abnormalities.</p>
<p><strong>Q: Which of the following is the most likely cause of this patient's ear drainage?</strong></p>
<p>A) Basilar skull fracture<br />
B) Mastoiditis<br />
C) Otitis externa<br />
D) Traumatic injury to the external auditory canal<br />
E) Tympanic membrane perforation</p>
<p><strong>Correct Answer: E</strong></p></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
</tbody>
</table>

---

## 1. Key Stem Clues / 题干关键词抓考点

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 50%" />
<col style="width: 50%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Key Stem Clue</strong><br />
<strong>关键词</strong></th>
<th><strong>Why It Matters</strong><br />
<strong>为什么重要</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>2-year-old girl<br />
2 岁女孩</td>
<td>Peak age for AOM; eustachian tube is short, horizontal, and floppy in toddlers, facilitating ascent of nasopharyngeal pathogens<br />
AOM 高发年龄；婴幼儿咽鼓管短、水平、松弛，鼻咽部病原体易逆行进入中耳</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Bloody drainage from right ear<br />
右耳血性分泌物</td>
<td>Hallmark of TM perforation from AOM — seropurulent middle ear pus under pressure ruptures the membrane<br />
AOM 所致鼓膜穿孔的标志性表现——中耳脓液蓄积压力升高后穿破鼓膜</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Woke up screaming, pain then improved<br />
剧烈耳痛后疼痛骤减</td>
<td>Classic sequence: pressure builds → TM perforates → drainage decompresses the middle ear → dramatic pain relief<br />
典型过程：压力积聚→鼓膜穿孔→分泌物引流→中耳减压→疼痛显著缓解</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>3-day URI (cough, congestion, runny nose)<br />
3 天上呼吸道感染（咳嗽、鼻塞、流涕）</td>
<td>AOM classically follows a viral URI; bacteria (S. pneumoniae, H. influenzae) superinfect the middle ear via the eustachian tube<br />
AOM 典型继发于病毒性 URI；细菌经咽鼓管超感染中耳</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Seropurulent fluid in right EAC, TM not visualized<br />
右侧外耳道浓血性分泌物，鼓膜不可视</td>
<td>Confirms perforation with drainage into the canal; normal left ear rules out bilateral pathology<br />
证实鼓膜穿孔伴分泌物流入耳道；左耳正常排除双侧病变</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Pain preceded cotton swab use<br />
疼痛早于棉签清洁</td>
<td>Excludes traumatic EAC injury; the timeline establishes spontaneous perforation, not iatrogenic<br />
排除外耳道外伤；时间线明确为自发性穿孔而非器械损伤</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

---

## 2. Mechanism / 机制理解

**Acute otitis media (AOM)** arises when **nasopharyngeal pathogens** ascend via the **eustachian tube** into the sterile middle ear space, triggering an inflammatory cascade with **pus accumulation** behind the tympanic membrane:

**急性中耳炎（AOM）**由**鼻咽部病原体**经**咽鼓管**逆行进入无菌中耳腔，引发炎症瀑布反应，**脓液积聚**于鼓膜后方：

- Viral URI disrupts eustachian tube function → negative middle ear pressure → bacterial superinfection (S. pneumoniae \> H. influenzae \> M. catarrhalis)\
  病毒性 URI 破坏咽鼓管功能→中耳负压→细菌超感染（肺炎链球菌 \> 流感嗜血杆菌 \> 卡他莫拉菌）

- Progressive pus accumulation elevates intratympanic pressure → erythematous, bulging, immobile TM → severe otalgia\
  脓液进行性积聚→鼓室内压升高→鼓膜充血、膨出、活动度消失→剧烈耳痛

- When pressure exceeds tensile strength of TM → spontaneous perforation → decompression → purulent/bloody otorrhea and dramatic pain relief\
  当压力超过鼓膜抗张强度→自发穿孔→减压→脓性/血性耳漏，疼痛骤然缓解

- Most perforations in AOM are small and heal spontaneously within weeks without surgical repair\
  AOM 所致穿孔多为小穿孔，数周内自行愈合，无需手术干预

**Anatomic rule of thumb:** In children \<2 years, the eustachian tube is ~18 mm long (vs. 35 mm in adults), oriented nearly horizontally, and lacks the cartilaginous support needed to resist nasopharyngeal reflux — explaining why AOM peaks in toddlers.

**解剖小窍门:** 2 岁以下儿童咽鼓管约 18 mm 长（成人约 35 mm），近乎水平走行，缺乏防止鼻咽反流的软骨支撑——这解释了 AOM 在幼儿中高发的原因。

---

## 3. Correct Answer (E) — Tympanic Membrane Perforation / 正确答案 (E) — 鼓膜穿孔

**Tympanic membrane perforation** secondary to AOM produces the classic triad of acute otalgia followed by sudden relief, bloody/purulent otorrhea, and a URI prodrome:

**鼓膜穿孔**继发于 AOM，产生典型三联征：急性耳痛后骤然缓解、血性/脓性耳漏、以及 URI 前驱症状：

- Middle ear pressure from AOM builds until it exceeds TM strength → spontaneous rupture releases seropurulent contents into the EAC\
  AOM 中耳压力积聚超过鼓膜强度→自发破裂，脓血性内容物流入外耳道

- The seropurulent fluid fills the EAC and obscures TM visualization — distinguishing it from otitis externa (where canal is swollen/tender but TM can often still be seen)\
  脓血性分泌物充满外耳道并遮挡鼓膜——与外耳道炎相区别（外耳道肿胀/压痛，但鼓膜通常仍可见）

- Conductive hearing loss may accompany the perforation but is typically transient\
  穿孔可伴随传导性听力下降，但通常是一过性的

**Diagnosis:** Clinical — URI prodrome + acute otalgia + sudden relief upon drainage + seropurulent otorrhea + inability to visualize TM due to canal fluid.

**诊断:** 临床诊断——URI 前驱症状 + 急性耳痛 + 引流后骤然缓解 + 脓血性耳漏 + 因耳道积液无法看到鼓膜。

**Treatment:** Oral antibiotics (amoxicillin-clavulanate) or topical fluoroquinolone ear drops (ciprofloxacin/ofloxacin); most perforations heal spontaneously without surgical intervention.

**治疗:** 口服抗生素（阿莫西林-克拉维酸）或局部滴耳氟喹诺酮类药物（环丙沙星/氧氟沙星）；多数穿孔无需手术，自行愈合。

---

<tr>
<td>A — Basilar skull fracture<br />
A — 颅底骨折</td>
<td>Why wrong — no significant head trauma; Battle sign (retroauricular ecchymosis) and hemotympanum are absent<br />
为什么错——无明显头外伤史；无 Battle 征（耳后瘀斑）及血鼓室</td>

为什么错——乳突炎表现为耳后疼痛、肿胀、充血及耳廓前移，本例均无</td>

<tr>
<td>C — Otitis externa<br />

<td>Why wrong — "swimmer's ear" causes watery discharge with tragal tenderness and a swollen canal, not acute otalgia with bloody drainage preceded by URI<br />
为什么错——"游泳者耳"表现为水样分泌物、耳屏压痛和外耳道肿胀，不伴 URI 前驱及急性耳痛后血性引流</td>
<td>In otitis externa, TM is usually visible (canal inflamed, not filled with pus); no URI history<br />
外耳道炎中鼓膜通常可见（耳道炎症，非积脓遮挡）；无 URI 病史</td>

<tr>
<td>D — Traumatic injury to EAC<br />
D — 外耳道外伤</td>
<td>Why wrong — pain and bloody drainage preceded the cotton swab use; trauma did not cause it<br />
为什么错——疼痛和血性引流在棉签清洁之前已出现，外伤非原因</td>
<td>Timeline rules this out: spontaneous rupture occurred before any manipulation<br />
时间线排除此项：自发穿孔发生于任何操作之前</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>E — Tympanic membrane perforation ✓<br />
E — 鼓膜穿孔 ✓</td>
<td>CORRECT — URI prodrome → AOM → pressure build-up → spontaneous TM perforation → bloody otorrhea + pain relief<br />
正确——URI 前驱→AOM→压力积聚→自发鼓膜穿孔→血性耳漏 + 疼痛缓解</td>
<td>URI + acute otalgia + sudden relief upon drainage = perforation from AOM<br />
URI + 急性耳痛 + 引流后骤然缓解 = AOM 所致穿孔</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

*The most tempting distractor is Choice D (traumatic EAC injury from cotton swab), but the timeline is the decisive discriminator — the pain and drainage began before the cotton swab was ever used.*

选项 D（棉签所致外耳道外伤）最具迷惑性，但时间线是关键鉴别点——疼痛和引流在使用棉签清洁之前就已经发生了。

## 6. One-Sentence Summary & Memory Hook / 一句话总结 & 记忆钩

**In a toddler with a URI prodrome, acute otalgia with sudden dramatic pain relief, and bloody/purulent otorrhea, the diagnosis is tympanic membrane perforation from acute otitis media — treat with antibiotics and expect spontaneous healing.**

**在有 URI 前驱症状的幼儿中，急性耳痛后突然显著缓解，伴血性/脓性耳漏，诊断为急性中耳炎所致鼓膜穿孔——抗生素治疗，多数自行愈合。**

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 100%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><p><strong>Memory Hook — BURST: AOM Perforation Sequence / 记忆钩 — BURST：AOM 穿孔序列:</strong></p>
<p>• <strong>B</strong>loody otorrhea — the hallmark drainage when TM ruptures / 血性耳漏——鼓膜破裂的标志性分泌物<br />
• <strong>U</strong>RI prodrome (cough, congestion) precedes the ear pain / URI 前驱（咳嗽、鼻塞）先于耳痛出现<br />
• <strong>R</strong>elief is sudden and dramatic when the TM perforates / 鼓膜穿孔时疼痛骤然显著缓解<br />
• <strong>S</strong>eropurulent fluid fills the EAC, obscuring TM view / 脓血性液体充满外耳道，遮挡鼓膜<br />
• <strong>T</strong>reat with antibiotics; most perforations heal Themselves / 抗生素治疗；多数穿孔自愈</p></th>

## 7. High-Yield Topic Knowledge — Acute Otitis Media and Tympanic Membrane Perforation / 高频知识表 — 急性中耳炎与鼓膜穿孔

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 50%" />
<col style="width: 50%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Topic</strong><br />
<strong>考点</strong></th>
<th><strong>Key Points</strong><br />
<strong>要点</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>AOM pathogens<br />
AOM 病原体</td>
<td>S. pneumoniae (most common) &gt; H. influenzae &gt; M. catarrhalis; first-line: amoxicillin; if PCN-allergic: azithromycin<br />
肺炎链球菌（最常见）&gt; 流感嗜血杆菌 &gt; 卡他莫拉菌；一线治疗：阿莫西林；青霉素过敏：阿奇霉素</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Risk factors for AOM<br />
AOM 危险因素</td>
<td>Age &lt;2 years, daycare attendance, pacifier use, bottle feeding supine, lack of breastfeeding, tobacco smoke exposure<br />
年龄 &lt;2 岁、日托、使用安抚奶嘴、平躺奶瓶喂养、非母乳喂养、二手烟暴露</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>TM perforation from AOM<br />
AOM 所致鼓膜穿孔</td>
<td>Spontaneous perforation → pain relief + bloody/purulent otorrhea; treat with oral amoxicillin-clavulanate or topical fluoroquinolone (avoid aminoglycosides due to ototoxicity risk)<br />
自发穿孔→疼痛缓解 + 血性/脓性耳漏；口服阿莫西林-克拉维酸或局部氟喹诺酮滴耳（避免氨基糖苷类，有耳毒性风险）</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Mastoiditis (complication)<br />
乳突炎（并发症）</td>
<td>Extension of AOM into mastoid air cells; presents with postauricular tenderness, edema, erythema, and anterior auricular displacement; treat with IV antibiotics ± mastoidectomy<br />
AOM 蔓延至乳突气房；表现为耳后压痛、水肿、充血及耳廓前移；静脉抗生素 ± 乳突切除</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Otitis externa vs. AOM<br />
外耳道炎 vs. AOM</td>
<td>Otitis externa: tragal tenderness, watery discharge, swollen canal, water exposure hx; TM usually visible; treat with topical ciprofloxacin drops<br />
外耳道炎：耳屏压痛、水样分泌物、外耳道肿胀、水暴露史；鼓膜通常可见；局部环丙沙星滴耳</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Recurrent AOM management<br />
反复 AOM 的处理</td>
<td>≥3 episodes in 6 months or ≥4 in 1 year → consider tympanostomy tubes (PE tubes); tubes equalize pressure and allow middle ear drainage<br />
6 个月内 ≥3 次或 1 年内 ≥4 次→考虑鼓膜置管（PE 管）；置管使压力平衡并允许中耳引流</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Cotton swab danger<br />
棉签的危害</td>
<td>Cotton swabs should NOT be inserted into the EAC — they can traumatize the canal or TM; however, in this case the damage preceded the swab use<br />
棉签不应插入外耳道——可损伤耳道或鼓膜；但本例损伤发生于使用棉签之前</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

---

## 8. Extensions / 延伸扩展

- **Differential of bloody otorrhea:** AOM with TM perforation (URI prodrome + pain relief), EAC trauma (manipulation history), basilar skull fracture (head trauma + Battle sign), cholesteatoma (chronic foul-smelling discharge, no pain)\
  **血性耳漏鉴别:** AOM 伴鼓膜穿孔（URI 前驱 + 疼痛缓解）、外耳道外伤（操作史）、颅底骨折（头外伤 + Battle 征）、胆脂瘤（慢性恶臭分泌物，无痛）

- **Antibiotic choice for AOM with perforation:** Amoxicillin-clavulanate orally is preferred; topical fluoroquinolone (ciprofloxacin-dexamethasone) ear drops are safe and effective; avoid topical aminoglycosides (neomycin) which are ototoxic with open TM\
  **AOM 伴穿孔的抗生素选择:** 优选口服阿莫西林-克拉维酸；局部氟喹诺酮滴耳剂（环丙沙星-地塞米松）安全有效；避免局部氨基糖苷类（新霉素），鼓膜穿孔时有耳毒性

- **Spontaneous healing timeline:** Most AOM-related TM perforations are small and heal within 2–4 weeks; large or chronic perforations (\>3 months) may require tympanoplasty\
  **自发愈合时间线:** 多数 AOM 相关鼓膜穿孔较小，2–4 周内愈合；大穿孔或慢性穿孔（\>3 个月）可能需要鼓膜修补术

- **Why cotton swab clue matters on NBME:** The distractor (Choice D) is designed to misattribute the cause to cotton swab trauma; the temporal sequence — pain and drainage before swab use — is the deliberate clue to rule it out\
  **棉签线索在 NBME 中的意义:** 干扰项（选项 D）旨在将原因误归于棉签外伤；时间顺序——疼痛和引流均发生于使用棉签之前——是特意设置的排除线索

# Question 194 — Gonococcal and Chlamydial Urethritis / 淋球菌与衣原体性尿道炎

## Question Stem / 题干

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 100%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><p>A <strong>20-year-old man</strong> comes to the student health services on his college campus because of <strong>painful urination</strong> and <strong>scant urethral discharge</strong> for the past week. He says that he has had no fever, chills, or back pain. For the past <strong>6 months</strong>, he has engaged in <strong>unprotected sexual activity</strong> with one partner. He has no history of sexually transmitted diseases or other disorders and takes no medications. He appears well. His temperature is 37°C (98.6°F), pulse is 64/min, respirations are 12/min, and blood pressure is 115/70 mm Hg. Examination shows no costovertebral angle tenderness, penile lesions, or expressible discharge. Urinalysis shows <strong>no RBCs</strong>, <strong>2–5 WBC/hpf</strong>, and no casts; throat cultures are pending.</p>
<p><strong>Q: Which of the following is the most appropriate management at this time?</strong></p>
<p>A) Amoxicillin therapy<br />
B) Ceftriaxone and azithromycin therapy<br />
C) Metronidazole therapy<br />
D) Trimethoprim-sulfamethoxazole therapy<br />
E) No treatment until culture and sensitivity test results are known</p>
<p><strong>Correct Answer: B</strong></p></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
</tbody>
</table>

## 1. Key Stem Clues / 题干关键词抓考点

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 50%" />
<col style="width: 50%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Key Stem Clue</strong><br />
<strong>关键词</strong></th>
<th><strong>Why It Matters</strong><br />
<strong>为什么重要</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>20-year-old male, college student<br />
20岁男性，大学生</td>
<td>Young sexually active males are the highest-risk demographic for STIs<br />
年轻性活跃男性是性传播感染的最高风险人群</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Unprotected sexual activity × 6 months<br />
6个月无保护性行为</td>
<td>Absence of barrier contraception is the key risk factor for gonorrhea and chlamydia transmission<br />
无屏障避孕是淋球菌和衣原体传播的关键危险因素</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Dysuria + scant urethral discharge<br />
排尿疼痛 + 少量尿道分泌物</td>
<td>Classic urethritis presentation; "scant/watery" character favors C. trachomatis over N. gonorrhoeae<br />
尿道炎的典型表现；"少量/水样"特征更提示衣原体而非淋球菌</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>No fever, no CVA tenderness<br />
无发热，无肋脊角压痛</td>
<td>Rules out pyelonephritis and upper urinary tract infection<br />
排除肾盂肾炎和上尿路感染</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>2–5 WBC/hpf, no organisms on UA<br />
尿分析2-5个WBC/高倍视野，无菌</td>
<td>Sterile pyuria — hallmark of chlamydial urethritis (standard cultures cannot grow intracellular organisms)<br />
无菌性脓尿——衣原体性尿道炎的标志性表现（标准培养无法培养胞内菌）</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>No RBCs, no casts<br />
无红细胞，无管型</td>
<td>Argues against glomerulonephritis or renal parenchymal disease<br />
不支持肾小球肾炎或肾实质疾病</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Throat cultures pending<br />
咽拭子培养结果待回</td>
<td>Signals clinical suspicion for pharyngeal gonorrhea; clinician already acting empirically before results<br />
提示对咽部淋球菌感染的临床怀疑；说明须在结果回报前经验性治疗</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

## 2. Mechanism / 机制理解

**Urethritis** in sexually active young men is most commonly caused by **Neisseria gonorrhoeae** and **Chlamydia trachomatis**, both transmitted via direct mucosal contact during unprotected intercourse：

性活跃年轻男性的**尿道炎**最常见由**淋病奈瑟菌**和**沙眼衣原体**引起，二者均通过无保护性行为中直接黏膜接触传播：

- N. gonorrhoeae is a gram-negative diplococcus that attaches to urethral epithelium via pili, triggering robust neutrophilic inflammation → **purulent, copious discharge**\
  淋病奈瑟菌是革兰阴性双球菌，通过菌毛附着尿道上皮，引发强烈中性粒细胞性炎症 → **脓性、大量分泌物**

- C. trachomatis is an **obligate intracellular pathogen** that elicits a milder mucosal response → **scant, watery discharge or no discharge**; frequently asymptomatic in both sexes\
  沙眼衣原体是**专性胞内菌**，引发较轻的黏膜免疫反应 → **少量水样分泌物或无分泌物**；男女均可无症状

- **Sterile pyuria** (WBCs without bacterial growth on standard urine culture) is characteristic of chlamydial infection because standard cultures cannot grow this obligate intracellular organism\
  **无菌性脓尿**（标准尿培养阴性但尿液WBC增多）是衣原体感染特征，因常规培养无法培养专性胞内菌

- Co-infection with both organisms is common, which is why dual-drug empiric therapy is always preferred over monotherapy\
  两种病原体共同感染常见，因此双药经验性治疗始终优于单药

**Clinical pearl:** Chlamydia is the most commonly reported STI in the US; because it is frequently asymptomatic, it silently spreads between partners.

**临床珍珠:** 衣原体是美国最常见的法定报告性传播疾病；因常无症状，可在性伴侣间隐性传播。

## 3. Correct Answer (B) — Ceftriaxone + Azithromycin Dual Therapy / 正确答案 (B) — 头孢曲松 + 阿奇霉素双联治疗

**Empiric dual-antibiotic therapy** is the CDC-recommended standard of care for suspected gonococcal/chlamydial urethritis, initiated before culture results return：

**经验性双联抗菌治疗**是CDC推荐的疑似淋球菌/衣原体性尿道炎标准治疗，在培养结果回报前即启动：

- **Ceftriaxone (IM)** is a third-generation cephalosporin with reliable bactericidal activity against N. gonorrhoeae, including most penicillinase-producing and fluoroquinolone-resistant strains\
  **头孢曲松（肌注）**是第三代头孢菌素，对淋病奈瑟菌（包括大多数产青霉素酶和氟喹诺酮耐药菌株）有可靠杀菌活性

- **Azithromycin (oral)** covers C. trachomatis by inhibiting bacterial 50S ribosomal subunit protein synthesis; single-dose 1 g formulation maximizes compliance\
  **阿奇霉素（口服）**通过抑制细菌50S核糖体亚基蛋白合成覆盖沙眼衣原体；单剂1g方案最大化依从性

- Empiric treatment (not waiting for cultures) is appropriate because: (1) STIs spread rapidly to partners during any delay; (2) same-day in-office treatment prevents loss to follow-up\
  经验性治疗（不等培养结果）的合理性：（1）任何延误期间STI迅速传播给性伴侣；（2）当日门诊治疗防止失访

- Treating the sexual partner simultaneously via expedited partner therapy prevents reinfection and further community spread\
  通过加速伴侣治疗同时治疗性伴侣，防止再感染和进一步社区传播

**Diagnosis:** Clinical diagnosis based on dysuria + urethral discharge + sexual risk history + sterile pyuria; confirmed by NAAT (nucleic acid amplification test) on first-catch urine or urethral swab — more sensitive than culture.

**诊断:** 基于排尿困难 + 尿道分泌物 + 性接触风险史 + 无菌性脓尿的临床诊断；通过晨尿或尿道拭子核酸扩增检测（NAAT）确认——比培养更灵敏。

**Treatment:** Ceftriaxone 500 mg IM × 1 dose + Azithromycin 1 g PO × 1 dose (CDC 2021 guidelines); test-of-cure recommended if symptoms persist at follow-up.

**治疗:** 头孢曲松500 mg肌注单次 + 阿奇霉素1 g口服单次（CDC 2021指南）；随访时若症状持续，建议治愈性检测。

## 4. Options Elimination / 错误选项排除逻辑

<col style="width: 33%" />

</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Option</strong><br />
<strong>选项</strong></th>
<th><strong>Why Wrong</strong><br />
<strong>为什么错</strong></th>
<th><strong>Key Discriminator</strong><br />
<strong>鉴别要点</strong></th>
</tr>

<tbody>
<tr>
<td>A — Amoxicillin therapy<br />
A — 阿莫西林治疗</td>
<td>Some chlamydial coverage but inferior to azithromycin; no reliable gonococcal coverage due to widespread beta-lactamase resistance<br />
对衣原体有一定覆盖但劣于阿奇霉素；因广泛β-内酰胺酶耐药对淋球菌无可靠覆盖</td>
<td>Amoxicillin is not first-line for any STI urethritis in current CDC guidelines<br />
现行CDC指南中阿莫西林对任何STI性尿道炎均非一线</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>B — Ceftriaxone and azithromycin therapy ✓<br />
B — 头孢曲松联合阿奇霉素治疗 ✓</td>
<td>CORRECT — CDC-recommended empiric dual therapy covering N. gonorrhoeae (ceftriaxone) and C. trachomatis (azithromycin)<br />
正确——CDC推荐的经验性双联治疗，覆盖淋球菌（头孢曲松）和衣原体（阿奇霉素）</td>
<td>Dual coverage for the two most common causes of STI urethritis in sexually active men<br />
对性活跃男性两种最常见STI性尿道炎病原体的双重覆盖</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>C — Metronidazole therapy<br />
C — 甲硝唑治疗</td>
<td>Effective for Trichomonas vaginalis and bacterial vaginosis; no activity against N. gonorrhoeae or C. trachomatis<br />
对阴道毛滴虫和细菌性阴道病有效；对淋球菌和衣原体无活性</td>
<td>Trichomoniasis can cause male urethritis but is less common; this presentation fits gonorrhea/chlamydia pattern<br />
滴虫病可引起男性尿道炎但较少见；此题表现符合淋病/衣原体模式</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>D — Trimethoprim-sulfamethoxazole therapy<br />
D — 甲氧苄啶-磺胺甲噁唑治疗</td>
<td>First-line for non-STI UTI (E. coli cystitis); not effective against N. gonorrhoeae or C. trachomatis<br />
非STI性尿路感染（大肠杆菌膀胱炎）的一线药物；对淋球菌和衣原体无效</td>
<td>TMP-SMX targets gram-negative facultative anaerobes, not sexually transmitted obligate intracellular or fastidious organisms<br />
TMP-SMX针对革兰阴性兼性厌氧菌，而非性传播的专性胞内菌或苛养菌</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>E — No treatment until culture results known<br />
E — 等待培养结果后再治疗</td>
<td>Dangerous delay: STIs spread to partners during waiting period; requiring a return visit dramatically reduces compliance<br />
危险的延误：等待期间STI传播给性伴侣；要求患者回诊大幅降低依从性</td>
<td>Empiric same-day treatment is the standard of care for clinically suspected STI urethritis<br />
当日经验性治疗是临床疑似STI性尿道炎的标准治疗</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

*The most tempting distractor is E — waiting for cultures sounds "evidence-based," but in STI management, empiric same-day treatment is always preferred over delayed treatment to prevent partner transmission and maximize compliance.*

等待培养结果（选项E）看似"循证"最具迷惑性，但在STI管理中，当日经验性治疗始终优于延迟治疗，以防止传播给性伴侣并最大化依从性。

## 6. One-Sentence Summary & Memory Hook / 一句话总结 & 记忆钩

**Young sexually active male with dysuria, sterile pyuria, and urethral discharge → empiric ceftriaxone + azithromycin for dual coverage of gonorrhea and chlamydia without waiting for culture results.**

**年轻性活跃男性出现排尿困难、无菌性脓尿和尿道分泌物 → 无需等待培养结果，经验性头孢曲松 + 阿奇霉素双联覆盖淋球菌和衣原体。**

<colgroup>
<col style="width: 100%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><p><strong>Memory Hook — "GC + Chlamydia = Ceftri + Azithro" / 记忆钩 — "淋球菌 + 衣原体 = 头孢曲松 + 阿奇霉素":</strong></p>
<p>• <strong>G</strong>onorrhea → <strong>C</strong>eftriaxone (3rd-gen cephalosporin, IM, single dose) / 淋病 → 头孢曲松（三代头孢，肌注，单次）<br />
• <strong>C</strong>hlamydia → <strong>A</strong>zithromycin (macrolide, oral, single dose) / 衣原体 → 阿奇霉素（大环内酯类，口服，单次）<br />
• <strong>S</strong>terile pyuria → think <strong>S</strong>TI urethritis, not standard cystitis / 无菌性脓尿 → 想到STI性尿道炎，而非普通膀胱炎<br />
• <strong>E</strong>mpiric now, cultures confirm later — never delay for results / 立即经验性治疗，培养事后确认——绝不因等结果而延误</p></th>

## 7. High-Yield Topic Knowledge — Sexually Transmitted Urethritis in Men / 高频知识表 — 男性性传播性尿道炎

<col style="width: 50%" />

<th><strong>Topic</strong><br />
<strong>考点</strong></th>
<th><strong>Key Points</strong><br />
<strong>要点</strong></th>

<tbody>
<tr>
<td>Most common STI pathogens causing urethritis<br />
尿道炎最常见STI病原体</td>
<td>1. C. trachomatis (most common reportable STI in US overall); 2. N. gonorrhoeae; 3. T. vaginalis (less common in men)<br />
1. 沙眼衣原体（美国总体最常见法定报告STI）；2. 淋病奈瑟菌；3. 阴道毛滴虫（男性中较少见）</td>

<tr>
<td>NAAT (nucleic acid amplification test)<br />
核酸扩增检测</td>
<td>Gold standard for both C. trachomatis and N. gonorrhoeae; performed on first-catch urine or urethral swab; far more sensitive than culture<br />
沙眼衣原体和淋球菌的金标准检测；使用晨尿或尿道拭子；灵敏度远高于培养</td>

<tr>
<td>CDC 2021 treatment regimen<br />
CDC 2021治疗方案</td>
<td>Ceftriaxone 500 mg IM × 1 (1 g if weight ≥150 kg) + Azithromycin 1 g PO × 1; fluoroquinolone resistance is now widespread and these agents should not be used<br />
头孢曲松500 mg肌注单次（体重≥150 kg则1 g）+ 阿奇霉素1 g口服单次；氟喹诺酮类耐药已广泛，不应使用</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Complications of untreated chlamydia in men<br />
男性衣原体未治疗的并发症</td>
<td>Epididymitis, orchitis (→ infertility), reactive arthritis (Reiter syndrome triad: urethritis + arthritis + uveitis)<br />
附睾炎、睾丸炎（→不育）、反应性关节炎（Reiter综合征三联征：尿道炎+关节炎+葡萄膜炎）</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Complications in women if partner untreated<br />
性伴侣未治疗对女性的危害</td>
<td>PID (pelvic inflammatory disease) → ectopic pregnancy, infertility, chronic pelvic pain; Fitz-Hugh-Curtis syndrome (perihepatitis)<br />
盆腔炎 → 异位妊娠、不孕、慢性盆腔痛；Fitz-Hugh-Curtis综合征（肝周围炎）</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Disseminated gonococcal infection (DGI)<br />
播散性淋球菌感染</td>
<td>Classic triad: migratory polyarthritis + tenosynovitis + skin lesions (pustular/hemorrhagic); blood cultures often negative; treat with IV ceftriaxone<br />
经典三联征：移行性多关节炎 + 腱鞘炎 + 皮损（脓疱/出血性）；血培养常阴性；头孢曲松静注治疗</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Mandatory public health reporting<br />
强制公共卫生报告</td>
<td>Both gonorrhea and chlamydia are nationally notifiable diseases in the US; clinicians must report confirmed cases to local health authorities<br />
淋病和衣原体均是美国全国法定报告传染病；临床医生必须向地方卫生部门报告确诊病例</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

## 8. Extensions / 延伸扩展

- **Expedited Partner Therapy (EPT):** Clinicians can prescribe medications directly for the sexual partner without examination; reduces reinfection rates substantially and is legally permitted in most US states\
  **加速伴侣治疗（EPT）:** 临床医生可在无需检查的情况下直接为性伴侣开具处方药；显著降低再感染率，在美国大多数州合法

- **Azithromycin resistance trend:** Rising C. trachomatis resistance to azithromycin in some regions has led some experts to prefer doxycycline 100 mg BID × 7 days as the chlamydia component; check local guidelines\
  **阿奇霉素耐药趋势:** 部分地区衣原体对阿奇霉素耐药率上升，部分专家倾向多西环素100 mg每日2次共7天作为衣原体治疗组分；需参照当地指南

- **Differential for sterile pyuria beyond STI:** Renal tuberculosis, interstitial nephritis, urethral stricture, partially treated bacterial UTI, urolithiasis, polycystic kidney disease\
  **无菌性脓尿的STI之外鉴别:** 肾结核、间质性肾炎、尿道狭窄、部分治疗的细菌性UTI、尿路结石、多囊肾

- **Reiter syndrome mnemonic:** "Can't see, can't pee, can't climb a tree" = Uveitis + Urethritis + Arthritis; triggered by C. trachomatis (sexually acquired) or enteric pathogens (Salmonella, Shigella, Campylobacter, Yersinia)\
  **Reiter综合征记忆法:** "看不见、尿不出、上不了树" = 葡萄膜炎 + 尿道炎 + 关节炎；由衣原体（性传播）或肠道病原体（沙门菌、志贺菌、弯曲菌、耶尔森菌）触发

# Question 195 — Negative PPD Skin Test in Low-Risk Patient / PPD皮试阴性（低风险患者）

## Question Stem / 题干

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 100%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><p>A <strong>62-year-old woman</strong> comes to the physician for PPD skin testing prior to beginning <strong>volunteer work in a school</strong>. She has hypertension treated with hydrochlorothiazide and osteoarthritis treated with acetaminophen. She was <strong>born in the USA</strong>. She has had <strong>no sick contacts</strong>. She does not smoke cigarettes, drink alcohol, or use illicit drugs. Physical examination shows no abnormalities. A PPD skin test produces <strong>6 mm of induration</strong> at 48 hours. Results of <strong>liver function tests are within the reference ranges</strong>. A <strong>chest x-ray shows no abnormalities</strong>. Which of the following is the most appropriate next step in management?</p>
<p><strong>Q: Most appropriate next step in management?</strong></p>
<p>A) Provide clearance to begin volunteer work<br />
B) Repeat PPD skin testing to assess for booster phenomenon<br />
C) Obtain culture of three induced sputum samples for acid-fast bacilli<br />
D) Begin isoniazid and pyridoxine therapy<br />
E) Begin isoniazid, rifampin, pyrazinamide, and ethambutol therapy<br />
F) Begin isoniazid therapy only</p>
<p><strong>Correct Answer: A</strong></p></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
</tbody>
</table>

## 1. Key Stem Clues / 题干关键词抓考点

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 50%" />
<col style="width: 50%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Key Stem Clue</strong><br />
<strong>关键词</strong></th>
<th><strong>Why It Matters</strong><br />
<strong>为什么重要</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>Born in the USA, no sick contacts<br />
出生于美国，无病患接触史</td>
<td>No TB exposure risk factors → positive PPD threshold is &gt;15 mm<br />
无结核暴露危险因素 → PPD阳性阈值为&gt;15 mm</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>6 mm of induration at 48 hours<br />
48小时6 mm硬结</td>
<td>Falls below the 15 mm threshold for low-risk patients → negative test result<br />
低于低风险患者的15 mm阈值 → 检测结果为阴性</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>No immunosuppression (no steroids, HIV, or transplant mentioned)<br />
无免疫抑制（无激素、HIV或器官移植）</td>
<td>Not in the ≥5 mm positive group; intact cell-mediated immunity<br />
不属于≥5 mm阳性组；细胞免疫功能完整</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Normal chest x-ray<br />
胸片正常</td>
<td>No evidence of active pulmonary TB or prior calcified granuloma requiring follow-up<br />
无活动性肺结核或需要随访的既往钙化肉芽肿证据</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Normal liver function tests<br />
肝功能正常</td>
<td>Relevant only if INH treatment were indicated (hepatotoxicity monitoring); moot here since PPD is negative<br />
仅在需要INH治疗时相关（肝毒性监测）；PPD阴性时无意义</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Routine pre-work PPD screening<br />
入职前常规PPD筛查</td>
<td>No clinical suspicion of TB; this is a surveillance test, not a diagnostic workup<br />
无结核临床疑似；此为监测性检测，非诊断性检查</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

## 2. Mechanism / 机制理解

**PPD (Purified Protein Derivative)** skin testing exploits **Type IV (delayed-type) hypersensitivity** to detect prior sensitization to **Mycobacterium tuberculosis** antigens:

**PPD（纯蛋白衍生物）**皮试利用**IV型（迟发型）超敏反应**检测对**结核分枝杆菌**抗原的既往致敏状态：

- Tuberculin antigen is injected intradermally → previously sensitized CD4⁺ T cells recognize antigen → cytokine release → local induration at 48–72 h\
  结核菌素抗原皮内注射 → 既往致敏CD4⁺ T细胞识别抗原 → 细胞因子释放 → 48-72小时局部硬结形成

- Induration (firmness), not erythema (redness), is measured in millimeters perpendicular to the forearm axis\
  测量硬结（组织变硬），而非红斑（皮肤发红），单位毫米，垂直于前臂长轴

- False positives: prior BCG vaccination, non-tuberculous mycobacteria (NTM) cross-reactivity\
  假阳性：既往BCG接种、非结核分枝杆菌（NTM）交叉反应

- False negatives: anergy from immunosuppression, very recent infection (\<8 weeks), improper administration technique\
  假阴性：免疫抑制所致无反应性、极近期感染（\<8周）、操作技术不规范

**Risk-stratified threshold rule:** The CDC defines three cutoff values — 5 mm, 10 mm, and 15 mm — based on the patient's pre-test probability of TB infection.

**风险分层阈值原则:** CDC根据患者结核感染的预测概率设定三个阈值——5 mm、10 mm和15 mm。

## 3. Correct Answer (A) — Negative PPD in Low-Risk Patient / 正确答案 (A) — 低风险患者PPD阴性

**Negative PPD result** applies to any patient whose induration falls below the threshold appropriate for their risk category; no further workup or treatment is warranted:

**PPD阴性结果**适用于硬结低于其风险类别对应阈值的患者；无需进一步检查或治疗：

- This patient is low-risk: US-born, no sick contacts, not immunocompromised, no high-risk comorbidities (HIV, DM, silicosis, CRF)\
  该患者属低风险：出生于美国，无病患接触史，无免疫抑制，无高危合并症（HIV、糖尿病、硅肺、慢性肾衰）

- 6 mm \< 15 mm threshold → PPD is **negative** for this patient's risk category\
  6 mm \< 15 mm阈值 → 该患者风险类别下PPD结果为**阴性**

- Normal CXR and normal LFTs further confirm no active or latent TB requiring investigation or therapy\
  正常胸片和肝功能进一步证实无需调查或治疗的活动性或潜伏性结核

**Diagnosis:** A 6 mm induration is below the 15 mm threshold required for a positive PPD in a patient with no TB risk factors; this is a negative result and requires no further action.

**诊断:** 6 mm硬结低于无危险因素患者PPD阳性所需的15 mm阈值；结果为阴性，无需进一步处理。

**Treatment:** No treatment indicated; patient should receive clearance to begin volunteer work.

**治疗:** 无治疗指征；应给予患者开始志愿者工作的许可。

<colgroup>

<tr>
<th><strong>Option</strong><br />
<strong>选项</strong></th>
<th><strong>Why Wrong</strong><br />
<strong>为什么错</strong></th>
<th><strong>Key Discriminator</strong><br />
<strong>鉴别要点</strong></th>
</tr>

<tbody>
<tr>
<td>A — Provide clearance to begin volunteer work ✓<br />
A — 允许开始志愿者工作 ✓</td>
<td>CORRECT — 6 mm is below the 15 mm threshold for a low-risk, US-born patient with no TB risk factors<br />
正确——6 mm低于无危险因素、美国出生低风险患者的15 mm阈值</td>
<td>Threshold for no-risk patients is &gt;15 mm; 6 mm is unambiguously negative<br />
无危险因素患者阈值为&gt;15 mm；6 mm明确为阴性</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>B — Repeat PPD skin testing to assess for booster phenomenon<br />
B — 重复PPD皮试评估回忆现象</td>
<td>Two-step testing is for serial testing programs (healthcare workers, nursing home employees); NOT needed for a one-time routine screening of a low-risk individual<br />
两步法适用于系列检测项目（医疗工作者、养老院工作人员）；低风险个体常规一次性筛查不需要</td>
<td>Booster phenomenon prevents false-negatives on serial testing; irrelevant here since result is already negative<br />
回忆现象防止系列检测中假阴性；此处结果本已阴性，不相关</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>C — Obtain culture of three induced sputum samples for AFB<br />
C — 采集三份诱导痰培养AFB</td>
<td>Sputum AFB cultures are for diagnosing suspected active TB; this patient has a negative PPD, no TB symptoms, and a normal CXR<br />
痰AFB培养用于诊断疑似活动性结核；该患者PPD阴性、无结核症状、胸片正常</td>
<td>No positive PPD and no clinical suspicion of active TB → no indication for sputum workup<br />
无阳性PPD且无活动性结核临床疑似 → 无痰液检查指征</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>D — Begin isoniazid and pyridoxine therapy<br />
D — 开始异烟肼+吡哆醇治疗</td>
<td>INH + pyridoxine is the treatment for latent TB infection (LTBI); this patient does not have LTBI because her PPD is negative<br />
INH+吡哆醇是潜伏性结核感染（LTBI）的治疗方案；该患者PPD阴性，不存在LTBI</td>
<td>LTBI treatment requires a positive PPD in the first place; treating a negative result exposes patient to INH hepatotoxicity without benefit<br />
LTBI治疗首先需要阳性PPD；治疗阴性结果会使患者承担INH肝毒性风险而无获益</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>E — Begin isoniazid, rifampin, pyrazinamide, and ethambutol therapy<br />
E — 开始四联RIPE方案治疗</td>
<td>RIPE regimen is for active TB disease; this patient has no active TB symptoms, a normal CXR, and a negative PPD<br />
RIPE方案用于活动性结核病；该患者无活动性结核症状、胸片正常且PPD阴性</td>
<td>Active TB diagnosis requires clinical symptoms + CXR findings + culture/PCR confirmation; none present here<br />
活动性结核诊断需要临床症状+胸片异常+培养/PCR确认；本题均不存在</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>F — Begin isoniazid therapy only<br />
F — 仅开始异烟肼单药治疗</td>
<td>INH monotherapy is also for LTBI treatment; same reasoning as D — no positive PPD means no LTBI diagnosis, no treatment indicated<br />
INH单药治疗同样用于LTBI治疗；与D理由相同——无阳性PPD即无LTBI诊断，无治疗指征</td>
<td>Pyridoxine is added when peripheral neuropathy risk exists; but the foundational error here is treating a negative PPD at all<br />
存在周围神经病变风险时加用吡哆醇；但此处根本错误在于治疗阴性PPD结果</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

*The most tempting distractors are D and F — students may assume any induration (even 6 mm) triggers LTBI treatment, failing to apply risk-stratified thresholds.*

D和F最具迷惑性——学生可能认为任何硬结（即使6 mm）均需启动LTBI治疗，忽略了阳性判断须依据风险分层阈值。

## 6. One-Sentence Summary & Memory Hook / 一句话总结 & 记忆钩

**In a low-risk, US-born patient with no TB exposure, PPD induration must exceed 15 mm to be positive, making this patient's 6 mm result negative and requiring no further workup or treatment.**

**在无结核暴露的低风险、美国出生患者中，PPD硬结须超过15 mm方为阳性，因此本患者6 mm结果为阴性，无需进一步检查或治疗。**

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 100%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><p><strong>Memory Hook — The 5-10-15 PPD Ladder / 记忆钩 — PPD 5-10-15 阶梯法则:</strong></p>
<p>• <strong>5</strong> mm — <strong>S</strong>everely immunocompromised (HIV, organ transplant, steroids, recent close contact with active TB) / 严重免疫抑制（HIV、器官移植、激素治疗、与活动性结核患者近期密接）<br />
• <strong>10</strong> mm — <strong>H</strong>igh-risk populations (immigrants from endemic countries, IVDU, congregate settings, silicosis, DM, CRF) / 高危人群（流行国家移民、静脉吸毒、群居场所、硅肺、糖尿病、慢性肾衰）<br />
• <strong>15</strong> mm — <strong>N</strong>o risk factors (healthy, US-born adults undergoing routine screening — like this patient) / 无危险因素（健康、美国出生的常规筛查成人——如本题患者）</p></th>
</tr>
</thead>

</table>

## 7. High-Yield Topic Knowledge — Tuberculosis Screening & LTBI Management / 高频知识表 — 结核病筛查与潜伏性结核管理

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 50%" />
<col style="width: 50%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Topic</strong><br />
<strong>考点</strong></th>
<th><strong>Key Points</strong><br />
<strong>要点</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>PPD mechanism<br />
PPD原理</td>
<td>Type IV (delayed-type) hypersensitivity; CD4⁺ T-cell mediated; read at 48–72 hours; measure induration perpendicular to forearm, not erythema<br />
IV型（迟发型）超敏反应；CD4⁺ T细胞介导；48-72小时判读；垂直于前臂测量硬结，而非红斑</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>BCG vaccine and false positives<br />
BCG疫苗与假阳性</td>
<td>Prior BCG vaccination is a common cause of false-positive PPD; IGRA (QuantiFERON-TB Gold) is preferred in BCG-vaccinated patients as it is not affected by BCG or most NTM<br />
既往BCG接种是PPD假阳性的常见原因；BCG接种者首选IGRA（QuantiFERON-TB Gold），不受BCG或大多数NTM影响</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Two-step PPD (booster phenomenon)<br />
两步法PPD（回忆现象）</td>
<td>For serial testing programs (healthcare workers, nursing home staff); initial test may be negative in patients with remote exposure (faded immune memory), but the tuberculin exposure itself boosts memory, making the second test positive; not needed for one-time routine screening<br />
适用于系列检测项目（医疗工作者、养老院工作人员）；远期暴露患者（免疫记忆消退）初次检测可能阴性，但结核菌素暴露本身增强记忆记忆，使第二次检测阳性；常规一次性筛查不需要</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>LTBI treatment — 9-month INH<br />
LTBI治疗——9个月INH</td>
<td>9 months isoniazid (INH) standard; add pyridoxine (vitamin B6) for those at risk of peripheral neuropathy: alcoholics, malnourished, pregnant women, elderly; alternative: 3 months INH + rifapentine (3HP)<br />
9个月异烟肼（INH）为标准方案；对周围神经病变风险者（酗酒、营养不良、孕妇、老年人）加用吡哆醇（维生素B6）；替代方案：3个月INH+利福喷汀（3HP）</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Active TB treatment — RIPE<br />
活动性结核治疗——RIPE方案</td>
<td>Isoniazid + Rifampin + Pyrazinamide + Ethambutol × 2 months (intensive phase), then INH + RIF × 4 months (continuation phase); for active disease, not LTBI<br />
异烟肼+利福平+吡嗪酰胺+乙胺丁醇×2个月（强化期），然后INH+RIF×4个月（巩固期）；用于活动性结核病，非LTBI</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>INH key side effects<br />
INH主要副作用</td>
<td>Hepatotoxicity (monitor LFTs — already checked in this case), peripheral neuropathy (prevented by pyridoxine/B6), drug-induced lupus (anti-histone antibodies), sideroblastic anemia<br />
肝毒性（监测肝功能——本题已检查）、周围神经病变（吡哆醇/B6预防）、药物性狼疮（抗组蛋白抗体）、铁粒幼细胞性贫血</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Anergy and false-negative PPD<br />
无反应性与PPD假阴性</td>
<td>Severely immunocompromised patients (advanced HIV with CD4 &lt;200, severe malnutrition) may fail to mount a Type IV response → false-negative PPD even with true TB infection; IGRA may also be falsely negative in advanced HIV<br />
严重免疫抑制患者（晚期HIV CD4&lt;200、严重营养不良）可能无法产生IV型反应 → 即使真正感染结核也出现PPD假阴性；晚期HIV患者IGRA也可能假阴性</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

## 8. Extensions / 延伸扩展

- **School volunteer vs. healthcare worker threshold:** Volunteer work in a school does NOT lower the PPD threshold to 10 mm — school workers are not listed among the CDC congregate-setting high-risk groups (prisons, homeless shelters, nursing homes qualify; schools do not)\
  **学校志愿者与医疗工作者阈值区别:** 在学校做志愿者工作不会将PPD阈值降至10 mm——学校工作人员不在CDC群居场所高危群体之列（监狱、收容所、养老院属高危；学校不属于）

- **IGRA as PPD alternative:** QuantiFERON-TB Gold measures IFN-γ release from sensitized T-cells in vitro; preferred over PPD in BCG-vaccinated patients, repeat-testing programs, or when booster phenomenon would confound results\
  **IGRA作为PPD替代:** QuantiFERON-TB Gold体外测量致敏T细胞释放的IFN-γ；在BCG接种者、重复检测项目或回忆现象会干扰结果时优先于PPD选用

- **Pyridoxine rationale:** INH inhibits pyridoxine (vitamin B6) metabolism by competing for pyridoxal phosphate-dependent enzymes → B6-deficiency peripheral neuropathy; supplementation is prophylactic (given alongside INH), not therapeutic\
  **吡哆醇使用原理:** INH通过竞争磷酸吡哆醛依赖性酶来抑制吡哆醇（维生素B6）代谢 → B6缺乏性周围神经病变；补充吡哆醇是预防性的（与INH同时给予），而非治疗性的

- **Differential of positive PPD with negative CXR:** Consider LTBI (most common), prior BCG vaccination (false positive), prior successfully treated TB, NTM infection; IGRA can help distinguish BCG-related false positives\
  **PPD阳性而胸片阴性的鉴别:** 考虑LTBI（最常见）、既往BCG接种（假阳性）、既往成功治疗的结核、NTM感染；IGRA有助于区分BCG相关假阳性

# Question 196 — Valproic Acid-Induced Acute Pancreatitis / 丙戊酸诱发急性胰腺炎

## Question Stem / 题干

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 100%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><p>A <strong>42-year-old man</strong> comes to the emergency department because of a <strong>2-day history of nausea, vomiting, and malaise</strong>. He has <strong>bipolar disorder</strong>, herpes simplex virus 2, and chronic shoulder pain secondary to a torn rotator cuff injury sustained 7 years ago. His medications are <strong>valproic acid</strong>, sertraline, acyclovir, hydrocodone-acetaminophen, and docusate. <strong>He does not drink alcohol or use illicit drugs.</strong> His temperature is 37.2°C (99°F), pulse is <strong>102/min</strong>, and blood pressure is 122/84 mm Hg. Physical examination shows dry mucous membranes. Abdominal examination shows <strong>tenderness to palpation</strong>. On mental status examination, he has a dysphoric mood and congruent affect. Laboratory studies show: Leukocyte count 8000/mm³; Serum AST 38 U/L, ALT 52 U/L, <strong>Amylase 465 U/L</strong>. Which of the following medications is the most likely cause of this patient's current symptoms?</p>
<p><strong>Q: Which of the following medications is the most likely cause of this patient's current symptoms?</strong></p>
<p>A) Acyclovir<br />
B) Docusate<br />
C) Hydrocodone-acetaminophen<br />
D) Sertraline<br />
E) Valproic acid</p>
<p><strong>Correct Answer: E</strong></p></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
</tbody>
</table>

## 1. Key Stem Clues / 题干关键词抓考点

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 50%" />
<col style="width: 50%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Key Stem Clue</strong><br />
<strong>关键词</strong></th>
<th><strong>Why It Matters</strong><br />
<strong>为什么重要</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>Amylase 465 U/L (markedly elevated)<br />
淀粉酶 465 U/L（显著升高）</td>
<td>Defines acute pancreatitis; normal &lt; 130 U/L; this is the diagnostic anchor of the entire case<br />
确立急性胰腺炎诊断；正常值 &lt; 130 U/L；是本题的核心诊断依据</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Valproic acid in medication list<br />
药物列表中含丙戊酸</td>
<td>Idiosyncratic cause of drug-induced pancreatitis; mechanism involves reactive oxygen species-mediated endothelial damage<br />
丙戊酸是特异质性药物性胰腺炎的经典原因；机制涉及活性氧介导的内皮损伤</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>No alcohol use, no illicit drugs<br />
不饮酒、不使用违禁药物</td>
<td>Eliminates alcohol — the most common cause of pancreatitis in adults; directs reasoning toward drug etiology<br />
排除酒精——成人胰腺炎最常见原因；引导推理转向药物性病因</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>AST 38, ALT 52 (near normal)<br />
AST/ALT 接近正常</td>
<td>Argues against gallstone/biliary pancreatitis, where transaminases (especially ALT) are typically markedly elevated<br />
不支持胆源性胰腺炎（胆源性时转氨酶尤其是 ALT 通常显著升高）</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Abdominal tenderness + nausea/vomiting/malaise<br />
腹部压痛 + 恶心/呕吐/乏力</td>
<td>Classic clinical triad of acute pancreatitis presentation<br />
急性胰腺炎的经典临床三联症状</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Bipolar disorder diagnosis<br />
双相情感障碍诊断</td>
<td>Explains the indication for valproic acid; builds the diagnosis → indication → adverse effect logic chain<br />
解释使用丙戊酸的适应症；建立诊断 → 适应症 → 不良反应的完整逻辑链</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

## 2. Mechanism / 机制理解

**Valproic acid** causes **idiosyncratic pancreatitis** via a mechanism unrelated to dose or duration, possibly through **reactive oxygen species (ROS)-induced endothelial damage** within the pancreatic microvasculature:

**丙戊酸**通过与剂量或疗程无关的**特异质性**机制引发胰腺炎，可能通过**活性氧（ROS）诱导的胰腺微血管内皮损伤**发生：

- Valproic acid metabolites generate toxic free radicals → oxidative stress → pancreatic endothelial injury → local inflammation\
  丙戊酸代谢物产生有毒自由基 → 氧化应激 → 胰腺内皮损伤 → 局部炎症

- Pancreatic acinar cell activation → autodigestion cascades → amylase and lipase released into circulation\
  胰腺腺泡细胞激活 → 自身消化级联反应 → 淀粉酶和脂肪酶释放入血

- Idiosyncratic reaction: can occur at any dose, any duration — not predictable by therapeutic drug level monitoring\
  特异质性反应：可发生于任何剂量、任何疗程——血药浓度监测无法预测

- Discontinuation of valproic acid leads to resolution in most cases (self-limited course)\
  停用丙戊酸后大多数病例胰腺炎可自行缓解（自限性病程）

**Anatomic rule of thumb:** The pancreas lies retroperitoneally at L1–L2; classic pancreatitis pain radiates to the back, but early or drug-induced cases may present predominantly with anterior tenderness and systemic symptoms.

**解剖小窍门:** 胰腺位于腹膜后 L1–L2 水平；经典胰腺炎疼痛向背部放射，但早期或药物性病例可能主要表现为前腹压痛和全身症状。

## 3. Correct Answer (E) — Valproic Acid / 正确答案 (E) — 丙戊酸

**Valproic acid** is a mood stabilizer and antiepileptic agent whose idiosyncratic, dose-independent induction of acute pancreatitis is a rare but well-recognized adverse effect:

**丙戊酸**是一种心境稳定剂兼抗癫痫药，其特异质性、与剂量无关的急性胰腺炎诱发作用是罕见但公认的不良反应：

- Prescribed here for bipolar disorder (mood stabilization); also used in epilepsy and migraine prophylaxis\
  本例用于双相情感障碍的心境稳定；也用于癫痫和偏头痛预防

- Pancreatitis is idiosyncratic — not dose-related, unpredictable, can occur at any point during therapy\
  胰腺炎为特异质性——与剂量无关、不可预测、可在治疗任何时间点发生

- Other idiosyncratic VPA reactions: hepatotoxicity (especially in young children), bone marrow suppression, alopecia\
  其他特异质性丙戊酸反应：肝毒性（尤其幼儿）、骨髓抑制、脱发

**Diagnosis:** Acute pancreatitis (amylase 465 U/L, abdominal tenderness, nausea/vomiting) in the setting of valproic acid use with no alternative etiology (no alcohol, near-normal LFTs)

**诊断:** 使用丙戊酸背景下出现急性胰腺炎（淀粉酶 465 U/L、腹部压痛、恶心呕吐），无其他病因（不饮酒、转氨酶接近正常）

**Treatment:** Discontinue valproic acid; supportive care (IV fluids, bowel rest, analgesia); switch to an alternative mood stabilizer such as lithium or lamotrigine

**治疗:** 停用丙戊酸；支持治疗（静脉补液、禁食、镇痛）；换用其他心境稳定剂，如锂盐或拉莫三嗪

## 4. Options Elimination / 错误选项排除逻辑

<colgroup>
<col style="width: 33%" />
<col style="width: 33%" />

</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Option</strong><br />
<strong>选项</strong></th>
<th><strong>Why Wrong</strong><br />
<strong>为什么错</strong></th>
<th><strong>Key Discriminator</strong><br />
<strong>鉴别要点</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>A — Acyclovir<br />
A — 阿昔洛韦</td>
<td>Not associated with pancreatitis; adverse effects are nausea, vomiting, diarrhea, and nephrotoxicity (especially high-dose IV)<br />
不与胰腺炎相关；不良反应包括恶心、呕吐、腹泻及肾毒性（尤其高剂量静脉给药）</td>
<td>No known pancreatic toxicity; nephrotoxicity is the primary organ concern, not pancreatitis<br />
无已知胰腺毒性；肾毒性是主要器官顾虑，非胰腺炎</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>B — Docusate<br />
B — 多库酯（大便软化剂）</td>
<td>Stool softener with minimal systemic absorption; not associated with pancreatitis; adverse effects limited to diarrhea and GI discomfort<br />
大便软化剂，全身吸收极少；不与胰腺炎相关；不良反应仅限于腹泻和胃肠不适</td>
<td>Trivial side-effect profile; never implicated in drug-induced pancreatitis in clinical literature<br />
不良反应谱极轻微；临床文献中从未被列为药物性胰腺炎的病因</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>C — Hydrocodone-acetaminophen<br />
C — 氢可酮-对乙酰氨基酚</td>
<td>Not commonly associated with drug-induced pancreatitis; main concerns are acetaminophen hepatotoxicity, reduced GI motility, respiratory depression, and sedation<br />
通常不与药物性胰腺炎相关；主要顾虑是对乙酰氨基酚肝毒性、胃肠蠕动减慢、呼吸抑制和镇静</td>
<td>AST/ALT near normal argues against significant acetaminophen hepatotoxicity; opioids may cause Oddi sphincter spasm but rarely frank pancreatitis at this amylase level<br />
AST/ALT 接近正常不支持明显对乙酰氨基酚肝毒性；阿片类可引起 Oddi 括约肌痉挛但很少引起淀粉酶升至此水平的真性胰腺炎</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>D — Sertraline<br />
D — 舍曲林</td>
<td>SSRI not frequently associated with pancreatitis; main risk is serotonin syndrome (especially with drug interactions); generally well-tolerated<br />
SSRI 不常与胰腺炎相关；主要风险是5-羟色胺综合征（尤其药物相互作用时）；总体耐受性良好</td>
<td>No serotonin syndrome features (no hyperthermia, clonus, agitation); amylase elevation specifically indicates pancreatic, not serotonergic, pathology<br />
无5-羟色胺综合征特征（无高热、阵挛、激越）；淀粉酶升高特异性指向胰腺病变而非5-羟色胺毒性</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>E — Valproic acid ✓<br />
E — 丙戊酸 ✓</td>
<td>CORRECT — idiosyncratic drug-induced pancreatitis is a well-recognized rare adverse effect of valproic acid; resolves with drug discontinuation<br />
正确——特异质性药物性胰腺炎是丙戊酸的已知罕见不良反应；停药后可缓解</td>
<td>Markedly elevated amylase + no alcohol/gallstone etiology + valproic acid use = drug-induced pancreatitis until proven otherwise<br />
淀粉酶显著升高 + 无酒精/胆石病因 + 使用丙戊酸 = 首先考虑药物性胰腺炎</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

*The trickiest distractor is hydrocodone-acetaminophen (C): opioids can cause sphincter of Oddi spasm and mild amylase elevation, but frank pancreatitis is rare; moreover, the degree of amylase elevation here (465 U/L, more than 3× ULN) strongly favors true pancreatic inflammation rather than sphincteric obstruction.*

最具迷惑性的干扰项是氢可酮-对乙酰氨基酚（C）：阿片类可引起 Oddi 括约肌痉挛和轻度淀粉酶升高，但真正的胰腺炎罕见；此外，本题淀粉酶升高程度（465 U/L，超过正常上限 3 倍以上）强烈提示真性胰腺炎而非括约肌源性梗阻。

## 6. One-Sentence Summary & Memory Hook / 一句话总结 & 记忆钩

**Valproic acid causes idiosyncratic, dose-independent acute pancreatitis — when a patient on VPA presents with elevated amylase and no other etiology, stop the drug.**

**丙戊酸可引起与剂量无关的特异质性急性胰腺炎——当使用丙戊酸的患者出现淀粉酶升高且无其他病因时，应立即停药。**

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 100%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><p><strong>Memory Hook — VPA's "BHAM" Idiosyncratic Reactions / 记忆钩 — 丙戊酸特异质性不良反应 "BHAM":</strong></p>
<p>• <strong>B</strong>one marrow suppression — thrombocytopenia, neutropenia / 骨髓抑制——血小板减少、中性粒细胞减少<br />
• <strong>H</strong>epatotoxicity — fatal in children &lt; 2 years on polytherapy / 肝毒性——2岁以下多药联用儿童可致死<br />
• <strong>A</strong>lopecia — diffuse hair loss, partially dose-related / 脱发——弥漫性脱发，部分与剂量相关<br />
• <strong>M</strong>etabolic pancreatitis — idiosyncratic, self-limited, stop VPA / 代谢性胰腺炎——特异质性、自限性，停用丙戊酸</p></th>

## 7. High-Yield Topic Knowledge — Valproic Acid & Drug-Induced Pancreatitis / 高频知识表 — 丙戊酸与药物性胰腺炎

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 50%" />
<col style="width: 50%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Topic</strong><br />
<strong>考点</strong></th>
<th><strong>Key Points</strong><br />
<strong>要点</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>VPA mechanism of action<br />
丙戊酸作用机制</td>
<td>Increases GABA activity (inhibits GABA transaminase), blocks voltage-gated Na⁺ channels, inhibits T-type Ca²⁺ channels<br />
增加 GABA 活性（抑制 GABA 转氨酶）、阻断电压门控 Na⁺ 通道、抑制 T 型 Ca²⁺ 通道</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>VPA clinical indications<br />
丙戊酸临床适应症</td>
<td>Epilepsy (broad-spectrum, including absence), bipolar disorder (acute mania + maintenance), migraine prophylaxis<br />
癫痫（广谱，含失神发作）、双相情感障碍（急性躁狂 + 维持治疗）、偏头痛预防</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Acute pancreatitis diagnostic criteria<br />
急性胰腺炎诊断标准</td>
<td>Two of three: (1) typical epigastric pain, (2) amylase or lipase ≥ 3× ULN, (3) characteristic CT findings<br />
以下三项满足两项：（1）典型上腹痛，（2）淀粉酶或脂肪酶 ≥ 3 倍正常上限，（3）特征性 CT 表现</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Classic drugs causing pancreatitis<br />
经典药物性胰腺炎病因药物</td>
<td>Valproic acid, azathioprine/6-MP, didanosine (ddI), pentamidine, sulfonamides, furosemide, tetracyclines, estrogens<br />
丙戊酸、硫唑嘌呤/6-MP、去羟肌苷（ddI）、喷他脒、磺胺类、速尿、四环素类、雌激素</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>VPA hyperammonemic encephalopathy<br />
丙戊酸高氨血症性脑病</td>
<td>VPA inhibits carbamoyl phosphate synthetase I → impaired urea cycle → ammonia accumulation → encephalopathy; occurs without hepatotoxicity<br />
丙戊酸抑制氨甲酰磷酸合成酶 I → 尿素循环障碍 → 血氨积聚 → 脑病；可在无肝毒性情况下单独发生</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>VPA teratogenicity<br />
丙戊酸致畸性</td>
<td>Neural tube defects (spina bifida) — highest teratogenic risk among all antiepileptics; Category D; supplemental folic acid required<br />
神经管缺陷（脊柱裂）——所有抗癫痫药中致畸风险最高；妊娠 D 类；必须补充叶酸</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>VPA therapeutic monitoring<br />
丙戊酸治疗监测</td>
<td>Target level 50–100 mcg/mL (epilepsy); monitor LFTs + CBC at baseline and periodically; check ammonia if mental status changes<br />
目标血药浓度 50–100 mcg/mL（癫痫）；基线及定期监测肝功能 + 全血细胞计数；精神状态改变时检测血氨</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

## 8. Extensions / 延伸扩展

- **Differential of hyperamylasemia:** Not all elevated amylase equals pancreatitis — also consider salivary gland disease (mumps), macroamylasemia, bowel ischemia, renal failure; lipase is more specific for pancreatic pathology\
  **高淀粉酶血症鉴别诊断:** 淀粉酶升高并不等同于胰腺炎——还需考虑唾液腺疾病（腮腺炎）、巨淀粉酶血症、肠道缺血、肾衰竭；脂肪酶对胰腺病变特异性更高

- **Variant — VPA hepatotoxicity in children:** Valproic acid hepatotoxicity (distinct from pancreatitis) is most feared in children \< 2 years on polytherapy — presents as Reye-like syndrome with hyperammonemia, elevated LFTs, and fulminant liver failure\
  **题目变式——丙戊酸在幼儿中的肝毒性:** 丙戊酸肝毒性（有别于胰腺炎）在2岁以下多药联用幼儿中最为凶险——表现类似 Reye 综合征，伴高氨血症、转氨酶升高和暴发性肝衰竭

- **Key complication — Ranson's criteria:** Severe acute pancreatitis is predicted by Ranson criteria or BISAP score; complications include pseudocyst, infected necrosis, ARDS, renal failure, and hemorrhage\
  **关键并发症——Ranson 标准:** 重症急性胰腺炎可由 Ranson 标准或 BISAP 评分预测；并发症包括假性囊肿、感染性坏死、ARDS、肾衰竭和出血

- **Risk factor — VPA + other pancreatotoxic drugs:** Concurrent use of valproic acid with other pancreatotoxic agents (e.g., azathioprine in transplant patients) dramatically increases pancreatitis risk\
  **危险因素——丙戊酸与其他胰腺毒性药物联用:** 丙戊酸与其他胰腺毒性药物（如移植患者使用的硫唑嘌呤）联用可显著增加胰腺炎风险

# Question 197 — Depression in Parkinson Disease / 帕金森病合并抑郁症

## Question Stem / 题干

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 100%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><p>A <strong>72-year-old woman</strong> comes to the office with her son for a follow-up examination. She was diagnosed with <strong>Parkinson disease 8 years ago</strong>. She says her health has <strong>declined substantially during the past 6 months</strong>. She feels weaker and has had increasing difficulty walking. She has <strong>stopped attending weekly luncheons with her friends</strong>. The patient's son says his mother <strong>sleeps poorly at night and naps frequently during the day</strong>. He has to <strong>encourage her to eat</strong> and take her medications. The patient's medications are carbidopa-levodopa and donepezil. She <strong>appears sad and is tearful</strong> as she discusses her difficulties. Examination shows a <strong>mild resting tremor of the hands and mild bradykinesia</strong>. When asked to stand and walk from a seated position, she moves slowly and pushes on the arms of the chair with her hands; she takes steps with <strong>no hesitation</strong> but walks slowly. Which of the following is the most appropriate next step in pharmacotherapy?</p>
<p><strong>Q: Which of the following is the most appropriate next step in pharmacotherapy?</strong></p>
<p>A) Add mirtazapine to the medication regimen<br />
B) Add rasagiline to the medication regimen<br />
C) Add zolpidem to the medication regimen<br />
D) Increase the dosage of carbidopa-levodopa<br />
E) Increase the dosage of donepezil</p>
<p><strong>Correct Answer: A</strong></p></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
</tbody>
</table>

## 1. Key Stem Clues / 题干关键词抓考点

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 50%" />
<col style="width: 50%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Key Stem Clue</strong><br />
<strong>关键词</strong></th>
<th><strong>Why It Matters</strong><br />
<strong>为什么重要</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>Appears sad and is tearful<br />
表情悲伤、流泪</td>
<td>Core mood symptom of depression; distinguishes psychiatric decline from pure motor deterioration<br />
抑郁症的核心情绪表现；区分精神心理性衰退与纯运动功能恶化</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Stopped attending weekly luncheons<br />
不再参加每周午餐聚会</td>
<td>Social withdrawal / anhedonia — classic neurovegetative symptom of depression<br />
社交退缩/快感缺失——抑郁症的经典神经植物性症状</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Sleeps poorly at night, naps frequently during the day<br />
夜间睡眠差、白天频繁打盹</td>
<td>Sleep disturbance as a neurovegetative symptom of depression; also highlights mirtazapine's sedating advantage<br />
睡眠障碍是抑郁症的神经植物性症状；同时暗示米氮平镇静作用的适应性优势</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Needs encouragement to eat<br />
需要被劝说进食</td>
<td>Decreased appetite — another neurovegetative symptom; mirtazapine stimulates appetite via H₁/5-HT₂C blockade<br />
食欲下降——另一神经植物性症状；米氮平通过H₁/5-HT₂C阻断促进食欲</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Mild resting tremor, mild bradykinesia; no hesitation in steps<br />
轻度静止性震颤、轻度运动迟缓；步行无犹豫</td>
<td>Motor symptoms are mild and stable — functional decline is NOT driven by motor worsening<br />
运动症状轻微且稳定——功能下降并非源于运动恶化，指向心理因素</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Already on donepezil<br />
已在服用多奈哌齐</td>
<td>Suggests PD dementia already diagnosed and addressed; increasing its dose treats cognition, not depression<br />
提示PD痴呆已被诊断并处理；增加其剂量改善认知，不治疗抑郁</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Declined substantially over 6 months<br />
过去6个月内病情明显下降</td>
<td>Subacute timeline consistent with a treatable secondary complication, not expected gradual PD progression<br />
亚急性时间线与可治疗的继发并发症一致，而非预期的PD缓慢自然进展</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

## 2. Mechanism / 机制理解

**Depression in Parkinson disease** arises from **neurodegeneration beyond the nigrostriatal pathway**, involving **serotonergic, noradrenergic, and mesolimbic dopaminergic circuits**:

帕金森病合并抑郁源于**黑质纹状体通路以外的神经退行性变**，累及**5-羟色胺能、去甲肾上腺素能及中脑边缘多巴胺能回路**：

- Dopamine loss in the **mesolimbic system** (VTA → nucleus accumbens) → anhedonia, loss of motivation\
  **中脑边缘系统**（腹侧被盖区→伏隔核）多巴胺丢失 → 快感缺失、动力丧失

- Serotonin depletion from **raphe nuclei** projections → depressed mood, disrupted sleep architecture\
  **中缝核**投射纤维5-羟色胺耗竭 → 情绪低落、睡眠结构紊乱

- Norepinephrine loss in the **locus coeruleus** → fatigue, cognitive slowing, neurovegetative symptoms\
  **蓝斑**去甲肾上腺素丢失 → 疲劳、认知迟缓、植物神经症状

- Depression further **worsens motor function** by reducing motivation for movement, mimicking motor progression\
  抑郁通过降低运动动力进一步**恶化运动功能**，可貌似运动进展

**Anatomic rule of thumb:** PD involves three dopamine pathways — nigrostriatal (motor), mesolimbic (mood), mesocortical (cognition) — each requiring separate therapeutic attention.

**解剖小窍门:** PD累及三条多巴胺通路——黑质纹状体（运动）、中脑边缘（情绪）、中脑皮质（认知）——每条通路需单独针对性治疗。

## 3. Correct Answer (A) — Mirtazapine for Depression in Parkinson Disease / 正确答案 (A) — 米氮平治疗帕金森病抑郁

**Mirtazapine** is an atypical NaSSA antidepressant that blocks α₂-adrenergic autoreceptors/heteroreceptors to increase norepinephrine and serotonin release, with additional H₁ and 5-HT₂C blockade producing sedation and appetite stimulation:

**米氮平**是一种非典型NaSSA抗抑郁药，通过阻断α₂肾上腺素能自受体/异受体增加去甲肾上腺素和5-羟色胺释放，并通过H₁和5-HT₂C阻断产生镇静和促食欲作用：

- Treats **depression** through NaSSA mechanism — appropriate first-line for PD-associated depression\
  通过NaSSA机制治疗**抑郁** — 适合作为PD合并抑郁的一线药物

- **H₁ blockade** produces clinically useful sedation → directly addresses nighttime insomnia\
  **H₁阻断**产生有临床价值的镇静 → 直接改善夜间失眠

- **H₁/5-HT₂C blockade** stimulates appetite → addresses weight loss and poor oral intake\
  **H₁/5-HT₂C阻断**刺激食欲 → 改善体重减轻和进食减少

- Lower serotonin syndrome risk than SSRIs when combined with dopaminergic agents\
  与多巴胺能药物联用时，5-羟色胺综合征风险低于SSRI类药物

**Diagnosis:** This patient meets criteria for major depression superimposed on PD: depressed mood, anhedonia (social withdrawal), insomnia, anorexia, and psychomotor slowing beyond her mild baseline motor findings. The absence of step hesitation and preserved gait argue against primary motor progression.

**诊断:** 该患者符合PD基础上叠加重度抑郁的诊断：情绪低落、快感缺失（社交退缩）、失眠、食欲下降，以及超出其轻微基础运动症状的精神运动性迟滞。无步态犹豫、步行基本保留，反对运动恶化为主要原因。

**Treatment:** Add mirtazapine; SSRIs (sertraline, citalopram) are also acceptable. Avoid TCAs (high anticholinergic burden in elderly/dementia patients) and MAOIs (serotonin syndrome risk with serotonergic agents).

**治疗:** 加用米氮平；SSRI（舍曲林、西酞普兰）同样可接受。避免TCA类（老年/痴呆患者抗胆碱负担过重）和MAOI类（与5-羟色胺能药物合用有5-羟色胺综合征风险）。

<td>Motor exam shows only mild findings with no hesitation; the primary driver of decline is psychiatric, not motor<br />

E — 增加多奈哌齐剂量</td>

多奈哌齐是乙酰胆碱酯酶抑制剂，改善PD痴呆和阿尔茨海默病的认知功能；无抗抑郁作用</td>
<td>No new cognitive complaints are described; the core problem is mood, not cognition — cholinergic boost does not treat depression<br />
无新发认知投诉描述；核心问题是情绪而非认知——胆碱能增强不能治疗抑郁</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

*The most seductive distractor is D (increase carbidopa-levodopa) because worsening mobility is mentioned — but the key discriminating details are mild motor findings and absent gait hesitation, which redirect the diagnosis toward depression rather than motor progression.*

最容易误选的干扰项是D（增加左旋多巴剂量），因为题干提到行动能力下降——但关键鉴别细节是轻微的运动体征和无步态犹豫，这些细节将诊断引向抑郁而非运动恶化。

## 6. One-Sentence Summary & Memory Hook / 一句话总结 & 记忆钩

**In a Parkinson disease patient with depressed mood, social withdrawal, insomnia, and anorexia, add mirtazapine — the single agent that simultaneously lifts mood, restores sleep, and stimulates appetite.**

**帕金森病患者出现情绪低落、社交退缩、失眠和食欲下降时，加用米氮平——一种同时改善情绪、恢复睡眠和刺激食欲的单药方案。**

<tr>
<td>Antipsychotic use in PD<br />
PD中抗精神病药的使用</td>
<td>Most antipsychotics worsen PD motor symptoms via D₂ blockade; only quetiapine and clozapine are acceptable (low D₂ affinity); avoid haloperidol, risperidone, olanzapine<br />
大多数抗精神病药通过D₂阻断恶化PD运动症状；仅喹硫平和氯氮平可接受（低D₂亲和力）；避免氟哌啶醇、利培酮、奥氮平</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

## 8. Extensions / 延伸扩展

- **Differential of functional decline in PD:** Motor wearing-off (carbidopa-levodopa dose timing), depression, dementia progression, medication side effects, intercurrent illness — assess each before adjusting dopaminergic therapy\
  **PD功能下降的鉴别:** 运动"剂末现象"（卡比多巴-左旋多巴给药时机）、抑郁、痴呆进展、药物副作用、并发疾病——在调整多巴胺能治疗前逐一评估

- **Mirtazapine dose paradox:** Low doses (7.5 mg) are MORE sedating than high doses (30–45 mg) because H₁ blockade dominates at low doses, while the activating noradrenergic effect overwhelms sedation at higher doses\
  **米氮平剂量悖论:** 低剂量（7.5mg）比高剂量（30–45mg）**更具镇静作用**，因为低剂量时H₁阻断效应占主导，高剂量时激活性去甲肾上腺素能效应压过镇静效果

- **Key complication — Lewy body spectrum:** PD → PD dementia → Dementia with Lewy bodies form a continuum; pimavanserin (5-HT₂A inverse agonist) is FDA-approved for PD psychosis without worsening motor symptoms\
  **重要并发症——路易体谱系:** PD → PD痴呆 → 路易体痴呆形成连续谱；匹莫范色林（5-HT₂A反向激动剂）获FDA批准用于PD精神症状且不恶化运动症状

- **Nonpharmacologic adjuncts:** Aerobic exercise slows PD progression and independently improves depression; cognitive behavioral therapy (CBT) has evidence for PD-associated depression; caregiver psychoeducation reduces patient burden\
  **非药物辅助手段:** 有氧运动减缓PD进展并独立改善抑郁；认知行为治疗（CBT）对PD合并抑郁有证据支持；照护者心理教育减轻患者负担

# Question 198 — Bicornuate Uterus: Preterm Delivery Risk / 双角子宫：早产风险

## Question Stem / 题干

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 100%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><p>A <strong>32-year-old primigravid woman</strong> at <strong>10 weeks' gestation</strong> comes to the physician for her first prenatal visit. She conceived after <strong>in vitro fertilization</strong>. Three years ago, a <strong>bicornuate uterus</strong> was noted on diagnostic laparoscopy for <strong>primary infertility</strong>. She is otherwise healthy, and her only medication is a prenatal vitamin. She is 163 cm (5 ft 4 in) tall. She weighed 50 kg (110 lb) prior to her pregnancy; <strong>BMI was 19 kg/m²</strong>. She has had a 1-kg (2-lb) weight gain during her pregnancy. Her blood pressure is 110/70 mm Hg. Examination shows a uterus consistent in size with a 10-week gestation. This patient is at greatest risk for which of the following pregnancy complications?</p>
<p><strong>Q: Which pregnancy complication is this patient at greatest risk for?</strong></p>
<p>A) Abruptio placentae<br />
B) Placenta accreta<br />
C) Placenta previa<br />
D) Preterm delivery<br />
E) Uterine rupture</p>
<p><strong>Correct Answer: D</strong></p></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
</tbody>
</table>

## 1. Key Stem Clues / 题干关键词抓考点

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 50%" />
<col style="width: 50%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Key Stem Clue</strong><br />
<strong>关键词</strong></th>
<th><strong>Why It Matters</strong><br />
<strong>为什么重要</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>Bicornuate uterus on laparoscopy<br />
腹腔镜确认双角子宫</td>
<td>Congenital müllerian duct fusion failure → two separate horns → reduced cavity volume → preterm labor risk<br />
先天性苗勒管融合不全 → 两个宫角 → 宫腔容积减小 → 早产风险增加</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Primary infertility → IVF conception<br />
原发性不孕 → 试管婴儿受孕</td>
<td>Confirms structural uterine anomaly is clinically significant; bicornuate uterus limits implantation surface<br />
证实子宫结构异常具有临床意义；双角子宫限制胚胎着床面积</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Primigravida, no prior uterine surgery<br />
初产妇，无子宫手术史</td>
<td>Rules out uterine rupture and placenta accreta, which require prior myometrial scarring<br />
排除子宫破裂和胎盘植入——两者均需既往子宫肌层瘢痕</td>
</tr>

BMI 19（偏低正常）</td>
<td>Low BMI compounds preterm birth risk and fetal growth restriction<br />
低 BMI 叠加早产及胎儿生长受限风险</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>10 weeks' gestation, first prenatal visit<br />
妊娠 10 周，首次产检</td>
<td>Early risk identification allows serial cervical surveillance and progesterone planning<br />
早期识别风险便于宫颈系列监测和孕激素方案规划</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

## 2. Mechanism / 机制理解

A **bicornuate uterus** results from **incomplete fusion of the paramesonephric (müllerian) ducts** during embryogenesis, creating two partially or completely separate **uterine horns** with a diminished total endometrial cavity:

**双角子宫**源于胚胎期**副中肾管（苗勒管）融合不全**，形成两个部分或完全独立的**宫角**，导致子宫内膜总容积减小：

- Reduced cavity volume forces earlier uterine distension as the fetus grows → triggers myometrial stretch receptors → preterm contractions\
  宫腔容积减小使胎儿生长时子宫更早过度扩张 → 激活子宫肌层牵张感受器 → 引发早产宫缩

- Abnormal myometrial architecture from fusion defect impairs coordinated contractility\
  融合缺陷导致的子宫肌层结构异常损害收缩协调性

- Diminished implantation surface increases risk of ectopic implantation and recurrent pregnancy loss\
  着床面积减小增加异位种植和反复流产风险

- Abnormal cavity geometry forces fetal malpresentation (breech, transverse lie)\
  宫腔形态异常导致胎儿异常先露（臀位、横位）

**Anatomic rule of thumb:** Bicornuate = external fundal cleft ≥ 1 cm (seen on laparoscopy/3D US/MRI); Septate = smooth external fundus with internal fibromuscular ridge — critical distinction because hysteroscopic septoplasty improves outcomes in septate uterus but has no role in bicornuate uterus.

**解剖小窍门:** 双角子宫 = 宫底外部切迹 ≥ 1 cm（腹腔镜/三维超声/MRI 可见）；纵隔子宫 = 宫底外形光滑，内有纤维肌性嵴——关键区别：宫腔镜纵隔切除术可改善纵隔子宫预后，对双角子宫无适应证。

## 3. Correct Answer (D) — Preterm Delivery / 正确答案 (D) — 早产

**Preterm delivery** (\< 37 weeks' gestation) is the most well-established obstetric complication of bicornuate uterus, driven by reduced uterine cavity volume and altered myometrial architecture:

**早产**（妊娠 \< 37 周）是双角子宫最明确的产科并发症，由宫腔容积减小和子宫肌层结构改变共同驱动：

- Incidence of preterm delivery in bicornuate uterus: ~25–35%, compared to ~10% in the general obstetric population\
  双角子宫早产发生率约 25–35%，而普通产科人群约 10%

- Accompanying risks: fetal growth restriction (FGR), malpresentation (breech/transverse), recurrent miscarriage\
  伴随风险：胎儿生长受限（FGR）、异常先露（臀位/横位）、反复流产

- Cervical incompetence may coexist → serial cervical length surveillance is indicated\
  可合并宫颈机能不全 → 需进行宫颈长度系列监测

**Diagnosis:** Bicornuate uterus confirmed by laparoscopy or 3D ultrasound/MRI; preterm risk stratified by uterine horn dimension and residual cavity depth.

**诊断:** 双角子宫由腹腔镜或三维超声/MRI 确认；早产风险根据宫角尺寸和残余宫腔深度分层评估。

**Treatment:** Serial cervical length monitoring, vaginal progesterone if cervix shortens, cerclage if cervical insufficiency identified; planned cesarean for persistent malpresentation.

**治疗:** 定期宫颈长度监测，宫颈缩短时阴道孕酮，发现宫颈机能不全时宫颈环扎；持续异常先露时择期剖宫产。

## 4. Options Elimination / 错误选项排除逻辑

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 33%" />
<col style="width: 33%" />
<col style="width: 33%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Option</strong><br />
<strong>选项</strong></th>
<th><strong>Why Wrong</strong><br />
<strong>为什么错</strong></th>
<th><strong>Key Discriminator</strong><br />
<strong>鉴别要点</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>A — Abruptio placentae<br />
A — 胎盘早剥</td>
<td>Premature placental separation; risk factors are hypertension, cocaine, trauma, smoking, preeclampsia — NOT congenital uterine anomalies<br />
胎盘过早剥离；危险因素为高血压、可卡因、外伤、吸烟、子痫前期——与先天性子宫异常无关</td>
<td>Bicornuate uterus does not impair uteroplacental adherence<br />
双角子宫不影响子宫-胎盘黏附</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>B — Placenta accreta<br />
B — 胎盘植入</td>
<td>Abnormal placental invasion into myometrium; requires prior uterine scarring (cesarean, curettage, ablation) — NOT congenital structural anomaly<br />
胎盘异常侵入子宫肌层；需有既往子宫瘢痕（剖宫产、刮宫、消融）——与先天性结构异常无关</td>
<td>This primigravida has had no prior uterine surgery<br />
此初产妇无既往子宫手术史</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>C — Placenta previa<br />
C — 前置胎盘</td>
<td>Placenta overlies internal cervical os; associated with prior cesarean, multiparity, or low-implantation embryo transfer — not bicornuate uterus specifically<br />
胎盘覆盖宫颈内口；与既往剖宫产、多产或低位胚胎移植有关——与双角子宫无特定关联</td>
<td>No classic placenta previa risk factors present<br />
无前置胎盘经典危险因素</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>D — Preterm delivery ✓<br />
D — 早产 ✓</td>
<td>CORRECT — Bicornuate uterus reduces cavity volume and alters myometrial architecture, directly triggering premature uterine distension and contractions<br />
正确——双角子宫减小宫腔容积并改变子宫肌层结构，直接触发宫腔过早扩张和宫缩</td>
<td>Most robustly established complication of müllerian duct fusion anomalies<br />
苗勒管融合异常最有据可查的并发症</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>E — Uterine rupture<br />
E — 子宫破裂</td>
<td>Requires transmural myometrial scar (prior cesarean, myomectomy); bicornuate uterus is a fusion-shape defect, not a full-thickness wall weakness<br />
需要经全层子宫肌层瘢痕（剖宫产、肌瘤切除术）；双角子宫是融合形态缺陷，而非全层宫壁薄弱</td>
<td>Primigravida with no prior uterine surgery — no scar to rupture<br />
无子宫手术史的初产妇——无瘢痕可破裂</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

*The most seductive distractor is (E) Uterine rupture — test-takers conflate "abnormal uterus" with "weak uterine wall," but bicornuate uterus is a shape anomaly from a fusion defect, not a structural weakness of the myometrium; rupture requires a prior transmural scar.*

最容易混淆的干扰项是 (E) 子宫破裂——考生易将"子宫异常"等同于"宫壁薄弱"，但双角子宫是融合缺陷导致的形态异常，而非子宫肌层结构性薄弱；子宫破裂需要既往经全层肌层的瘢痕。
