## 6. One-Sentence Summary & Memory Hook / 一句话总结 & 记忆钩

**A bicornuate uterus, caused by incomplete müllerian duct fusion creating two reduced-volume horns, primarily increases the risk of preterm delivery — not rupture, accreta, or abruption, which each require specific prior uterine injury.**

**双角子宫因苗勒管融合不全形成两个容积减小的宫角，主要增加早产风险——而非子宫破裂、胎盘植入或早剥，后三者均需特定的既往子宫损伤。**

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 100%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><p><strong>Memory Hook — BICORN Obstetric Risks / 记忆钩 — BICORN 产科风险:</strong></p>
<p>• <strong>B</strong>reech &amp; malpresentation — abnormal cavity geometry forces abnormal fetal lie / 臀先露及异常先露——异常宫腔几何形态迫使胎位异常<br />
• <strong>I</strong>nfertility &amp; implantation failure — reduced endometrial surface area / 不孕与着床失败——子宫内膜面积减小<br />
• <strong>C</strong>ervical incompetence — may coexist; monitor cervical length serially / 宫颈机能不全——可能合并；需系列监测宫颈长度<br />
• <strong>O</strong>bstetric loss — recurrent miscarriage + fetal growth restriction / 产科丢失——反复流产 + 胎儿生长受限<br />
• <strong>R</strong>upture NOT increased — no transmural scar, shape defect only / 破裂风险不增加——无经全层瘢痕，仅为形态缺陷<br />
• <strong>N</strong>eonatal prematurity — preterm delivery is the #1 tested complication / 新生儿早产——早产是考频最高的并发症</p></th>
</tr>

## 7. High-Yield Topic Knowledge — Bicornuate Uterus & Müllerian Anomalies / 高频知识表 — 双角子宫与苗勒管异常

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 50%" />
<col style="width: 50%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Topic</strong><br />
<strong>考点</strong></th>
<th><strong>Key Points</strong><br />
<strong>要点</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>Embryology: müllerian duct development<br />
胚胎学：苗勒管发育</td>
<td>Paramesonephric (müllerian) ducts fuse medially → uterus, fallopian tubes, upper 2/3 vagina; failure at any point = spectrum of anomalies (AFS Class I–VII)<br />
副中肾管（苗勒管）向中线融合→子宫、输卵管、阴道上 2/3；任何阶段融合失败=系列异常（AFS I–VII 类）</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Bicornuate vs. septate: critical distinction<br />
双角子宫 vs. 纵隔子宫：关键鉴别</td>
<td>Bicornuate: external fundal indentation ≥ 1 cm → two true horns; Septate: smooth fundus, internal septum only → hysteroscopic resection is the treatment (NOT for bicornuate)<br />
双角子宫：宫底外部切迹 ≥ 1 cm → 两个真实宫角；纵隔子宫：宫底光滑，仅有内部纵隔 → 宫腔镜切除是治疗方法（不适用于双角子宫）</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Preterm delivery mechanism<br />
早产机制</td>
<td>Reduced cavity volume → early distension → myometrial stretch → premature contractions; coexistent cervical incompetence amplifies risk<br />
宫腔容积减小 → 早期扩张 → 子宫肌层牵张 → 早产宫缩；合并宫颈机能不全使风险叠加</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Placenta accreta risk factors<br />
胎盘植入危险因素</td>
<td>Prior cesarean section (risk increases with number: 1 CS = 0.3%, 3+ CS = 6.7%), placenta previa, prior D&amp;C, uterine ablation; congenital anomaly is NOT a risk factor<br />
既往剖宫产（风险随次数增加：1 次剖宫产 0.3%，3 次以上 6.7%）、前置胎盘、既往刮宫、子宫内膜消融；先天性异常不是危险因素</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Uterine rupture risk factors<br />
子宫破裂危险因素</td>
<td>Classical (vertical) uterine incision scar &gt;&gt; low transverse scar; prior myomectomy; obstructed labor; oxytocin over-stimulation; NOT congenital uterine shape anomaly<br />
古典式（纵切）子宫瘢痕 &gt;&gt; 低横切口瘢痕；既往肌瘤切除术；梗阻性难产；催产素过度刺激；先天性子宫形态异常不是危险因素</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Obstetric surveillance for bicornuate uterus<br />
双角子宫产科监测</td>
<td>Serial cervical length by transvaginal ultrasound every 2 weeks from 16–24 weeks; vaginal progesterone if CL &lt; 20 mm; cerclage if incompetent cervix; growth ultrasounds for FGR<br />
16–24 周每两周经阴道超声系列监测宫颈长度；宫颈长度 &lt; 20 mm 时阴道孕酮；宫颈机能不全时环扎；FGR 时生长超声监测</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

## 8. Extensions / 延伸扩展

- **Differential of müllerian anomalies by primary obstetric failure mode:** Septate uterus → highest rate of recurrent miscarriage (poor vascular supply within fibromuscular septum); Bicornuate → highest rate of preterm delivery; Unicornuate → highest rate of ectopic pregnancy (rudimentary horn)\
  **苗勒管异常的主要产科失败模式鉴别:** 纵隔子宫 → 反复流产率最高（纤维肌性纵隔血供差）；双角子宫 → 早产率最高；单角子宫 → 宫外孕率最高（残角子宫）

- **Variant — Uterus didelphys (Class III):** Complete non-fusion of both müllerian ducts → two entirely separate uteri, two cervices, often with longitudinal vaginal septum; paradoxically better live-birth rates than bicornuate due to each horn having near-normal individual volume\
  **题目变式——双子宫（III 类）:** 两侧苗勒管完全不融合 → 两个完全独立的子宫、两个宫颈，常伴阴道纵隔；由于每个宫腔接近正常容积，活产率反而优于双角子宫

- **Key complication at delivery if unrecognized:** Persistent breech or transverse lie → emergency cesarean; external cephalic version (ECV) has low success rate with bicornuate uterus due to structural constraint\
  **分娩时未识别的关键并发症:** 持续性臀位或横位 → 急诊剖宫产；双角子宫因结构限制导致外倒转术（ECV）成功率低

- **IVF in structural uterine anomalies:** Single embryo transfer preferred; if twin pregnancy occurs in bicornuate uterus, each embryo implanting in a separate horn (synchronous dichorionic-diamniotic twins in separate horns) carries extreme preterm risk and is a high-yield "surprise" exam scenario\
  **结构性子宫异常中的 IVF:** 优选单胚胎移植；若双角子宫发生双胎妊娠，每个胚胎分别着床于一侧宫角（同期双绒双羊双胎分居两角），早产风险极高，是高频考试"意外"场景

# Question 199 — Radial Nerve Palsy (Saturday Night Palsy) / 桡神经麻痹（周六夜麻痹）

## Question Stem / 题干

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 100%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><p>A <strong>22-year-old man</strong> with <strong>alcohol use disorder</strong> comes to the physician because of a <strong>3-week history of weakness in his right hand</strong>. His symptom <strong>began after drinking a bottle of whiskey</strong>. He has no history of serious illness and takes no medications. He <strong>drinks six cans of beer daily</strong>. On examination of the right upper extremity, muscle strength is <strong>2/5 in the supinator, wrist extensors, and finger extensors</strong>; <strong>strength is 5/5 in all other muscles</strong>. <strong>Sensation to pinprick is decreased over the dorsum of the right hand from the wrist to the base of the thumb and index finger</strong>. Which of the following is the most appropriate next step in diagnosis?</p>
<p><strong>Q: Most appropriate next step in diagnosis?</strong></p>
<p>A) Determination of erythrocyte sedimentation rate<br />
B) Electromyography and nerve conduction studies<br />
C) MRI of the brachial plexus<br />
D) MRI of the brain<br />
E) MRI of the cervical spine</p>
<p><strong>Correct Answer: B</strong></p></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
</tbody>
</table>

## 1. Key Stem Clues / 题干关键词抓考点

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 50%" />
<col style="width: 50%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Key Stem Clue</strong><br />
<strong>关键词</strong></th>
<th><strong>Why It Matters</strong><br />
<strong>为什么重要</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>Alcohol use disorder + symptom began after drinking a bottle of whiskey<br />
酒精使用障碍 + 大量饮酒后起病</td>
<td>Acute intoxication → unconscious prolonged arm compression = classic "Saturday night palsy" mechanism<br />
急性醉酒 → 无意识状态下手臂长时间受压 = 经典"周六夜麻痹"机制</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>2/5 strength in supinator, wrist extensors, and finger extensors<br />
旋后肌、腕伸肌、指伸肌肌力 2/5</td>
<td>This triad localizes injury to the radial nerve at or distal to the spiral groove; triceps-sparing confirms level<br />
此三组肌肉无力将损伤定位于桡神经螺旋沟处或其远端；肱三头肌保留确认病变平面</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Strength 5/5 in all other muscles<br />
所有其他肌群肌力均为 5/5</td>
<td>Focal mononeuropathy, not plexopathy or central lesion; isolated radial nerve territory<br />
局灶性单神经病变，而非臂丛病或中枢病变；选择性累及桡神经支配区</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Sensation decreased over dorsum of hand, wrist to base of thumb and index finger<br />
手背（腕至拇指、示指根部）针刺觉减退</td>
<td>Matches superficial radial nerve distribution; confirms peripheral (not central, not root) origin<br />
符合桡神经浅支感觉分布区；确认为外周神经（非中枢、非神经根）病变</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Triceps strength intact (5/5 in all other muscles)<br />
肱三头肌肌力正常（其他肌群均 5/5）</td>
<td>Triceps branch exits proximal to spiral groove → localizes lesion to spiral groove, not axilla<br />
肱三头肌支从螺旋沟近端发出 → 病变定位于螺旋沟，而非腋部</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>3-week subacute onset, no prior serious illness<br />
3 周亚急性起病，无严重疾病史</td>
<td>Excludes acute stroke (hyperacute); subacute peripheral mononeuropathy → EMG/NCS is next step<br />
排除急性脑卒中（超急性起病）；亚急性外周单神经病 → EMG/NCS 是合适的下一步</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

## 2. Mechanism / 机制理解

The **radial nerve** arises from the **posterior cord** of the brachial plexus (C5–T1) and spirals around the **spiral groove** of the humerus before dividing into the superficial sensory branch and the **posterior interosseous nerve** (deep motor branch)：

**桡神经**起源于**臂丛后束**（C5–T1），绕行于肱骨**螺旋沟**，随后分为浅支（感觉支）和**骨间后神经**（深支，运动支）：

- Triceps innervation exits proximal to the spiral groove → triceps spared in spiral groove compression; brachioradialis, supinator, wrist/finger extensors are all affected\
  肱三头肌支从螺旋沟近端发出 → 螺旋沟压迫时肱三头肌保留；肱桡肌、旋后肌、腕伸肌/指伸肌均受累

- In Saturday night palsy, the patient falls asleep drunk with the arm draped over a chair back or hard edge, compressing the nerve against the humeral shaft for hours\
  周六夜麻痹中，患者醉酒后手臂悬搭在椅背或硬物上入睡，桡神经被长时间压迫于肱骨干数小时

- The superficial radial nerve (sensory only) carries sensation from the dorsum of the hand and lateral 3½ digits; loss here confirms nerve involvement distal to the motor branch bifurcation\
  桡神经浅支（纯感觉）传导手背及外侧 3½ 指的感觉；此处感觉缺失确认神经损伤在运动支分叉远端

**Anatomic rule of thumb:** Triceps intact + wrist drop = spiral groove; triceps weak + wrist drop = axillary or posterior cord injury.

**解剖小窍门:** 肱三头肌正常 + 腕下垂 = 螺旋沟损伤；肱三头肌无力 + 腕下垂 = 腋部或臂丛后束损伤。

## 3. Correct Answer (B) — Electromyography and Nerve Conduction Studies / 正确答案 (B) — 肌电图与神经传导检查

**Electromyography (EMG) and nerve conduction studies (NCS)** are the gold standard for confirming peripheral nerve injury, localizing the lesion along the nerve, and characterizing its type (axonal vs. demyelinating)：

**肌电图（EMG）和神经传导检查（NCS）**是确诊外周神经损伤、定位病变并判断损伤类型（轴索性 vs. 脱髓鞘性）的金标准：

- NCS measures conduction velocity and amplitude; a conduction block or slowing at the spiral groove level localizes the lesion precisely\
  NCS 测量传导速度和波幅；螺旋沟水平的传导阻滞或减慢可精确定位病变

- EMG detects denervation potentials (fibrillations, positive sharp waves) in affected muscles, appearing 2–3 weeks after injury — exactly the timeline here\
  EMG 检测受累肌肉中的去神经电位（纤颤波、正锐波），损伤后 2–3 周出现——与本题病程吻合

- Together EMG/NCS distinguishes radial nerve compressive mononeuropathy from plexopathy, radiculopathy, or inflammatory myopathy\
  EMG/NCS 联合可将桡神经压迫性单神经病与臂丛病、神经根病或炎症性肌病区分开来

**Diagnosis:** Wrist drop + supinator/finger extensor weakness + dorsal hand sensory loss + heavy alcohol use/compression history → radial nerve palsy at spiral groove; EMG/NCS confirms and grades severity.

**诊断:** 腕下垂 + 旋后肌/指伸肌无力 + 手背感觉缺失 + 大量饮酒/压迫病史 → 螺旋沟处桡神经麻痹；EMG/NCS 确诊并评估严重程度。

**Treatment:** Compressive neuropathies typically resolve spontaneously over weeks to months; cock-up wrist splint + physical therapy; repeat EMG/NCS at 4–6 weeks to assess reinnervation and guide prognosis.

**治疗:** 压迫性神经病通常在数周至数月内自发恢复；腕托固定 + 物理治疗；4–6 周复查 EMG/NCS 评估神经再支配情况并判断预后。

## 4. Options Elimination / 错误选项排除逻辑

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 33%" />
<col style="width: 33%" />
<col style="width: 33%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Option</strong><br />
<strong>选项</strong></th>
<th><strong>Why Wrong</strong><br />
<strong>为什么错</strong></th>
<th><strong>Key Discriminator</strong><br />
<strong>鉴别要点</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>A — Determination of erythrocyte sedimentation rate<br />
A — 红细胞沉降率检测</td>
<td>ESR is a nonspecific inflammatory marker; useful for myositis/polymyositis but this patient has a focal peripheral nerve deficit, not diffuse inflammatory myopathy<br />
ESR 是非特异性炎症标志物；适用于肌炎/多发性肌炎，但本患者为局灶性外周神经损伤，而非弥漫性炎症性肌病</td>
<td>Focal mononeuropathy does not raise ESR; extensor-selective weakness pattern rules out myopathy<br />
局灶性单神经病不升高 ESR；选择性伸肌无力模式可排除肌病</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>B — Electromyography and nerve conduction studies ✓<br />
B — 肌电图与神经传导检查 ✓</td>
<td>CORRECT — Gold standard for confirming radial nerve palsy, localizing the lesion to the spiral groove, and characterizing injury type to guide prognosis<br />
正确——确诊桡神经麻痹、将病变定位于螺旋沟并判断损伤类型以指导预后的金标准</td>
<td>EMG/NCS directly evaluates peripheral nerve integrity and identifies axonal vs. demyelinating pathology<br />
EMG/NCS 直接评估外周神经完整性，鉴别轴索性与脱髓鞘性病变</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>C — MRI of the brachial plexus<br />
C — 臂丛 MRI</td>
<td>Brachial plexus injury causes multi-nerve deficits (radial + axillary + musculocutaneous), not isolated mononeuropathy; this patient has a single nerve distribution<br />
臂丛损伤引起多神经受累（桡神经 + 腋神经 + 肌皮神经），而非孤立性单神经病；本患者损伤局限于单一神经分布区</td>
<td>Mononeuropathy (one nerve territory) vs. plexopathy (multiple nerve territories); isolated radial distribution excludes plexus<br />
单神经病（一条神经分布区）vs. 臂丛病（多条神经分布区）；孤立桡神经分布区排除臂丛病变</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>D — MRI of the brain<br />
D — 脑部 MRI</td>
<td>Brain MRI is for acute ischemic stroke; stroke causes UMN signs (hyperreflexia, spasticity), contralateral face/leg involvement — none present here<br />
脑 MRI 用于急性缺血性脑卒中；脑卒中出现上运动神经元体征（反射亢进、痉挛状态）、对侧面/腿部受累——本例均无</td>
<td>Peripheral nerve findings (flaccid weakness, dermatomal sensory loss, no hyperreflexia) exclude central lesion<br />
外周神经体征（弛缓性无力、感觉缺失局限于神经分布区、无反射亢进）排除中枢性病变</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>E — MRI of the cervical spine<br />
E — 颈椎 MRI</td>
<td>Cervical radiculopathy (C7 most similar) affects triceps as well and follows dermatomal, not peripheral nerve, sensory distribution; no UMN signs here<br />
颈神经根病（C7 最相似）同样累及肱三头肌，感觉缺失沿皮节而非外周神经分布；本例无上运动神经元体征</td>
<td>Radial nerve sensory territory ≠ C7 dermatome; spared triceps + peripheral nerve sensory pattern localizes to spiral groove, not root<br />
桡神经感觉区 ≠ C7 皮节；肱三头肌保留 + 外周神经感觉模式将病变定位于螺旋沟，而非神经根</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

*The most tempting distractor is Choice C (MRI of brachial plexus) — test-takers who recognize radial nerve involvement but overestimate the lesion level may reach for plexus imaging; the critical insight is that a strict mononeuropathy is too focal for a plexus lesion, which would also involve the axillary and musculocutaneous nerves.*

最易误选的干扰项是 C（臂丛 MRI）——考生识别到桡神经受累但高估病变范围时可能选择臂丛影像；关键在于严格单神经病对臂丛病变而言过于局限，臂丛损伤还会累及腋神经和肌皮神经。

## 6. One-Sentence Summary & Memory Hook / 一句话总结 & 记忆钩

**A patient with alcohol use disorder who wakes up with wrist drop, finger extensor weakness, and dorsal hand sensory loss has Saturday night palsy from radial nerve compression at the spiral groove, diagnosed by EMG and nerve conduction studies.**

**酒精使用障碍患者醒来后出现腕下垂、指伸肌无力和手背感觉缺失，为螺旋沟处桡神经压迫所致的"周六夜麻痹"，通过肌电图和神经传导检查确诊。**

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 100%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><p><strong>Memory Hook — SPIRAL for Radial Nerve Palsy / 记忆钩 — SPIRAL 记桡神经麻痹:</strong></p>
<p>• <strong>S</strong>piral groove = site of compression — / 螺旋沟 = 压迫部位<br />
• <strong>P</strong>reservation of triceps (branch exits proximal) — / 肱三头肌保留（支从近端发出）<br />
• <strong>I</strong>ntoxication → prolonged unconscious compression — "Saturday night palsy" / 醉酒 → 长时间无意识压迫——"周六夜麻痹"<br />
• <strong>R</strong>adial nerve: wrist drop + finger drop + dorsal hand numbness — / 桡神经：腕下垂 + 指下垂 + 手背麻木<br />
• <strong>A</strong>xonal vs. demyelinating: EMG/NCS distinguishes and predicts recovery — / 轴索性 vs. 脱髓鞘性：EMG/NCS 鉴别并预测恢复</p></th>
</tr>

## 7. High-Yield Topic Knowledge — Radial Nerve Anatomy, Injuries, and Diagnosis / 高频知识表 — 桡神经解剖、损伤与诊断

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 50%" />
<col style="width: 50%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Topic</strong><br />
<strong>考点</strong></th>
<th><strong>Key Points</strong><br />
<strong>要点</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>Radial nerve origin and course<br />
桡神经起源与走行</td>
<td>Posterior cord of brachial plexus (C5–T1); winds around spiral groove of humerus; divides into superficial (sensory) and posterior interosseous nerve (deep motor) at lateral epicondyle<br />
臂丛后束（C5–T1）；绕行于肱骨螺旋沟；在外上髁处分为浅支（感觉）和骨间后神经（深部运动支）</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Spiral groove injury — motor deficits<br />
螺旋沟损伤——运动缺陷</td>
<td>Triceps spared; brachioradialis + supinator + wrist extensors + finger extensors all weak → classic "wrist drop" and "finger drop"<br />
肱三头肌保留；肱桡肌 + 旋后肌 + 腕伸肌 + 指伸肌均无力 → 经典"腕下垂"和"指下垂"</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Spiral groove injury — sensory deficits<br />
螺旋沟损伤——感觉缺陷</td>
<td>Loss over dorsum of hand (anatomical snuffbox + base of thumb, index, middle fingers); posterior forearm sensation often preserved (branch exits proximal to groove)<br />
手背（鼻烟壶区 + 拇指、示指、中指根部）感觉缺失；前臂背侧感觉通常保留（支从螺旋沟近端发出）</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Posterior interosseous nerve (PIN) palsy<br />
骨间后神经（PIN）麻痹</td>
<td>Pure motor deficit; NO sensory loss; wrist drop with radial deviation (ECRL intact); caused by radial head fracture, radial tunnel syndrome, or supinator arcade compression<br />
纯运动损伤；无感觉缺失；腕下垂伴桡偏（桡侧腕长伸肌完好）；由桡骨头骨折、桡管综合征或旋后肌弓压迫引起</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>EMG/NCS findings in radial nerve palsy<br />
桡神经麻痹的 EMG/NCS 表现</td>
<td>NCS: reduced CMAP amplitude (axonal injury) or prolonged latency/conduction block (demyelinating); EMG: fibrillations + PSWs in affected muscles at 2–3 weeks; predicts prognosis and recovery timeline<br />
NCS：复合肌肉动作电位波幅降低（轴索损伤）或潜伏期延长/传导阻滞（脱髓鞘）；EMG：2–3 周后受累肌肉出现纤颤波 + 正锐波；预测预后和恢复时间</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Common causes of radial nerve palsy<br />
桡神经麻痹的常见病因</td>
<td>Saturday night palsy (compression in spiral groove during intoxication); midshaft humerus fracture; crutch palsy (axillary compression, also affects triceps); Monteggia fracture (PIN injury)<br />
"周六夜麻痹"（醉酒时螺旋沟压迫）；肱骨干中段骨折；腋杖麻痹（腋部压迫，同时累及肱三头肌）；Monteggia 骨折（PIN 损伤）</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Management of Saturday night palsy<br />
"周六夜麻痹"的处理</td>
<td>Conservative: wrist cock-up splint (30° extension) + physical therapy; most recover in 6–8 weeks; EMG/NCS at 4–6 weeks to confirm reinnervation; surgery only if no improvement at 3–6 months<br />
保守治疗：腕背伸 30° 夹板固定 + 物理治疗；大多数在 6–8 周恢复；4–6 周 EMG/NCS 确认神经再支配；3–6 个月无改善才考虑手术</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

## 8. Extensions / 延伸扩展

- **Differential of wrist drop:** Radial nerve palsy at spiral groove (triceps spared, sensory loss), posterior interosseous nerve palsy (no sensory loss, radial deviation), C7 radiculopathy (triceps also weak, dermatomal sensory loss), central lesion (UMN signs)\
  **腕下垂鉴别:** 螺旋沟处桡神经麻痹（肱三头肌保留，有感觉缺失）、骨间后神经麻痹（无感觉缺失，腕桡偏）、C7 神经根病（肱三头肌同样无力，皮节感觉缺失）、中枢性病变（上运动神经元体征）

- **Variant — Crutch palsy:** Axillary compression (proximal to spiral groove) causes same wrist/finger drop but additionally weakens triceps; distinguishes from Saturday night palsy by triceps involvement\
  **题目变式——腋杖麻痹:** 腋部压迫（螺旋沟近端）引起相同的腕/指下垂，但同时累及肱三头肌；通过肱三头肌受累可与"周六夜麻痹"区分

- **Key complication:** Untreated wrist drop → flexor contracture of wrist and fingers; early splinting in functional position prevents this while awaiting nerve recovery\
  **关键并发症:** 未处理的腕下垂 → 腕和手指屈曲挛缩；在等待神经恢复期间早期功能位夹板固定可预防此并发症

- **Cause of sensory-only radial nerve injury:** Superficial radial nerve entrapment (Wartenberg syndrome) — sensory loss over dorsal thumb/index only, no motor deficit; caused by tight watch band or handcuffs ("handcuff neuropathy")\
  **纯感觉性桡神经损伤的原因:** 桡神经浅支卡压（Wartenberg 综合征）——仅拇指/示指背侧感觉缺失，无运动损伤；由紧手表带或手铐引起（"手铐神经病"）

# Question 200 — Postpartum Endometritis / 产后子宫内膜炎

## Question Stem / 题干

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 100%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><p>One day after delivery of a <strong>healthy newborn at term</strong>, a <strong>22-year-old woman</strong>, gravida 2, para 2, has <strong>fever</strong>. Pregnancy and delivery were uncomplicated. Her temperature is <strong>39.4°C (103°F)</strong>, pulse is <strong>110/min</strong>, respirations are 22/min, and blood pressure is 125/70 mm Hg. Examination shows <strong>normal lochia rubra</strong>. The <strong>uterus is tender</strong>, and the fundus extends to the umbilicus. Her <strong>leukocyte count is 17,000/mm³ with a shift to the left</strong>. While awaiting results of additional laboratory studies, which of the following is the most likely causal organism?</p>
<p><strong>Q: Most likely causal organism?</strong></p>
<p>A) Candida albicans<br />
B) Escherichia coli<br />
C) Mycoplasma pneumoniae<br />
D) Staphylococcus aureus<br />
E) Staphylococcus epidermidis</p>
<p><strong>Correct Answer: B</strong></p></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
</tbody>
</table>

## 1. Key Stem Clues / 题干关键词抓考点

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 50%" />
<col style="width: 50%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Key Stem Clue</strong><br />
<strong>关键词</strong></th>
<th><strong>Why It Matters</strong><br />
<strong>为什么重要</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>1 day postpartum, term delivery<br />
产后第1天，足月分娩</td>
<td>Temporal clue narrows differential to puerperal causes; postpartum fever within first few days points to endometritis<br />
时间线缩小鉴别诊断范围；产后数日内发热首先考虑子宫内膜炎</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Temperature 39.4°C, pulse 110/min<br />
体温39.4°C，心率110/min</td>
<td>Fever ≥38.0°C on 2+ days (excluding day 1) = puerperal fever definition; tachycardia suggests systemic infection<br />
产褥期发热定义：产后除第1天外连续2天体温≥38.0°C；心动过速提示全身性感染</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Uterine tenderness<br />
子宫压痛</td>
<td>Hallmark physical finding of endometritis; inflamed endometrium causes direct uterine tenderness on palpation<br />
子宫内膜炎的标志性体征；炎症子宫内膜触诊时有直接压痛</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Normal lochia rubra<br />
正常血性恶露</td>
<td>Rules out retained products of conception or abnormal discharge; endometritis can present with normal or mucopurulent lochia<br />
排除胎盘残留；子宫内膜炎可表现为正常或脓性恶露</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>WBC 17,000/mm³ with left shift<br />
白细胞17,000伴核左移</td>
<td>Leukocytosis with left shift = bacterial infection with increased immature neutrophil release; supports bacterial etiology<br />
白细胞增多伴核左移=细菌感染伴幼稚中性粒细胞增多；支持细菌性病因</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Uncomplicated vaginal delivery<br />
无并发症阴道分娩</td>
<td>Provides context; even without C-section, ascending vaginal flora can seed the endometrium during labor<br />
提供背景；即使阴道分娩，产程中阴道菌群上行也可播种子宫内膜</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

## 2. Mechanism / 机制理解

**Postpartum endometritis** arises from **ascending polymicrobial contamination** of the uterine cavity during labor and delivery, with **gram-negative enteric organisms** like *E. coli* being the most commonly isolated pathogens:

**产后子宫内膜炎**由分娩过程中**多种微生物上行污染**子宫腔引起，**革兰阴性肠道菌**（如大肠杆菌）是最常分离出的病原体：

- After delivery, the **denuded endometrial surface** and the placental implantation site become vulnerable to bacterial colonization\
  分娩后，**裸露的子宫内膜表面**和胎盘附着部位易受细菌定植

- **E. coli** and other Enterobacteriaceae ascend from the lower genital tract (vagina/cervix), where they normally reside as part of the perineal/GI flora\
  **大肠杆菌**等肠杆菌科细菌从下生殖道（阴道/宫颈）上行，它们本就作为会阴/肠道菌群的一部分定植于此

- The infection triggers an **inflammatory cascade**: cytokine release → fever, uterine edema → fundal tenderness, bone marrow stimulation → leukocytosis with left shift\
  感染触发**炎症级联**：细胞因子释放→发热，子宫水肿→宫底压痛，骨髓刺激→白细胞增多伴核左移

- Endometritis is **polymicrobial** overall, but single-organism cultures most often grow *E. coli*, *Enterococcus*, *Enterobacter*, *Bacteroides*, or *Clostridium*\
  子宫内膜炎总体上是**多菌性的**，但单菌培养最常见大肠杆菌、肠球菌、阴沟肠杆菌、拟杆菌或梭菌

**Pathophysiology pearl:** The uterine fundus size (at umbilicus on day 1) is normal postpartum involution; tenderness at that site is the key abnormal finding.

**病理生理要点:** 宫底位于脐部（产后第1天）属正常复旧；该部位的压痛才是关键异常体征。

## 3. Correct Answer (B) — Escherichia coli / 正确答案 (B) — 大肠杆菌

**Escherichia coli** is the most common gram-negative organism isolated in postpartum endometritis and the most likely single pathogen when cultures are performed:

**大肠杆菌**是产后子宫内膜炎中最常分离出的革兰阴性菌，也是培养时最可能的单一病原体：

- Normally colonizes the **perineum and lower GI tract**, providing a reservoir for ascending infection during delivery\
  正常定植于**会阴和下消化道**，在分娩期间为上行感染提供来源

- Causes **endotoxin-mediated** fever, uterine inflammation, and can progress to **bacteremia and sepsis** if untreated\
  引起**内毒素介导的**发热、子宫炎症，若未治疗可进展为**菌血症和脓毒症**

- Produces **lipopolysaccharide (LPS)**, a potent pyrogen that explains the high fever (39.4°C) and pronounced leukocytosis\
  产生**脂多糖（LPS）**，一种强效致热原，解释了高热（39.4°C）和明显白细胞增多

**Diagnosis:** Clinical diagnosis based on postpartum fever + uterine tenderness + leukocytosis; blood and endometrial cultures guide definitive therapy.

**诊断:** 临床诊断依据为产后发热+子宫压痛+白细胞增多；血培养和子宫内膜培养指导最终治疗。

**Treatment:** IV antibiotics (classically gentamicin + clindamycin, or ampicillin-sulbactam); continued until afebrile for 24–48 hours.

**治疗:** 静脉抗生素（经典方案为庆大霉素+克林霉素，或氨苄西林-舒巴坦）；持续至退热24-48小时。

## 4. Options Elimination / 错误选项排除逻辑

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 33%" />
<col style="width: 33%" />
<col style="width: 33%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Option</strong><br />
<strong>选项</strong></th>
<th><strong>Why Wrong</strong><br />
<strong>为什么错</strong></th>
<th><strong>Key Discriminator</strong><br />
<strong>鉴别要点</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>A — Candida albicans<br />
A — 白色念珠菌</td>
<td>Why wrong: fungal pathogen causing vulvovaginitis (itching, thick white discharge); does not cause systemic fever or uterine tenderness; no leukocytosis with left shift<br />
为什么错：真菌病原体引起外阴阴道炎（瘙痒、厚白色分泌物）；不引起全身发热或子宫压痛；无核左移白细胞增多</td>
<td>No fever, no left shift; typically follows antibiotic use<br />
无发热、无核左移；通常继发于抗生素使用</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>B — Escherichia coli ✓<br />
B — 大肠杆菌 ✓</td>
<td>CORRECT — most common gram-negative enteric organism in postpartum endometritis, ascending from perineal/GI flora<br />
正确——产后子宫内膜炎中最常见的革兰阴性肠道菌，从会阴/肠道菌群上行感染</td>
<td>Gram-negative, enteric, LPS-driven fever and leukocytosis<br />
革兰阴性、肠道源性、LPS驱动发热和白细胞增多</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>C — Mycoplasma pneumoniae<br />
C — 肺炎支原体</td>
<td>Why wrong: respiratory pathogen causing atypical pneumonia; presents with cough, rhinorrhea, dyspnea — not uterine tenderness or postpartum fever<br />
为什么错：呼吸道病原体引起非典型肺炎；表现为咳嗽、流涕、呼吸困难——而非子宫压痛或产褥热</td>
<td>Pulmonary symptoms, no genital tract involvement<br />
肺部症状，无生殖道受累</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>D — Staphylococcus aureus<br />
D — 金黄色葡萄球菌</td>
<td>Why wrong: can occur in endometritis but far less common than E. coli; classically associated with toxic shock syndrome (exotoxin-mediated rash, hypotension) — absent here<br />
为什么错：可见于子宫内膜炎但远少于大肠杆菌；经典上与中毒性休克综合征相关（外毒素介导皮疹、低血压）——本例无此表现</td>
<td>Would expect desquamating rash and hypotension in TSS; BP here is normal<br />
中毒性休克综合征应有脱皮性皮疹和低血压；本例血压正常</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>E — Staphylococcus epidermidis<br />
E — 表皮葡萄球菌</td>
<td>Why wrong: skin commensal associated with catheter/hardware infections, surgical site infections, endocarditis in immunocompromised patients; not an expected endometritis pathogen<br />
为什么错：皮肤共生菌，与导管/植入物感染、手术部位感染、免疫缺陷者心内膜炎相关；不是预期的子宫内膜炎病原体</td>
<td>Requires foreign body or immunosuppression; no uterine tropism<br />
需要异物或免疫抑制；无子宫亲向性</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

*The most tempting distractor is Staphylococcus aureus (D) — remember that S. aureus can cause endometritis but E. coli is the more common isolated pathogen; S. aureus would also be expected to produce toxic shock features (hypotension, rash) not seen here.*

最容易迷惑人的干扰项是金黄色葡萄球菌（D）——需记住金黄色葡萄球菌可引起子宫内膜炎，但大肠杆菌是更常见的分离病原体；金黄色葡萄球菌还应产生本例不具备的中毒性休克特征（低血压、皮疹）。

## 6. One-Sentence Summary & Memory Hook / 一句话总结 & 记忆钩

**Postpartum fever + uterine tenderness + leukocytosis with left shift on day 1 after uncomplicated delivery = endometritis, most commonly caused by ascending E. coli.**

**产后发热+子宫压痛+核左移白细胞增多（无并发症分娩后第1天）= 子宫内膜炎，最常见病因为上行性大肠杆菌感染。**

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 100%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><p><strong>Memory Hook — FEVER after delivery / 记忆钩 — 产后发热 "FEVER" 助记:</strong></p>
<p>• <strong>F</strong>undal tenderness — the hallmark exam finding of endometritis / 宫底压痛——子宫内膜炎的标志性体征<br />
• <strong>E</strong>. coli — most common isolated organism (ascending GI/perineal flora) / 大肠杆菌——最常见分离菌（肠道/会阴菌群上行）<br />
• <strong>V</strong>aginal ascending route — bacteria travel up from lower genital tract / 阴道上行途径——细菌从下生殖道向上蔓延<br />
• <strong>E</strong>nteric polymicrobials — Enterococcus, Enterobacter, Bacteroides also involved / 多种肠道菌——肠球菌、阴沟肠杆菌、拟杆菌也参与其中<br />
• <strong>R</strong>x = gentamicin + clindamycin IV until afebrile 24–48 h / 治疗=静脉庆大霉素+克林霉素直至退热24-48小时</p></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
</tbody>
</table>

## 7. High-Yield Topic Knowledge — Postpartum Endometritis / 高频知识表 — 产后子宫内膜炎

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 50%" />
<col style="width: 50%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Topic</strong><br />
<strong>考点</strong></th>
<th><strong>Key Points</strong><br />
<strong>要点</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>Definition of puerperal fever<br />
产褥热定义</td>
<td>Temperature ≥38.0°C (100.4°F) on any 2 of the first 10 days postpartum, excluding the first 24 hours<br />
产后10天内（除第1个24小时外）任意2天体温≥38.0°C（100.4°F）</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Polymicrobial nature<br />
多菌性特点</td>
<td>Endometritis involves mixed flora: gram-negatives (E. coli, Klebsiella), gram-positives (Enterococcus, Streptococcus), anaerobes (Bacteroides, Clostridium)<br />
子宫内膜炎涉及混合菌群：革兰阴性菌（大肠杆菌、肺炎克雷伯菌）、革兰阳性菌（肠球菌、链球菌）、厌氧菌（拟杆菌、梭菌）</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Risk factors<br />
危险因素</td>
<td>Cesarean delivery (highest risk), prolonged rupture of membranes (&gt;18 hours), multiple vaginal examinations, chorioamnionitis, low socioeconomic status<br />
剖宫产（最高风险）、胎膜破裂时间延长（&gt;18小时）、多次阴道检查、绒毛膜羊膜炎、低社会经济地位</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Standard treatment regimen<br />
标准治疗方案</td>
<td>Gentamicin (2 mg/kg load, then 1.5 mg/kg q8h) + clindamycin 900 mg IV q8h; alternative: ampicillin-sulbactam or piperacillin-tazobactam<br />
庆大霉素（负荷量2 mg/kg，后1.5 mg/kg q8h）+克林霉素900 mg静脉q8h；替代方案：氨苄西林-舒巴坦或哌拉西林-他唑巴坦</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>S. aureus endometritis vs. TSS<br />
金黄色葡萄球菌子宫内膜炎 vs. 中毒性休克综合征</td>
<td>S. aureus in endometritis can release TSST-1 exotoxin → toxic shock syndrome: high fever, diffuse erythematous rash, desquamation, hypotension; absent in this case<br />
子宫内膜炎中金黄色葡萄球菌可释放TSST-1外毒素→中毒性休克综合征：高热、弥漫性红斑皮疹、脱皮、低血压；本例不存在</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Complications if untreated<br />
未治疗的并发症</td>
<td>Bacteremia, septic shock, septic pelvic thrombophlebitis (requires anticoagulation), tubo-ovarian abscess, pelvic inflammatory disease with future infertility<br />
菌血症、脓毒性休克、感染性盆腔血栓性静脉炎（需抗凝治疗）、输卵管卵巢脓肿、盆腔炎性疾病导致日后不育</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

## 8. Extensions / 延伸扩展

- **Differential of postpartum fever (the "5 W's mnemonic"):** Wind (pneumonia/atelectasis, day 1–2), Water (UTI, day 3–5), Wound (surgical site, day 5–7), Womb (endometritis, day 1–3), Walk (DVT/PE, day 5+)\
  **产褥热鉴别（"5个W"助记）:** Wind（肺炎/肺不张，第1-2天）、Water（尿路感染，第3-5天）、Wound（手术切口，第5-7天）、Womb（子宫内膜炎，第1-3天）、Walk（深静脉血栓/肺栓塞，第5天后）

- **Septic pelvic thrombophlebitis variant:** If fever persists despite 48–72 hours of IV antibiotics with no identified source, think septic pelvic thrombophlebitis; diagnosis by CT showing ovarian vein thrombus; treat with anticoagulation + antibiotics\
  **感染性盆腔血栓性静脉炎变式:** 若静脉抗生素治疗48-72小时后仍持续发热且未找到病灶，需考虑感染性盆腔血栓性静脉炎；CT显示卵巢静脉血栓可确诊；抗凝+抗生素联合治疗

- **Key distinction — chorioamnionitis vs. endometritis:** Chorioamnionitis occurs antepartum/intrapartum (fever + uterine tenderness + fetal tachycardia before/during delivery); endometritis is postpartum (after delivery, same clinical features minus fetal signs)\
  **关键鉴别——绒毛膜羊膜炎 vs. 子宫内膜炎:** 绒毛膜羊膜炎发生于产前/产时（分娩前后出现发热+子宫压痛+胎心过速）；子宫内膜炎为产后（分娩后出现相同临床特征但无胎儿体征）

- **E. coli virulence factor relevance:** E. coli LPS (endotoxin) triggers TLR4 signaling → IL-1, IL-6, TNF-α release → fever, leukocytosis, vasodilation; understanding this explains why gram-negative sepsis can be rapidly life-threatening\
  **大肠杆菌毒力因子的临床意义:** 大肠杆菌LPS（内毒素）触发TLR4信号→释放IL-1、IL-6、TNF-α→发热、白细胞增多、血管扩张；理解这一机制可解释为何革兰阴性菌脓毒症可迅速危及生命
